piziologia
 ekonomika da soplis meurneoba 
  . tsinasitqvaobamiukhedavad „vardebis revolutsiis“ shemdeg sakartveloshi gatarebuli repormebisa, kveqnisekonomikashi kvlavats aramdgradi vitareba da bevri gamotsvevaa. ertis mkhriv,   tslidansagadasakhado garemos gaumjobesebam da biurokratiis shemtsirebam sainvestitsio nakadebis damshp-s zrda gamoitsvia, magram meores mkhriv, sakutrebis uplebis datsvis da skhva problemebma,shemdgom   tslis rusulma agresiam, msoplio krizisis gavlenam da biznes-garemoshikhelisuplebis negatiurma charevam ekonomikis mdgradoba mnishvnelovnad sheasusta. gaizardakveqnis sagareo vali, gauaresda sagadamkhdelo balansis mdgomareoba da shemtsirdasainvestitsio nakadebi. nominaluri mshp-s pormaluri zrda ekonomikuri ganvitarebistsinapirobad ver iktsa, ris gamots sazogadoebis ketildgheoba bolo tslebshi argaumjobesebula. pirikit, gaizarda umushevroba da sigharibis zghvars kvemot mqopiadamianebis raodenoba, kveqnis mosakhleobis  %-ze meti kvlav sotsialurad dautsvelia. esmkholod problemebis arasruli chamonatvalia da mkholod zogadad asakhavs kveqnisekonomikashi arsebul mdgomareobasa tu tendentsiebs.aset pirobebshi mnishvnelovania, shestsavlili iknas kveqnis sotsialur-ekonomikurimdgomareoba da tendentsiebi, mightsevebi da khelisuplebis mier dashvebuli shetsdomebi, ratadaisvas stsori diagnozi samomavlod ekonomikis mdgradi ganvitarebis uzrunvelsaqopadda sazogadoebis ketildgheobis shesamchnevad gasaumjobeseblad.amitomats, sakartvelos ganvitarebis kvlevitma institutma, mkvlevar ekonomisttajguptan ertad gadatsqvita chaetarebina sakartvelos ekonomikashi arsebuli mdgomareobissamagido kvleva da moemzadebina mokrdzalebuli kontseptsia kveqanashi sotsialur-ekonomikuri mdgomareobis gaumjobesebisatvis.nashromshi motsemulia sakartvelos ekonomikashi arsebuli problemebi da mati sighrme (m.sh.ideologiuri problemebi), aseve khelisuplebis ekonomikuri politikis naklovanebebi dachveneuli rekomendatsiebi mdgomareobis gasaumjobeseblad. nashromshi tsalkea gamoqopilibiznes-garemoshi arsebuli mdgomareoba da khelisuplebis sainvestitsio politika,konkurentsiis spero da momkhmareblis uplebebis datsvis sakitkhebi. ojakhis da individisproblematika, mati mdgomareobis gaumjobesebis gzebi da sashualebebi nashromshi aseve tsalketavad aris gamoqopili. am qvelapertan ertad, moqvanilia aseve makroekonomikuristabilizatsiis mimartulebebi rogorts piskaluri, aseve monetaruli tvalsazrisit(sabiujeto sistema da sagareo valis problematika, gatsvliti kursi da inplatsia).titeul tematikas tan akhlavs rekomendatsiebi, tu rogor unda gaumjobesdes mdgomareobaama tu im mimartulebit.kveqnis mosakhleobis nakherze meti agrarul sektorshia dakavebuli da am sektoris tsili mshp-shi meatedsats ver aghtsevs, is gansakutrebuli shestsavlis sagani unda iqos. amitomats, chveni   
  . samushao jgupis mier shestsavlili ikna aseve sakartvelos soplis meurneobis mdgomareobada tendentsiebi. detaluri analizi da shesabamisi rekomendatsiebi am gamotsemis meorenatsilshia tsarmodgenili. agrarul sektorshi problemebis gamokvetis garda, shedarebitghrmadaa momzadebuli rekomendatsiebi sam umnishnelovanes temaze. esenia: sasoplo-sameurneo teknikit uzrunvelqopa; melioratsia; soplis meurneobis dapinanseba dadazghveva.sakartvelos ganvitarebis kvleviti instituti da mkvlevarta jgupi madlierebitmiigheben qvela sakmian shenishvnas da mosazrebas, rats emsakhureba tsinamdebare dokumentissrulqopas da sakartvelos ekonomikashi arsebuli mdgomareobis gaumjobesebas.sakartvelos ganvitarebis kvleviti instituti,mkvlevarta jgupi.   
  . shesabamisad, ganvitarebis strategia tsarmoudgenelia misi samizne indikatorebshisrulpasovani aghtseris gareshe. amastan indikatorebis rogorts struktura, aseveoptimaluri machveneblebi, dinamiur kavshirshi unda iqos mimdinare ekonomikurgamotsvevebtan da sazogadoebrivi ketildgheobis realur surats unda asakhavdes.tskhadia, rom samizne parametrebis simravle guliskhmobs am parametrebisaken stsrapvispunktsiis arsebobasats. tumtsa akhali ekonomikuri politikis mizani araa qvela am punktsiisshesruleba sakhelmtsipom aighos sakutar tavze. pirikit, chveni urqevi rtsmenit, qvela ispunktsia, sadats kerdzo initsiativa upro met epektianobas, energias da initsiativasganapirobebs, tsalsakhad unda gaimijnos sajaro administrirebis sivrtsisagan. meore mkhriv,migvachnia, rom uaris tkma tavisupali konkurentsiis khelshetsqobis, momkhmarebeltauplebebis datsvis, sasursato usaprtkhoebis uzrunvelqopis da mit umetes sotsialuripasukhismgeblobis punktsiebze pirdapir miutitebs mtavrobis mier sazogadoebisinteresebis ignorirebaze.mokmedi ekonomikuri politikis mier gaukmebuli punktsiebis aghdgena, iseve rogortsarsebuli da damakhinjebuli punktsiebis optimizatsia sheudzlebelia dzireuliinstitutsionaluri repormis gareshe. prosakhelisuplo propaganda mokmed sajaromokheleebs umtkitsebs, rom institutsionaluri reporma qvela matganis usapudzvlodatkhovnas nishnavs. martlats, aseti kmedeba khshirad hkonda adgili iqo „vardebisrevolutsiis“ shemdgom periodshi, magram chven printsipulad migvachnia sajaro samsakhurshikompetenturi gadatsqvetilebis uplebamosilebis dabruneba, tanats ise, rom mokhelemudmivad shishis kvesh ar iqos kanonieri kmedebebis gamo. sajaro samsakhuris sazogadoebrivisargeblianobis amaghlebis autsileblobastan dakavshirebuli chveni pozitsia, upirvelesqovlisa stsored sajaro mokheleta mier inpormirebuli, kompetenturi da damoukidebeligadatsqvetilebebis mighebis stimulirebashi gamoikhateba.dghes arsebuli sagangasho realobisagan ganskhvavebit, institutsionaluri repormis chvenikhedva nishnavs evropuli tipis institutebisaken stsrapvas. ra tkma unda chveni mizani ar arisevrokavshirtan sruli sistemuri identuroba (radgan totaluri unipitsirebaevrokavshirshits ar arsebobs), magram evrointegratsia grantebis misaghebad gankhortsielebulipasaduri tsvlilebebi ar da ver ikneba - chveni mizania sakartvelo evropuli ojakhissrulpasovani tsevri gakhdes.ganvitarebis strategiis pormirebisas chven srulad vatsnobierebt im organul riskebs,romlebits geopolitikuri tu globaluri ekonomikuri realiebit aris gamotsveuli,magram mokmedma ekonomikurma politikam shekmna problemebi, romlebits aris organulikhasiatis. pirvel rigshi, importze orientirebulma ekonomikurma politikam ganapirobadanazogebis sagangasho gamopitva da khangrdzlivi droit uarqopit nishnulshi gadasvlats ki,rats imas nishnavda, rom sazogadoeba imaze mets kharjavda vidre gamoimushavebda. paktiuradmtavrobam mizanmimartulad sheutsqo kheli „samomkhmareblo sazogadoebis“ shekmnas. chveniprintsipuli amotsanaa mozmarebaze orientatsia (konsumerizmi), sheitsvalos dagrovebaze   
  . utskhoetidan shemosuli sakredito resursebis sashualebit. es nishnavs imas, rom ekonomikurizrdis qvela paktoris absoluturi umravlesoba iqo sagareo, umetes tsilad, atarebdapinansuri inektsiebis rols da motsqvetili iqo ekonomikis realur sektors. pinansuriinektsiebis dzalzed mtsire natsili ikna mimartuli iset speroebshi, romelits tsarmoebismotsulobis gapartovebaze/tsarmoebis zrdaze ikneboda orientirebuli da dziritadadganapiroba mokhmarebis tempebis zrda gatsilebit metad, vidre ekonomikis tsarmoebis unariszrda. tu mokhmarebas uporo mkvetrad vzrdit, vidre satsarmoo shesadzleblobebs,autsilebel kanonzomierebas tsarmoadgens, rom es politika migviqvans chikhamde da, aseve,skhvadaskhva tipis kreditorul davalianebebamde, rogorts kveqnis shignit, aseve misparglebs garet, radgan tviton es mokhmareba umetestsilad uzrunvelqopilia kveqnisdavalianebebis zrdit, da ara mtsarmoeblurobis. kidev erti makhasiatebeli chveniekonomikisa aris is, rom mnishvnelovnad gaizarda importis motsuloba eksporttanshedarebit, ris gamots utskhouri inektsiebis da shemosuli sakhsrebis shemosuli natsili isevutskhoetshi gaitsova importis gzit ise, rom kveqnis realur sektorze mnishvnelovani kvali ardautovebia. es gansakutrebit sheekheba vachrobis, msheneblobis, pinansuri sektoris dasakhelmtsipo sektoris kharjebis tsalkeul mskhvil mimartulebebs.rodesats ekonomikuri ganvitarebaze vsaubrobt, upirveles qovlisa, mnishvnelovania, turamdenad gaizarda kveqnis unari atsarmoos meti sasoplo-sameurneo, samretsvelo sakonelida momsakhureba. arts sakhelmtsipo politika, arts utskhouri investitsiebi da arts komertsiulibankebis mier gamartuli sakredito dapinanseba ar itvalistsinebda soplis meurneobisganvitarebas. shesabamisad, sakartvelos regionebis absolutur umravlesobashi, sadatsmosakhleobis  % tskhovrobs da samushao dzalis  %, romlebits dakavshirebulni arianushualod soplis meurneobastan, mdgomareoba gauaresda. dghes damushavebulia gatsilebitnaklebi sasoplo sameurneo savargulebi (  tsels natesi kulturebis partobi sheadgenda .  at. ha-s,   tsels -  .  at. ha-s da   tsels -  .  at ha-s), vidre ramdenime tslis tsinda dghes itsarmeoba gatsilebit naklebi soplis meurneobis produktsia (  tsels  tseltan shedarebit pulad gamokhatulebashi (optsialuri inplatsiis gatvalistsinebit)   %it naklebi produktsia ikna tsarmoebuli soplis meurneobashi da es klebadi tendentsiagrdzeldeba qoveltsliurad da amastan inplatsiis upro adekvaturi asakhvis shemtkhvevashishemtsireba savaraudod upro metia), vidre ramdenime tslis tsin, kholo sursatis mokhmarebashimnishvnelovnad gazrdilia importirebuli produktsiis tsili samamulo produktsiastanshedarebit. mkholod es paktorits ki sakmarisia, itkvas, rom, sul mtsire, mosakhleobisnakhevristvis „ekonomikur zrdas“ mdgomareoba ar gaumjobesebia da, pirikit, gaauaresa. amistkmis sapudzvels idzleva, agretve, is garemoeba, rom ekonomikis skhva sektorebshi, kerdzod,mretsvelobashi ar dapiksirebula ganmapirobeblad, im sakitkhis, rom „ghmertebs noqieri zetsa dakhvdat“
postsabchota sivrtseshi. tamaz panjikidze tsers :postsabchour sivrtseshi qvelgan asea,
asea chvenshits. martlats, vighas ar nakhavt kartul zetsaze - kristianul samebas,

iehovas, skhvadaskhva denominatsiebis mier taviseburad gagebul ghmertebs, mravals
da mravals. titoeul matgans zetsashi akvs michenili bina da matze mati
taqvanismtsemlebi aghavlenen lotsvas... tu im mtsir statistikur analizs
daveqrdnobit rats sakartveloshi arsebobs, chveni kveqnis  % gakhlavt
martlmadidebeli kristiani, danarchen  %s inatsileben skhvadaskhva konpesiebi da
sektebi. aris tu ara chems kveqanashi rtsmena tavisupali? anu, edzleva tu ara qvela

chems azrze daqrdnoba momitsevs, rodesats temaze mushaoba davitsqe davinteresdi
kvlevebit da dzalian gamaotsa paktma rom msgavsi tipis kvleva praktikulad ar
arsebobs. am ramdenime khnis tsin sakartvelos sakhalkho damtsveltan momitsia
intervius chatsera, kitkhvaze ramdenad khshiria religiuri nishnit adamianebis
uplebebis darghveva, batonma ucha nanuashvilma mipasukha, rom erteuli shemtkhvevebi,
romlebits piksirdeba msgavsi tipis darghvevebad sagangashod ver chaitvleba, rom
chvens kveqanashi rtsmena tavisupalia. man ikve problemad dasakha sakhelmtsipo
politika, romelits mkholod ert konpesias apinansebs sakhelmtsipo biujetidan.
ori tslis tsin sakartvelos samokalako kodeksshi tsvlileba shevida, am tsvlilebis
tanakhmad sakartveloshi arsebul qvela konpesias upleba mietsa daregistrirdes
rogorts arasametsarmeo iuridiuli piri, anu hkondes statusi. didi vnebataghelva
mohqva martlmadidebeli mrevlisgan mashin am sakitkhs, akats or sakitkhze
gavamakhvilebdi me piradad mashin quradghebas, rit iqo ganpirobebuli kanonis
dachkarebulad migheba? tu es sakitkhi aseti aktualuri gakhldat ratom
daregistrirda sajaro samartlis iuridiul pirad mkholod baptistur
evangelisturi eklesia? me mashinve gaminchda kitkhvebi, arsebobda tu ara realurad
problema? rad ar gakhda tsvlilebebis shetanamde kanonproekti sajaro da ratom ar
mokhda misi gankhilva sajaro sivrtseshi? ristvis iqo sachiro kanonis dachkarebuli
tsesit migheba, mashin rotsa amisi motkhovna skhva konpesiebis mier ar qopila? sajaro
gankhilva sheutsqobda tu ara khels mosakhleobis stsor inpormirebulobas, (rogorts
dominanti eklesiis mrevlis aseve umtsiresobebis), avitsilebdit tu ara
vnebataghelvas tavidan? sainteresoa ra khdeba am tvalsazrisit msoplios tsamqvan
kveqnebshi? evropis kveqnebis umravlesoba sekularulia, mkholod ramdenime kveqanas
akvs sakhelmtsipo eklesiaebi. imisda miukhedavad, rom sekularul kveqnebs rtsmenis
tavisupleba konstitutsiit akvt gatskhadebuli, maints arsebobs dominanti eklesia,
romelsats sakhelmtsipo apinansebs. dapinansebis tsessats titoeuli kveqana tavad
tsqvets, raime modeli, romelzetsaa morgebuli evropuli politika am
tvalsazrisit ar arsebobs. tu parlamentis analitikur kvlevas daveqrdnobit,
evropashi sakhelmtsiposa da eklesiis urtiertoba dziritadad istoriuli da
kulturuli taviseburebebis gatvalitsinebit tsarimarteba da dapinansebis tsessats
tavad tsqvets, zoggan mkholod erti eklesia pinansdeba sakhelmtsipos mier, zoggan
mkholod saganmanatleblo sakmianoba, zoggan mrevlis simravlis proportsiulad....
(mogekhsenebat inpormatsiis simtsire araertkhel aghvnishne temis mimokhilvisas, akve
dzalian sainteresoa sakhelmtsipo biujetidan dapinansebuli eklesia vistanaa
angarishvaldebuli? anu rogor khdeba im pulis modzieba da kontroli romlitats
eklesia pinansdeba. rogorts sakartveloshi, ise evropis kveqnebshi). chvens kveqanashi
dominant religias, anu kartul samotsikulo avtokepalur eklesiasa da
sakhelmtsipos shoris urtiertobas aregulirebs konkordati, sakonstitutsio
shetankhmeba, romelits itvalistsinebs ra sakartvelos istoriashi eklesiis
rols,garkveul privilegiebs anichebs kartul samotsikulo eklesias.(ramdenadats
chemtvis tsnobilia,es shetankhmeba daido skhva religiis msakhurebtan konsultatsiebis
shemdeg da matgan mighebuli pormaluri tankhmobis arsebobis pirobebshi) chemi
dghevandeli msjelobit akhali araperi mitkvams, mkholod im tsesebze mogakhsenet,
rats chems kveqanashia. religia tavsebadia tu ara chems kveqanashi demokratiastan? am
kitkhvaze dzalian saintereso pasukhi gastsa samotsikulo eklesiis mghvdelma,
damghupvelia tu ara sekularizmi kartuli eklesiisatvis? man gastsa pasukhi:
sekularizmi araa damghupvel-damzianebeli samotsikulo eklesiis, iseve rogorts
skhva konpesieb tu sektebi. namdvili problema eklesiis aris eklesiis tsiaghshi
mqopi arakompetenturi adamianebi.“ tanamedrove eklesiis shignit arsebul
problemebze tu avlaparakdebit es mkholod siketes moutans chvens kveqanas. . me

problema dgas msoplio masshtabit, globalizatsia postreligiur samqaros
gvikadis, tavad religia tsdilobs sakutar tavshi chaiketos da ase sheinarchunos
tvitmqopadoba, (dzalauplebao amtkitsebs mavani) pakti ertia , globalizatsiam ver
gakhada samqaro religiastan mimartebashi gulgrili. amitom sachiroa okros
shualedis gamonakhva. rats chvens kveqanas sheekheba, bolodroindelma kvlevebma achvena
rom sakartvelos eklesia qvela politikosze
maghali ndobit sargeblobs
sakartvelos mosakhleobashi, pakti ertia, religia adamianta gulebsa da gonebaze
isev didi gavlenis mkonea, stsored amadaa sachiro reporma tavad eklesiashi.
reporma vakhsene, tema sensitiuria, mrevli mgrdznobiare kritikis mimarto
gamkitskhavs mavani, tumtsa erti paktia, tavad kristianuli religia siketis
siqvarulis da satnoebis tsqaroao khshirad visment, religia tu akhal stadiashi ar
shevida tuki pekhi ar autsqo progress anu mrevlis ganvitarebas, sotsialur protsess,
da bolosdabolos, tu tavad ar iktsa mimteveblobis, satnoebis siqvarulis da
maghali zneobis magalitad, nelnela dakargavs ndobas. es problemats, anu religia
maradiuli unda iqos tu progresirebadi, mkholod kartul realobashi ar dgas.
metsnierebis da teologebis gansjis sagania, me vetankhmebi azrs, rom religia ar
unda dashordes khalkhs.
bevri avtori iqenebs amatuim eris an rasis dasakhasiateblad shesastsavli khalkhis
religiur shekhedulebebs.sazogadoebis politikur organizatsiastan ertad es
parametri uaghresad mnishvnelovania imis gasarkvevad,ganvitarebis ra etapze
dgas es tu is khalkhi.khalkhis tsnobiereba qvelaze upro imashi vlindeba,rogoria
adamianis tvitidentipikatsia ghmerttan mimartebashi,aseve mnishvnelovania
rogor atsnobierebs sakutar pirovnebas adamiani sazogadoebastan mimartebashi.

protsesia.religiur nairgvarobaze bevri ramis tkma sheidzleba, aseve
mravalperovania demokratiuli sakhelmtsipoebis mmartvelobis porma,ase,rom
