 iberiul-kavkasiuri saertashoriso sametsniero tsentri 
 tariel putkaradze tariel putkaradze "evropuli kartia regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb" da 
 "evropuli kartia regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb" da sakartveloshi enobrivi politikis dagegmvis sakitkhi 
 tsarmodgenil tsignshi avtors miznad akvs achvenos, rom: - "regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartia" ("enis kartia") tavisi arsit nateli da maghali donis dokumentia; igi ar sheitsavs romelime kveqnistvis sakhipato debulebebs. "enis kartia" khels utsqobs skhva sakhelmtsipoebriv velshi moktseuli avtoktoni umtsiresobis enobriv-kulturuli memkvidreobis shenarchunebas. - "enis kartiisa" da haagis tu oslos "rekomendatsiebis" miznebis gamijvnisa da printsipebis gatvalistsinebis shemtkhvevashi, sakhelmtsipo enis punktsiis dakninebis gareshe sakartveloshits da skhva kveqnebshits shesadzlebelia: ¾ satanado statusi ganesazghvros kveqanashi arsebul qvela lingvistur erteuls; ¾ khelisuplebis mier daisakhos nateli amotsanebi istoriuli umtsiresobis enis, rogorts kulturuli memkvidreobis, shenarchuneba-ganvitarebisatvis; ¾ realurad iknas datsuli dziritadi mosakhleobis, istoriuli umtsiresobis, akhali umtsiresobisa tu migrantebis tsarmomadgenelta enobrivi uplebebi. 
 shesavali ........................................................................................................  evrosabchos tsinashe aghebuli ori valdebulebis mokle istoria ...  
 "evropuli kartiis" dziritadi termini: regionuli an umtsiresobis ena................................................................................   
 evrosabchos tsevr romel sakhelmtsiposhi mtskhovreb kartvelta enis mimart unda gavrtseldes, erti mkhriv, evropuli kartiis debulebebi, meore mkhriv - haagisa da oslos rekomendatsiebi, mesame mkhriv ki - kanoni migrantta shesakheb? ....................................  daskvniti msjeloba ..............................................................................  
 ratom sheikmna evropuli kartia regionuli an umtsiresobis enis shesakheb? .............................................................................................   "erovnul umtsiresobata shesakheb charcho konventsiisa" da "oslos rekomendatsiebis" mizani: akhali umtsiresobebis enobrivi uplebebis datsva ..............................................................................  "evropuli kartiis" mizani: istoriuli umtsiresobebis dedaenis datsva .................................................................................  enata sakheebi "kartiis" mikhedvit......................................................   sakartvelo: sakhelmtsipos opitsialuri ena da misi adgilobrivi sakheskhvaobani ........................................................    . . sakhelmtsipo ena ............................................................................    . . sakhelmtsipo enebi avtonomiur tsarmonakmnshi ....................    . . sakhelmtsipo enis adgilobrivi sakheskhvaoba ......................   sakartveloshi romelia istoriuli etnikuri umtsiresobis ena? ........................................................................................................    . . istoriuli regionuli ena....................................................    . . regionshits umtsiresobis ena.....................................................    . . konkretuli regionis armkone istoriuli ena teritoriis armkone ena...........................................................   
 araistoriuli umtsiresobis enebi: diasporata da migrantta enebi sakartveloshi ................................................................................  aris tu ara sakartvelo multietnikuri tu mravalerovani kveqana? vin sheidzleba chaitvalos: istoriul etnikur 
 evrosabchos tsinashe aghebuli ori valdebulebis mokle istoria evrosabchos tsinashe aghebuli valdebulebis shesabamisad, sakartvelos khelisuplebam   tslis   ianvars kheli moatsera "konventsias erovnul umtsiresobata shesakheb" . sakartvelos parlamentma am saertashoriso dokumentis ratipikatsia moakhdina   tsels . amis miukhedavad,   tsels evrosabchos saparlamento asambleis  -e   rezolutsiis me-  punkti sakartvelos khelisuplebas saqvedurobs am evrokonventsiis miugheblobis gamo . gaugebaria:   tsels evrosabchos saparlamento asambleis  -e rezolutsia ratom itkhovs sakartvelosgan   tsels ratipitsirebuli "erovnul umtsiresobata datsvis shesakheb charcho konventsiis" ratipitsirebas? aseti didi mnishvnelobis mkone dokumentis dadasturebis shesakheb inpormatsia   tslis mandzilze ar mietsoda evrosabchos?  
 evrosabchos saparlamento asambleis saqvedurebi; tsarmovadgent zogierts:   tseli,   sektemberi, evrosabchos saparlamento asambleis angarishi: "sakartvelos mier tavisi valdebulebebisa da danapirebis shesruleba": "asamblea tsukhils gamotkvams imis gamo, rom sakartvelom khelmotseris da ratipikatsiis gareshe datova "evropis kartia regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb" ...   tseli:   ivniss strasburgshi evropis sabchos generalur mdivans - teri deviss shekhvda sakartvelos iustitsiis ministri kote kemularia; evropis sabchos inpormatsiit, mkhareebma ganikhiles organizatsiis tsinashe sakartvelos valdebulebebis shesrulebis sakitkhi; kerdzod, erovnul umtsiresobata datsvis charcho konventsiis, regionuli da umtsiresobis enebis evropuli kartiisa da ganakhlebuli sotsialuri kartiis ratipitsirebis   sakitkhebi .   tseli: evrosabchos saparlamento asambleis rezolutsia (№ ) sakartvelos mier aghebuli   valdebulebebisa da shetankhmebebis shesakheb : "asamblea rekomendatsias adzlevs sakartvelos   mtavrobas, rom ratipitsirebul iqos konventsia erovnuli umtsiresobebis shesakheb, aseve evropuli konventsia transsasazghvro tanamshromlobis shesakheb da evrosabchos siskhlis samartlis konventsia koruptsiis shesakheb. samtsukharod, evropuli konventsia “regionuli da umtsiresobata enebis shesakheb ” ratipitsirebuli ar aris da arts aranairi progresi amastan dakavshirebit ar sheimchneva (me-  punkti). ...im dros, rotsa sakhezea repormebis gankhortsielebis tanmimdevroba, asamblea tvlis, rom spetsialuri   
 ghonisdziebebi unda iknes gankhortsielebuli, rata daachkaros politikuri repormebis gankhortsieleba, romelits sakartvelos miaakhlovebs stabilur da tsarmatebul evropul demokratiastan... kerdzod, evrokonventsiastan dakavshirebit, aghsanishnavia shemdegi: qovelgvari dabrkolebis gareshe kheli moetseros da ratipitsireba mokhdes evropis kartiis regionul an umtsiresobebis enaze" (me-  punkti) . rogorts zemot itkva, evrokavshiris tsevri sakhelmtsipoebis erti natsili jerjerobit "kartias" khels ar atsers (mag., turketi, albaneti, bulgareti, latvia, litva, portugalia...).. meore natsili (ruseti, saprangeti, italia, azerbaijani, poloneti...) ki ratipikatsias aqovnebs ; mizezi: problemuria istoriuli (avtoktoni) da akhali umtsiresobebis (etnikuri jgupebis) enebis gamijvna; garda amisa, chans, mtavrobebi uprtkhian dezintegratsiul protsesebs. amgvarive shishit sheidzleba aikhsnas sakartvelos khelisuplebis siprtkhilets; sashishroeba martlats arsebobs, magram ara sakartvelos realobidan gamomdinare, aramed "regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartiis" debulebebis arastsori, sakartvelostvis sakhipato interpretatsiebis gamo. problemas kmnis isits, rom sakartvelos shesabamisi institutebis mier dghemde ver chamoqalibda is 
 upro zustad: terminologiuri shesitqveba. ikh., me-  ganmarteba.   da ara - akhali umtsiresobis enas.   shdr.: "kartiis" mizania istoriuli umtsiresobis enis datsva da ara etnikuri (kulturuli) umtsiresobis enobrivi uplebebis chamoqalibeba (ikh., kvemot).   targmanisatvis ikh.:   
 opitsialurad sakartvelos aseti valdebuleba ar aughia; garda amisa, tsesit, sakartvelos ekspertebis/khelisuplebis opitsialuri daskvnis gareshe evrosabchos dokumentshi ar sheidzleba iqos saubari sakartvelos romelime konkretuli enis, an misi sakheskhvaobis tu kilos shesakheb.   
 ikh., pirveli mukhli da me- -  ganmartebani. 
 mashasadame, shegvidzlia davaskvnat: kartiis miznidan  gamomdinare, termini: regionuli an umtsiresobis ena guliskhmobs erti kategoriis, magram sami variantit gamovlenil enas:  . regionuli ena - sakhelmtsipos motsemuli regionis avtoktoni mosakhleobis ena, tuki am enaze metqveli sazogadoeba umravlesobaa motsemul regionshi (kartiis me  ganmarteba) ;  . umtsiresobis ena - sakhelmtsipos motsemuli regionis avtoktoni mosakhleobis ena, tuki am enaze metqveli sazogadoeba umtsiresobaa motsemul regionshits (kartiis me  ganmarteba) ;  . teritoriis armkone ena - motsemul sakhelmtsiposhi mtskhovrebi iseti istoriuli mosakhleobis ena, romelsats ar gaachnia gansazghvruli geograpiuli areali ( -e   ganmarteba) . 
 istoriuli etnikuri umtsiresobis enobriv-kulturuli tvitmqopadobis datsva.   kvalipikatsia skhvagvarad asets sheidzleba chamoqalibdes: motsemul sakhelmtsiposhi istoriulad mtskhovrebi iseti etnikuri umtsiresobis ena, romelzets metqvelebs am kveqnis ert regionshi mtskhovrebi mosakhleobis umravlesoba; an: sakhelmtsiposhi avtoktoni umtsiresobis, magram motsemul regionshi umravlesobis ena.   motsemul sakhelmtsiposhi istoriulad mtskhovrebi iseti erovnuli/etnikuri umtsiresobis ena, romelzets metqvelebs am kveqnis ert regionshi kompakturad mtskhovrebi mosakhleoba, magram es khalkhi umtsiresobaa am regionshits; an: sakhelmtsiposhi avtoktoni umtsiresobis da motsemul regionshits umtsiresobis ena.   motsemul sakhelmtsiposhi istoriulad mtskhovrebi iseti erovnuli/etnikuri umtsiresobis ena, romelits kompakturad ar/aghar tskhovrobs am kveqnis arts ert regionshi. 
 ratom sheikmna evropuli kartia regionuli an umtsiresobis enis shesakheb? "kartiis" preambula imtavitve atskhadebs: "evropis istoriuli regionuli tu umtsiresobis enebis datsva, romeltaganats zogierts saboloo gakroba emukreba, khels utsqobs evropis kulturuli simdidrisa da traditsiebis shenarchuneba-ganvitarebas". ganmartebiti mokhsenebis pirvelive punktshi vkitkhulobt: "evropis mravali sakhelmtsipos teritoriaze tskhovroben ama tu im regionis mkvidri avtoktoni romelta dedaena ganskhvavdeba kveqnis jgupebi , mosakhleobis umravlesobis enisagan. es imitaa ganpirobebuli, rom istoriulad sakhelmtsipota pormireba ar khdeboda mkholod enobrivi nishnit da mati tsarmokmnis protsesshi mimdinareobda mtsire khalkhebis shertsqma upro mskhvil etnikur erteulebtan" . "kartiis" umtavresi mizani kulturulhumanitaruli khasiatisaa. igi motsodebulia daitsvas da kheli sheutsqos regionuli tu umtsiresobis enebis, rogorts evropis saerto kulturuli memkvidreobis ganuqopeli natsilis, gamoqenebasa da ganvitarebas... misi amotsanaa, shedzlebisdagvarad uzrunvelqos regionuli tu umtsiresobis enebis gamoqeneba ganatlebis sistemasa da masobrivi inpormatsiis sashualebebshi; kheli sheutsqos am enebze mkhatvruli literaturisa da samtsignobro kulturis chamoqalibebas, dasashvebi gakhados mati 
 gamoqeneba martlmsajulebisa da administratsiuli organoebis sakmianobashi, agretve sazogadoebis ekonomikur, sotsialur da kulturul tskhovrebashi... kartiis mizania evropashi regionuli tu umtsiresobis enebis datsva, erovnuli identobis pormirebaze khelshetsqoba (da ara - enobrivi umtsiresobebis enobrivi uplebebis datsva). shesabamisad, mtavari quradgheba etmoba sakitkhis kulturul aspektebs da regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis gamoqenebas am enebze molaparake khalkhis tskhovrebis qvela speroshi. "kartia" ar adgens regionul tu umtsiresobis enebze molaparaketa individualur tu kolektiur uplebebs (me- -  ganmartebani). shdr., agretve: "regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartiis" mizania evropashi istoriulad gavrtselebuli regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis datsva, romeltagan zogs gakroba emukreba . akve ikh. agretve,  -e da  -e punktebi: "kartiis debulebebi moitsavs mkholod istoriul enebs, anu im enebs, romlebits didi khania gavrtselebulia motsemuli sakhelmtsipos teritoriaze" "; es enebi mkapiod unda ganskhvavdebodes im enis an enebisagan, romelzets sakhelmtsiposhi mtskhovrebi danarcheni mosakhleoba saubrobs. kartiis debulebebi ar ekheba erti enis adgilobriv sakheskhvaobebsa tu dialektebs". evrosabchos skhva dokumentebshits araertkhelaa khazgasmuli, rom "regionuli da umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartiis" mizania im enebis datsva, 
 miukhedavad amisa, saertashoriso tanamegobrobam maints chatvala sachirod, ertmanetisgan gaemijna da sakanonmdeblo aktebits tsal-tsalke gamoetsa istoriuli (avtoktoni) etnikuri umtsiresobis enisa da akhali tsarmomadgenelta individualuri umtsiresobebis  enobrivi uplebebis dasatsavad. mag., eksperti asborn eidi tsers: "gaeros sistemashi nateli ganskhvavebaa chamoqalibebuli istoriuli (aborigeni) umtsiresobebis uplebebsa da im pirta uplebebs shoris, romlebits umtsiresobebs miekutvnebian" . zogadad, erovnuli (etnikuri) umtsiresobebis enobrivi uplebebi datsulia qvela normaluri sakhelmtsipos konstitutsiita  da shida kanonmdeblobis skhva samartlebrivi dokumentebit; aseve: "erovnul an etnikur, religiur da enobriv umtsiresobata uplebebis gaeros deklaratsiit" , eutos oslosa  da lundis  
   termin "akhali umtsiresobis" shesakheb ikh., robert dunbaris akve (zemot) damotsmebuli statia, sadats sagangebo msjelobaa aseve istoriuli umtsiresobisa da akhali umtsiresobis enobrivkulturuli uplebebis skhvadaskhvaobis shesakheb.   "komentarebi: globaluri da regionuli midgomebi umtsiresobebis situatsiebtan", charchos shevseba, dokumentebis krebuli,  , gv.  .   ikh., mag., sakartvelos konstitutsia, mukhli  :  . sakartvelos mokalakeni tanastsori arian sotsialur, ekonomikur, kulturul da politikur tskhovrebashi ganurchevlad mati erovnuli, etnikuri, religiuri tu enobrivi kutvnilebisa. saertashoriso samartlis saqoveltaod aghiarebuli printsipebisa da normebis shesabamisad, mat upleba akvt tavisuplad, qovelgvari diskriminatsiisa da charevis gareshe ganavitaron tavianti kultura, isargeblon dedaenit pirad tskhovrebashi da sajarod... .mukhli  : samartaltsarmoeba khortsieldeba sakhelmtsipo enaze. pirs, romelmats sakhelmtsipo ena ar itsis, miechineba tarjimani... 
 rekomendatsiebit; evrosabchos "charcho konventsiit erovnul umtsiresobata datsvis shesakheb" . kholo, "evropuli kartia regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb" aris is ertaderti sagangebo saertashoriso samartlebrivi dokumenti, romelits miedzghvna im avtoktoni mosakhleobis enobriv-kulturuli tvitmqopadobis datsvas, romelits motsemul sakhelmtsiposhi umtsiresobas tsarmoadgens da, amave dros, misi dedaena am kveqanashi (an mis romelime mkhareshi) ar aris sakhelmtsipo ena. "enis kartiashi" aktsenti gaketebulia kulturul mravalperovnebaze; kerdzod, kulturisa da traditsiebis gadarchena-shenarchunebasa da ganvitarebaze da ara umtsiresobis tsarmomadgenelis individualur enobriv uplebebze . shdr.: charcho konventsiit gansazghvruli "umtsiresobata uplebebi moiazreba rogorts individualuri uplebebi, tumtsa zogjer sheidzleba mokmedebdes skhva individebtan ertobliobashi. umtsiresobata uplebebi tavisi bunebit ar aris jgupuri uplebebi".   meti tvalsachinoebistvis, momdevno paragrapebshi mokled tsarmovadgent masalebs akhali umtsiresobebis enobrivi uplebebisa da istoriuli umtsiresobis enis datsvis shesakheb. 
 imave   tsels haagashi shemushavda "rekomendatsiebi erovnul umtsiresobata ganatlebis uplebata shesakheb"; am dokuments   tslis shemdeg mohqva erovnul umtsiresobata enobrivi uplebebis damtsveli dokumentits: "oslos rekomendatsiebi erovnul umtsiresobata enobriv uplebebtan dakavshirebit" (tebervali,   tseli), sadats detaluradaa chamoqalibebuli motsemul sakhelmtsiposhi erovnul umtsiresobas mikutvnebuli sazogadoebis enobrivi uplebebi; kerdzod, tsarmovadgent ramdenime mukhls:  . erovnul umtsiresobebs mikutvnebul pirebs upleba akvt isargeblon tavianti sakhelebita da gvarebit mshobliur enaze, sakutari traditsiebisa da lingvisturi sistemebis shesabamisad. es gvar-sakhelebi opitsialurad unda iknes aghiarebuli da gamoqenebuli khelisuplebis organoebis mier.  . amgvaradve, kerdzo organizatsiebs, rogorebitsaa erovnul umtsiresobebs mikutvnebuli pirebis mier daarsebuli kulturuli asotsiatsiebi da satsarmoebi, igive upleba akvt mat sakheltsodebebtan dakavshirebit.  . im adgilebshi, sadats romelime erovnul umtsiresobas mikutvnebuli pirebis mnishvnelovani raodenoba sakhlobs da rotsa shesabamisi motkhovna arsebobs, khelisuplebis organoebma unda izrunon, rata adgilobrivi sakhelebi da sakheltsodebebi, kuchebis dasakhelebebi da sazogadoebrivi danishnulebis skhva topograpiuli nishnebi erovnuli umtsiresobis enazets gamoikras.  . im regionebsa da adgilebshi, sadats romelime erovnul umtsiresobas mikutvnebuli pirebis mnishvnelovani raodenoba sakhlobs, sakhelmtsipom unda miighos zomebi, rata regionuli da adgilobrivi khelisuplebis organoebis archeul tsevrebs, mati samsakhurebrivi sakmianobis protsesshi, erovnuli umtsiresobis enitats sheedzlot sargebloba.  . umtsiresobebs mikutvnebul pirebs upleba akvt, tavisuplad isargeblon sakutari enit, rogorts sazogadoebriv, ise kerdzo tskhovrebashi, qovelgvari 
 diskriminatsiis gareshe, rogorts zepirad, ise tserilobit, rogorts damoukideblad, ise skhvebtan ertobliobashi. samokalako da politikuri uplebebis shesakheb saertashoriso paktis me-  mukhlis me-  punkti da adamianis uplebata da dziritad tavisuplebata datsvis evropuli konventsiis me-  mukhlis pirveli punkti uzrunvelqops azris gamokhatvis tavisuplebas ara mkholod im ideebtan da shekhedulebebtan mimartebashi, romlebits skhvebs sheidzleba gadaetses (anu komunikatsiis shinaarstan mimartebashi), aramed enastan, rogorts komunikatsiis sashualebastan mimartebashits. es uplebebi, tanastsorobis uplebastan da diskriminatsiis daushveblobis printsiptan ertad, guliskhmobs erovnul umtsiresobebs mikutvnebuli pirebis uplebas, atsarmoon sakutari sametsarmeo sakmianoba im enaze, romelsats tavad aircheven. gamomdinare ikidan, rom kerdzo metsarmeebisatvis uaghresad mnishvnelovania epekturi urtiertobebis damqareba klientebtan da sakutari initsiativebis samartlianobis pirobebshi gankhortsieleba, daushvebelia enis archevis tavisuplebaze aramartlzomieri shezghudvebis datseseba... shdr., agretve, sakartvelos konstitutsia, mukhli,  : "qvela adamiani dabadebit tavisupalia da kanonis tsinashe tanastsoria, ganurchevlad rasisa, kanis perisa, enisa, skesisa, religiisa, politikuri da skhva shekhedulebebisa, erovnuli, etnikuri da sotsialuri kutvnilebisa, tsarmoshobisa, konebrivi da tsodebrivi mdgomareobisa, satskhovrebeli adgilisa. mukhli,  :  . sakartvelos mokalakeni tanastsori arian sotsialur, ekonomikur, kulturul da politikur tskhovrebashi ganurchevlad mati erovnuli, etnikuri, religiuri tu enobrivi kutvnilebisa. saertashoriso samartlis saqoveltaod aghiarebuli printsipebisa da normebis shesabamisad mat upleba akvt, tavisuplad, qovelgvari diskriminatsiisa da charevis gareshe, ganavitaron tavianti kultura, isargeblon dedaenit pirad tskhovrebashi da sajarod. 
 mukhli,  :  . samartaltsarmoeba khortsieldeba sakhelmtsipo enaze. pirs, romelmats sakhelmtsipo ena ar itsis, miechineba tarjimani. im raionebshi, sadats mosakhleoba ar plobs sakhelmtsipo enas, uzrunvelqopilia sakhelmtsipo enis shestsavlisa da samartaltsarmoebastan dakavshirebuli sakitkhebis gadatsqveta. ikh. agretve: "haagis rekomendatsiebi erovnul umtsiresobata ganatlebis uplebebtan dakavshirebit"   ( ) , "ganatlebis speroshi diskriminatsiis tsinaaghmdeg iuneskos konventsia (mukhli  )" da skhv. 
 shdr.: "evropuli kartiis" avtorta tu ekspertta samartliani shenishvnit, avtoktoni umtsiresobebis tsarmokmnis ert-ert mizezad michneulia mezobel khalkhebs shoris iseti politikuri sazghvrebis gavleba, romelits ar emtkhveva enobriv-etnikur sazghvrebs (avtokton etnosta natsili moektsa skhva etnosis dominantobit shekmnili sakhelmtsipos sazghvrebshi). 
 e) kartiit motsul speroebshi regionul an umtsiresobis enebze molaparake jgupebsa da sakhelmtsiposhi imave an msgavs enaze molaparake jgupebs shoris kavshiris shenarchuneba da ganvitareba, iseve, rogorts kulturuli urtiertobebis damqareba sakhelmtsiposhi skhva jgupebtan, romlebits iqeneben ganskhvavebul enebs; v) shesabamisi pormebisa da sashualebebis uzrunvelqopa qvela shesabamis sapekhurze regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis stsavlebisa da shestsavlisatvis; shenishvna: kartiis  -e ganmartebis mikhedvit, "zogiert shemtkhvevashi sachiro ikneba regionuli/umtsiresobis enaze stsavleba". 
 tsaakhalison an uzrunvelqon regionul an umtsiresobis enebze an am enebis stsavleba ganatlebis qvela shesabamis sapekhurze, tu regionul an umtsiresobis enaze molaparaketa raodenoba amas amartlebs... mukhli   - kulturuli sakmianoba da sashualebebi  . ... mkhareebi valdebulebas igheben: a) tsaakhalison regionuli an umtsiresobis enisatvis damakhasiatebeli tvitgamokhatvis sashualebebi da initsiativebi da mkhari dauchiron am enebze shekmnili natsarmoebebisadmi khelmisatsvdomobis skhvadaskhva sashualebebs; b) tsaakhalison regionul an umtsiresobis enaze shekmnili nashromebisadmi khelmisatsvdomoba skhva enebshi satargmano, dublirebis, post-sinkronizatsiisa da subtitrirebis sakmianobisatvis dakhmarebis gatsevis gzit; g) tsaakhalison skhva enebze shekmnili natsarmoebebisadmi khelmisatsvdomoba regionul an umtsiresobis enebze mtargmnelobiti, dublirebis, post-sinkronizatsiisa da subtitrirebis sakmianobisatvis dakhmarebis gatsevis gzit; d) uzrunvelqon, rom skhvadaskhva sakhis kulturuli sakmianobis organizebisa da mkhardacherisatvis pasukhismgebelma organoebma daatseson shesabamisi anazghaureba regionuli an umtsiresobis enebisa da kulturis tsodnisa da gamoqenebisatvis im ghonisdziebebshi, romlebsats isini tsamoitsqeben, an romlebistvisats isini uzrunvelqopen mkhardacheras; e) kheli sheutsqon im zomebs, romlebits miznad isakhaven, rom kulturuli sakmianobis organizebisa da mkhardacherisatvis pasukhismgebel organoebs hqavdet iseti personali, romelits srulad plobs shesabamis regionul an umtsiresobis enas, iseve rogorts mosakhleobis danarcheni natsilis enas (enebs); v) tsaakhalison regionuli an umtsiresobis enaze molaparaketa tsarmomadgenlis monatsileoba kulturuli sakmianobisatvis sashualebebis uzrunvelqopashi da mat dagegmvashi; 
 z) tsaakhalison da/an mkhari dauchiron iseti organos an organoebis shekmnas, romlebits pasukhismgebelni iknebian regionul an umtsiresobis enaze shekmnili natsarmoebebis shekrebaze, aslis shenakhvasa da tsarmodgenaze an gamokveqnebaze; t) autsileblobis shemtkhvevashi, shekmnan da/an kheli sheutsqon da daapinanson mtargmnelobiti da terminologiis kvleviti samsakhurebi, kerdzod im miznit, rom shenarchunebul iknas da ganvitardes shesabamisi administratsiuli, komertsiuli, ekonomikuri, sotsialuri, teknikuri an samartlebrivi terminologia titoeul regionul an umtsiresobis enashi.  . im teritoriebis mimart, imat garda, sadats traditsiulad gamoiqenebian regionuli an umtsiresobis enebi, tuki regionul an umtsiresobis enaze molaparaketa raodenoba amas amartlebs, mkhareebi valdebulebas igheben neba darton, tsaakhalison da/an uzrunvelqon shesabamisi kulturuli sakmianoba da sashualebebi tsina punktis shesabamisad.  . mkhareebi valdebulebas igheben kulturis speroshi mati politikis sazghvargaret gankhortsielebisas, satando quradgheba miaktsion regionul da umtsiresobis enebs da im kulturas, romlis gamokhatulebats isini arian . 
 sotsiolingvisturi tvaltakhedvit, “kartiashi“ skhvadaskhva terminit gamokhatuli idiomebi sam dziritad jgupad sheidzleba tsarmovadginot:  . sakhelmtsipos opitsialuri ena da misi adgilobrivi sakheskhvaobani (dialektebi):  . . ertaderti (an ert-erti) sakhelmtsipo ena;  . . sakhelmtsipo ena avtonomiur tsarmonakmnshi;  . . sakhelmtsipo enis regionuli sakheskhvaoba (/dialekti).  . istoriuli regionuli an umtsiresobis ena:  . . regionshi istoriuli umravlesobis ena regionuli ena: regionshi avtoktoni umtsiresobis ena  . . umtsiresobis ena:  . . konkretuli regionis armkone istoriuli ena teritoriis armkone ena.  . araistoriuli umtsiresobis ena - diasporis an migrantta ena:  . . sakhelmtsipos mokalakeobis mkone kompakturad mtskhovreb dzvel migrantta ena (diasporis ena):  . . sakhelmtsipos mokalakeobis mkone arakompakturad mtskhovreb dzvel migrantta ena (diasporis ena);  . . mokalakeobis armkone akhal migrantta ena. “kartiashi“ motsemuli terminologiuri shepasebebis ponze kvemot tsarmovadgent sakartveloshi dgheistvis arsebuli enebistvis savaraudo statusebs; paralelurad, kritikulad gavaanalizebt sakartvelos enata im sias, romelzets, tomash vikherkevichis jgupis azrit, unda gavrtseldes "regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartiis" debulebebi. 
 sakartvelo: sakhelmtsipos opitsialuri ena da misi adgilobrivi sakheskhvaobani (dialektebi)  . . sakartvelos sakhelmtsipo ena. istoriuli tsqaroebis mikhedvit, dzv.ts. me-  saukunidan dghemde sakartveloshi sakhelmtsipo enaa kartuli saliteraturo ena, romelits, aseve utsqvetad aris ghvtismsakhurebis ena. drois im monakvetshi, rotsa sakartvelo dapqrobili hqavda rusetis imperias, sakhelmtsipo enis punktsias dziritadad imperiis ena asrulebda; amave periodshi sakartveloshi mosul dzvel tu akhal migrantebtan saurtierto enad damkvidrda rusuli ena. sakartvelos deokupatsiis protsesi datsqebulia ; shesabamisad, imedia, male dadgeba dro, rodesats skhvadaskhva etnikuri tsarmomavlobis sakartvelos mokalakeebs shoris sakomunikatsio enis rolshi isev mogvevlineba kartuli ena sakartvelos sakhelmtsipo ena .  . . sakhelmtsipo enebi avtonomiur tsarmonakmnshi. sakartveloshi amzhamad iuridiulad arsebobs apkhazetis avtonomiuri respublika, romelshits sakhelmtsipo enebia kartuli ena da apkhazuri ena .  . . sakartvelos sakhelmtsipo enis – kartuli saliteraturo enis adgilobrivi sakheskhvaobani (/dialektebi). mravali istoriuli pakti tskhadqops, rom skhvadaskhva kutkhis kartvelebi (acharlebi, gudamaqrelebi, gurulebi, tushebi, imerlebi, imerkhevlebi, kakhelebi, lazebi,   tslis agvistos ruset-sakartvelos omis shemdeg sakartvelos teritoriaze mqop rusetis jars opitsialurad aghudga okupantis statusi (romelits sakartvelos khelisuplebisgan mas pirvelad mienicha   tslis   oktombers).   am tvalsazrisit saintereso msjelobisatvis ikh., mitropoliti anania (japaridze), eklesia - sakartvelos kutkheta makavshirebeli dughabi, sakartvelos sapatriarkosa da konrad adenaueris pondis mier organizebuli sametsniero konperentsiis masalebi, tb.,  .   ikh., mag., sakartvelos konstitutsia, mukhli  : sakartvelos sakhelmtsipo ena aris kartuli, kholo apkhazetis avtonomiur respublikashi, agretve - apkhazuri.   
 lechkhumlebi, livanelebi, machakhlelebi, megrelebi, meskhebi, mtiulebi, mokheveebi, rachvelebi, svanebi, taoelebi, pshavlebi, kartlelebi, khevsurebi, javakhebi, herebi/ingiloebi) khangrdzlivi tsarsulis mkone ert istoriul etnoss tsarmoadgenen . am etnosis umtavres tvalsachino dughabs kmnis didi istoriis mkone samtsignobro kultura. mravalsaukunovani saerto kulturul-samtsignobro shemokmedeba  da istoriuli mekhsiereba uamrav pakts inakhavs, sadats natlad chans sakartvelos qvela kutkhis kartvelobis tavgantsiruli brdzola da ghvatsli kartvelobis shenarchunebisatvis. shegvidzlia vtkvat, rom kartvelta erovnuli meobis mtavari ganmsazghvreli paktoria zogadkartul enaze qvela kartul mkhareshi tvisobrivad ertnairad shekmnili samtsignobro kultura. mravali saukunea kartul samtsignobro enastan ertad tanaarsebobs kartvelta erovnuli enis adgilobrivi variantebi, romlebits kartuli saliteraturo enis gamamdidrebel ushret nakadulebs tsarmoadgenen; kerdzod, kartulis (/kartveluris) adgilobrivi sakheskhvaobebia: megruli, lazuri, svanuri, khevsuruli, mokheuri, pshauri, mtiulurgudamaqruli, tushuri, heruli (ingilouri), kakhuri, kartluri, samtskhuri, javakhuri, taouri, imerkheulshavshuri, livanuri, machakhluri, acharuli, guruli, imeruli, lechkhumuri, rachuli... . kartvelta erovnuli 
 enis - kartulis - am sakheskhvaobebs (dialektebs), sabchota metsnierebis inertsiit, zogi dghesats  -  damoukidebel enad ganikhilavs; shesadareblad ishvelieben zemo da kvemo germanuli kontinuumebis mimartebas (da ara, mag., germanuli enisa da bavariuli metqvelebisa). aghvnishnavt, rom kartveluri enobrivi realobistvis samagalitod ar gamodgeba zemo germanulisa da kvemo germanulis mimartebis sakitkhi; kvemo (chrdilo) germanulisgan ganskhvavebit, arts erti kartveluri kutkhuri metqveleba (idiomi) arasodes qopila kveqnis natsilis traditsiuli samtsignobro-saeklesio ena . 
 shdr.: sakartveloshi istoriulad qvela kartveluri samtsignobro ena iqo da aris temis  zogadkartul/saertokartvelur enaze dapudznebuli standartuli ena. am saertoerovnul movlenastan ar sheidzleba gavatanabrot kartvelta erti romelime regionis mosakhleobis zepiri sashinao metqveleba. garda amisa, zemogermanuli da kvemogermanuli istoriulad ertmanets miemarteba, rogorts paraleluri enobrivi monatsemebi, romeltagan ert-erti akhlo tsarsulshi gabatonda opitsialur enad; shdr.: arkaul kartul samtsignobro enastan - sakartvelos saeklesio/sakhelmtsipo enastan - mimartebit chventvis tsnobili qvela skhva kartveluri metqveleba meoreuli tsarmonakmnia; kerdzod, ponematuri strukturis, morpologiuri qalibebis tu pudzeebis pirveladi sakheebi datsulia arkaul samtsignobro enashi - kartvelta istoriul opitsialur enashi. megrullazuri, svanuri, khevsuruli tu meskhuri variantebi ki tsarmokmnilia arkauli kartuli/kartveluri enisgan. 
 shesabamisad, paralelur enobriv variantebad ver miichneva amosavali ena da misi transpormatsiit mighebuli zepiri lokaluri varianti . akve aghvnishnav, rom tanamedrove globaluri sainpormatsio kselis qoveldghiuri sachiroeba zghudavs ara mkholod adgilobriv dialektebs, aramed geopolitikurad susti zogi evropuli sakhelmtsipos opitsialur enasats ki; shesabamisad, sakartveloshits sagangebo zomebia misaghebi rogorts kartuli standartuli enis, aseve, kartvelta zepiri metqvelebebis gadarchenisa da datsvis miznit; mag., chvens shemtkhvevashi namdvilad esachiroeba sagangebo quradgheba qvela kartvelur zepir metqvelebas (sakartvelos sakhelmtsipos sazghvrebshi arsebul tu sakartvelos sazghvrebs mighma darchenil kartvelta kiloebs). am mimartulebit sakhelmtsipom sagangebo zomebi unda miighos; kerdzod: - saskolo sakhelmdzghvaneloebshi didi dozit unda shevides kartveluri dialekturi leksika (megruli, lazuri, svanuri, khevsuruli, taouri, acharuli, meskhuri, heruli, kakhuri, tushuri...), rogorts kartvelta samtsignobro enis gamdidrebis sashualeba; aseve, sakartvelos skolebis mostsavleebi bavshvobidanve unda eziaron khalkhuri poeziis, zogadad, polkloris nimushebs tsalkeuli kartveluri dialektebis mikhedvit; - sakhelmtsipos mier seriozulad unda dapinansdes is kartvelologiuri tsentrebi, romlebits stsavloben kartvelur dialektebs; maksimalurad amomtsuravad unda dapiksirdes dghemde moghtseuli dialektebis leksikuri tu gramatikuli taviseburebebi; unda momzaddes da gamokveqndes akhali dialekturi leksikonebi da polklorul-etnograpiuli masalebi ; 
 shdr.: zemo da kvemo germanuli erti pudze-enis paraleluri standartuli variantebi iqo uakhloes tsarsulshits.   samtsukharod, bolo tslebshi sakartveloshi mkvetrad shemtsirda dialektologiuri ekspeditsiebisa da arapolitizebuli kartvelologiuri kvlevebis dapinanseba. sakartvelos ganatlebisa da metsnierebis saministros mtsdari sagranto politikit 
 - istoriulad kartuli samtsignobro ena sazrdoobda qvela kartveluri kilodan, shesabamisad, logikuri ikneboda, saliteraturo enis sabazo leksikonshi (kartuli enis ganmartebiti leksikonis rvatomeulshi) tavidanve shesuliqo megrul-lazuri da svanuri leksikats. dghes maints unda momzaddes kartuli enis ganmartebiti leksikonis akhali redaktsia, romelshits ukhvad sheva ara mkholod kartluri tu pshav-khevsuruli, aramed megrul-lazuri da svanuri leksika . akve aghvnishnav, rom am tipis samushaoebis gankhortsielebisatvis   tsels akaki tseretlis sakhelmtsipo universitetis kartveluri dialektologiis institutshi daarsda sametsniero-saganmanatleblo tsentri, romlis ushualo mizania kartveluri (megrul-lazuri, svanuri tu rachul-imeruli...) dialektebis monatsemebisgan samtsignobro enistvis sarekomendatsio leksikonis momzadeba.   tslis   marts tsmida ambrosi khelaias khsenebis dghes, am tsentrs etsoda 
 (dapinanasebis tsentralizebul-klanuri sistema; artur tsutsievis msgavs utskhoel an arapropesional "inkognito" ekspertta mier kartvelologiis prioritetebis araadekvaturi gansazghvra, kartvelologiuri da humanitaruli metsnierebis skhva dargebis proektebis "shercheva" saerto reitingit...)  -  tslebshi gansakutrebit dazaralda 
 tsmida ambrosi khelaias sakhelobis sametsnierosaganmanatleblo tsentri . sasurvelia, sakartvelos qvela regionis universitettanats sheikmnas msgavsi miznis mkone ganqopileba/tsentri, kholo tbilisshi - kartvelologiis sametsniero-kvleviti instituti, romelits koordinatsias gautsevs am tipis samushaoebs. 
 shdr.:   tsels evropis sabchos saparlamento asambleam miigho  -e rekomendatsia, romelits miznad isakhavs, sheetsqos kheli evropashi umtsiresobata enebisa da dialektebis movla-patronobas. am etapze martlats rom dasakargavadaa gantsiruli bevri opitsialuri enis peradovani dialekti; sruli pasukhismgeblobit vatskhadeb: amzhamad kartveluri kiloebis (tushurit datsqebuli, lazurit damtavrebuli) mdgomareoba katastropulia! sul mokle khanshi bevri kartuli dialekti dvaluris  beds gaiziarebs . istoriul kartul kiloebtan dakavshirebit, akve tsarmovadgent r. topchishvilis daskvnas;   
 kerdzod, qizlar-mozdokursa da plastunkurze msjelobis shemdeg is tsers: "drota ganmavlobashi kartuli dialektebi tvit sakartvelos teritoriazets gakra; kerdzod: dvaluri, trialuri, erushuli, klarjuli, artaanuli, kolauri da skhv . 
 r. topchishvili, sakartvelos etnologia, tb.,  , gv.  - . 
 sakartveloshi romelia istoriuli etnikuri umtsiresobis ena? sakartvelos arts ert regionshi ar tskhovrobs arakartuli tsarmomavlobis avtoktoni mosakhleoba; shesabamisad, tuki mkatsrad davitsavt kartiis kriteriumebs, sakartvelos khelisupleba valdebuli ar aris, romelime etnikuri jgupis enas mianichos regionuli an umtsiresobis enis statusi. mit umetes, "teritoriis mkone istoriuli umtsiresobis" enis (regionuli/umtsiresobis) statusi; shesabamisad, sakartveloshi ver davapiksirebt pirveli ( . .) da meore tipis ( . .) regionul an umtsiresobis enebs; kerdzod: - kveqanashi istoriuli umtsiresobis, magram motsemul regionshi umravlesobis ena ( . .) - regionuli ena: sakartveloshi ar aris; - kveqanashi istoriuli umtsiresobis da motsemul regionshits umtsiresobis ena ( . .) - umtsiresobis ena: sakartveloshi ar aris. shdr.: mitskevichis sakhelobis universitetis enobrivi politikisa da umtsiresobata kvlevis departamentis khelmdzghvaneli, doktori tomash vikherkevichi da misi kartveli tanaavtorebi ratomghats tvlian, rom sakartveloshi regionuri enebia da, shesabamisad, "umtsiresobata enebis shesakheb evropuli kartiis" mesame natsili gavrtseldeba somkhur da azerbaijanul enebze (gv.  ). tsnobilia, rom samtskhe-javakhetsa da trialetshi dghes kompakturad mtskhovrebi somekhta etnikuri jgupi ak ar aris istoriuli, avtoktoni mosakhleoba; turketisgan kontrolirebadi teritoriebidan aqrili somkhebi sakartvelos am mkhareshi rusetis imperiam chaasakhla  -  tslebshi ; shesabamisad, am etnikur jgups ver mivichnevt sakartvelos istoriul umtsiresobad da verts mis enas chavtvlit sakartvelos aradziritadi erovnuli (etnikuri) 
 r. topchishvili, kavkasiis khalkhta etnograpia, tb.,  , gv.   
 umtsiresobis enad; iset enad, romelits, rogorts kulturuli movlena, aris saprtkhis kvesh . aseve, samkhret sakartveloshi avtoktonad, istoriul mosakhleobad ver chaitvlebian azerbaijanelebi; tsnobilia, rom sakartvelos ert-ert istoriul mkhareshi - kvemo kartlshi - debedas kheobashi me-  saukunis dasatsqisshi chamosakhlda turkmanuli tomi borchalu . am etnikuri jgupis enats sakhelmtsipo enaa mezobel azerbaijanshits da turketshits; shesabamisad, sakartveloshi verts azerbaijanuli (turkuli) miichneva avtoktoni mosakhleobis iset regionul enad, romelzets unda gavrtseldes "kartiis" mesame natsili. politikosta tu metsnierta erti jgupi  intensiurad avrtselebs mosazrebas, rom umtserlobo "regionuli enebis" statusi unda mienichos megrulsa da svanurs ; samagalitod moviqvant zhurnalist nato berulavas inpormatsias: 
 shekhvedris monatsileebi shetankhmdnen bevr sakitkhshi da miighes dadgenileba:  . megruli da svanuri enebis datsva, romlebits drota ganmavlobashi sheidzleba saertod gakres.  . kheli sheutsqon kartuli sakhelmtsipo enis kulturuli traditsiebis shenarchunebasa da ganvitarebas;  . am enata datsvita da ganvitarebit mnishvnelovani tsvlili sheitanon akhali kartuli sakhelmtsipos msheneblobashi, rats emqareba demokratiisa da kulturata mravalperovnebis printsipebs, erovnuli suverenitetisa da teritoriuli mtlianobis parglebshi. 
 literaturis  shekmnis mtsdelobebi, romlebits adekvaturad shepasda rogorts kartul saeklesio, aseve saero sazogadoebashi ; kerdzod, gaketda logikuri daskvna: es aris imperiuli gegma, romelits kartvelta kutkhuri metqvelebebis - kartuli enis sakheskhvaobebis (kiloebis) damoukidebel umtserlobo enebad gamotskhadebit, miznad isakhavs kartvelta enobriv-etnikur da eklesiur dashlas. am problemis gamo sakartvelos samotsikulo eklesiis tsmida sinodma miigho sagangebo ganchinebats: 
 saquradgheboa isits, rom, paralelurad, ganakhlda  kutkhuri metqvelebebis mikhedvit "dedaenebis" shekmnisa da am kiloebze bibliis targmnis  tu mkhatvruli 
 megrul-svanurad bibliis targmnas akhortsielebs "bibliis targmnis saertashoriso instituti"; am institutis sakartvelos pilials tsarmoadgenen baptistebis episkoposi malkhaz songhulashvili da propesori zurab kiknadze; svanur-megrulad bibliis targmnas mkhars uchers sozar subari; misi "argumentebis" kritika tsarmodgenilia giorgi andriadzisa da zurab tskhovrebadzis msjelobebshi (amis shesakheb ikh.: nino mikiashvilis masalebi gazet "rezonansis"   tslis   da   agvistos nomrebshi (№  ,  ). zanur-svanuris damoukidebel enebad gamotskhadeba da am kiloebze bibliis targmnis mtsdeloba sametsniero literaturashits shepasda, rogorts "kartuli tsnobierebis tsinaaghmdeg sheteva" (r. gujejiani, kartvel mtielta mentalobis istoriidan, tb.,  , gv.  - ). amave mkvlevarma dziritad daskvnad tsarmoadgina sakartvelos katalikos-patriarkis, ilia meoris shemdegi praza: "tsdiloben, kartul enas megruli da svanuri dialektebi chamoashoron da isini damoukidebel enebad gamoatskhadon. upro metits, mat ganzrakhuli akvt, biblia da lotsvebi megrulad da svanurad targmnon. es aris udidesi danashauli eris tsinashe" (ikve, gv.  ). 
   v. kharchilavas "bilingvuri" leksebis kritikis shesakheb ikh., prop. r. sherozias tserili, romelits danartshia tsarmodgenili. arts samegrelo-svanetis tanamedrove sazogadoebas uchirs archevanis gaketeba chqondidelgamsakhurdiebsa da kiloebis mikhedvit "akhali saliteraturo enebis" shemkotsitsebelta shoris. 
 qipiani, episkoposi grigol dadiani, tsm. ambrosi khelaia, tsm. aleksi shushania, ilia, akaki da skhva didi moghvatseni" . analogiurad pikrobs kartuli sametsniero   sazogadoebis udidesi natsili da parto sazogadoebrioba. upirveles qovlisa, mkapio pozitsia akvs samegrelosa da svanetis kartvelobas, risi dasturitsaa am kutkheebshi aghzrdili tsnobili adamianebis mravalritskhovani publikatsiebi analogiuri shepasebebit; mag., vrtseli analizia tsarmodgenili sergi sajaiasa da dazmir jojuas tserilshi  "akhali saetnopabrikatsio poligonisatvis: ganatlebis tsentri "kolkhida" erovnul sulshi khrtsnis shemoparebas tsdilobs" . mitropoliti anania japaridze: "chvenma tsinaprebma itsodnen, romelia saerto-saliteraturo ena da romelia adgilobrivi dialekti", "sakartvelos respublika",   tebervali,   ts. (№  ).   nashromis danartshi ikh., kartvel metsnierta "kutaisuri memorandumi".   
 pirvel rigshi, utskhoeli mkitkhvelistvis vitqvi:   saukunis mandzilze sakartvelos eklesiis tsiaghshi ishva kartveli eris kulturuli memkvidreobis udidesi natsili; eklesia mudam iqo kartuli kulturis savanets da utskhoel tu kartvel ltolvilta tavshesapari; garda amisa, sakartvelos samotsikulo eklesiis iurisdiktsia qoveltvis vrtseldeboda sakartvelos mtel teritoriaze... amitomaa, rom kartuli eklesia dghes ertaderti institutia, romelsats endoba sakartveloshi arsebuli qvela politikuri jgupi tu umtsiresoba. am mizezta gamo akvs kartul eklesias maghali reitingi tanamedrove sakartvelos mokalakeebshi. 
 vpikrob, sinamdvilis obiekturad aghmkmeli qvela adamianistvis natelia: sul mtsire,   saukunis mandzilze megrelits, svanits, lazits, meskhits da acharelits skhva kartvelebtan ertad saerto dedaenit asrulebs ghvtismsakhurebas, kmnis mkhatvrul literaturas da tsarmartavs sakhelmtsipo kantselariis sakmianobas. shesabamisad, dghes svanta, megrelta tu meskhta dialektebis mikhedvit akhali saeklesio tu saliteraturo enebis shekmna da enis kartiis" debulebebis gavrtseleba kartuli enis am sakheskhvaobebze (tu dialektebze) moemsakhureba mkholod ert mizans: mezobeli imperiebis strategiuli gegmebis mikhedvit daishalos kartuli etnosi, kartuli kultura da sakartvelo, rogorts sakhelmtsipo . mqari sapudzveli gvakvs, vtkvat: "regionuli da umtsiresobis enebis" shesakheb kartiis debulebebis ganskhvavebuli interpretatsiebis garda, sakartveloshi mimdinare diskusias garkveultsilad gansazghvravs geopolitikurad saintereso regionis - amierkavkasiis gakontrolebis mosurne agresiuli mezoblebis mizanits: "evropuli kartiis" debulebebis arsis gaqalbebit jer kartveli eris enobriv-etnikuri danatsevreba, sakartvelos ktseva konpederatsiul sakhelmtsipod; shemdgom ki igegmeba am mqipe tsarmonakmnis sruli dashla . 
 konkretuli regionis armkone istoriuli ena teritoriis armkone ena ( . .). bolo ramdenime saukunis mandzilze tbilissa tu sakartvelos skhva mkhareebshi dasakhldnen da akhlats tskhovroben sakartveloshi migrirebuli etnikuri jgupebi: somkhebi , borchaloeli tatrebi ebraelebi ,   (azerbaijanelebi) da osebi ; akve sheidzleba ganvikhilot udiuri enats. am etnikur jgupta natsils garkveuli kvali akvt datovebuli sakartvelos sakhelmtsipoebriobisa da kulturis istoriashi; shesabamisad, ramdenime saukunis tsin sakartveloshi dasakhlebuli umtsiresobebis enebi sakartvelos khelisuplebis sagangebo zrunvis sagani unda 
 shdr., didi britanetis, germaniisa tu espanetis analogiuri siebi, romlebits "kartiis" printsipebis datsvitaa shedgenili . polonetis khelisuplebas jer ar moukhdenia "kartiis" ratipitsireba; ikmneba shtabechdileba, rom polonelma doktorma da misma kartvelma kolegebma somkhetisa da ruminetis "enebis siit" ikhelmdzghvaneles da ara - dasavlet evropashi aghiarebuli printsipebit. sakartvelos sakhalkho damtsvelis (sozar subaris), sakhalkho ganatlebis tsentris tanamshromlebis, aseve, doktor tomash vikherkevichisa da misi tanaavtorebis azrit, "evropuli kartiis" meore natsilis debulebebi unda gavrtseldes aseve umtserlobo kartveluri enebis: megrullazurisa da svanuris mimart (gv.  ,  )  . rogorts zemot aghvnishnet, tanamedrove lingvistta tu etnologta natsilis azrit, megrul-lazur-svanuri tsarmoadgenen kartvelta sashinao (dialektur) metqvelebebs, romlebits kartvelta istoriuli dedaenis - sakartvelos opitsialuri enis - kartulis - 
 adgilobrivi sakheskhvaobebia da ara arakartuli etnosebis damoukidebeli enebi. shdr. kartiis ganmartebiti natsilis  -e da  -e punktebi: "kartiis debulebebi moitsavs mkholod istoriul enebs..." ; es enebi mkapiod unda ganskhvavdebodes im enis an enebisagan, romelzets sakhelmtsiposhi mtskhovrebi danarcheni mosakhleoba saubrobs. kartiis debulebebi ar ekheba erti enis adgilobriv sakheskhvaobebsa tu dialektebs" . "kartiis" printsipebidan tu amovalt, arts am shemtkhvevashi unda iqos raime sakamato: "regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartia" shekmnilia motsemuli sakhelmtsipos mkvidri, magram aradziritadi mosakhleobis (etnikuri umtsiresobis) enis dasatsavad ; dziritadi mosakhleobis erovnuli enis adgilobrivi sakheskhvaobis datsva ar aris am saertashoriso konventsiis mizani. kveqnis dziritadi mosakhleobis enasa da mis adgilobriv variantebze (dialektebze, kilokavebze) normaluri sakhelmtsipo isedats unda zrunavdes. shdr.: istoriuli umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartia itsavs politikuri tu sotsialuri mizezebis gamo saprtkhis kvesh mqopi aradziritadi mosakhleobis enebsa da kulturebs. miukhedavad tsarmodgenili nateli debulebebisa, megrul-lazurisa da svanuris sotsiolingvisturi 
 kerdzod,   tslis   dekembers sakartvelos khelisuplebisadmi tsardgenil "rekomendatsiebshi" ("enobrivi politika sakartveloshi") isini tseren: "zanuri da svanuri sotsiolingvisturad khasiatdeba, rogorts umtserlobo enebi" (gv.  ). 
 statusis sakitkhi dghemde diskusiis temaa rogorts sakhelisuplebo, ise sametsniero tsreebshi. chemi azrit, am diskusias stimuls adzlevs rusulsabchouri imperiis tsiaghshi shekmnili modzvelebuli, aralogikuri lingvokulturuli kvalipikatsiebi, romelta dadzleva dghemde ver mokherkhda sakartvelos ganatlebisa da metsnierebis saministros araadekvaturi sakmianobis gamo ; kerdzod, am saministrom araperi gaaketa saertashoriso sainpormatsio tu sametsniero kselshi rusetis imperiis mier kartvelologiashi damkvidrebuli politizebuli kvalipikatsiebis  uarsaqopad. shdr.: stsored bolo attsleulebshi rusetis imperiis mtsdelobit skhva kveqnebis sametsniero tu politikur tsreebshi gabatonda dausabutebeli mosazrebebi sakartvelos enobriv-etnikuri situatsiis shesakheb; mravaltagan ak ert-erts tsarmovadgent: 
 iguliskhmeba mdgomareoba   tslis chatvlit. 
 mag.: a. duginis "tvitshemokmedebis" charchoebshi kremlis sametsnieroideologiuri diversiis ert-ert bolo "metsnierul" traktatad tsarmochnda rustem vakhitovis statia "khalkhis gaqopa", romelits daibechda   tslis  -  noembris "literaturnaia gazetashi"; ak metsnieruli kartvelologia, kerdzod ki sakartvelos obiekturi istoria gamotskhadebulia etnonatsionalistur teoriad; dots. r.vakhitovis gvaris mkone kremlis ideologis azrit, megrelebi da svanebi kartvelebi ar arian ("natsmenshestvebi" arian), kholo ertiani kartveli eri ar arsebobda me-  saukunemde; turme, "etnonatsionalizmi" politikursakhelmtsipoebriv doktrinad aktsia zviad gamsakhurdiam, amzhamad ki etnonatsionalistur sakhelmtsipos ashenebs mikheil saakashvili... am shekvetil "istoriograpiul" mimokhilvashi "etnonatsionalizmis" ertert gamovlinebad michneulia isits, rom, turme, sakartvelos khelisupleba megrelebsa da svanebs kartvelebad atskhadebs da mat "enebs" ar ganikhilavs erovnuli umtsiresobebis enebad; es turme gamoikhateba imashi, rom sakartvelo ar uertdeba "evropul kartias regionuli an umtsiresobebis shesakheb" (nishandoblivia isits, rom r. vakhitovi "enis kartias" "shetsdomit" utsodebs "konventsias natsionalur umtsiresobata da mati enebis shesakheb"). am "ideologiuri diversiis" kritikisatvis danartshi ikh. mitropolit anania japaridzis tserili; ikh., agretve: m.lortkipanidze, g. otkhmezuri, "sheugnebeli arakompetenturoba tu shegnebuli siqalbe..." ("sakartvelos respublika",  ,  ,   ianvari,  ). 
   am chamonatvalshi mosakhleobis ritskhviti monatsemebits mtsdaria; skhva msgavsi politizebuli masalebis kritikuli analizisatvis ikh. t. putkaradze, kartvelta dedaena da dialektebi, kutaisi,  .   shdr.: n. maridan moqolebuli, dghemde metsnierta natsili tvlis, rom "sotsiolingvisturi gansazghvrit zanuri da svanuri kartulis dialektebia, kholo tsminda lingvisturit - damoukidebeli enebi"; skhvata azrit, megrul- 
 ratomghats kartvelebad ar tvlian, am idioms "regionalur enad" ganikhilaven, ramdenadats svanurad metqvelebs lentekhisa da mestiis raionebis mosakhleobis umravlesoba. vpikrob, zanur-svanuris gamotskhadeba "umtserlobo enebad" aris stalinis tvalsazrisis modipitsireba . aghvnishnavt imasats, amgvari araadekvaturi kvalipikatsia (mravalsaukunovani samtsignobro kulturis avtori kartvelobis gamotskhadeba umtsignobro etnosebad) aris sakartvelos 
 mravalgzis tanjuli da kartveli eris ertianobisatvis mebrdzoli kutkheebis (samegrelo-lazetisa da svanetis) mosakhleobis sheuratskhqopa. shdr.: umtserlobo enad (/umtsignobro enad) miichneva ganuvitarebeli etnikuri jgupis dedaena, romelits ar aris standartuli (normalizebuli) da ar gamoiqeneba opitsialur enad propesiuli shemokmedebis protsessa tu sakmistsarmoebashi (es etnosi am miznit moikhmars skhva sazogadoebis mier shekmnil samtsignobro enas) . qvela kutkhis kartvelis istoriuli samtsignobro ena aris kartuli; shdr.: kartuli samtsignobro kulturis istoria tvalnatliv achvenebs, rom skhva kartvelta msgavsad, megrel-lazebitsa da svanebits, mravali saukunea, sakutari saerto istoriuli dedaenit  - kartuli enit 
 - kmnian msoplioshi ert-ert udzveles tserilobit kulturas. qvela kartveluri temi (istoriuletnograpiuli mkharis mosakhleoba) mravalsaukunovani shesabamisad, tserilobiti kulturis shemokmedia ; istoriis gaqalbebaa svanetisa da egrisis (odishis, samegrelos) kartvelobis gamotskhadeba umtserlobo dedaenis mkone sazogadoebebad. tomash vikherkevichis jgups kidev erti "originaluri" rekomendatsia akvs: isini tvlian, rom kheli unda sheetsqos megrul-lazur da svanur enebze mkhatvruli da musikaluri natsarmoebebis shekmnas (gv.  ).   saukunis mandzilze mkhatvrul literaturasa da musikalur natsarmoebebs megrelebi, svanebi tu lazebi (chqondidlebi, iovane minchkhi, iovane petritsi... ambrosi khelaia, konstantine gamskhurdia...) zogaderovnuli enit kmnian; khalkhuri shemokmedeba am kiloebzets iseve ikmneboda da sheikmneba, rogorts khevsuretis, tushetisa tu acharis 
 kartvelobis mier. sakartvelos khelisuplebisadmi rekomendatsiebis avtorebi ratom tsdiloben megrel-lazsvanebi gamijnon skhva kartvelebisgan (kartlelebisgan, tushebisgan, meskhebisgan...) da istoriulad shekmnili kartuli mkhatvruli literaturis alternativad ratom gvtavazoben svanuri tu megruli kiloebis mikhedvit "mkhatvruli literaturis" shekmnas?  kartvelta saertoerovnuli klasikuri mkhatvruli shemokmedebats da khalkhuri memkvidreobats (megrul-lazursvanur-khevsurul-taouri... polklori, dialekturi leksika, tses-chveulebebi, etnograpiuli taviseburebebi) ertnairadaa mosaprtkhilebeli da shesanarchunebeli, vinaidan isini kmnian im mtlian unikalur kartvelur sagandzurs, romelits metad dzvirpasia mteli katsobriobistvis. tomash vikherkevichis jgupis mosazreba, rom "kartiis" meore natsilis (me-  mukhlis) debulebebi unda gavrtseldes "umtserlobo kartvelur enebze" (megrul-lazursa da svanurze) dausabutebelia tvit "kartiis" printsipebis mikhedvitats; kerdzod, avtorebs gamorchat, rom "kartiis" meore natsili sheidzleba sheekhos mkholod istoriuli umtsiresobis enas, romelits sam variantad sheidzleba iqos tsarmodgenili: - istoriuli etnikuri umtsiresobis ena, romelits regionshi umravlesobis enaa; - istoriuli etnikuri umtsiresobis ena, romelits motsemul regionshits umtsiresobis enaa; 
 qvela adamians akvs upleba, tseros dialektzets da kilokavzets; mag., sakartveloshi aravis aukrdzalavs eter tataraidzistvis, tushur hangze sheekmna shesanishnavi leksebi; tumtsa, tataraidzes rom ganetskhadebina, arsebobs tushuri mkhatvruli literaturao, tushuri skhvaa, kartuli skhvao, is, pirvel rigshi, sakutar tavs gamijnavda tavisi khalkhis erovnuli kulturisgan - didi kartuli kulturisgan. eter tataraidze didi petritsis, chqondidlebis, ilias, akakis, vazhas, konstantines (konstantine gamsakhurdias kontseptsiisatvis ikh., danarti) da mraval skhva kartvel mtseralta mier natsadi gzis gamgrdzelebelia da ertian samtsignobro enas tushuri koloritit amdidrebs.   
 mkatsrad tu davitsavt "kartiis" printsipebs, apkhazuristvis sakhelmtsipo enis statusis gatvalistsinebit, sakartvelos sheudzlia ise moakhdinos "regionuli da umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartiis" ratipikatsia, rom saertod ar gaaketos regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis chamonatvali, an ar aamokmedos kartiis mesame natsili (amis sapudzvels tu sashualebas idzleva "ganmartebiti mokhsenebis"  -e da  -e punktebi). sakartvelos khelisuplebis ketili nebis shemtkhvevashi, "kartiis" meore natsili sheidzleba amokmeddes, araumtsires,   saukunis migrantebis (diasporis) enebis: ebraulis, somkhurisa da azerbaijanulis, aseve, didi saprtkhis tsinashe tsinashe mqopi udiurisa da osuris mimart, romelsats, rogorts chans, skhvagan arsad akvs gadarchena-ganvitarebis perspektiva  (msjelobisatvis ikh. kvemot). shdr.: t. vikherkevichis jgupis dausabutebeli rekomendatsiebis mikhedvit, "kartiis" debulebebi unda gavrtseldes   enis mimart, mat shoris, sakartveloshi maghali khariskhis datsvit unda aghichurvos somkhuri da azerbaijanuli, kholo dabali khariskhit -   ena: rusuli, berdznuli, ebrauli, kurtuli/ieziduri, ukrainuli, chechnuri/kisturi, asiriuli, avariuli, megrul-lazuri, svanuri (gv.  - ). 
 osta dziritad satskhovrisshi - osetshi (e.ts. chrdolo osetshi), romelits amzhamad shedis rusetis pederatsiis shemadgenlobashi, sakhelmtsipo ena tu ganatlebis ena mkholod rusulia; shesabamisad, ak am enas namdvilad emukreba saprtkhe. sakartveloshi osuri enis statusis sakitkhi didadaa damokidebuli sabchota periodshi arsebuli qopili samkhret osetis avtonomiuri olkis - tskhinvalis mkharis - administratsiis chamoqalibebis im printsipebze, romlebits zhenevis pormatit mimdinare dialogis shemdeg ganisazghvreba. 
 araistoriuli umtsiresobis enebi: diasporata da migrantta enebi sakartveloshi kartveli eris satskhovrisi (sadats kartveli aris avtoktoni) gatsilebit didia, vidre sakartvelos amzhamindeli sazghvrebi. momkhvdurta zetsolit, saukuneebis mandzilze sakartvelo kargavda tavis istoriul teritoriebs; shesabamisad, tanamedrove sakhelmtsipoebrivi sazghvrebis pirobebshi avtoktoni kartvelebi moektsnen skhva etnosta dominantobit shekmnili sakhelmtsipoebis shemadgenlobashi. amzhamindeli sakartvelos sakhelmtsipos sazghvrebshi ar tskhovrobs arts erti iseti avtoktoni etnikuri jgupi; mit umetes iseti, romelsats mezoblad akvs sakhelmtsipo ; shesabamisad, sakartveloshi avtokton erovnul umtsiresobad veravin chaitvleba. sakartveloshi migrirebuli qvelaze dzveli etnikuri jgupia ebrauli temi. ltolvil ebraelta sakartveloshi  -saukunovani ushpotveli tskhovreba kartveli eris tolerantobis didi traditsiis dasturia. dadaenobriv vels motsqvetilma ebraulma temma verts sakartveloshi sheinarchuna tsinaprebis salaparako ena; sakartveloshi isini metqveleben kartulad (romelits garkveuli taviseburebebit khasiatdeba). sakartvelo araertkhel ikna dapqrobili damezoblebuli imperiebis mier. kartvel ers arasodes gamouchenia simkatsre sakartveloshi damkvidrebuli im etnosis mimart, romelits dziritadi mosakhleoba iqo am imperiistvis da romelits mshvidobian tanaarsebobas itsqebda. amzhamindeli vitarebats samagalitoa: sakartveloshi ar tsarmokmnila agresia sakartvelos mokalake rusebis mimart, aseve rusi khalkhis mimart, miukhedavad imisa, rom eltsin-putin-medvedevis ruseti mizanmimartulad tsdilobs, dashalos sakartvelos   
 saqoveltaod tsnobilia, rom somkhebi, rusebi, azerbaijanelebi da turkebi sakartveloshi avtoktonebi ar arian. 
 sakhelmtsipo. aseve, agresia arts osebis mimart tsarmokmnila, miukhedavad imisa, bolo periodshi stsored osebis erti natsilis gamoqenebit akherkhebs ruseti sakartvelos teritoriebis okupatsiasa da aneksias. sakartveloshi migrirebuli etnikuri jgupebis shtamomavlebis didi natsili sakartvelos sakhelmtsipos ertguli shvilebi iqvnen; amitomatsaa, rom sakartvelos tsmindanta tu erovnul gmirta natsili dzvel migrantta (samagalitod davasakhelebt tsarmomadgenlebi arian sakartvelostvis mebrdzol gmirs - khudia borchaloels). paktia: sakartveloshi arasodes qopila etnokonpliktebi. migrant utskhoelebtan damokidebuleba kartul enis sitqvatkmnadobasa tu gamotkmebshitsaa asakhuli: "stumari ghvtisaa", sa-utskho-o (sauketeso) da skhv. shesabamisad, dzveli migrantebisa tu diasporebis uplebebis damtsavi saertashoriso dokumentebis arsi  bunebrivad sheesabameba kartul khasiatsa da kartuli sakhelmtsipos istoriul printsipebs ; kerdzod, diasporebis tu akhali migrantebis enobrivi uplebebis damtsveli saertashoriso samartlebrivi dokumentebi: "erovnul an etnikur, religiur da enobriv umtsiresobata uplebebis gaeros deklaratsia" , "oslos rekomendatsiebi" , "lundis rekomendatsiebi" , "erovnul umtsiresobata datsvis shesakheb 
 charcho konventsia"  da skhva saertashoriso aktebi edzghvneba motsemuli sakhelmtsipos mokalakeobis mkone, magram araistoriuli (migrirebuli) etnikuri jgupebis diasporebis - tsarmomadgenelta enobrivi uplebebis datsvas (msjelobisatvis ikh., agretve, zemot). etnikuri umtsiresobebis enobrivi uplebebi shtambechdavadaa datsuli agretve, sakartvelos kanonmdeblobit; mag., ikh.: sakartvelos konstitutsia , kanoni mokalakeobis shesakheb", kanoni geograpiuli obiektebis sakhelis shesakheb", kanoni reklamis shesakheb", "zogadi administratsiuli kodeksi" (me-  mukhli), "kanoni sajaro samsakhuris shesakheb", "sakartvelos saarchevno kodeksi" (tb.,  ,  , ,  ,  ,   mukhlebi), "kanoni ganatlebis shesakheb", "siskhlis samartlis saprotseso kodeksi", samokalako samartlis saprotseso kodeksi", "administratsiuli kodeksi", "kanoni adgilobrivi tvitmmartvelobis shesakheb" da skhv. etnikur umtsiresobata "enobriv uplebebze" msjelobisas khelisuplebis mier, pirvel rigshi, gasatvalistsinebelia dasavletevropuli khedva avtoktoni (istoriuli) umtsiresobebisa da akhali umtsiresobebis skhvadaskhvaobis shesakheb; aseve, diperentsirebuli midgomaa sachiro araistoriuli umtsiresobebis (diasporebis) sami sakhis sazogadoebis enis mimart: 
   mukhli  :  . sakartvelos mokalakeni tanastsori arian sotsialur, ekonomikur, kulturul da politikur tskhovrebashi ganurchevlad mati erovnuli, etnikuri, religiuri tu enobrivi kutvnilebisa. saertashoriso samartlis saqoveltaod aghiarebuli printsipebisa da normebis shesabamisad, mat upleba akvt tavisuplad, qovelgvari diskriminatsiisa da charevis gareshe ganavitaron tavianti kultura, isargeblon dedaenit pirad tskhovrebashi da sajarod... .mukhli  : samartaltsarmoeba khortsieldeba sakhelmtsipo enaze. pirs, romelmats sakhelmtsipo ena ar itsis, miechineba tarjimani... 
 shdr., mag., mukhli  . : "saarchevno biuleteni ibechdeba tseskos gankargulebis sapudzvelze, mis mier dadgenili nimushis mikhedvit, kartul enaze, apkhazetshi - agretve apkhazur enaze, kholo sachiroebis shemtkhvevashi - adgilobrivi mosakhleobistvis gasageb skhva enazets. 
 etnosis enis saprtkhis kves mqopobisa ( ) tu umtsiresobis raodenobis ( ) gatvalistsinebit ar mokhdeba migranti etnikuri jgupebis daqopa istoriul migrantebad (diasporebad) da akhal migrantebad. akve shevnishnavt, rom am temis irgvliv diskusiaa mtel msoplioshi . akve erti kitkhvats: aris tu ara sakartvelo multietnikuri kveqana? am kitkhvis logikuri da argumentirebuli pasukhits mkholod im shemtkhvevashia shesadzlebeli, tuki ganvsazghvravt im kriteriumebs, ris sapudzvelzets unda mokhdes motsemul kveqanashi ama tu im sazogadoebistvis istoriuli erovnuli/etnikuri tu migranti umtsiresobis statusis minicheba. 
 aris tu ara sakartvelo multietnikuri tu mravalerovani kveqana? sakartveloshi vin sheidzleba chaitvalos: - istoriul etnikur (erovnul) umtsiresobad? - akhal etnikur (erovnul) umtsiresobad? - akhal migrantad? tomash vikherkevichisa da misi kartveli tanaavtorebis mier sakartvelo itsodeba mravalerovan (multietnikur) kveqnad, sadats terminit: "etnikuri jgupebi" moikhseneba: apkhazebi, osebi (gv.  ), azerbaijanelebi, somkhebi, rusebi, berdznebi, ukrainelebi, polonelebi, kurtebi, iezidebi, ebraelebi, asirielebi, kistebi, chechnebi, lekebi, udiebi, qabardoelebi, cherkezebi (gv.  )... svanebi, megrelebi, lazebi (gv.  ). sakartvelos aseti "etnikuri" mravalperovneba skhvaganats araertkhel aghnishnula . sakartvelos enobrivetnikuri situatsiis shesakheb avtoritetul saertashoriso gamotsemebshits aris msgavsi araadekvaturi "shepasebebi" . shdr.: tomash vikherkevichis samshobloshi "erovnul umtsiresobad" miichneva skhvagan sakhelmtsipoebriobis mkone erovneba, mag., germanelebi; kholo etnikur umtsiresobad - polonetshi mtskhovrebi iseti jgupi, romelsats arts skhvagan akvs sakhelmtsipoebrioba (mag., boshebi) . ama tu im kveqnis gamotskhadeba mravalerovnul sakhelmtsipod unda mokhdes am kveqanashi mtskhovrebi etnikuri jgupebis obiekturi istoriisa da saertashoriso samartlebrivi aktebis sapudzvelze minichebuli statusis   
 mikhedvit; am mkhriv sakartveloshi jer kidev bevri ramaa gasaketebeli . am etapze samartlebrivi printsipebitaa dasadgeni, tu sakartveloshi romeli sazogadoebebi miekutvnebian erovnul (etnikur) umtsiresobas, romlebi tsarmoadgenen diasporebs da romeli unda chaitvalos akhal migrantad. amtavitve vitqvit, rom, mag.,   tslis aghtserit sakartveloshi ar tskhovrobda arts erti iezidi, kholo   tslis mikhedvit dapiksirebulia     suli . problemas artulebs isits, rom saertashoriso samartalshi am etapze ar arsebobs terminebis: erovnuli umtsiresoba, istoriuli erovnuli umtsiresoba, akhali erovnuli umtsiresoba, diaspora, dzveli migranti, akhali migranti... iseti ganmartebani, romlebzets konsensusia mightseuli; tumtsa, depinitsiebs akvs saerto tsakhnagebits; mag., "erovnuli umtsiresobis" shesakheb spetsialistta ganskhvavebul mosazrebebs saerto akvt ganmartebis zogadi "charcho": erovnuli umtsiresoba aris motsemul kveqanashi mudmivad mtskhovrebi mosakhleobis aradominirebuli natsili, romelits umravlesobisagan ganskhvavdeba tavisi etnikuri, religiuri tu lingvisturi makhasiateblebit da surs sheinarchunos sakutari tvitmqopadoba . "mudmivad mtskhovreb" mokalaked chaitvleba qvela piri, vints miigho am kveqnis mokalakeoba, magram aset pirta jgupi itvleba ki erovnul umtsiresobad? gamotkmulia mosazreba, rom migrantta meore an mesame taoba chaitvalos erovnul umtsiresobad .   
 mati istoriats da raodenobats; mag.:   tslis aghtseris mikhedvit, sakartveloshi dapiksirebulia mokalakeobis mkone  -ze meti etnikuri jgupi; amatgan, mag., tajikebi   suli; chinelebi -  ; bosha -  ; koreeli -  ; sparseli  ; kurti -  ; ingushi -  ; kisti -  ; chekhi -  ... shdr., agretve:        .  sakartvelos mokalake kartvelebi        ,       .  azerbaijaneli      .  somekhi      .  rusi      .  osi      .  berdzeni      .  ukraineli      .  kurti bunebrivia, sakartvelos mokalakeobis mkone, magram sakartvelostvis araistoriuli (akhali) etnikuri jgupebis enebis mimart ar unda gavrtseldes "evropuli kartia regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb". amave dros, droulad unda ganisazghvros is kriteriumebi (mkvidrobis istoria, mokalaketa raodenoba, enis saprtkhis kvesh qopnis khariskhi...), romelta mikhedvit etnikuri jgupebis erti natsili miichneva sakartvelos etnikur (erovnul) umtsiresobad, meore natsili diasporis (akhali umtsiresobis) uplebis mkone pirebad, mesame natsili ki - akhal migrantebad. akve erti arsebiti kitkhvats: sakartvelos msgavsad, msoplios titkmis qvela sakhelmtsiposhi tskhovrobs ateulobit migranti etnosis tsarmomadgeneli; ra kriteriumebis mikhedvit unda ganisazghvros is mijna, romlits mikhedvitats mokalakeobis mkone migrirebul jgupebs mienichebat etnikuri   umtsiresobis (diasporis) tu akhali migrantebis statusi?   
 vpikrob, kartuli sinamdvilidan gamomdinare, am etapze akhali etnikuri umtsiresobebis (diasporis) statusi sheidzleba mienichos im dzvel migrantebs , romelta raodenoba saerto mosakhleobis   %-s sheadgens. logikuri ikneba, tuki mati enebis mimart gavrtseldeba oslosa tu haagis "rekomendatsiebi" (da ara - "evropuli kartia regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb"). amgvari midgomis mikhedvit unda mokhdes sakartvelos michneva mravaletnikur tu chveulebriv sakhelmtsipod (sadats  -  etnikuri umtsiresoba da aseve ramdenime diaspora tskhovrobs). 
 azerbaijaneli ( .  %), somekhi ( .  %), rusi ( .  %). logikis mikhedvit, stsored amat mimart unda gavrtseldes haagisa da oslos rekomendatsiebi (da ara: "enis kartiis" debulebebi). shesabamisad, terminologiuri shesitqveba: "multietnikuri kveqana" sakartvelostvis sheusabamod migvachnia. akve kidev ertkhel shevnishnav: saertashoriso kselshi arsebuli araadekvaturi kvalipikatsiebisa tu t. vikherkevichis jgupis dausabutebeli rekomendatsiebis mikhedvit tu mokhdeba "regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartiis" ratipikatsia, saprtkhe sheekmneba ara mkholod sakartvelos sakhelmtsipo enas (dairghveva evropuli konventsiis ert-erti umtavresi motkhovna ), aramed sakartvelos sakhelmtsipoebriobasats . 
 ikh., evropuli kartiis preambula. didia albatoba imisa, rom t. vikherkevichis rekomendatsiebis realizebis shemtkhvevashi stimuli dezintegratsiul protsesebs ara mkholod sakartveloshi... 
 dasazustebelia aseve, ra dro unda viguliskhmot "dzvelshi". 
 jgupis mietseba 
 sakitkhis istoriis, masalisa da msjelobisatvis ikh., shushana putkaradze, chveneburebis kartuli, batumi,  ; t. putkaradze, imerkhevis metqveli mitsa-tsqali, kutaisi,  ; manana tabidze, sakartvelos parglebs garet mtskhovreb kartvelta enobrivi orientatsiisatvis, lazet-chaneti: istoria da tanamedroveoba (tezisebi), tb.,  ; ikh., agretve, g. alasanias, n. tsetskhladzis, i. koplatadzis, m. tsintsadzis, l. tandilavas, i. tandilavas, r. diasamidzis, t. putkaradzis, e. makaradzis, m. shahinis... gamokvlevebi da zhurnal "chveneburebsa" tu "pirosmanshi" gamokveqnebuli masalebi.   ikh. kartiis  -e da  -e ganmartebani.   
 kartvelebi kompakturad tskhovroben iranshits. irani ar aris evrosabchos tsevri kveqana, magram ak maints shevekhebit am kveqanashi mtskhovreb kartvelta enis temas:   saukunis tsin kartvelebi sakartvelodan idzulebit aqara da iranshi gadaasakhla mashindelma sparsetis imperiam; shesabamisad, iranis amzhamindel khelisuplebas meti motivatsia akvs, daitsvas pereidnel kartvelta dedaenobrivi kulturats da enobrivi uplebebits. dghes iranshi kartuli ena ar idevneba, magram arts sakhelmtsipo skolebshi istsavleba. rusetshi, amerikis sheertebuli shtatebshi, saberdznetsa da skhva kveqnebshi kartuli ena diasporata an migrantta enaa; migrantta enobriv uplebebs qvela kveqnis kanonmdebloba itsavs, magram kartvel migrantebsa tu diasporis tsarmomadgenlebs tavianti identobis dasatsavad tanadgoma, pirvel rigshi, sakartvelos sakhelmtsipom unda gautsios. amastan dakavshirebit, sainteresoa t. vikherkevichisa da misi kartveli kolegebis ert-erti "rekomendatsiats"; kerdzod,  -e gverdze vkitkhulobt: "gansakutrebuli adgili unda daetmos turketshi mtskhovrebi lazebisa da apkhazetis teritoriaze mosakhle megrelebis sotsiolingvistur kvlevas. dasazustebelia da gansasazghvria ik arsebuli enobrivi situatsia, maksimaluri dzaliskhmevis gagheba sakartvelos iurisdiktsiis garet moktseuli chveni tanamodzmeebis enobrivi da kulturuli memkvidreobisa da tvitshegnebis  shenarchunebisa da ganvitarebisatvis" (stili datsulia - t.p.). kargi ikneboda, am rekomendatsiis avtorebs gakhsenebodat turketis avtoktoni skhva kartvelebits: machakhlelebi, livanelebi, imerkhevlebi, taoelebi... turketis mokalake avtoktoni kartvelebis enobrivkulturuli "tvitshegnebis" shesakheb sametsniero mimoktsevashi ukve diddzali literaturaa. vpikrob, sjobda   
 ajobebda, am kontekstshi gamoeqenebinat termini: "meoba", an "tvitmqopadoba". 
 khazgasmuliqo turketis kartvelobis dedaenis kartulis - datsvis problema. samtsukharod, rekomendatorebma paktobrivad, ulogikod gaatanabres apkhazetsa da turketshi megrelta da lazta enobriv-kulturuli identobis sakitkhi. t. vikherkevichis jgupis mier motsonebuli (gv.  - ) prop. i. gipertis "kavkasiis enebis rukis" mikhedvit, turketis respublikashi moktseul istoriul kartul teritoriaze tao-klarjetshi, aseve, apkhazet-samegrelosa da tskhinvalis mkhareshi saertod ar aris kartuli ena. saquradgheboa isits, rom bolo periodshi ruset-sakartvelos omis shemdeg apkhazetsa da tskhinvalis mkhareshi, paktobrivad, gankhortsielda kartvelta genotsidi da am mkhareta enobrivi situatsia martlats daemsgavsa gipertis rukisas . sakartvelos khelisuplebis zrunvis sagani ertnairad unda gakhdes sakartvelos sakhelmtsipos amzhamindel sazghvrebs garet mtskhovrebi rogorts avtoktoni, aseve migrirebuli jgupebi tu diasporebi. rats sheekheba rusetis mier  -  tslebshi okupirebuli kartuli mitsa-tsqlidan (apkhazetidan, gamodevnil kartvelta tskhinvalis mkharidan)  
 mokalakeobriv tu enobriv-kulturul uplebebs: es skhva rigis gamotsvevaa sakartvelos tsinashe; turketis sazghvrebshi moktseuli kartvelebis enobriv-kulturuli uplebebisgan ganskhvavebit, es problema ver gadatsqdeba rusetis saokupatsio rezhimis mier "regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartiis" amokmedebis shemtkhvevashits ki. apkhazetsa da tskhinvalis mkhareshi realurad unda aghdges sakartvelos iurisdiktsia. 
 daskvniti msjeloba "regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartia" ("enis kartia") tavisi arsit nateli da maghali donis dokumentia; igi ar sheitsavs romelime kveqnistvis sakhipato debulebebs. "enis kartiisa" da haagis tu oslos "rekomendatsiebis" miznebis gamijvnisa da printsipebis gatvalistsinebis shemtkhvevashi, sakhelmtsipo enis punktsiis dakninebis gareshe sakartveloshits da skhva kveqnebshits shesadzlebelia, rom satanado statusi ganesazghvros kveqanashi arsebul qvela lingvistur erteuls da realurad datsul iknas dziritadi mosakhleobis, istoriuli umtsiresobis, akhali umtsiresobisa tu migrantebis tsarmomadgenelta enobrivi uplebebi. "enis kartia" khels utsqobs sakhelmtsipoebriobis armkone, an skhva sakhelmtsipoebriv velshi moktseuli avtoktoni - istoriuli (da ara - akhali) umtsiresobis mier enobriv-kulturuli (erovnuli) memkvidreobis shenarchunebas. garda amisa, regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartia" itkhovs, prioriteti mienichos saprtkhis tsinashe mqopi, dautsveli istoriuli umtsiresobebis enebs" . "enis kartiis" debulebebi ar vrtseldeba motsemuli sakhelmtsipos "akhali umtsiresobebis" enis mimart; am mimartulebit arsebobs skhva saertashoriso samartlebrivi dokumentebi (haagisa da oslos rekomendatsiebi da skhv.). "enis kartiis" debulebebs tu gavitvalistsinebt, motsemul sakhelmtsiposhi sheidzleba vivaraudot   sakhis enis arseboba: - traditsiuli (avtoktoni) dziritadi mosakhleobis ena sakhelmtsipo ena (romelzets zrunavs motsemuli sakhelmtsipo); 
 - avtonomiur tsarmonakmnshi - avtonomiuri tsarmonakmnis sakhelmdebeli sazogadoebis ena - meore sakhelmtsipo ena am tsarmonakmnshi (romelzets zrunaven sakhelmtsiposa da avtonomiuri tsarmonakmnis khelisuplebebi); motsemul sakhelmtsiposhi mtskhovrebi istoriuli, avtoktoni etnikuri umtsiresobis ena; igi unda daitsvas sakhelmtsipom "enis kartiis" mesame natsilis gatvalistsinebit (datsulobis maghali khariskhi); - motsemul sakhelmtsiposhi saukuneebis tsin damkvidrebuli migranti etnikuri jgupis ena, romelsats skhvagan ara akvs datsulobis perspektiva; motsemuli sakhelmtsipos ketili nebis shemtkhvevashi, am tipis enaze sheidzleba natsilis gavrtseldes "enis kartiis" meore debulebebi; skhva shemtkhvevashi, mat mimart amokmeddeba oslosa tu haagis "rekomendatsiebi"; - motsemul sakhelmtsiposhi saukuneebis tsin damkvidrebuli iseti migranti etnikuri jgupis (diasporis) ena, romelsats mezoblad (skhvagan) akvs sakhelmtsipo ena; am tipis enebis datsulobis khariskhi unda ganisazghvros oslosa tu haagis "rekomendatsiebis" da skhva msgavsi saertashoriso dokumentebis mikhedvit; - motsemul sakhelmtsiposhi okupantis mier tavsmokhveuli ena, romelsats deokupatsiis shemdeg statusi da datsulobis khariskhi unda ganesazghvros postokupatsiuri vitarebis gatvalistsinebit; - akhali migrantebis ena; migrantta enobrivi uplebebi sakhelmtsipom unda daitsvas shesabamisi saertashoriso dokumentebis motkhovnebis gatvalistsinebit . 
   robert dunbari, "komentarebi: charcho khelshekrulebisa da enis kartiis urtiertobebi", charchos shevseba, dokumentebis krebuli,  , gv.  . 
 vpikrob, tu gavitvalistsinebt sakartvelos enobrivetnikuri situatsiis realur istoriul dinamikas, evrosabchostvis droulad momzaddeba "regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartiis" shesakheb sakartvelos sakhelmtsipos iseti gantskhadeba, romelits: 
 d a n a r t i danarti №   kutaisuri memorandumi  
 - ar daazaralebs sakartvelos sakhelmtsipo enis statuss; - evropashi aghiarebul kanonier standartebshi moaktsevs sakartveloshi arsebuli istoriuli tu akhali umtsiresobebis enobriv-kulturuli paseulobebisa da enobrivi uplebebis datsvas. 
 mighebul ikna kutaisshi   tsels; paksimileebiturt pirvelad gamokveqnda krebulshi: ksu dialektologiis sametsniero-kvleviti instituti ( -  tslebi), kutaisi,  , gv.  ; "memorendumis" shesakheb ikh., agretve: t. gvantseladze, enisa da dialektis sakitkhi kartvelologiashi, tb.,  , gv.  - ,  - . 
 kartvelobas: acharlebs, livanelebs, taoelebs, klarjelebs, javakhebs, samtskhelebs... am ponze kartvelta kutkhuri enobrivi variantebis gamotskhadeba "umtserlobo enebad", pirvel rigshi, tvit am kartvelebs daukargavs did kulturul tsarsuls, tundats im tekvsmetsaukunovan tsarsuls, romelits ioane lazisa da petre iberis moghvatseobit itsqebs tavisi ganvitarebis akhal etaps. garda amisa, kartvelta kutkhuri metqvelebebis tsalke enebad gamotskhadebit ikmneba seriozuli sapudzveli kartvelta enobrivi da etno-kulturuli ertianobis dashlisa. akve aghvnishnavt, rom, miukhedavad istoriuli ganvitarebis gzebis skhvadaskhvaobisa, zemot chamotvlil kartvelur etnograpiul-teritoriul jgupta kiloebis ponologiuri struktura, gramatikuli modeli da leksikuri pondi ertnairia. tanamedrove kartuli samtsignobro ena tavisi agebulebit saertokartveluri enis pirdapiri memkvidrea, amdenad, igi qvela kartvelistvis dedaenas tsarmoadgens, shesabamisad, kartuli samtsignobro ena kartvelta tvitidentipikatsiis udzvelesi sapudzvelia: kartveluri kiloebis umtserlobo enebad gamotskhadeba stsored am sapudzvels shlis. simpoziumze tsarmodgenili mokhsenebebidan aseve tsarmochnda, rom bevr gaugebrobas udebs sataves sametsniero literaturashi arsebuli terminologiuri sichrele. tsarmodgenil memorandumze khelmomtser kartvelologebs sachirod migvachnia:  . humanitarul dargebshi moghvatse kartvel metsnierta pozitsiebis shejereba da saerto tvalsazrisis gamomushaveba aghnishnul sakitkhtan dakavshirebit;  . tsarmodgenili problematikis shesakheb saertashoriso simpoziumebisa da seminarebis organizeba;  . sakartvelos etnolingvistur problematikastan dakavshirebuli utskhouri publikatsiebis mudmivi monitoringi;  . spetsialuri veb-gverdis shekmna, misi sistematuri ganakhleba; 
  . mravalenovani sametsniero zhurnalis sainterneto variantis momzadeba, sadats asakhuli ikneba kartvelologta simpoziumis mushaobis shedegebi... tsarmodgenili amotsanebis shesasruleblad autsilebelia: gapartovdes, satanado dapinansebita da aparaturit aghichurvos kutaisis akaki tseretlis sakhelobis sakhelmtsipo universitettan arsebuli dialektologiis sametsniero-kvleviti instituti; - sheikmnas tsnobil kartvelologta sakonsultatsio sabcho, romelits sheimushavebs satanado rekomendatsiebs. khels vatsert:  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .  .
