 danarti №   
 konstantine gamsakhurdias enobrivi kontseptsia (pragmentebi): "kartuli enis ganmartebiti leksikonis shemdgenlebs umtavresi quradgheba unda miektsiat khalkhuri metqvelebisatvis. es momenti mtlad ignorirebuli araa, magram sasurveli ikneboda, kartuli dialektebidan, tvit chanur-megrul-svanuridanats upro charbad shemoeshvat sitqvieri masala. kartuli enis skhvadaskhva ganshtoebani, e.i. misi dialektebi ulevi da jerats aghunuskhveli masalaa rogorts mtserlistvis, ise enatmetsnieristvis...” . "me shemovushvi akhal kartulshi mravali gardasuli sitqva; samagierod aseve ukhvad vaskhure chems leksikas khevsurulidan, imerulidan, kartl-kakhuridan da megrul-gurul enakavebidan motanili sitqvebi... me sachirod davinakhe kartuli tomebis (ganskhvavebuli) leksikis shekrebis lozungi gadamesrola da es pirvelad vtsade kidevats "dionisos ghimilshi" da chems novelebis tsignshiats. mashasadame, kartuli sitqvieri inventaris gamdidreba akhal saukuneshi unda momkhdariqo tsalkerdz dzveli kartulis maragidan, tsalkerdz tsotskhali dialektebisa da enakavebis tsiaghidan, rata kartuli ena martooden mshrali, mtsignobruli ena ar gamkhdariqo... kartul enas ar gaachnia monatesave enata ojakhi, rogorts tundats pranguls - romanuli enebi, germanulsa da inglisurs - germanta enebisa da rusuls - slavuri enebisa da enakavebis ojakhi. amitomats saliteraturo kartulis zrda ar sheidzleba martooden garegan seskhs - barbarizmebs daeqrdnos. ak umtavresia "shinagani seskhi", kartuli enakavebidan, svanur-chanur da odishur dialektebidan akhali da ukhmari leksikuri masalis mokhvecha... "  
 shesadzlebel varianttagan ertis gamorcheva tsinadadebis shinaarsis (azris) gatvalistsinebit ioli ar aris. asevea satanado (sauketeso) pormis gamonakhvats, radgan tsinadadebashi, prazashi sitqva marto ar aris iseve, rogorts vazis mtevani chukurtmashi, - kartveluri eklesiamonastrebis ert-erti mnishvnelovani atributi, chukurtma ostatisagan moitkhovda ara marto masalis gansazghvradamushavebas, tadzris parametrebisa da skhvadaskhva makhasiateblebis gatvalistsinebas, aramed, rats mtavaria, qvela detalshi kartveluri sulieri da materialuri kulturis taviseburebata tsarmochenas, asakhvas. k. gamsakhurdiam kargad itsoda, rom "...did da dzvel traditsiata matareblis, enis shesastsavlad adamianis ertjeri sitsotskhlets moklea", magram tavisi nichita da daughalavi shromit akherkhebda mshobliuri enis labirintebshi shesvlas, ik chabudebuli enobrivi shesadzleblobebis gamovlena-gamoqenebas kartveluri "tadzrebis" asagebad. amave dros, sitqvieri da pormaluri masalis sadzebnad enis sighrmeshi chasuli mtserali atskhadebda, rom daushreteli rezervuari chveni enisa es gakhlavt dzvelkartuli da chveni tomebis mravalkilovani dialektebi", rom ".. udzvelesi, magram literaturashi jerats ukhmari kartuli sitqvebi moipovebian guriashi, zemo da kvemo imeretshi, racha-lechkhumshi, samegrelosa da svanetshi". leksikuri masalis mudam madziebeli shemokmedi gapatsitsebit adevnebda tvalqurs akhali saenatmetsniero literaturis gamosvlas, - saquradgheboa misi kritikuli tserilebi kiziquris, kartuli enis ganmartebit leksikonebze... tavadats poulobda da dialektebidan saliteraturo enashi shemohkonda araerti saintereso sitqva. erti aseti shemtkhvevis shesakheb mas aghnishnuli akvs tanamedrove romanis sakitkhebze datseril meekvse tserilshi: "...toilo - priad sachiro sitqva, nishnavs sabels, romlitats sabalakhoze daabamen kholme tskhens". dznelia saubari imaze, ,"toilo"-s ukavshirebda tu ara mtserali megrulsa da lazurshi dadasturebul imave dziris zmnur pormas "kigiotoule" (daabi!). amis shesakheb igi arapers ambobs, 
 danarti №   revaz sherozia konstantine gamsakhurdia da kartveluri enobrivi samqaro "... erts kartvelurad kidev shesdzakhebs..." n. baratashvili 
 porma da verts "shinaarsi" kartvel poets ghirsebas ver shematebs. khelovnebisadmi aseti zerele damokidebuleba qoveltvis daupirispirdeba chveni tsinaprebis mier erovnuli, kartveluri tvalit danakhul shemokmedebas. 
 saukuneebis kartvel moghvatseta analogiuri pozitsia, rats miughebeli aghmochnda tanamedrove kartvelologta natsilisatvis. zogiertma matganma dasakhelebul propesorebs qovlad uvargisi termini -"sameuli..." "miatseba". samartliani ikneboda da madlobelits davrchebodi, tu sami tsertilidan ert-ertshi am statiis avtors iguliskhmebdnen. 
 danarti №   konstantine gamsakhurdias enobrivi kontseptsiis mikhedvit shekmnili proekti : "kartveluri dialekturi leksika samtsignobro enisatvis" (sarekomendatsio sitqvata elektronuli leksikoni)  
  . kvlevis siakhle, mizani da amotsanebi  . . problemis aktualoba da kvlevis siakhle kartuli samtsignobro ena saukuneebis ganmavlobashi utsqvetad ikmneboda da mdidrdeboda sakartvelos qvela kutkhis tsarmomadgenelta (kartlelta, imerelta, megrelta, svanta, khevsurta...) aktiuri monatsileobita da dzaliskhmevit. amitomats aris igi qvela kartvelisatvis ertnairad mshobliuri da dzvirpasi. chveni klasikosi mtserlebi, sazogado moghvatseebi da kartuli enis mkvlevrebi kartvelur dialektur masalas 
 proekti ar dapinansda: ganatlebisa da metsnierebis saministros ("rustavelis") pondis ekspertebs ar moetsonat proektis mizani da amotsanebi; metits, r.vakhitovis msgavsi miznis mkone ert-ertma ekspertma danashaulad gamoatskhada megrul-lazurisa da svanuris gatanabreba kartvelta skhva sashinao metqvelebebtan da am kartuli khalkhuri simdidris gamotskhadeba erovnuli enis - kartuli samtsignobri enis - sabazo leksikad. es arapropesionali "eksperti" ar itsnobs tsnebas: "kartveluri dialektebi"; garda amisa, mas hgonia, rom kartuli enis sakheskhvaobebi (megruli, lazuri, svanuri...) isetive damoukidebeli enebia, rogorts monatesave - apkhazuri, chechnuri, daghestnuri da aramonatesave - chinuri, germanuli... paktia, rom ramdenime 
 ketilsindisieri ekspertis gamoklebit, "rustavelis pondshi" "daregistrirebul" ekspertta didi natsili orientirebulia iseti kartvelologiuri proektebis dapinansebaze, romlebits khels utsqoben kartveli eris enobriv-etnikur dashlas (ikh., agretve:  -e da me-  skolioebi, msjeloba  -e gverdze da me-  danarti).   momzadda atssu kartveluri dialektologiis sametsnierokvlevit institutis tsmida ambrosi khelaias sakhelobis sametsnierosaganmanatleblo tsentrshi prop. e. dadianis khelmdzghvanelobit. 
 dialekturi 
 leksikis 
 tvalsazrisit, 
 sainteresoa 
 "masalebi shinamretsvelobisa da khelosnobis istoriisatvis",   tomad ( - ; iv. javakhishvilis saerto redaktsiit)... 
 miukhedavad dialektur leksikonta simravlisa, dghemde ar arsebobs kiloebshi datsul iset sitqvata leksikoni, romelits rekomendatsiis sakhit mietsodeba parto momkhmarebels. stsored amgvari leksikuri erteulebi aris saliteraturo enis gamdidrebisa da gamravalperovnebis sapudzveli. mati aghnuskhva da tsalke leksikonad sistematizatsia autsilebelia. dghes, globalizatsiisa da utskhoenovani leksikuri erteulebis modzalebis ponze, sakitkhi gansakutrebul aktualobas idzens. enashi khshirad umartebulod ikidebs pekhs utskhouri sitqva-gamotkmebi, barbarizmebi, mashin rodesats misi shesatqvisi kartul enashi arsebobs. es ki saliteraturo enis leksikur ponds nel-nela saprtkhes ukmnis. dialektebidan zomierad da sachiroebisamebr shercheuli leksikis saliteraturo enashi shemotanita da gaaktiurebit natsilobriv maints sheneldeba utskhouri leksikis mocharbebis tendentsia. bolo periodis mtseralta shemokmedebashi titkosda shesustda dialekturi leksikis dziebis tsqurvili (aktsenti upro zhargonul gamonatkvamebsa da utskhour sitqvebzea gadatanili); enatmetsnierta (dialektologta) valia, mtserlebs gavuiolot chvens kiloebshi davanebuli "bajaghlo okro" sitqvebis povna. vpikrobt, proektis tsarmatebit gankhortsieleba problemis gadatsqvetas didad sheutsqobs khels. proektshi chartul spetsialistebs kartvelur dialektta kvlevisa da leksikonebze mushaobis didi gamotsdileba akvt. atssu kartveluri dialektologiis sametsniero-kvlevit institutshi punktsionirebs tsminda ambrosi aghmsareblis (khelaias) sakhelobis sametsniero-saganmanatleblo tsentri, romlis sakmianobis dziritadi mimartuleba kartveluri dialekturi leksikis kvleva-dziebaa. proekti tavis arsit martlats mnishvnelovani da sachiroa chveni enis sitsmindis datsvisa da sitqvieri pondis ganakhlebisatvis. kartveluri dialektebis sapudzvelze momzadebuli leksikoni "kartveluri dialekturi leksika samtsignobro enisatvis" (sarekomendatsio sitqvata 
  . kvlevis metodika da mosalodneli shedegebi  . . kvlevis metodikis shesabamisoba proektis mizansa da amotsanebtan proektze mushaobisas gamoqenebuli ikneba aghtseriti metodi, rats guliskhmobs dialektur leksikonebsa da tekstebshi, agretve etnograpiul gamokvlevebshi arsebuli saintereso leksikuri erteulebis amokrebas, mat sistematizatsias, shedarebas gamokveqnebul dialektur da ganmartebit leksikonebtan... tsalkeuli saleksikono erteulebi dalagdeba anbantrigze, mietiteba, tu romel dialektshi (an dialektebshi) aris gavrtselebuli. gansamartav sitqvastan tsarmodgenili ikneba shesabamisi sailustratsio nimushebi. shemotsmebul-shejerebuli masala (saleksikono momzaddeba erteulebi) aikripeba kompiutershi; leksikonis elektronuli versia. 
 proektis miznis misaghtsevad metsnieruli kvlevisas gamoqenebuli ikneba agretve diasistemuri da istoriulshedarebiti metodebi.  .  kvlevis mosalodneli shedegebi da mati mnishvneloba kartveluri dialektebis sapudzvelze shekmnili kartuli samtsignobro enis sarekomendatsio sitqvata elektronuli leksikoni, dghemde gamokveqnebuli leksikonebisagan ganskhvavebit, unikaluri ikneba tavisi danishnulebit, tematikis mravalperovnebit; maghal metsnierul doneze damushavebuli leksikoni sando tsqaro moghvatse ikneba kartvelologiis speroshi spetsialistebisatvis (enatmetsniertatvis, etnologtatvis...). proektis gankhortsielebis shedegad mivighebt: tanamedrove teknikuri sashualebebita da akhleburi metodologiit kartveluri dialektebidan (megruli, lazuri, svanuri, imeruli, lechkhumuri, rachuli) shercheul leksikur erteulebs, romelta damkvidreba saliteraturo enas gaamravalperovnebs. shesabamisad, proektis dapinansebit sametsniero sazogadoeba miighebs khalkhuri metqvelebis tsiaghidan momdinare saintereso sitqvata elektronul korpussa da pundamentur gamokvlevebs; igi khelmisatsvdomi ikneba qvela dainteresebuli pirisatvis... kartuli samtsignobro enisatvis sarekomendatsio sitqvata leksikonis shekmna khels sheutsqobs kartuli saliteraturo enis gamdidrdebas saintereso dialekturi sitqvapormebit; amit natsilobriv maints avitsilebt tavidan utskhoenovani sitqvebis modzalebas. proektis tsarmateba kartuli enatmetsnierebis shemdgomi ganvitarebisatvis tvalsachino da natelia. amdenad, proektis shedegebi utuod tsaadgeba kartuli saliteraturo enisa da misi mravalritskhovani dialektebis kvleva-dziebit, shestsavlita tu stsavlebit dainteresebul pirebs. es kidev upro zrdis proektis 
 mnishvnelobas da sartsmunos khdis misi gankhortsielebis autsileblobas. stsori metodologiit shedgenili "kartuli samtsignobro enisatvis sarekomendatsio sitqvata leksikonis" shekmna mnishvnelovania agretve kartveluri kulturuli (enobrivi) memkvidreobis srulqopilad tsarmochenis tvalsazrisit.  . proektis shemsruleblebi  . . dziritadi personali: dadiani eka - sametsniero khelmdzghvaneli, menejeri; sherozia revaz - lazuri masalis mkvlevari pirtskhelani davit - svanuri masalis mkvlevari kashia rusudan - imeruli masalis mkvlevari bandzeladze onise - lechkhumuri masalis mkvlevari khachapuridze luiza - rachuli masalis mkvlevari katsarava marine - leksikograpi. 
 romlebits tsaikitkheba dghes. minda madloba movakhseno qvelas, vints ishroma am mokhsenebebze. mtsams, kartveli eri ar daushvebs, rom mokhdes daqopa chveni erisa. chven gvakvs erti geni, erti kultura, erti sartsmunoeba da chven qvelapers gavaketebt imisatvis, rom kartvelma erma es mtlianoba sheinarchunos. 
 sapatriarko rezidentsia,   ivnisi   tseli kalbatonebo da batonebo, gulitadad mogesalmebit qvelas. mokharuli var, rom dghes shedga chveni shekhvedra sapatriarkoshi. es konperentsia tardeboda lentekhsa da mestiashi da dghes ak, tbilisshi dasruldeba. svanetshi davanebuli kartuli kultura metad sachiro da mnishvnelovania. kargad mogekhsenebat, rom samtsukharod, arseboben iseti adamianebi, romeltats surt gahqon kartveli eri da akvt survili, tsarmoachinon svaneti da svanuri dialekti, rogorts kartuli erisagan damoukidebeli, ganskhvavebuli kultura. es aseve sheekheba samegrelos da skhva kutkheebsats. chven kargad vitsit, saidan momdinareobs es. es jer kidev   tslis tsin daitsqo, rotsa ruseti tsdilobda, gaeqo kartveli eri. vpikrob, rom is adamiani, romelits tsdilobs tsarmoadginos svanuri kultura, rogorts damoukidebeli kartuli kulturisagan, - aris mteri ara marto svanebisa, aramed mteli kartveli erisa. me didi quradghebit tsavikitkhe konperentsiis programa, romelits kvemo da zemo svanetshi chatarda. dzalian mnishvnelovania is mokhsenebebi, romelits ukve gaketda da 
 ghmertma daglotsot, ghmertma gagakharot da ghmertma gaamtlianos sruliad sakartvelo! 
 sakartvelos katalikos-patriarkis lotsva-kurtkhevita da sakartvelos sapatriarkos tsagerisa da lentekhis episkoposis, stepanes didi ghvatslit   tslis  -  ivniss lentekhshi gaikhsna svanetisadmi midzghvnili sametsniero konperentsia: svaneti - kartuli kulturis savane; sametsniero porumi gagrdzelda  -  ivniss mestiashi da shemajamebeli skhdomit daikhura   ivniss tbilisshi, sapatriarko rezidentsiis did darbazshi. konperentsiaze tsarmodgenili iqo   mokhseneba.   
 ikh. agretve,  -e skolio 
 inteligentsiis tsinaaghmdegobis gamo man es idea (kartvelta enobriv-etnikuri dashla!) ver ganakhortsiela. dghes rusets surs, `evropuli kartiis" arastsori gaazreba moakhvios tavs sakartvelos parlaments. "evropuli kartiis" miznebsa da sakartvelos parlamentis mier ratipikatsiis perspektivas araerti gamokvleva udzghvna b-ma t. putkaradzem, amitom am temas ak aghar shevekhebit. msjelobas gavagrdzelebt avtonomiis motkhovnis "ideis" shesakheb: tserilshi: "khalkhis gaqopa" moskoveli ideologebi sakartvelos ert-ert regionis mosakhleobas moutsodeben, moitkhovon avtonomia; amasve ubidzgeneb skhvebsats. amave tserilshi dzalze tsukhan "acharis avtonomiis paktobrivi gaukmebis gamots"; tumts avtori tavs imit imshvidebs, rom, misi azrit, sakartvelos gaertianebis idea tsarumatebeli aghmochnda, is tsers: "apkhazetisa da samkhret osetis chamoshoreba mkholod sakhelmtsipos daqopisa; dasatsqisia sakartvelos sakartvelo am katastropisatvis rusets adanashaulebs, magram sakartvelo stabiluri sakhelmtsipo rom qopiliqo, es ar mokhdeboda". avtori dums da arapers ambobs imis shesakheb, rom sakartveloshi destabilizatsiis stimulatori qoveltvis postsabchota ruseti iqo. sainteresoa, rom bashkirel dotsents ukve stsodnia tanamedrove kartvel enatmetsnierta erti natsilis tvalsazrisi, rom svanuri ert-erti dialektia kartuli enisa. es teoria mas dzalze aghashpotebs da tsers: "shua saukuneebshi, ra tkma unda, kartveli eri ar arsebobda, ara tu dzvelad, amzhamadats ki iseti ganskhvavebaa, vtkvat, kartvelebsa da svanebs shoris, rom sachiroa sagangebo "kartul-svanuri leksikoni"... misive dezinpormatsiit: "natsionalist gamsakhurdias mmartvelobis dros svani "opalchentsebi" iaraghit khelshi gamodiodnen kartveli natsionalistebis tsinaaghmdeg. skhvata shoris, es khels ar 
 ushlis tbilisel khelmdzghvanelebs utsodon svanebs "kartvelt subetnosi", kholo svanur enas _ "kartuli enis dialekti" ("literaturnaia gazeta",  - , noemberi,  ). avtoris am sitsrueebs mosdevs sashinlad damtsinavi tsilistsamebani kartveli khalkhis mimart; kerdzod, is tsers: "aravitari kartuli natsia da, shesabamisad, aravitari kartveli saertod ar arsebobda rusettan samkhret kavkasiis sheertebamde. kartvelurma khalkhebma rusetis kveshevrdomoba tsaltsalke miighes. kartveli natsia da misi natsionalizmi chamoqalibda rusetis politikur sivrtseshi. mtavari roli am sakmeshi ikonia tsentraluri sabchota khelmdzghvanelobis uquradghebobam. amis mizezi iqo kartvelebis qopna sabchota khelmdzghvanelobashi - stalini, orjonikidze, beria. kartveli etnonatsionalistebis saboloo mizania kartveli natsiis konsolidatsia, sakartvelos sakhelmtsipos teritoriebis gazrda samkhedro-politikuri operatsiebit ajanqebul regionebshi, kholo rusetis, somkhetisa da turketis dasustebis shemtkhvevashi, chamochra mati teritoriebisa"... rusulimperiuli ideologi, epareba ra dotsentis tsodebas, umalavs mkitkhvels, rom stsored stalinisa da orjonikidzis monatsileobit rusetma   tsels daipqro sakartvelos ertiani, tsentralizebuli, demokratiuli sakhelmtsipo da amis shemdgom kartveli natsiis, anu sakartvelos sakhelmtsipos teritoriebis mnishvnelovani natsili gadastsa mezobel kveqnebs, mat shoris, rusetis pederatsias. ironiuli landzghvis shemdgom statiis avtori idzulebuli gakhda, maints eghiarebina simartle, rom sakartvelos amzhamindeli sakhelmtsipoebrioba qalibdeba evropuli sistemebis shesabamisad. avtori tvitonve ganarchevs ertmanetisgan msoplioshi sakhelmtsipota msheneblobis or gzas - evropulsa da araevropuls. avtors mohqavs ingliseli kulturis pilosoposis - arnold toinbis tvalsazrisi sakhelmtsipos msheneblobis dasavluri institutis shesakheb: 
 "natsionaluri sakhelmtsipoebis msheneblobis evropuli instituti guliskhmobs, rom kompakturad dasakhlebuli erti an monatesave enebze molaparake etnosebi akherkheben mat irgvliv "shua saukuneta etnosebis" konsolidatsias da qalibdebian natsiebad. ase chamoqalibdnen evropuli sakhelmtsipoebi, kholo planetis skhva regionebshi sakhelmtsipota msheneblobis am institutebma ver imushava." statiis avtori, rogorts aghvnishnet, idzulebulia aghiaros, rom sakartvelos sakhelmtsipoebrioba shendeba evropuli sistemebis shesabamisad, mas dzlier atsukhebs da surs, rogorme ar daushvas es. otsnebobs, rom aprikisa da aziis zogierti regionis msgavsad, sakartveloshits marad ghviodes samokalako omebis kerebi, rata kartvelebma ar airchion "dasavletis proekti"... mokled, asetia "literaturnaia gazetas" "megobruli" gegmebi sakartvelos dasakutsmatseblad da survili, rom sakartvelos parlamentma am protsess kheli sheutsqos; kerdzod, moskovel tu bashkirel avtors surs, "regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartiis" ratipikatsiis dokumentshi kartvelta tsalkeuli kutkhuri metqvelebebi dapiksirdes erovnuli umtsiresobebis enebad. 
 danarti  : sakartvelos ganatlebisa da metsnierebis saministros gantskhadeba 
 ¾ ,,tu am mukhlis pirveli punktit gansazghvruli uplebis gankhortsieleba sheudzlebelia standartuli vaucheris meshveobit, sakhelmtsipo aset mostsavleebs uzrunvelqops gazrdili vaucherit an/da damatebiti dapinansebit sakartvelos ganatlebisa da metsnierebis saministros mier damtkitsebuli shesabamisi miznobrivi programis parglebshi” (me-  mukhlis me-  punkti); ¾ ,,skola tanastsorobis sapudzvelze itsavs umtsiresobebis tsevrebis individualur da kolektiur uplebas, tavisuplad isargeblon mshobliuri enit, sheinarchunon da gamokhaton tavianti kulturuli kutvnileba” (me-  mukhlis me-  punkti). 
 sakhalkho damtsvelis aparattan arsebulma erovnuli umtsiresobebis sabchom tsarmodgenili rekomendatsiebis da shepasebebis sapudzvelze sheimushava shemtsqnareblobisa da samokalako integratsiis erovnuli kontseptsiis parglebshi samokmedo gegma. tsarmodgenili rekomendatsiebis da shepasebebis gankhilvashi monatsileobda qvela dainteresebuli mkhare, mat shoris statiashi mokhseniebuli organizatsiebi. gankhilvebi aktiurad mimdinareobda regionebshits da am protsesshi aktiurad iqvnen chartulebi ganatlebis da metsnieris ministri, ministris moadgile, strukturuli erteulebis da ssip-ebis khelmdzghvanelebi. samokmedo gegmis sapudzvelze ganisazghvra amotsanebi, mat shoris: sakhelmtsipos mier erovnuli umtsiresobebis enebze ganatlebis mighebis khelshetsqobis mimartulebit, multilingvuri stsavlebis danergvis mimartulebit (eutos umaghlesi komisartan ertad shemushavda stsavlebis kontseptsia, daitsqo stsavlebis modelebis danergva da skhv). mimdinareobs aktiuri tanamshromloba somkhetisa da azerbaijanis ganatlebis saministroebtan, konsultatsiebis sapudzvelze ukve shemushavda azerbaijanuli da somkhuri enis, rogorts mshobliuri enis stsavlebis standarti. aseve, ganisazghvra amotsanebi umaghlesi ganatlebis khelshetsqobis mimartulebit (mat shoris gamotsdebis erovnulma tsentrma rusul, somkhur, azerbaijanul enebze targmna abiturientta mosamzadebeli testebi zogad 
 unarebshi da mat akvt shesadzlebloba misaghebi gamotsda zogad unarebshi mshobliur enaze chaabaron), ,,sotsialuri grantebis programis” parglebshi dapinansdnen arakartulenovani studentebi samtskhe-javakhetidan da kvemo kartlidan da skhv. aseve, saministrom etnikuri azerbaijanelebistvis mshobliur enaze ganatlebis khelmisatsvdomobis, stsavlisa da stsavlebis uzrulvelqopis miznit ganakhortsiela skhvadaskhva ghonisdzieba, magalitad: erovnuli sastsavlo gegmebisa da shepasebis tsentris mier azerbaijanuli skolebistvis mshobliur enaze itargmna skolis   sakhelmdzghvanelo skhvadaskhva saganshi; mastsavleblebis propesiuli ganvitarebis tsentrma azerbaijanul enaze targmna mastsavleblis damkhmare sakhelmdzghvaneloebi, azerbaijanul enaze gamodis zhurnali ”mastsavlebeli”;   tsels igegmeba skolis direktorobis arakartulenovani kandidatebis testirebistvis momzadeba. programa ”iakob gogebashvilis” parglebshi mimdinareobs azerbaijanulenovani da somkhurenovani skolebis reabilitatsia da programa ”irmis nakhtomis” parglebshi kompiuterizatsia. es skolebi chartulebi arian mimdinare saskolo programebshi da skhv. sakartveloshi   azerbaijanulenovani skola da sektoria. ganatlebis saministro ar gegmavs artserti azerbaijanulenovani skolis likvidatsias. qovelive akedan gamomdinare, saministro statiashi moqvanil mosazrebebs apasebs, rogorts dezinpormatsiis gavrtselebis mtsdelobas.  . .  
 danarti №   
 ssip. iv. javakhishvilis istoriisa da etnologiis instituti   k.tbilisi, melikishvilis k. #  tel.  - -  #  .    /  "   " dekemberi   ts. 
 mis aghmatebulebas sakartvelos prezidents sruliad sakartvelos katolikos-patriarks, mis utsmindesobas da unetaresobas, ilia meores sakartvelos parlamentis tavmjdomares sakartvelos premier-ministrs   tslis   noembers shedga ssip iv. javakhishvilis istoriisa da etnologiis institutis sametsniero sabchos gapartoebuli skhdoma. skhdomas estsrebodnen: mitropoliti anania (japaridze), episkoposi stepane (kalaijishvili), episkoposi petre (tsaava), institutis direktori propesori vazha kiknadze, sametsniero sabchos tavmjdomare propesori tamaz beradze, sametsniero sabchos tsevrebi: doktori nino mindadze, propesori mariam chkhartishvili, propesori giorgi saitidze, propesori avtandil songhulashvili; institutis tanamshromlebi: propesori gia gelashvili, doktori rozeta gujejiani; motsveuli stumrebi: propesori manana tabidze, propesori teimuraz gvantseladze, propesori tariel putkaradze, propesori merab chukhua, propesori lia akhaladze, propesori bezhan khorava, propesori jemal gamakharia, propesori omar ardashelia, propesori merab nachqebia, doktori lado mirianashvili. skhdomam sagangebod ganikhila "evropuli kartia regionuli da umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb", "charcho konventsia erovnul umtsiresobata shesakheb" da is problemebi, romlebits am dokumentebis 
 ratipikatsiis shemdeg dgeba kartuli sakhelmtsipos tsinashe (dokumentebis teksti ikh. danartshi). evrosabchos normativebis mikhedvit, sakhelmtsipom tviton unda gansazghvros, tu romeli enebi unda chaitvalos erovnuli umtsiresobis enebad; ikvea dazustebats; kerdzod, enebis shesakheb evropuli kartiis mikhedvit, umtsiresobata enad ar miichneva migrantta ena (chvens shemtkhvevashi: somkhuri, rusuli, azerbaijanuli...) da sakhelmtsipo enis ganshtoebebi. dghes enatmetsnierta natsili aktiurad tsdilobs, regionuli an umtsiresobis enis statusi mianichos kartuli enis dialektebs: lazurs, megruls, svanurs, rats gamoitsvevs samegrelosa da svanetshi am kartveluri kiloebis gadaktsevas sakmistsarmoebis, ghvtismsakhurebisa da ganatlebis enad. ashkaraa, rom saprtkhe emukreba kartveli eris mravalsaukunovan enobriv da etnokulturul ertianobas. ketilshobiluri miznis mkone evropuli dokumentebi aravitar saprtkhes ar sheitsavs, tumtsa mat ratipikatsias sakartvelostvis savalalo shedegebi sheidzleba mohqves, tuki sakartvelos enobriv-etnikuri situatsia opitsialurad aghitsereba e.ts. sami/otkhi kartveluri enis teoriis mikhedvit (es dausabutebeli mosazreba ertadert cheshmaritebad iqo gamotskhadebuli sabchota epokashi da mas dghesats aaktiurebs enatmetsnierta erti jgupi): kerdzod, "regionuli da umtsiresobis enebis" shesakheb evropuli kartiis ratipikatsiis shemdeg sakartvelos enata chamonatvalshi tuki  -  "umtsignobro kartveluri ena" dapiksirdeba, khelovnurad tsakhalisdeba kartvelta etnikuri partsiatsia da separatsia; dzirpesvianad sheirqeva kartveli eris (etnosis) mravalsaukunovani ertoba da, drota ganmavlobashi, sheidzleba gagvichndes isetive problemebits, rogorits gvakvs apkhazebsa da osebtan dakavshirebit. sabchota periodamde sakartveloshi arsebobda mravalsaukunovani kartuli saistorio traditsia, romlis mikhedvitats kartvelebs gvakvs erti dedaena da misi mravalperovani dialekturi nairsakheobani. tanamedrove lingvisturi kvlevebits adasturebs, rom megruli, 
 lazuri da svanuri metqvelebani kartvelta dedaenis kutkhuri sakheskhvaobania da am zogadkartuli enis dialektebs tsarmoadgenen (da ara - damoukidebel enebs). martalia, megrul-lazuri da svanuri dashorebulia tanamedrove kartul saliteraturo enas, magram istoriuli, sotsiolingvisturi tvalsazrisit gatanabrebuli arian kartuli enis dialektebtan. ertiania kartvelta etnokulturul-sakhelmtsipoebrivi tsarsulits, rats, aseve, metsnieruladatsaa dasabutebuli arkeologta, istorikosta, antropologta, khelovnebatmtsodneta da etnologta mier. sakartvelos lingvokulturuli istoria da atsmqo mkholod amgvarad akvs aghkmul-gaazrebuli sakartvelos eklesiasa da sapatriarkos. ssip ivane javakhishvilis istoriisa da etnologiis institutis sametsniero sabchos gapartoebuli skhdoma miichnevs, rom sachiroa sakhelmtsipo doneze shedges sagangebo komisia istorikosebis, etnologebisa da enatmetsnierebis shemadgenlobit: sakhelmtsipo komisiam konsensusis tsesit unda chamoaqalibos opitsialuri khedva sakartvelos enobriv-etnikuri situatsiis shesakheb, ritats bolo moegheba gautavebel politikur insinuatsiebs am sakitkhis garshemo. imeds gamovtkvamt, amis shemdeg maints dasruldeba megrullazuri da svanuri metqvelebebis tsalke enebad da, shesabamisad, megrel-lazebisa da svanebis tsalke etnikur jgupebad gamotskhadeba (rasats satave daedo rusetis imperiashi); amgvari opitsialuri khedvis chamoqalibeba tavidan agvatsilebs sakartvelos garedan inspirirebul saprtkheebs. ghrma pativistsemit, 
 ssip iv. javakhishvilis istoriisa da etnologiis institutis sametsniero sabchos gapartoebuli skhdomis sakhelit: 
 institutis direktori 
 propesori vazha kiknadze 
 sametsniero sabchos tavmjdomare propesori tamaz beradze 
 tsarmodgenil tsignshi avtors miznad akvs achvenos, rom: - "regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartia" ("enis kartia") tavisi arsit nateli da maghali donis dokumentia; igi ar sheitsavs rom... 
 tsarmodgenil tsignshi avtors miznad akvs achvenos, rom: 
 - "regionuli an umtsiresobis enebis shesakheb evropuli kartia" ("enis kartia") tavisi arsit nateli da maghali donis dokumentia; igi ar sheitsavs romelime kveqnistvis sakhipato debulebebs. "enis kartia" khels utsqobs skhva sakhelmtsipoebriv velshi moktseuli avtoktoni umtsiresobis enobriv-kulturuli memkvidreobis shenarchunebas. - "enis kartiisa" da haagis tu oslos "rekomendatsiebis" miznebis gamijvnisa da printsipebis gatvalistsinebis shemtkhvevashi, sakhelmtsipo enis punktsiis dakninebis gareshe sakartveloshits da skhva kveqnebshits shesadzlebelia: - satanado statusi ganesazghvros kveqanashi arsebul qvela lingvistur erteuls; - khelisuplebis mier daisakhos nateli amotsanebi istoriuli umtsiresobis enis, rogorts kulturuli memkvidreobis, shenarchuneba-ganvitarebisatvis;  realurad iknas datsuli dziritadi mosakhleobis, istoriuli umtsiresobis, akhali umtsiresobisa tu migrantebis tsarmomadgenelta enobrivi uplebebi. 
 batono prezidento, sakartvelos ganvitarebis dghis tsesrigi, pirvel rigshi, chveni mokalakeebisa da mati tanastsori uplebebistvisaa gankutvnili. chven gvakvs tavisupali mokalakeebis dzalisa da mattvis tavisuplebisa da shesadzleblobebis uzrunvelqopashi mtavrobis rolis rtsmena. mdgradi ganvitareba sheudzlebelia adamianis uplebata datsvis, samartlis khelmisatsvdomobisa da epektiani, gamchvirvale, angarishvaldebuli da inkluziuri institutebis gareshe. chven mivighet mnishvnelovani zomebi kanonis uzenaesobis gansamtkitseblad. chven ganvakhortsielet sasamartlo sistemis, prokuraturis, martlmsajulebis etikisa da advokatta pasukhismgeblobata dzireuli reporma. chven gavapartovet braldebulta uplebebi da tsertili davusvit khelisuplebis tsarmomadgenelta tu tanamdebobis pirta dausjelobas. dghes qvela sakartvelos mokalake tanastsoria kanonis tsinashe da qvelas akvs shesadzlebloba, isargeblos martlmsajulebis sistemit, romelits intensiuri repormebis shedegad gamoircheva damoukideblobisa da propesionalizmis maghali khariskhit. chven vagrdzelebt martlmsajulebis sistemis repormas, rata vupasukhot umaghles saertashoriso standartebs. dghes, msoplios martlmsajulebis proektis kanonis uzenaesobis indeksis tanakhmad, sakartvelo  -e adgilzea da ustsrebs evrokavshiris bevr dzvel da akhal tsevrs. mnishvnelovani nabijebi idgmeba memkvidreobit mighebul seriozul problemastan sabrdzolvelad, es aris tsarsulshi adamianis uplebata darghvevebi, gansakutrebit ki tsikheebshi momkhdari umdzimesi darghvevebi. am problemis aghmosapkhvrelad chven mivighet stsrapi da gadamtsqveti zomebi. gaeros spetsialurma momkhsenebelma tsamebisa da araadamianuri da damamtsirebeli mopqrobis sakitkhebshi akhlakhan aghnishna, rom   tsels kveqnis sataveshi mosvlis shemdeg, sakartvelos mtavrobam radikalurad shetsvala vitareba am mkhriv da shesabamisi tsvlilebebi kmediti da khariskhiania. am miznis misaghtsevad chven avamokmedet samartlebrivi da protsesualuri mekanizmebi patimarta mimart arasatanado mopqrobastan sabrdzolvelad, mskhverpltatvis kompensatsiis chatvlit. chven mivighet mkatsri antidiskriminatsiuli kanoni. chven dzal-ghones ar vishurebt, rata realurad shevutsqot kheli genderul tanastsorobas da kalta gadzlierebas. shezghuduli shesadzleblobebis mkone pirtatvis tanastsori shesadzleblobebis uzrunvelsaqopad, chven vakhortsielebt erovnul samokmedo gegmas, tumtsa tsin kidev bevria gasaketebeli, ristvisats chven mivighet adamianis uplebata grdzelvadiani da qovlismomtsveli strategia da samokmedo gegma. sam kvirashi sakartveloshi chatardeba saparlamento archevnebi. tsinasaarchevno periodi, romelits sami tvis tsin daitsqo, motsmobs, rom sakartvelo realurad demokratiulad vitardeba. chven uzrunvelvqopt tavisupal, samartlian da gamchvirvale saarchevno protsess, romelits gamoircheva mediisa da politikuri garemos tavisuplebita da pluralizmit, dzlieri da aktiuri samokalako sazogadoebit da shesabamisi sakanonmdeblo da institutsiuri bazit.   oktombers kartveli khalkhi gaimarjvebs da chveni demokratia momavalshits kveqnis mdgrad ganvitarebas uzrunvelqops. dzvirpaso kolegebo, mdgradi ganvitareba arasrulia, tuki is motsqvetilia usaprtkhoebis qovlismomtsvel sakitkhs, rasats sakartveloshi arsebuli mtsare realoba qoveldghiurad shegvakhsenebs - kveqnis   protsenti dghesats okupirebulia utskho kveqnis jarebis mier. 
 asobit atas adamians dghesats ar adzleven shin dabrunebis uplebas. chven madlobas mogakhsenebt im moraluri mkhardacherisatvis, romelits asakhulia gaeros generaluri asambleis rezolutsiashi „apkhazetidan (sakartvelo) da tskhinvalis regionidan/egret tsodebuli samkhret osetidan (sakartvelo) idzulebit gadaadgilebul pirta da ltolvilta statusis shesakheb“. dadga dro, rom es mkhardachera konkretul mokmedebashi aisakhos. okupantebis mier aghmartuli mavtulkhlartebi da gamqopi konstruktsiebi ertmanets ashorebs kartul ojakhebsa da temebs. okupirebul teritoriebze mtskhovrebi mosakhleoba ganitsdis mudmiv diskriminatsias da adamianis uplebata ukhesh darghvevebs. shezghudulia mati gadaadgilebisa da sakutrebis uplebebi. mat mshobliur enaze ganatlebis mighebis shesadzleblobats ki ara akvt. me vgmob sakartvelos okupirebul teritoriebze rusetis sakhelmtsipo dumas archevnebis chatarebis pakts, rogorts moskovis mkhridan aneksiisken gamiznuli politikis parglebshi gadadgmul kidev ert nabijs. qvelaperi es ki khdeba saertashoriso monitoringis mekanizmis ararsebobis pirobebshi, evrokavshiris sadamkvirveblo misiis shezghuduli sakmianobis chatvlit, romelsats uari etkva okupirebul teritoriebze shesvlaze. 
 mimdinare okupatsia da aneksiisken gadadgmuli nabijebi es aris qvelaze mnishvnelovani gamotsveva, romelits chvenma mtavrobam memkvidreobit miigho. chven vtsdilobt rusettan iseti urtiertobebis damqarebas, romlis parglebshits realuri mushaoba ikneba shesadzlebeli. chven mivaghtsiet konkretul shedegebs dadzabulobis shemsubukebis kutkhit, tumtsa, sakartvelos qvela nabijs jer ar mohqolia sapasukho mokmedeba. 
 rusetis pederatsia agrdzelebs   tsels evrokavshiris shuamdgomlobit tsetskhlis shetsqvetis shesakheb mightseuli shetankhmebis pirobebis darghvevas. zemoaghnishnulis gatvalistsinebit, kidev ertkhel vatskhadeb, rom es konplikti unda mogvardes mshvidobiani gzebit, sakartvelos suverenitetisa da saertashorisod aghiarebul sazghvrebshi chveni teritoriuli mtlianobis pativistsemit. 
 chven momavalshits movakhdent reagirebas apkhazetisa da tskhinvalis regionebshi mtskhovrebi mosakhleobis problemebze da gavaertianebt saokupatsio khazis gaqolebaze ertmanettan idzulebit dashorebul mosakhleobas. am miznit chven okupirebuli teritoriebis mosakhleobistvis khelmisatsvdoms gavkhdit chveni evropuli dghis tsesrigit gatvalistsinebul qvela sargebelsa da ekonomikur shesadzleblobas. ertiani sakartvelos nateli momavlisken mimartuli chveni dzaliskhmeva ikneba ndobis aghdgenisa da sherigebis kidev erti stimuli. shemdegi otkhi tslis ganmavlobashi chven ganvakhortsielebt   miliard dolarze meti odenobis investitsiebs kavshirgabmulobasa da inprastrukturashi. chven ertmanettan davakavshirebt sakartvelos regionebs da tavad sakartvelosats davakavshirebt parto regiontan. sakartvelos strategiuli mdebareobis gatvalistsinebit, chveni portebi, gzebi da satransporto kselebi mnishvnelovan rols sheasrulebs ambitsiuri da revolutsiuri abreshumis gzis ganvitarebis gegmashi, romelits ertmanettan daakavshirebs evropasa da azias. inprastrukturis garda, chven aseve vakhortsielebt investitsiebs strategiuli mimartulebebit. tbilisis abreshumis gzis porumi, romelshits monatsileoba miighes   kveqnis tsarmomadgenlebma, didi tsarmatebit chatarda. chventvis sapatio da sasikharuloa tanamshromloba chinetsa da abreshumis gzis proektis skhva monatsile kveqnebtan, agretve mnishvnelovani tsvlilis shetana im savachro da sainvestitsio derepnis uzrunvelqopashi, romelits mtel msoplios moutans sargebels. rodesats vlaparakobt kavshirgabmulobaze, ar unda dagvavitsqdes interneti, romelits tsarmoadgens globaluri tanamshromlobis, albat, qvelaze seriozul mamodzravebel dzalas. kavshirgabmulobis gaumjobesebis miznit, chven davitsqet saqoveltao internetizatsiis sistemis danergva, romelits internetit sargeblobis shesadzleblobas mistsems qvelaze miutsvdomeli soplebis mosakhleobasats ki. siamaqit aghvnishnavt, rom internetis tavisuplebis mkhriv sakartvelo ert-erti lideria. batonebo da kalbatonebo, batono prezidento, pativtsemulo kolegebo, me vamaqob, rom gamovdivar sakartvelos sakhelit dghes, rodesats chveni kveqana aghmavlobis gzazea da aghmosavletisa da dasavletis akhali damakavshirebeli movlenebis tsentrshi imqopeba. 
 stsored es suliskveteba gvamodzravebs chven regionshi usaprtkhoebisa da ketildgheobis uzrunvelqopis gzaze, romelits epudzneba mdgradi ganvitarebis printsipebs. chven qoveldghiur rezhimshi daughalavad vshromobt da vdgamt konkretul nabijebs chveni mokalakeebis mdgomareobis gasaumjobeseblad da am protsesshi uzrunvelvqopt mati uplebebis, mrtsamsisa da kulturis pativistsemas. 
 chven imedit shevqurebt gaerostan shemdgom tanamshromlobas, rata khortsi sheeskhas uketesi momavlis saerto khedvas. 
 sakartvelo  -tslamdel pekhburtelta saertashoriso turnirs umaspindzlebs 
 khelburtelta nakrebi   tslis evropis chempionatis shesarchev etaps itsqebs 
  . .  tv-maestro: sportisa da akhalgazrdobis sakmeta ministrma da erovnuli bibliotekis khelmdzghvanelma kheli moatseres khelshekrulebas romelits utsqebebs shoris t... 
 sotsialuri kselis meshveobit gamo ... vlinda khalkhis rcheuli motkhroba da aseve zhiuris rcheuli   motkhroba. sportisa da akhalgazrdobis sakmeta ministris moadgilem, revaz javelidzem gamoavlina statiebisa da potokonkursshi pirvel adgilze gasuli monatsileebi. 
 gamarjvebulebi daajildoes sportisa da akhalgzardobis saministrosa da ssip bavshvta da akhalgazrdobis pondis, a.(a).i.p. „sainpormatsio banki - sakartvelos akhalgazrdobis" tsarmomadgenlebma. 
 konkursis gamarjvebulia goris erovnuli tavdatsvis akademiis meotkhe kursis iunkeri, shio qandorashili. 
 proektis mizania shemokmedebiti nichit dajildoebuli akhalgazrdebis aghmochena, sazogadoebisatvis gatsnoba da mati shesadzleblobebis realizeba. 
 ghonisdziebashi monatsileoba miigho skhvadaskhva umaghlesi sastsavleblisa da akhalgazrdobis tematikaze momushave arasamtavrobo organizatsiebis tsarmomadgenlebma. 
 sportisa da akhalgazrdobis sakmeta saministrom erovnul bibliotekastan ertad kidev ert proektze daitsqo mushaoba. 
 proektis parglebshi, sheikmneba erovnul bibliotekashi datsuli sportuli gamotsemebis elektronuli arkivi, romelits gantavsdeba saministrosa da bibliotekis opitsialur gverdebze da khelmisatsvdomi ikneba rogorts sportuli zhurnalistebistvis, aseve nebismieri dainteresebuli piristvis. 
 proektis satsqis etapze elektronul arkivshi gantavsdeba uakhlesi gamotsemebi, mogvianebit ki arkivshi sh ... eva bibliotekashi datsuli, qvelaze dzveli zhurnal-gazetebi. 
 amastan dakavshirebit, akhal sportis sasakhleshi   oktombers, saministrosa da sakartvelos parlamentis ilia chavchavadzis sakhelobis erovnul bibliotekas shoris urtierttanamshromlobis memorandumi gapormda, romelsats kheli moatseres sportisa da akhalgazrdobis sakmeta ministrma tariel khechikashvilma da erovnuli bibliotekis generalurma direktorma giorgi kekelidzem. 
 memorandumi itvalistsinebs grdzelvadian tanamshromlobas da dzalashi shedis khelis motseris dghidan. 
 dghes msoplio dziudos dghea. gilotsavt dziudos qvela gulshematkivars! msoplio dziudos dghe dziudos saertashoriso pederatsiis gadatsqvetilebit   tslidan qovel   oktombers ... aghinishneba da ukavshirdeba dziudos pudzemdeblis dzigoro kanos dabadebis dghes. qoveltsliurad msoplio dziudos dghes skhvadaskhva devizit aghnishnaven. tslevandeli devizia „dziudos msopliostvis“. 
 borjghalosnebis noembris test-matchebistvis biletebis gaqidva daitso 
 aghsanishnavia, rom evropis chempionatis mogebis shemdeg, irakli chkheidze msoplio pirvelobazets ert-erti pavoriti iqo. 
 irakli chkheidze, chabukta nakrebis tsevrebtan ertad malaiziidan tbilisshi   oktombers dabrunda. 
 tsarmatebul dzalosans, dzalosnobis pederatsiis prezident kakhi kakhiashviltan da mtsvrtnel zurab antaurtan ertad gamarjveba sportisa da akhalgazrdobis sakmeta ministrma tariel khechikashvilma moadgile shalva gogoladzestan ertad miulotsa. 
 tu khar  -dan   tslamde aktiuri akhalgazrda, gainteresebs ekstremaluri situatsiebi da mati kontroli, khar tavdajerebuli da mizanstsrapuli, mashin proekti „norch mashve ... lta klubi“ shentvis aris!!! 
 k.tbilisis sajaro skolebidan   akhalgazrda aircheva , romlebits gaivlian kulturul gadamzadebas „bavshvta da akhalgazrdobis erovnul tsentrshi“, kholo samashvelo tsvrtnebs sagangebo situatsiebis martvis saagentos bazaze. akhalgazrdebis sherchevisas quradgheba miektseva pizikur normativebs da shemokmedebit nichs (tsekva,simghera, khatva). gadamzadebebis dasrulebis shemdeg, sauketesoebi sakartvelos sakhelit monatsileobas miigheben sazghvargaret gamartul „norch mashvelta“ saertashoriso shejibrshi. 
 „norch mashvelta klubi“ „bavshvta da akhalgazrdobis erovnuli tsentrisa“ da „sagangebo situatsiebis martvis saagentos“ shoris dadebuli urtierttanamshromlobis memorandumis parglebshi   tslis   ivnisidan mokmedebs.

 sadghats premiebistvis gadanakhul skivrshi ar gamoinakheba am kalistvis msoplio chempionatze gasapreni biletis puli? :) 
 mtavari » saredaktsio statia » vin arian ivanishvilis mier deputatobabodzebuli: kakha okriashvili, endzel mkoiani da tsezar chocheli 
 vin arian ivanishvilis mier deputatobabodzebuli: kakha okriashvili, endzel mkoiani da tsezar chocheli 
 miukhedavad imisa, rom am saparlamento siis shedgenashi dziritadi monatsileoba ivanishvilma gushin uarqo - kaladze, kobakhidze da skhvebi adgeneno, masshi mokhvedrili odiozuri pigurebi rom mis mier mtsvaneantebulni da motsonebulni arian, praktikulad, aghiara. 
 rogorts gushindel preskonperentsiaze tavad ganatskhada, piradadaa shekhvedrili kakha okriashvils, tsezar chochels, goderdzi bukias da qvela matgans itsnobs. is mat kargad akhasiatebs "nichierebsa" da "sakmis mtsodneebs" utsodebs, romlebits turme saakashvilis tsqalobit ar aghzevebulan da isini saakashvils ar sheukmnia. 
 ivanishvilma gushin isits gamoaashkarava, rom kohabitatsiats misi gadtsqvetilebaa da is biznesmenebits daasakhela, romlebits kvebavdnen tsina rezhims, tavadats kargad itbobdnen khels da asetive tsarmatebit gamokvebaven amatats, oghond khelsheukhebloba hkondet garantirebulad. vin - vin da bidzina ivanishvilis mier dasakhelebulma biznesmenebma kargad itsian khelisuplebashi qopnis pasi. 
 vin aris kakha okriashvili 
 kartul parmamapiaze, mat shoris, ert-erti parmatsevtuli kompaniis mplobel kakha okriashvilis kompaniaze   tsels, "monitoris" gamomdziebel zhurnalist nino zuriashviltan ertad, zhurnalisturi gamodzieba sataurit - "parmatsiis bneli mkhare" - gamovakveqne. miukhedavad imisa, rom statiashi nachvenebia, tu ra katasropuli mdgomareobaa parmatsevtul speroshi, gansakutrebit khariskhis tvalsazrisit, khelisuplebis mier "dakrishul" parmkompaniebs betsvits ar chamovardniat. 
   tsels, kakha okriashvilis parlamentis deputatobisas, kanonshi  tsvlileba mokhda da tsamlis registratsia gamartivda 
 es nishnavs, rom tsamlis registratsiis madzieblistvis medikamentis shemotanis da gaqidvis uplebis mopoveba gatsilebit ioli gakhda. tsvlilebis tanakhmad, "registratsiaze uaris tkmis shemtkhvevashi, tsamlis saagento valdebuli gakhda, dauqovnebliv tserilobit etsnobebina dasabutebuli uari registratsiis madzieblistvis". tu kanonit gansazghvrul vadashi "registratsiis madziebels ar etsnobeboda gadatsqvetileba registratsiaze uaris tkmis shesakheb, samkurnalo sashualeba registrirebulad itvleboda da saagento valdebuli iqo gaetsa saregistratsio motsmoba", ra dghemde asea. anu shemmotsmebels (sakhelmtsipos) praktikulad ar edzleva tsamlis shemotsmebis sashualeba da sheumotsmebeli an saechvo tsamali maints unda daaregistriros. 
 tsvlilebebi komitetshi kakha okriashvilis initsiativit momzadda da man parlamentis skhdomas am "kanonproektis shekmnis mizani" ganumarta, rogorts "biznestan dakavshirebuli sakhelmtsipo prioritetis mkhardachera, rats biznesistvis zedmeti biurokratiuli protsedurebis gamartivebashi gamoikhateba". 
 manamde,   tsels jandatsvis imzhamindel ministr amiran gamqrelidzes parmamapiozebma gamoatsemines kanoni, romlis sapudzvelzets gaaukmebines qvela im medikamentis seriuli shemotsmeba, romelits kerdzo biznesis tsarmomadgenlebs shemokondat sakartveloshi, rats nishnavda imas, rom khariskhi kidev upro ukontrolo gakhda. 
 “katsma ar itsis, risgan mzaddeba tsamali. parmatsevtuli kompaniebi tviton aketeben substantsiisa da gamzadebuli tsamlis analizs da tavadve gastsemen sarealizatsio sertipikats. shercheviti kontroli maints unda tardebodes normalurad da es unda khdebodes sistematurad da ara tselitsadshi ertkhel an orjer", - atskhadebda laboratoria "jeolabis" direktori, ketevan baramidze. 
 garda amisa, okriashvili, romelits sami motsvevis parlamets tsevria (is ertkhel shevardnadzis da orjer mishas dros gakhda parlamenti tsevri), gasul saparlamento archevnebshi, samkvdro-sasitsotskhlod upirispirdeboda „kartuli otsnebis“ saarchevno shtabs. misi shtabis khelmdzghvanelis mier oponentta ezoshi shechrisa da mankanistvis mankanis dajakhebis videokadrebi mashin mtelma sakartvelom nakha. mishas mier „daterorebuli“ biznesmeni ase umtkitsebda mashin ertgulebas mmartvel partias. 
 „kakha okriashvili aris kriminali, romelis khalkhis daterorebit tsdilobs kidev ertkhel gainaghdos tavisi mandati da amis sashualebas ar mivtsemt“- atskhadebda   tslis saparlamento archevnebamde   kvirit adre "kartuli otsnebis" ert-erti lideri sozar subari. 
   tseli ivnisshi mediashi gamochnda videochanatseri, romelshits dmaniseli glekhebi qvebian, rogor tsartva mat mitsebi kakha okriashvilma. adgilobrivebis tkmit, sami tselia, irganchais sadzovrebi dmanisis mazhoritari deputatis, kakha okriashvilis ojakhma miisakutra. 
   tsels pirvel arkhze gavida siuzheti, romlis tanakhmadats mtavar prokuraturas rusetshi mtskhovrebma kartvelma biznesmenma dimitri beruashvilma mimarta, romelits deputat kakha okriashvils misi gatatsebis dakvetashi adanashaulebs da parlamentaristvis sadeputato uplebamosilebis shetsqvetas moitkhovda. tumtsa gamodzieba arts tsarmartula. 
 kholo   tslis saparlamento archevnebze, okriashvilma akhla ukve "kartul otsnebas"shestsira   atasi lari. 
 natsionali deputatebi: kakha okriashvili da enzel mkoiani (ninotsmindis mazhoritari) „kartul otsnebashi“ gasuli tslis ivlisshi gadabargdnen. 
 vin aris enzel mkoiani 
 otkhi motsvevis parlamentaria enzel mkoiani.   tslis   sektembers, media tserda im dzaladobaze, rats mkoianis mkhardamcherebma chaidines. „ninotsmindashi „kartuli otsnebis“ mazhoritari deputatobis kandidati, albert nurbegiani, sainitsiativo jguptan ertad sopel satkhashi adgilobriv mosakhleobas khvdeboda. ekstsesebis tavidan atsilebis miznit „kartuli otsnebis“ tsarmomadgenlebma gadatsqvites daetovebinat sopeli. am dros mat uknidan mieparnen „ertiani natsionaluri modzraobis“ mazhoritari deputatobis kandidatis, enzelas mkoianis natesavebi (bidzashvilebi) da „kartuli otsnebis“ aktivists, sokolovs tavshi kva chaartqes. sokolovma goneba dakarga. igi ninotsmindis saavadmqoposhi gadaiqvanes, kholo mogvianebit ninotsmindis politsiis ganqopilebashi mas akhsna-ganmarteba daatserines“. 
 enzel mkoiani   tsels kartuli otsnebis aktivistis gatatsebasa da tsemashits iqo mkhilebuli. „  tsels ki gaitatsa „kartuli otsnebis“ aktivisti, razets mis tsinaaghmdeg siskhlis samartlis sakme  aghidzra. iaraghis tarit tsema, dashineba, mukara - es qvelaperi dapiksirebulia“ - atskhadebs "kartuli otsnebis" qopili aktivisti merab shatirishvili. 
   tsels, ninotsmindis sakrebuloshi pizikuri dapirispireba mokhda, ris gamots raionis mazhoritar deputats politsiashi uchivles. endzel mkoiani sakrebulos gadamdgarma tavmjdomarem tsemashi daadanashaula. vladimer sambosianis mtkitsebit, mkoianma ,,kartuli otsnebis" sakhelit isargebla da tanamdebobidan tsasvla aidzula. koalitsiis adgilobrivi shtabi mazhoritar deputattan raime sakhis kavshirs kategoriulad uarqops.  saparlamento archevnebshi is mazhoritarad ,,natsionaluri modzraobis" siit iqrida kenchs, tumtsa,   tslis   oktombris shemdeg damartskhebul partias gaemijna da damoukidebeli praktsia shekmna. 
 qoveli archevnebi ninotsmindashi qalbdeboda da qvela gaqalbeba natsionalebis dros mkoianis sakhels ukavshirdeboda. 
 vin aris tsezar chocheli 
   tslis   ianvars, mtskheta-mtianetis mkhareshi qopili sakhelmtsipo rtsmunebuli tsezar chocheli pinansuri makinatsiebisa da pulis gatetrebis braldebit daakaves da      laris giraos sanatsvlod   dgheshi gatavisuplda . 
 pinansta saministros sagamodziebo samsakhuris inpormatsiit, tsezar chocheli ukanonod monatsileobda samsheneblo kompania “niu enerjis” sakminobashi. is khels utsqobda shps–s da  sakhelmtsipo biujetidan dapinansebuli proektebis shesrulebastan dakavshirebuli kontraktebis gapormebashi. am sakminobis sanatsvlod ukanond ighebda didi raodenobit shemosavlebs da pulis gatetrebis gzit adzlevda kanonier sakhes. 
 pinansta saministros sagamodziebo samsakhuris inpormatsiit,   tslis zapkhulshi tsezar chochelis motkhovnis sapudzvelze, chogburtis da kalatburtis moednebis mosatsqobad, “niu enerjim” turketidan chamoitana     laris ghirebulebis sachiro inventari da tbilisshi, sopel dighomshi,  tsezar chochelis meughlis, svetlana chochelis satskhovrebeli sakhlis ezoshi daamontazha. 
 gamodzieba mimdinareobda siskhlis samartlis kodeksis   -e da  -e mukhlis mesame natsilit, rats  -dan   tslamde tavisuplebis aghkvetas itvalistsinebda. 
 tsezar chocheli   tsels akhalgoris sakrebulos tavmjdomared airchies. amave tsels iqo akhalgoris raionis gamgebelits.    tslis   noembers chocheli  sakartvelos parlamentis tsevri akhalgoris mazhoritarul saarchevno olkidan gakhda. 
   tslis tebervlidan, prezident saakashvilisis brdzanebulebit, tsezar chocheli mtskheta-mtianetis mkhareshi sakhelmtsipo rtsmunebulad dainishna.  chocheli dakavebuli tanamdebobidan   tslis   noembers gadadga. 
 saakashvilis droindel qvela mskhvili biznesis ukan chochelis gvari pigurirebda. mas „vanos biznesmenadats“ moikhseniebdnen. saakashvilis periodshi mistvis milionobit sakhelmtsipo valebi akvs chamotserili khelisuplebas. mis sakhels ukavshirdeba „rkina betonis shpalebis karkhana“, „barambo“, ludsakharshi „lomisi“, „zedazenis“ ludis karkhana, samsheneblo kompania "niu- enerji" - es misi biznesis arasruli chamonatvalia. 
 gansakutrebuli tsarmatebebi biznesshi chochels saakashvilis khelisuplebis mmartvelobis periodshi, misi tanamdebobaze qopnis periodebshi konda, tumtsa is tanamdebobebis gamoqenebas am miznit mudmivad uarqopda. 
 da bolos, mokalakeebis reaktsia sotsialur kselebshi: 
 es kakha okraiashvils udevs volze. mousminet. visats mosmena gezarebat, tsaikitkhet. ar damezara amobechdva: 
 • rogorts ki chven movedit khelisuplebashi, meore dghesve,   tu   katsi - ganatskhades, rom chven movdivart aket mkhares. • arts natsmodzraobas sheukmnia okriashvili da arts chven shegvikmnia. okriashvili aris dzalian nichieri katsi. • mat ganskhvavebit skhvebisgan, romlebits dghesats ver akherkheben stsori stsoreba airchion, rogorts ki mietsat sashualeba, modzalade khelisuplebas, qopils - uari tkves ada aket gadmoviden. gadmoviden da dadgen stsor adgilze. 
 • aba tsarmoidginet mashin, vints gautsia tsinaaghmdegoba biznesmenebidan, saakashvils mashin, sad arian dghes? zogi daarbies, zogi gadatsves, zogi tsikheshi sheiqvanes. 
 • am khalkhs goneba eqo, rom am dzalas, gauazrebel dzalas, tsin ar daudgnen. • ar daudgnen, mara saakashvilit ar sheukmnia biznesi okriashvils. • es khalkhi aris khalkhi, romlebmats tsarmatebas miaghtsies sakutari nichierebit da rogorts ki mietsat sashualeba, stsori stsoreba gaaketes, stsori pozitsia daichires. • aba gaeketebinat saakashvilis dros da gaetsiat? • imdeni chkua eqot, rom arts tavi moaklevines, arts daacherines da arts daarbevines. • amaze nu vusaqvedurebt. abidzia -   mtsneba bidzinasgan. daimakhsovret! chven, visats ar gveqo chkua da mogvkles, dagvichires da dagvarbies, aket vart sasaqveduroebi. tskhadia, chven magari   vart. dzaan magari   tan. imitom ro dghesats ver vakherkhebt stsori stsoreba avirchiot. ertshi martalia - saakashvils ar sheukmnia okriashvili. pirikit, okriashvilma & kampaniam shekmnes saakashvili. ivanishvilis tamadobit. tavidanve ro airchies stsori stsoreba da khelpasebs ukhdiden konvertit. sorosis marka ro ertqa konverts. bijo, amas aminazini gauketet, daadzinet archevnebamde, nu atsopebs khalkhs, tore natsebi ki ara, sheidzleba stalinistebi mobrunden da parto masebis motkhovnit ekspropriatsia chaataron, tavis kolektivizatsiit. shevrtskhvebit evroatlantikur sivrtseshi.- tsers vakis mazhoritarobis damoukidebeli kandidati gia patsuria. 
 aba, kargad tsaikitkhet: "mashin vints gautsia tsinaaghmdegoba saakashvils, sad arian dghes? zogi daarbies, zogi gadatsves, zogi tsikheshi sheiqvanes. am khalkhs goneba eqo da gauazrebel dzalas tsin ar daudgnen, magram saakashvilit ar sheukmnia biznesi okriashvils. imdeni chkua eqot, arts tavi moakvlevines, arts tavi daacherines da arts daarbevines, amaze nu vusaqvedurebt“, - ganatskhada bidzina ivanishvilma. amas proiduli tsamotsdena kvia, ara, mgoni? es imas magonebs, vighatseebi rom gamodian: gamsakhurdia da kostava ras ebrdzodnen sabchota kavshirs, ager, tavisit maints khom daingreodao... qvela medroves, konpormistisa da sindisgaretskhilis kredo gaazhghera, paktobrivad. gvapatiet, batono bidzina, vints ver sheveguet darbevas, koruptsias, avtoritarizms, tsamebas, atasgvar sashinelebas da chveni sisulelit sistemas davupirispirdit... tkvengan ganskhvavebit! mapatiet me piradad, rom adamianebis tsamebis qurebas tsikhe, shimshiloba da tanjva varchie... okriashvili da chocheli - chveni drois gmirebi... printsipshi, adrets vkhvdebodit, magram ager tkva pirdapir ;) ai, turme ratom mokhda kohabitatsia da ratom daikides tsamebisa da konebis tsartmevebis gamodzieba.. - tsers tsotne gamsakhurdia. 
 gamokitkhva 
 romel kandidats mistsemt khmas saparlamento archevnebshi? 
 avtoris/avtorebis mier sainpormatsio masalashi gamotkmuli mosazreba shesadzloa ar gamokhatavdes pond ”ghia sazogadoeba-sakartvelos” pozitsias. shesabamisad, pondi ar aris pasukhismgebeli masalis shinaarsze

matematika
samartalmtsodneoba
matematika
geograpiasamushao jgupis mier shestsavlili ikna aseve sakartvelos soplis meurneobis mdgomareobada tendentsiebi. detaluri analizi da shesabamisi rekomendatsiebi am gamotsemis meorenatsilshia tsarmodgenili. agrarul sektorshi problemebis gamokvetis garda, shedarebitghrmadaa momzadebuli rekomendatsiebi sam umnishnelovanes temaze. esenia: sasoplo-sameurneo teknikit uzrunvelqopa; melioratsia; soplis meurneobis dapinanseba dadazghveva.sakartvelos ganvitarebis kvleviti instituti da mkvlevarta jgupi madlierebitmiigheben qvela sakmian shenishvnas da mosazrebas, rats emsakhureba tsinamdebare dokumentissrulqopas da sakartvelos ekonomikashi arsebuli mdgomareobis gaumjobesebas.sakartvelos ganvitarebis kvleviti instituti,mkvlevarta jgupi.

gverdi  samushao jgupis mier shestsavlili ikna aseve sakartvelos soplis meurneobis mdgomareobada tendentsiebi. detaluri analizi da shesabamisi rekomendatsiebi am gamotsemis meorenatsilshia tsarmodgenili. agrarul sektorshi problemebis gamokvetis garda, shedarebitghrmadaa momzadebuli rekomendatsiebi sam umnishnelovanes temaze. esenia: sasoplo-sameurneo teknikit uzrunvelqopa; melioratsia; soplis meurneobis dapinanseba dadazghveva.sakartvelos ganvitarebis kvleviti instituti da mkvlevarta jgupi madlierebitmiigheben qvela sakmian shenishvnas da mosazrebas, rats emsakhureba tsinamdebare dokumentissrulqopas da sakartvelos ekonomikashi arsebuli mdgomareobis gaumjobesebas.sakartvelos ganvitarebis kvleviti instituti,mkvlevarta jgupi.  
sahaero khomaldebisa da saaviatsio dzravebis teknikuri ekspluatatsia
- sahaero khomaldebis avionikisa da elektruli sistemebis teknikuri ekspluatatsia
- sapreni aparatebis konstruireba da tsarmoeba
- inpormatsiuli teknologiebi da prenis martvis kontrolis avtomatizebuli

– inpormatsiuli teknologiebi menejmentshi

kimiasamushao jgupis mier shestsavlili ikna aseve sakartvelos soplis meurneobis mdgomareobada tendentsiebi. detaluri analizi da shesabamisi rekomendatsiebi am gamotsemis meorenatsilshia tsarmodgenili. agrarul sektorshi problemebis gamokvetis garda, shedarebitghrmadaa momzadebuli rekomendatsiebi sam umnishnelovanes temaze. esenia: sasoplo-sameurneo teknikit uzrunvelqopa; melioratsia; soplis meurneobis dapinanseba dadazghveva.sakartvelos ganvitarebis kvleviti instituti da mkvlevarta jgupi madlierebitmiigheben qvela sakmian shenishvnas da mosazrebas, rats emsakhureba tsinamdebare dokumentissrulqopas da sakartvelos ekonomikashi arsebuli mdgomareobis gaumjobesebas.sakartvelos ganvitarebis kvleviti instituti,mkvlevarta jgupi.

matematika
gverdi  
 sazogadoebrivi metsnierebebi-erovnuli sastsavlo gegma  -  
  . kveqnis sakhelmtsipoebrivi, kulturuli, ekonomikuri da politikuriinteresebi. imavdroulad, mostsavlem unda itsodes, rogor bunebrivgaremoshi tskhovrobs, ra ziani sheidzleba miaqenos garemos adamianis ama tu immokmedebam, rogor sheinarchunos da daitsvas bunebrivi garemo. stsored,sazogadoebrivi metsnierebebis shestsavlit uvitardeba mozards tsodna pirad,ojakhur da sazogadoebriv tskhovrebashi damoukidebeli gadatsqvetilebebismigheba-gankhortsielebis shesakheb. dghevandel dinamikur, etnikurad dakulturulad mravalperovan samqaroshi sazogadoebispunktsionirebisatvis gansakutrebul mnishvnelobas idzensurtiertshemetsneba. stsored, sazogadoebrivi metsnierebebis shestsavlisaskhdeba tsodnis migheba, romelits ekhmareba mostsavles adamianis uplebebisdatsvasa da pirovnebis pativistsemashi, sakutari da skhvisi tvitmqopadobisshenarchuneb . ashi,mostsavlem asakis shesabamisad, tsodnis nabij-nabij shedzenis gzit, undaitsodes tu ra aris politikuri sistema, kanoni, rogori politikurisistemebi arsebobs; unda gaatsnobieros sakutari pasukhismgeblobebi dauplebebi demokratiuli sazogadoebisa da kanonis uzenaesobis tsinashe;unda itsnobdes adamianis uplebata datsvis saertashoriso charchoebs, adamianisuplebata datsvis mekanizmebsa da sashualebebs sakartveloshi da a.sh.mostsavle unda atsnobierebdes tavs, rogorts sakutari ojakhis,sazogadoebis, saskolo temisa tu klasis, samezoblo temis, reperentulijgupis (ikneba es etnikuri tu religiuri umtsiresoba tu satitulo natsiada a.sh.), kartuli sazogadoebis tsevrad; itsnobdes sakutari kveqnis,sazogadoebisa da reperentuli temis kulturas; sakartveloshi tumsoplioshi mtskhovrebi skhva sazogadoebebis kulturas; iazrebdes, rasnishnavs zrunvis etika, ratom aris is ghirebuli da a.sh.mostsavle nabij-nabij, sapekhurebrivad, unda gaetsnos tavisi kveqnisekonomikuri mdgomareobis dziritad aspektebs: sakonlis, momsakhureobis,shromisa da samomkhmareblo bazars, minimalur khelpass,msqidveltunarianobas da a.sh.; shedzlebisdagvarad, unda iqos inpormirebulimomkhmareblis uplebebsa da movaleobebze, pasukhismgeblobiti da etikurimokhmarebis mnishvnelobasa da printsipebze; gamchvirvalobis mnishvnelobaze daa.sh.mostsavlem unda nabij-nabij, sapekhureobrivad sheitvisos tsodna isetsperoebze, rogoritsaa mdgradi ganvitareba, garemos datsva, tskhovrebisjansaghi tsesi, sitsotskhlisa da janmrtelobisatvis sashishi situatsiebisshepaseba, sagangebo vitarebebshi mokmedeba, individualuri da kolektiuridatsvis sashualebebis gamoqeneba, dazaralebultatvis ekimamdeligadaudebeli dakhmarebis aghmochena; unda sheigrdznos sakutari kveqnis,regionis kavshiri evropasa da msoplioshi mimdinare protsesebtan; undagaatsnobieros qvela am protsesis urtiertkavshiri; unda gaatsnobieroskatsobriobis, rogorts msoplios ertiani sazogadoebis, tsinashe mdgaripolitikuri, ekonomikuri, garemosdatsviti da sotsialuri gamotsvevebi.am protsesshi iguliskhmeba, rom mostsavles inpormatsiis dauplebisparalelurad uvitardeba spetsipikuri da zogadi unar-chvevebi, uqalibdebamaghalzneobrivi ghirebulebebi.konkretuli tematika/sakitkhebi/kontseptsiebi gashlilia titoeuliklasisa da sagnis programis shinaarsshi. aghnishnuli tsodnis shedzenaitvalistsinebs rogorts sagnobriv spetsipikasa da utsqvetobas, isemostsavleebis asakobriv shesadzleblobebs.unar-chvevebi  
  . gakvetilis chasatareblad mastsavlebeli unda iqenebdes mravalperovantsqaroebsa da tvalsachinoebebs. es sheidzleba iqos sakhelmdzghvaneloebshiarsebuli skhvadaskhva sakhis tsqaroebi, mastsavleblis mier temis shesabamisadmomzadebuli, mostsavlis mier shekmnili da shegrovebuli masala,dokumenturi tu mkhatvruli pilmi; saojakho poto albomebi, dokumentebi,mimotsera, dzveli nivtebi (mag. samushao iaraghi, tu dzveli teleponis aparati).tsqaroebsa da tvalsachinoebebtan mushaoba khdeba rogorts saklaso otakhshi, aseveklasis garetats, magalitad, muzeumebshi, skolis ezoshi.zemot aghtserili dziritadi sainpormatsio tsqaroebi ise unda sheirches, rommostsavleebs nel-nela ganuvitardet kitkhvis sabaziso unarebi(shinaarsis gamotana, sakvandzo sakitkhebis gamotsalkeveba paralelebismodziebisa da daskvnebis gamotanistvis). bavshvebi unda gaerkvnen, rom„tsakitkhva“ tekstisats sheidzleba da potosuratis an nivtisats. es qoveliveinpormatsiis modziebas guliskhmobs.shemdeg etapze mostsavleebi mighebuli inpormatsiisshedareba/klasipitsirebaze mushaoben mag.:· tskhrilis an baratebis sashualebit ajgupebs bechdvis, kompiuteris anskhva tanamedrove elektronuli sakomunikatsio sashualebebisgamogonebebis shedegebs;· rukis dakhmarebit tskhrilshi ajgupebs kalakebs sakartvelos mkhareebismikhedvit;· adarebs ertmanets sakhelmtsipo mmartvelobis skhvadaskhva pormas dairchevs, misi azrit mistvis misaghebs;· asakhelebs skhvadaskhva dasakhlebis punktsionirebistvis autsilebelpirobebs; msjelobs mat mnishvnelobaze.· am asakshi unda chaeqaros sapudzveli mostsavleebis unars, tavadgamokhaton inpormatsia vizualurad (grapiki, tskhrili, nakhati).mostsavleta monatsileobit shekmnili tvalsachinoebebis gamoqenebasastsavlo resursad zrdis mostsavleta motivatsias.simulatsiazemot chamotvlili sabaziso tsnebebis kargad gasagebadmostsavleebisatvis sakmaod saintereso da naqopieri ikneba situatsiuri anprotsesis simulatsiis teknikis gamoqeneba.· mastsavleblis dakhmarebit tanaklaselebtan ertad mostsavle dgamssaklaso spektakls gamorcheul sakhelmtsipo moghvatseze; msjelobsspektaklshi gadmotsemuli istoriuli paktebis shesakheb (mag.: "patarakakhi")· monatsileobs konkretuli resursis araratsionalurad gamoqenebissimulatsiur tamashebshi, (mag.: saakhaltslo nadzvis kheebit an bzobaze tqeshimochrili bzit vachroba).· amgvari aktivobebi daekhmareba bavshvebs problemis/tsnebisdekonstruktsiasa da shemdeg ertian, gaazrebul aghkmashi. simulatsiisert-erti pormaa aseve roluri tamashebi. roluri tamashebisasmostsavleebi gaitamasheben skhvadaskhva situatsias, sadats skhvadaskhvadainteresebuli mkhareebis an pirovnebebis perspektividan aghtserenmovlenas, protsess an tsnebas.msjeloba/gaazreba - am etapisatvis dagegmili savarjishoebi da aktivobebiunda epudznebodes met-naklebad ukve atvisebul inpormatsias mag:· chamotvlis da akhasiatebs mmartvelobashi monatsile istoriul pirtamier gatarebul sakhelmtsipo ghonisdziebebs. gansazghvravs mat shedegebs;  
  . · drois skalaze aghnishnavs, misi azrit, qvelaze mnishvnelovan otkh (ankhut) kartvel politikur moghvatses udzvelesi droidan dghemde daakhasiatebs mat;· chamotvlis omebs ( tavdatsviti, dampqrobluri), akhasiatebs misshedegebs;· msjelobs gadamtsqveti brdzolebis, gamochenili mepeebisa da skhvatsnobil istoriul pirta moghvatseobis shesakheb.tanagrdznoba da gatavisebatsarsulis simulatsiur rekonstruktsiastan ertad gansakutrebitsakhaliso da naqopieria gasatavisebeli savarjishoebis shemotanaqoveldghiuri qopis, tses-chveulebebis aghtserisas, rats sashualebas mistsemsmostsavleebs aramarto gaiazron aramed sheigrdznon tsarsulshi mtskhovrebiadamianebis motivatsiebi, survilebi, otsnebebi. mati tvalit dainakhonsamqaro, ganitsadon skhva epokis adamianebis tskhovreba.mostsavleta satanado organizeba sotsialuri da sakomunikatsio unar-chvevebis mravalmkhrivi ganvitarebistvis autsilebeli elementia.sazogadoebrivi metsnierebebis mastsavlebelma klasis organizebisas,magalitad jgupuri mushaobisas, mostsavleebs mistses shesadzleblobaertoblivad gadatsqviton dasakhuli amotsanebi, moirgon ganskhvavebulirolebi: nebismier mostsavles unda edzleodes sashualeba skhvadaskhva drosiqos tsarmdgeni an lideri. tuki mostsavle aris kargi prezentatori, es arnishnavs imas, rom mas qoveltvis unda evalebodes jgupshi chatarebulisamushaos tsardgena.ghirebulebebis chamoqalibebaadamiani da sazogadoeba - mimartulebis shedegebis misaghtsevadmnishvnelovania mati gankhilva mostsavlis pirad gamotsdilebaze daqrdnobit.ojakhisa tu mshobliuri mkharis magalitebis gankhilvit. mastsavlebelmasastsavlo protsesi unda tsarmartos ise, rom mostsavleebs ganuvitarosadamianis ghirsebis, tavisuplebisa da tanastsorobis pativistsema. amghirebulebebze daqrdnobit kheli unda sheutsqos mostsavleebis etikuri dapasukhismgebeli ktsevis chamoqalibebas. ghirebulebebi vitardeba adamianis,mokalakis upleba-movaleobebis stsavlebis gzit, rats eqrdnoba chveni kveqniskulturul memkvidreobas, traditsiebs. mastsavlebelma samokalakoghirebulebebis chamoqalibebit unda ganuvitaros samshoblos siqvaruli. manunda gamoiqenos iseti tsqaroebi, romlebits mostsavleebs daapikrebsaktualur sakitkhebze da ganuvitarebs pozitiur damokidebulebebs.klasgareshe mushaoba orientirebulia inpormatsiis skhvadaskhva sashualebitmodziebis unaris ganvitarebaze.am asakobriv jguptan, sagnis spetsipikidan gamomdinare, autsilebeliadaigegmos klasgareshe samushaoebi. es advilad gansakhortsielebelia, radganmostsavleta ushualo sotsialur da bunebriv garemos ekheba (ojakhs, ubans,kuchas, skolas, tems). skolis garet mostsavleebs unda daevalot atsarmoondakvirvebebi (mag. transportis modzraobaze, arkitekturaze), moidzion sachiroinpormatsia intervius sakhit, lokaluri istoriebis shegroveba gvarisgenealogiaze, tu kuchis, soplis, kalakis shesakheb da a.sh. gaaketon azomvebimarshrutis tu skemis shesakmnelad, shekmnan chanakhatebi. amgvari aktivobebi  
  . sagnis shestsavlas upro sakhalisos gakhdis, kholo tsodnis mighebis gzebi uproepekturi ikneba.dasakhelebuli metoduri midgomebi aramarto zepirad, aramedtserilobitits shesadzloa gankhortsieldes.sabazo sapekhurisabazo sapekhurze istoriis, geograpiis da samokalako ganatlebisstsavlebam mostsavles unda daanakhos adamianis gamotsdilebismravalperovneba. katsobriobis monapovarta ponze tavisi kveqnis mightsevebismnishvneloba. mostsavles unda mietsodos inpormatsia rogorts sakartvelos,aseve msoplios bunebriv, politikur, sotsialur, ekonomikur, kulturul,religiur da etnikur mravalperovnebaze. am inpormatsiaze daqrdnobit manunda shedzlos tsarsulisa da tanamedroveobis umnishvnelovanesi istoriulitu geograpiuli movlenebis, protsesebis gaaanalizeba da skhvadaskhvaepokebisa da sazogadoebebis ganvitarebis msgavseba-ganskhvavebebis danakhva.istoriaam sapekhurze mostsavles unda chamouqalibdes istoriuli azrovnebisunari: shedzlebisdagvarad unda sheedzlos istoriuli movlenis mizezebisakhsna da misi shedegebis gaanalizeba; istoriuli protsesis skhvadaskhvakutkhit (politikuri, sotsialuri, ekonomikuri, kulturuli, religiuri)danakhva; istoriul movlenaze da pirovnebaze ganskhvavebuliinterpretatsiebis arsebobis mizezebis dadgena, ganskhvavebuli akhsna-ganmartebebis shedareba da shepaseba. istoriuli tsqaroebis modzieba, istoriuli masalis (istoriuli tserilobiti tsqaroebi, arkeologiuri tuetnograpiuli masala, istoriul temaze shekmnili mkhatvruli natsarmoebebi,potosuratebi da a.sh.) shedareba da analizi; istoriuli temis datsera; istoriul temaze gamartul debatebshi monatsileoba.geograpiasabazo sapekhuris dasrulebisatvis mostsavlem unda itsodes zogadigeograpiuli tsnebebi; lokalur, regionul da globalur doneebzemimdinare bunebrivi, sotsialur-ekonomikuri tu politikuri protsesebissivrtsobrivi aspektebi; teritoriebis gamoqopis printsipebi; mosakhleobis,satsarmoo da arasatsarmoo dargebis sivrtsobrivi ganatsileba. mas aseve undasheedzlos sakartvelosa (bunebrivi pirobebis, resursebis, gansakhlebebis,ekonomikis dargebis, sotsialuri speros, ekologiuri vitarebis, regionulierteulebis) da skhva kveqnis geograpiuli makhasiateblebis shedareba da amissapudzvelze msgavseba-ganskhvavebebisa da kavshirebis dadgena; rukebidan daskhva geograpiuli sashualebebidan mighebuli inpormatsiis shejereba daanalizi; martivi tematuri rukebis shedgena; geograpiuli temis datsera;  sasurvelia, rom istoriuli tu geograpiuli masalis mopovebisa da damushavebisasmostsavlem gamoiqenos sainpormatsio teknologiebi (internetisa da si-di-rom-is sashualebitinpormatsiis modzieba, kompiuteruli programebis dakhmarebit masalis damushaveba daelektronuli postit inpormatsiis gatsvla).  am sapekhurze mostsavles unda vastsavlot mis mier chatarebuli kvlevis sapudzvelzeargumentirebuli temis datsera, rats guliskhmobs: shesavalshi temis mtavari problemis moklemimokhilvasa da am problemisadmi sakutari pozitsiis gamokhatvas; dziritad natsilshi sakutaripozitsiis dasamtkitseblad argumentebisa da magalitebis moqvanas; daskvnashi ki – temisdziritad natsilshi gamotkmuli argumentebisa da mosazrebebis shejamebas.  
  . geograpiul problemebtan dakavshirebul debatebshi monatsileoba. qovelivezemotkmulis shestsavla unda daekhmaros mostsavles - ekologiuri kulturischamoqalibebashi.samokalako ganatlebahumanur ghirebulebebze dapudznebuli samokalako ganatleba mostsavlesunda daekhmaros sazogadoebisa da sakhelmtsipos tsinashe tavisi upleba-movaleobebis gatsnobierebashi da adamianis uplebebis, mmartvelobisa daekonomikis ganvitarebis shesakheb mighebuli teoriuli tsodnis qoveldghiurtskhovrebastan misadagebashi. sagnis stsavlebisas mas unda ganuvitardesmnishvnelovani samokalako unar-chvevebi: sakutari pozitsiis chamoqalibeba dadatsva; sakutari saktsielis kritikulad shepaseba; ganskhvavebuli azris,erovnebis, sartsmunoebisa da kulturis mkone adamianebis pativistsema;sazogadoebrivad sasargeblo sakmianobashi monatsileoba da kanonispativistsema.samokalako ganatleba mostsavles unda daekhmaros identobisganvitarebashi, tvitgamorkvevashi. misi stsavlebis shedegad mozardma undashesdzlos sakutari tavisa tu skhvebis skhvadaskhva kontekstis tsevrebad aghkmada pirovnebebad gatsnobiereba; man unda gaiazros tavisupleba, rogortsupleba da imavdroulad pasukhismgebloba da shedzlos sazogadoebis, rogortsganskhvavebuli interesebis, ghirebulebebis, motkhovnilebebis mkonesubiektebis urtiertkavshirebuli kompleksuri mtlianobis gaazreba. ratsmtavaria, samokalako ganatlebis dakhmarebit mostsavlem unda shesdzlossakutari momavali saganmanatleblo tu shromiti gzis gansazghvra.samokalako ganatlebis dakhmarebit mostsavle gaiazrebs garemos datsvisautsileblobas da mis kavshirs sazogadoebis mdgrad ganvitarebastan;aghmoachens tu ra mnishvnelovania mdgradi ganvitareba tanamedrove samqarosgadarchenistvis; mostsavlem unda istsavlos aktiuri monatsileobis mighebaiseti garemos shekmnashi, sadats ketilgantsqoba, adamianuri ghirsebispativistsema, urtiertdakhmareba, tanaziaroba tskhovrebis tsesia.samokalako ganatlebis stsavlebis protsesshi mostsavlem unda: gaatsnobierossakartvelo, rogorts sakhelmtsipo; aghikvas sakutari tavi mis mokalaked;sheistsavlos sazogadoebriv, politikur, ekonomikur, kulturultskhovrebashi monatsileobis pormebi da sashualebebi; gaiazros demokratiis,konstitutsiis, erovnuli da saertashoriso kanonmdeblobis, rogortssakhelmtsipos samartlebrivi bazis mnishvneloba; gaiazros sakutar daskhvis uplebebsa da pasukhismgeblobebs shoris arsebuli kavshiri dakonkretuli nabijebis gadadgas sakutari da skhvisi uplebebis dasatsavad;gaiazros adamianis/bavshvta uplebebis mnishvneloba da mati datsvistvisganakhortsielos konkretuli kmedeba; gaatsnobieros adamianta spetsipikurijgupebis uplebebis datsvis mnishvneloba da mati datsvistvis gadadgaskonkretuli nabijebis.sashualo sapekhuriistoriis, geograpiisa da samokalako ganatlebis stsavleba zogadiganatlebis mesame sashualo sapekhurze epudzneba skolashi sabazo sapekhurzemostsavlis mier mighebul tsodnas da sashualebas adzlevs mozards upro ghrmadsheistsavlos savaldebulo da mis mier archeuli sagnebi, daeuplossametsniero kvlevis zogad spetsipikas.  
  . istoriasakartvelosa da msoplio istoriis tsodna aris mostsavlis patriotad dapolitikurad ganatlebul mokalaked chamoqalibebis tsinapiroba. istoriisstsavlebam mostsavles unda daanakhos, rom istoria aris utsqveti protsesi, romtanamedrove sazogadoebisatvis umnishvnelovanesi politikuri, sotsialurida moraluri problemebi mettsilad ganpirobebulia saukuneebisa daatastsleulebis ganmavlobashi momkhdari tsvlilebebit. istoriis stsavlebammostsavles aseve unda ganuvitaros problemis gadachris unari.am amotsanebis shesruleba moitkhovs, rom mostsavles hkondes istoriuliazrovneba: mas unda sheedzlos istoriuli epokis aghkma (istoriuli epokisaghtserisas movlenebis danakhva im periodshi mtskhovrebi adamianebis tvalit;tsarsulshi momkhdari movlenebis shepaseba ara mkholod dghevandeligadasakhedidan, aramed im epokis paseulobebisa da shekhedulebebisgatvalistsinebit);  istoriul movlenebs shoris rtuli mizez-shedegobrivikavshirebis dadgena da analizi; istoriuli movlenis mizezebisa dashedegebis ganskhvavebuli shepasebebis shedareba da analizi; kanonzomierebebis shesakheb sakutari mosazrebis dasabuteba; damoukidebeli istoriuli kvleva (istoriuli kvleva-dziebis miznisgansazghvra da dagegmva; tserilobiti, vizualuri, literaturuli tsqaroebismodzieba; istoriuli dokumentis analizi; istorikosta ganskhvavebulishekhedulebebis shedareba; chatarebuli kvlevis sapudzvelze istoriulitemis datsera).geograpiaam sapekhurze mostsavle sheistsavlis msoplios kveqnebis dziritadmakhasiateblebs, matshi mimdinare skhvadaskhva protsesebsa da movlenebs;ganikhilavs da gaanalizebs bunebis datsvisa da zogadad mdgradiganvitarebis problemebs, am sakitkhebisadmi alternatiul midgomebs, matigadatsqvetis shesadzlo gzebs, globaluri problemebis geograpiultaviseburebebs; gaatsnobierebs, tu ra didi tsvlilis shetana sheudzliatsodnita da gamotsdilebit aghchurvil titoeul adamiansa da sazogadoebasgaremos gajansaghebashi, misi mdgradobis shenarchunebashi.sashualo sapekhuris damtavrebis shemdeg mostsavles unda sheedzlosgaremoshi mimdinare movlenebis dakvirvebis sapudzvelze gansazghvrosmosakhleobis dziritadi motkhovnebi da problemebi, gamoikvlios dagamotkvas varaudi problemebis gadachris gzebze. shedzlos geograpiulikvlevis dagegmva, chatareba da kvlevis shedegis rogorts tserilobit, asevezepirad tsarmodgena; kvlevis protsesshi vizualuri masalis (ruka da skhvageograpiuli sashualebebi) shekmna.samokalako ganatlebaam sapekhurze samokalako ganatleba mostsavles sashualebas mistsemsdaeuplos politikuri, iuridiuli da ekonomikuri metsnierebebissapudzvlebs; daekhmareba mas sotsialuri, moraluri, samokalako  autsilebelia, rom istoriuli epokis aghkmis unaris chamoqalibeba datsqebiti da sabazoskolis sapekhurze daitsqos.  am miznis misaghtsevad autsilebelia sakhelmdzghvanelos garda mostsavles kheli miutsvdebodesskhvadaskhva istoriul masalaze.  mostsavles unda esmodes, rom pirovnebas akvs tavisupali neba da archevanis gaketebisunari. mas gaazrebuli unda hkondes, rom istoria skhva gzitats sheidzleba ganvitarebuliqo. amshemtvevashi mas ar sheekmneba shtabechdileba, rom momavali tsinastsar aris gansazghvruli da rompirovnebis kmedebas da mis mier gaketebul archevans mnishvneloba ar akvs.  
  . dro da sivrtsesazogadoebrivi metsnierebebis mimartulebashi ”dro da sivrtse”gaertianebuli shedegebi pirvel rigshi mostsavles drosa da sivrtseshiorientirebis unars sdzens.es mimartuleba gamcholia geograpiashi. igi aertianebs geograpiisatvisiset mnishvnelovan temebsa da unar-chvevebs, rogorebitsaa rukis kitkhva,tvalsachinoebebis analizi, interpretatsia da shekmna; aseve teritoriebisgeograpiuli mdebareobis gansazghvra; geograpiul garemos, geologiurdros, geograpiuli movlenebis, protsesebisa da kanonzomierebebisgavrtselebis tsodnas.istoriis shemtkhvevashi mostsavle eupleba iset pundamentur tsnebebs,rogorebitsaa: drois erteulebi, mimartebebi adre/gvian, tsarsuli, atsmqo,momavali, kronologia (m.sh. geokronologiuri tseltaghritskhva), tseltaghritskhva,periodizatsia, saukune, atastsleuli, kalendari, istoriuliepokebi/periodebi, epoka da regioni.garemo da ekonomikamimartulebis ”garemo da ekonomika” mizania mostsavles daanakhosbunebrivi garemosa da ekonomikis mnishvneloba sazogadoebisatvis. esmimartuleba aertianebs bunebrivi garemos, bunebrivi resursebis,mosakhleobis, ekonomikis dargebis gatsnobierebisa da shestsavlisakenmimartul shedegebs. mostsavles sashualeba edzleva gaatsnobierosgeograpiuli paktorebis urtiertkavshiri da urtiertdamokidebuleba.amave mimartulebashi gamcholadaa tsarmodgenili garemosdatsviti tsnobierebischamoqalibebebisken mimartuli shedegebi.ak gaertianebuli shedegebi mostsavles sashualebas adzlevs aghikvasekonomikisa da bunebrivi paktorebis urtiertgavlena. gaatsnobieros amkavshirebis tsvalebadoba drosa da sivrtseshi mati kanonzomierebebi.sakhelmtsipo mmartveloba da politikaam mimartulebis mizania mostsavles sashualeba mistses gaatsnobierossakhelmtsipos raoba da punktsiebi. aghikvas politikuri protsesebismnishvneloba da zogadi kanonzomierebebi. daekhmaros mostsavles istoriulipaktebis ganzogadebashi.kultura da religiaam mimartulebis mizania mostsavles daanakhos dedamitsaze adamianisshekmnili kulturuli memkvidreobis mravalperovneba da daekhmaros misklasipitsirebashi. kheli sheutsqos mas istoriuli epokebi da mkhareebiganaskhvavos mattvis damakhasiatebeli etnograpiuli qopisa da kulturismightsevebis sapudzvelze. daekhmaros mostsavles religiis raobisa damnishvnelobis gansazghvrashi. tsarmodgena sheukmnas msoplioshi arsebulireligiuri sistemebis mravalperovnebaze.adamiani da sazogadoebaam mimartulebis mizania mostsavles daanakhos, rom istoriis mtavarshemokmeds adamiani tsarmoadgens, romelsats tavisi uplebebi dasazogadoebis tsinashe garkveuli valdebulebebi gaachnia. sazogadoebaskhvadaskhva sotsialuri penisgan shedgeba. mostsavlem unda itsodes tu rogori  
  . is tsvlilebata protsesia, romelshits bunebrivi resursebis mokhmareba,investitsiebi, metsnierul-teknikuri ganvitareba, pirovnebis ganvitareba dainstitutsiuri tsvlilebebi urtiertshetankhmebulia da amqarebs adamianismotkhovnilebebisa da mistsrapebebis dasakmaqopileblad sachiro atsmqo dasamomavlo potentsials. garkveultsilad, saubaria adamianta tskhovrebiskhariskhis uzrunvelqopaze.tvitmmartveloba da mmartvelobatvitmmartveloba da mmartveloba ukavshirdeba im gadatsqvetilebebs(individualur, ojakhis, temis, kveqnis doneze), romlebits gansazghvravsmolodinebs, dzalauplebis minichebas an sakmianobis kontrols. is moitsavsindividualuri, an jgupuri tu sazogadoebrivi sakmianobis martvisprotsesebisa da liderobis spetsipikur natsils.geograpiuli kvlevaam mimartulebis mtavari mizania, mozardma gaatsnobieros geograpiisa dageograpiuli tsodnis mnishvneloba adamianis sakmianobis skhvadaskhvasperosatvis. gaetsnos geograpiuli kvlevebis traditsiul (aghtseriti,shedarebit-geograpiuli, kartograpiuli) da akhal (matematikuri,distantsiuri, geoinpormatsiuli) metodebs. sheistsavlos geograpiuliprognozisa da modelirebis sakitkhebi. shedzlos shesabamis problemastandakavshirebuli teoriuli masalis da tsqaroebis modzieba; savele pirobebshiinpormatsiis shegroveba, masalis organizeba, analizi da geograpiuli temisstrukturis shemushaveba.samokalako tavdatsvisa da usaprtkhoebis stsavla -stsavlebamimdinareobs sami dziritadi mimartulebit:· piradi usaprtkhoebis uzrunvelqopa qoveldghiur tskhovrebashi;· sagangebo vitarebebshi usaprtkho ktsevis sapudzvlebi;· gadaudebeli ekimamdeli dakhmareba.adamianis sitsotskhlisa da janmrtelobis saprtkheebi skhvadaskhvagvariatavisi tsarmoshobis/mizezebis, gavrtselebis, zemokmedi paktorebis,shedegebisa da shesabamisi usaprtkhoebis zomebis mikhedvit. imavdroulad,bavshvis zrdastan ertad itsvleba rogorts mastan dakavshirebuli saprtkheebistipebi, ise usaprtkhoebis zomebis datsvis shesadzleblobebi.mostsavlesa da stsavlis shedegze orientebuli saganmanatleblo protsesi,bunebrivia, unda itvalistsinebdes rogorts saprtkheebisa da mastangamklavebis, ise bavshvebis asakobriv taviseburebebs.mnishvnelovania, rom samokalako tavdatsvisa da usaprtkhoebissaganmanatleblo programa itvalistsinebdes mravalperovanshesadzleblobebs skhvadaskhva motivatsiisa da shesadzleblobis mostsavletatvis.v) shepaseba sazogadoebriv metsnierebebshishepasebis komponentebi sazogadoebriv metsnierebebshi:

 sulkhan saba orbeliani – „ ormoshi chagdebuli mepe “ 
 „orni mepeni sheibnen. ertman mepeman meoresa sdzlo, sheipqra da ormoshi chaagdo. gamokhda khani. movida erti metsnieri katsi da eneba aghmoqvaneba da gapareba misi. chasdzakha ormosa shigan da utkhra: kargad ara vikm, rom gagaparoo? man mepeman madli ubrdzana. tokit amozidna da amoiqvana. kide vutkhra: kargad ara vkmen, rom amogiqvaneo? mepeman kidev madli ubrdzana. mesamed kidev utkhra: kargada vkmeno? etsqina mepesa da daidzakha: vina khart, am katsman gamaparao! movidnen mtsvelni, sheipqrnes ornive. hkitkhes mepesa: rad gaamzhghavne da rad ar gaipareo? man tkva: virem amomiqvanda, saqvedurit amavso, tu shin mimetsia, kidets damarchobda, akav qopna virchiveo.
