 sakhelmtsipod 
 damkvidrebis 
 sasargeblod. chven khelisupleba gadmovibaret im politikuri dzalisgan, romlis mmartvelobasats mohqva damatebiti teritoriebis okupatsia da akhali devnilebi, adamianis ghirsebis pekhkvesh gatelva da misi pundamenturi uplebebis sruli shelakhva, mosakhleobis udidesi natsilis masobrivi gaghatakeba, sakhelmtsipostan shezrdili biznesi da monopoliebi, ukiduresad dzviri, mosakhleobis udidesi umravlesobistvis sruliad khelmiutsvdomeli jandatsva, moshlili ganatlebis sistema, politizebuli politsia, khelisuplebisgan martuli sasamartlo da media sashualebebi. chven davdzliet krizisi da davitsqet iseti sakhelmtsipos mshenebloba, romelits epudzneba realuri demokratiis umtavres printsipebs, sadats datsulia titoeuli mokalakis pundamenturi uplebebi, khelsheukhebelia sakutreba, tavisupalia biznesi, khelisuplebis gavlenisgan gatavisuplebulia sasamartlo da media, politsia aghar emsakhureba ert politikur dzalas da khalkhis samsakhurshi dgas; sadats qvelas akvs ganatlebisa da sameditsino dakhmarebis mighebis sashualeba. chven vashenebt sakhelmtsipos, sadats khortsieldeba realuri da gegmazomieri repormebi. partia „kartuli otsneba-demokratiuli sakartvelo“ archevnebshi gamarjvebis shemdeg ighebs pasukhismgeblobas, rom sakartvelo ikneba tavisupali, demokratiuli, samartlebrivi, ertiani, dzlieri da tsarmatebuli kveqana, romlis titoeul mokalakes ekneba qvela piroba sakutari shesadzleblobebis realizebisa da ghirseuli tskhovrebisatvis. amis misaghtsevad: datsuli ikneba adamianis pundamenturi uplebebi; ganmtkitsdeba kanonis uzenaesoba, sasamartlos damoukidebloba da samartaldamtsavi organoebis sakmianoba kidev upro dauakhlovdeba evropul standartebs; khelsheukhebeli ikneba gamokhatvisa da mediis tavisupleba; ganatleba da jandatsva khelmisatsvdomi ikneba sakartvelos titoeuli mokalakisatvis; daikhvetseba sakhelmtsipo sotsialuri programebi; datsuli ikneba kerdzo sakutreba da shromiti uplebebi, gachndeba akhali samushao adgilebi da daidzleva sigharibe; sakartvelos stsrapi ganvitarebistvis gankhortsieldeba repormebis  -punktiani gegma, romelits garghvevas moakhdens kveqnis ekonomikashi, gankhortsieldeba upretsedento masshtabis inprastrukturuli proektebi, romelta shedegadats sakartvelos regionebi umoklesi gzebit daukavshirdeba ertmanets, kveqnis masshtabit gadaadgileba gakhdeba stsrapi da komportuli rogorts shida mimosvlisatvis, ise tranzitistvis. am repormebis shedegebi umokles vadashi -   tselitsadshi aisakheba titoeuli chveni moka­ lakis ketildgheobaze. prioritetuli ikneba mtsire da sashualo biznesis khelshetsqoba, metsarmeobisa da akhali biznesis tsakhaliseba, soplis meurneobis ganvitareba da msoplio ekonomikur sistemashi kveqnis integrireba; gamqardeba kveqnis usaprtkhoeba da sakartvelos regionaluri pozitsiebi, kidev upro gaghrmavdeba evrokavshirsa da natostan integratsiis protsesebi; sagareo politikis dghis tsesrigis mtavari tema ikneba okupirebuli regionebis araghiarebis politika da, saertashoriso tanamegobrobis chartulobit, kveqnis deokupatsiis mightseva. gagrdzeldeba mushaoba apkhazebsa da osebtan pirdapiri dialogisa da sherigebis protsesis dasatsqebad. kveqnis gamtlianeba mokhdeba mshvidobiani gzit, romelsats alternativa ara akvs. partia ,,kartul otsneba - demokratiuli sakartvelo“ moakhdens garghvevas kveqnis ganvitarebashi da khalkhtan ertad miaghtsevs qvela dasakhul mizans. tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba - es aris chveni mizani! chven ertad gavimarjvebt! 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 demokratiuli ganvitareba  . demokratiuli ganvitareba  -  tslebshi sakartvelom ganitsada punda­ menturi tsinsvla demokratiuli ganvitarebis qvela mimartulebit: adamianis ghirsebis, misi uplebebis da tavisuplebis datsva iktsa khelisuplebis sakmi­ anobis mtavar prioritetad, tvisebrivad amaghlda mmartvelobisa da politikuri sistemebis demokratiulobis, agretve samokalako sektoris aktiurobis khariskhi.  . . adamianis uplebebi: ghirseba, tavisupleba da usaprtkhoeba adamiani aris mtavari ghirebuleba da khelisuplebis qoveli mokmedeba am ghirebulebis datsvas unda emsakhurebodes. adamiani unda iqos sakhelmtsipos qoveli mokmedebis mizani da artsert shemtkhvevashi miznis mightsevis sashualeba. adamianis ghirsebisa da tavisuplebis masobrivi khelqopis aghkveta da adamianis uplebebis datsva   tslis demokratiuli gardatekhis ert-erti umtavresi monapovaria. adamianis ghirsebis shemlakhavi represiuli rezhimi chanatsvlda humanuri, adamianze orientirebuli mmartvelobit. „kartuli otsnebis“ mmartvelobis pirobebshi, adamianis ghirsebisa da misi uplebebis datsva iktsa khelisuplebis umtavres prioritetad da   tslidan gankhortsielebuli qvela sistemuri reporma am prioritets daepudzna. sakartveloshi adamianis uplebebis datsvis standartis mudmivi gaumjobeseba uzrunvelqopilia adamianis uplebata datsvis erovnuli strategiis shesabamisad, romelits pirvelad damoukidebeli sakartvelos istoriashi „kartuli otsnebis“ mmartvelobis pirobebshi, misi khelisuplebashi mosvlistanave shemushavda da damtkitsda. pundamenturad sheitsvala siskhlis samartlis represiuli siskhlis samartlis politika liberalurma, humanurma da damnashaveta resotsializatsia-reabilitatsiaze dapudznebulma politikam shetsvala. sasjelaghsrulebis datsesebulebebis gadavsebis, „nulovani tolerantobis“ politikisa da khelisuplebis totaluri tvitnebobis aghkvetis ponze, kveqanashi gaumjobesda kriminogenuri vitareba.   tseltan shedarebit,   tsels danashaulis (mat shoris mkvlelobis, qachaghobis, dzartsvis, kurdobis) machvenebeli  %-it shemtsirda.  %-s gadaacharba danashaulis gakhsnis machvenebelma, romelits   tslebshi  %-s ar aghemateboda. gaukmda sasjelis upirobo shekrebitobis tsesi, rats chadenil danashaultan shedarebit, araadekvaturad mdzime sasjelis dakisrebas itsvevda. gankhortsielda saprotseso shetankhmebis reporma - gaizarda mosamartlis uplebamosilebebi saprotseso shetankhmebis gapormebis protsesshi; gapartovda saprotseso shetankhmebis gasachivrebis sapudzvlebi; prokuraturam shetsvala saprotseso shetankhmebis gapormebisas jarimis gadakhdis politika, ris shedegadats jarimis sakhit gadakhdili tankhebis odenoba titkmis samjer shemtsirda - saprotseso shetankhmeba aghar gamoiqeneba sakhelmtsipo biujetis shevsebis tsqarod. adamianebi politika. 
 datsuli arian mati uplebebis danashaulebrivi khelqopisgan khelisuplebis mkhridan. aghikveta sistemuri danashauli sasjelaghsrulebis sistemashi.   tsels sakartvelo     patimrit 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 pinansur mkhardacheras. chamoqalibda religiuri temebis pinansuri mkhardacheris mekanizmi, saidanats dapinansebas muslimuri, iudeuri, katolike da somekhta kristianuli samotsikulo temebi igheben. ganvitarda religiuri politikis shemushavebasa da gankhortsielebashi interreligiuri chartulobis mekanizmebi. gadaidga mnishvnelovani nabijebi religiuri gaertianebebis konebrivi uplebebis aghdgenis mimartulebit; - khelisuplebam gadadga mnishvnelovani nabijebi erovnuli umtsiresobebis uplebebis datsvisa da mati samokalako integratsiis uzrunve­ lsaqopad.   tsels sakartvelos mtavrobam daamtkitsa „samokalako tanastsorobisa da integratsiis sakhelmtsipo strategia da   tsts. samokmedo gegma“, romelits sauketeso praktikas da gamotsdilebas daepudzna, agretve gansazghvra arsebul sachiroebebsa da gamotsvevebze epekturi reagirebis mekanizmebi. mnishvnelovan prioritetad ganisazghvra khariskhian ganatlebaze khelmisatsvdomoba. shemushavda etnikuri umtsire­ sobebis ganatlebis politikis dokumenti skolamdeli, zogadi, propesiuli da umaghlesi ganatlebis doneebze. khortsieldeba kartuli enis spetsialuri kursebi rogorts sauniversiteto, ise propesiuli ganatlebis mighebis msurveltatvis da sajaro mokheleebistvis. meti quradgheba daetmo mtsireritskhovan etnikur jgupebs, mat kulturul tvitmqopadobas da sachiroebebs. sakhelmtsipos mier gatarebuli politikis shedegad, amaghlda erovnuli umtsiresobebistvis sakhelmtsipo enis stsavlebis epektianobis khariskhi. khortsieldeba spetsialuri programebi, romlis parglebshi   skolashi gaikhsna kartuli enis klubebi, ritats  -ze meti mostsavle,  -mde mastsavlebeli da  -ze meti adgilobrivi temis tsevri sargeblobs. kartuli enis   mastsavlebeli mivlenil ikna samtskhe-javakhetis, kvemo kartlisa da kakhetis arakartulenovan skolebshi; -   tslis ganmavlobashi gatarda mteli rigi ghonisdziebebi genderuli tanastsorobis uzrun­ ve­lsaqopad da kalta mimart dzaladobis aghmo­ sapkhvrelad. gadzlierda genderuli nishnit diskriminatsiis gamovlenisa da aghmopkhvris insti­tutsiuri mekanizmebi; - gadaidga kmediti nabijebi ojakhshi dzaladobis aghmosapkhvrelad, dzaladobis mskhverplta rea­bilitatsiis uzrunvelsaqopad, agretve sazo­gadoebrivi tsnobierebis asamaghleblad. gamkatsrda sanktsiebi ojakhshi dzaladobastan dakav­ shirebul danashaulta mimart, gankhortsielda idzulebiti kortsinebis kriminalizatsia,   tslidan aikrdzaleba   tslamde kortsineba;  realizeba da sazogadoebriv tskhovrebashi mati aktiuri chartulobis uzrunvelqopa „kartuli otsnebis“ erterti prioritetia.   tsels khelisuplebam ganakhortsiela shshmp gaeros konventsiis

 kartuli otsneba“ aris da ikneba garanti imisa, rom sakartveloshi ar dabrundeba khelisuplebis mier adamianis ghirsebis ugulvebelqopisa da shelakhvis praktika da kveqana ganvitarebas ganagrdzobs adamianis ghirsebis, tavisuplebisa da usaprtkhoebis ganukhreli datsvis pirobebshi. siskhlis samartlis politikis shemdgomi gaumjobesebis uzrunvelsaqopad, gagrdzeldeba siskhlis samartlis reporma: siskhlis samartlis materialuri da saprotseso kanonmdebloba daikhvetseba samokalako sektoris chartulobit, saertashoriso standartebisa da sauketeso praktikis shesabamisad; uzrunvelqopili ikneba siskhlis samartlis politikis orientireba msjavrdebulta reabilitatsiasa da resotsializatsiaze - gapartovdeba arasapatimro sasjelebis tsre da dainergeba shesabamisi servisebi; sasjelaghsrulebis sistemis shemdgomi gaumjo­ 
 besebis miznit: 
 - sul upro meti msjavrdebulistvis khelmisatsvdomi gakhdeba propesiuli ganatleba; shesadzlebeli gakhdeba umaghlesi ganatlebis migheba dabali 
 riskis datsesebulebebshi; msjavrdebultatvis sheikmneba dasakmebis akhali kerebi; gadzlierdeba patimarta psiko-sotsialuri reabilitatsiis, mat shoris skhvadaskhva damokidebulebis mkone pirta reabilitatsiis programebi; - dainergeba arasapatimro sasjelis akhali sakhe - shinapatimroba srultslovani msjavr­ debulebistvis, rats naklebad mdzime danashaulshi msjavrdebul pirta resotsializatsias da sabiujeto sakhsrebis dazogvas sheutsqobs khels. shinapatimrobis aghsrulebis kontroli gankhortsieldeba elektronuli monitoringis meshveobit, rats minimumamde daiqvans ganmeorebiti danashaulis chadenis risks. mokhdeba shinapatimrobis gamoqeneba pirobit vadamde gatavisuplebis protsesshits, rats sakhelmtsipos sashualebas mistsems, gatavisuplebuli piris satanado ktseva masze epekturi kontrolis gankhortsielebis gzit uzrunvelqos. dainergeba akhali arasapatimro aghkvetis ghonisdzieba tsinasasamartlo probatsia, rats saertashoriso standartebisa da rekomendatsiebis shesabamisad, mnishvnelovnad sheamtsirebs tsinastsar patimrobashi mqopi braldebulebis raodenobas. kvlavats

 ikneba 
 sakutrebis 
 gagrdzeldeba samartlianobis aghdgenis protsesi - konstitutsiur parglebshi da saertashoriso valdebulebebis shesabamisad, khelisupleba gamoiqenebs qvela samartlebriv mekanizms, rata titoeul adamians aghudges tsina khelisuplebis mier darghveuli upleba da daisajon shesabamis danashaulshi braldebuli pirebi. uzrunvelqopili ikneba gamokhatvisa da mediis tavisupleba, mediapluralizmi da saredaktsio politikis tavisupleba. 
 khelisupleba uzrunvelqops shekrebis tavisu­ srulpasovan realizatsias. daikhvetseba spontanuri shekrebebis momtsesrigebeli sakanon­ mdeblo normebi da kidev upro gadzlierdeba shekrebebis, aseve gamokhatvis skhva pormebis khelis sheshlis paktebis aghkvetisa da preventsiis mekanizmebi. uzrunvelqopili ikneba shekrebis uplebis darghvevis paktebze kmediti samartlebrivi reagireba da uplebis darghvevis preventsia. plebis 
 kidev upro standartebtan 
 daikhvetseba da saertashoriso shesabamisobashi mova piradi tskhovrebis khelsheukheblobis maregulirebeli kanonmdebloba da zedamkhedvelobis sistema. gagrdzeldeba shida da gare kontrolis mekanizmebis ganvitareba, romlebits operatiul-samdzebro ghonisdziebata gankhortsielebisas, uzrunvelqops piradi tskhovrebis khelsheukheblobis datsvas upro maghali standartit da minimumamde daiqvans khelisuplebis mkhridan piradi tskhovrebis uplebis shezghudvis borotad gamoqenebis risks. aghnishnuli tsvlilebebi gankhortsieldeba imgvarad, rom datsuli iqos gonivruli balansi piradi tskhovrebis 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 demokratiuli ganvitareba khelsheukheblobisa da kveqnisa da adamianebis usaprtkhoebis interesebs shoris. gankhortsieldeba kmediti ghonisdziebebi piradi tskhovrebis khelsheukheblobisa da personalur monatsemta datsvis shesakheb sazogadoebis tsnobierebis asamaghleblad. gatardeba kmediti ghonisdziebebi tanastsorobis uplebis realizebisatvis da adamianebis nebismieri nishnit diskriminatsiis tavidan asatsileblad da aghsakvetad. gadzlierdeba „diskriminatsiis qvela pormis aghmopkhvris shesakheb“ kanonis aghsrulebis mekanizmebi: - uzrunvelqopili ikneba rtsmenis tavisuplebis datsva qvela religiuri gaertianebisa da titoeuli adamianistvis. gagrdzeldeba da kidev upro gaghrmavdeba interreligiuri dialogi. khelisupleba khels sheutsqobs sazogadoebashi shemtsqnareblobis kulturis shemdgom ganvitarebas; - erovnuli umtsiresobebis uplebebis datsvisa da realizebis uzrunvelsaqopad, gankhor­ tsieldeba samokalako tanastsorobisa da integratsiis  -  tslebis samokmedo gegma. aghnishnuli gegma miznad isakhavs momdevno tslebis ganmavlobashi kmediti nabijebis gadadgmas, rata sakartvelos qvela mokalakes, ganurchevlad etnikuri tsarmomavlobisa, hkondes shesadzlebloba, srulpasovnad chaer­ tos sazogadoebrivi tskhovrebis qvela speroshi, kveqnis ekonomikur ganvitarebashi, poli­ tikur da samokalako protsesebshi. gaaktiurdeba dzaliskhmeva qoveltsliuri detaluri gegmis gankho­rtsielebisatvis shesabamisi utsqe­be­ bis koordinirebuli mushaobit, mat sho­ris samokalako integratsiis sakitkhebze arse­ buli komisiis parglebshi. gansakutrebit prioritetuli ikneba sakhelmtsipo enis tsodnis donis gaumjobeseba, rats khshirad kmnis tsinaghobas etnikuri umtsiresobebis tsarmomadgenlebis srulpasovani chartulobisatvis. shesabamisad, gaizrdeba sakhelmtsipo enis stsavlebis programebis epekturoba, gapartovdeba tsvdoma sakhelmtsipo enis programebze akademiuri protsesis mighmats. uzrunvelqopili ikneba kartuli enis miznobrivi stsavleba sajaro sektorshi dasakmebuli etnikuri umtsiresobis tsarmomadgenlebistvis. kompakturad dasakhlebul regionebshi etnikuri umtsiresobebistvis gaumjobesdeba adminis­ tratsiuli tsarmoebis dokumentebisa da sazogadoebrivi momsakhurebis khelmisatsvdomoba. ganatlebis strategiuli dokumentis shesabamisad, gadaidgmeba kmediti nabijebi da mnishvnelovnad gaumjobesdeba khariskhian ganatlebaze khelmisatsvdomoba ganatlebis qvela sapekhurebze. gaumjobesdeba mediasa da inpormatsiaze khelmisatsvdomoba da shesabamisad, erovnuli umtsiresobebis ertian sainpormatsio sivrtseshi chartva, rats tsarmatebuli samokalako integratsiis protsesis ert-erti tsinapirobaa. etnikuri umtsiresobebit dasakhlebul regionebshi gagrdzeldeba inprastrukturis, sotsialuri da ekonomikuri shesadzleblobebis ganvitareba, mat 
 shoris sakhelmtsipos shesabamis programebsa da servisebze mattvis gasageb enaze srulqopili inpormatsiis khelmisatsvdomobis gazrdit; uzrunvelqopili ikneba erovnul umtsiresobata kulturuli tvitmqopadobis shenarchunebis da ganvitarebis shesadzleblobebi, tolerantuli garemos tsakhaliseba mtlianad sazogadoebashi; - gankhortsieldeba kmediti ghonisdziebebi sazogadoebrivi tskhovrebis qvela speroshi, gansakutrebit politikur da ekonomikur sakmianobashi da gadatsqvetilebis mighebis doneze, genderuli tanastsorobis dasatsavad; uzrunvelqopili ikneba stsrapi da kmediti reagireba genderuli tanastsorobis darghvevis titoeul paktze; khelisupleba khels sheutsqobs genderuli tanastsorobis sakitkhebze tsnobierebis amaghlebis kampaniis tsarmartvas; - gagrdzeldeba repormebi ojakhshi dzaladobis mskhverpltatvis samartlebrivi datsvis da psiko-sotsialuri reabilitatsiis progra­ mebis da tavshesapris khelmisatsvdomobis uzrunvelsaqopad; ojakhuri dzaladobis mskhver­ pltatvis amokmeddeba sakhelmtsipo kompensatsiis sistema; gagrdzeldeba ojakhshi dzaladobis sakitkhebze tsnobierebis amaghlebis kampania; - datsuli ikneba shshm pirta uplebebi gonivruli misadagebis printsipis sapudzvelze, mati sachiroebebis gatvalistsinebit; sazogadoebriv da politikur tskhovrebashi shshm pirta srulqopili monatsileobis uzrunvelsaqopad, sakhelmtsipo khels sheutsqobs shshm pirta dasakmebas, aseve administratsiuli shenobebis shshm pirta sachiroebebis gatvalistsinebit adaptirebas; khelisupleba khels sheutsqobs sazogadoebrivi satransporto sashualebebis, gadaadgilebisa da mogzaurobis tanabar khelmisatsvdomobas, shesabamisi regulatsiebis shemushavebisa da danergvis gzit. gagrdzeldeba

 trepikingis 
  . . adamianis uplebebis datsvis institutsiuri mekanizmebi pundamenturad gaumjobesda adamianis uplebebis datsvis institutsiuri mekanizmebi, romlebits gasuli   tslis ganmavlobashi, khelisuplebis tanmimdevruli da printsipuli politikis shedegad, tandatanobit gatavisuplda qopili mmartveli partiis gavlenisgan. sasamartloebis personaluri shemadgenlobis arsebitad shenarchunebis pirobebshi, sasamartlo khelisupleba gatavisuplda politikuri gav­lenisgan.   tslis noembershi daitsqo martlmsajulebis institutsiuri repormis pirveli etapi, romlis shedegad - pirvelad chatarda iustitsiis sabchos tsevrta archevnebi demokratiuli tsesebis datsvit, sabchoshi tsevroba sheutsqdat parlamentis tsevrebs da isini saeksperto tsreebis, samokalako sazogadoebisa da advokatta asotsiatsiis tsevrebma shetsvales; daikhvetsa mosamartleta distsiplinuri 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 demokratiuli ganvitareba devnis protsedurebi. sasamartlo darbazebshi dabrunda satelevizio kamerebi, ris shedegadats sasamartlo protsesebi parto sazogadoebrivi metvalqureobis kvesh moektsa.   tslis tebervalshi daitsqo repormis meore etapi, romlis shedegad sistemashi pirvelad ikna shemoghebuli mosamartlis shepasebis instituti. repormis shedegad, shejibrebitobis printsipma siskhlis samartlis protsesshi realuri mnishvneloba sheidzina. mkhareta uplebebis satanadod realizebis uzrunvelsaqopad, sheikmna mkhareta mier sasamartloshi mtkitsebulebebis pirveladi pormit tsardgenis meti shesadzlebloba. gardaikmna da gadamushavda normebi, romlebits ekheba aghkvetis ghonisdziebis, gansakutrebit - patimrobis gamoqenebas, shetsvlasa da gaukmebas. mosamartleebi upirobod aghar akmaqopileben braldebis mkharis shuamdgomlobebs patimrobis motkhovnit. sasamartlo praktikashi gamochnda aghkvetis ghonisdziebis iseti sakhe, rogorits aris shetankhmeba gausvlelobisa da satanado ktsevis shesakheb. stsrapi martlmsajulebis samartlianad da gamchvirvaled gankhortsielebis uzrunvelsaqopad, gapartovda dazaralebulis saprotseso uplebebi. dazaralebuls mietsa upleba - miighos inpormatsia gamodziebis mimdinareobis shesakheb da gaetsnos sakmis masalebs; gansakutrebit mdzime danashaulis shemtkhvevashi, sasamartloshi gaasachivros siskhlissamartlebrivi devnis shetsqvetis shesakheb prokuroris dadgenileba. repormis shedegad sheitsvala tsinastsari gamodziebis dros motsmis dakitkhvis tsesi. savaldebulo dakitkhva nebaqoplobiti gamokitkhvit sheitsvala. administratsiuli patimrobis vada shemtsirda   dghidan   dghemde. gankhortsielda napits msajulta sasamartlos reporma, romlis shedegad napits msajulta sasamartloebi sakartvelos shvid kalakshi amokmeddeba. sasamartlos damoukideblobis khariskhis pundamenturi gaumjobesebis shedegad,   tseltan shedarebit, administratsiul sakmeebze khelisuplebis sasargeblod mighebuli gadatsqvetilebebis raodenoba  %-it aris shemtsirebuli, kholo sasamartlos mier tsinastsari patimrobis shepardebis machvenebeli  %-dan  %mde shemtsirda.  -  tslebshi qopili mmartveli partia inarchunebda gadamtsqvet gavlenas sakartvelos sakonstitutsio sasamartlos sakmianobaze. politikuri interesebis shesabamisad, tvisebrivad sheitsvala sasamartlos praktika. sakonstitutsio sasamartlos tavmjdomaris gadatsqvetilebit, politikuri datvirtvis mkone qvela sakme ertsa da imave kolegias etsereboda. shedegad, tu   tslebshi sakonstitutsio sasamartlom arsebitad mkholod   sakme ganikhila,   tslidan es machvenebeli ornakhevarjer gaizarda da   tslis ivlisis mdgomareobit,   sheadgina.   tsels gankhortsielebuli sakanonmdeblo tsvlilebebis shedegad, amaghlda sakonstitutsio sasamartloshi sakmeta gadatsqvetis standarti, ritats gadaidga umnishvnelovanesi nabiji misi politikuri damoukideblobis uzrunvelsaqopad da politikuri gavlenis tavidan asatsileblad. garda amisa, 
 sheitsvala sakonstitutsio sasamartlos tavmjdomaris archevis tsesi da igi   tslidan sakonstitutsio sasamartlos mosamartleebis mier aircheva. pundamenturad sheitsvala prokuraturis sakmia­ nobis printsipebi. prokuratura, romelits   tslamde srulad akontrolebda sasamartlo khelisuplebas da adamianebze zetsolis ert-ert mtavar iaraghad iqo ktseuli, dghes depolitizebulia da siskhlissamartlebriv devnas kanonmdeblobis motkhovnata datsvit akhortsielebs. prokuraturis damoukideblobis ganmtkitsebas damatebit sheutsqo kheli shesabamisma sakanonmdeblo da institutsiurma tsvlilebebma - iustitsiis ministri aghar sargeblobs saprokuroro zedamkhedvelobis uplebit; pro­ kuratura gatavisuplda aghmasrulebeli kheli­ suplebis gavlenisagan. mtavari prokuroris archevis uplebamosileba ganatsilda parlamentze, mtavrobasa da saprokuroro sabchoze; mtavar prokurors   tslis vadit irchevs parlamenti; gadaidga mnishvnelovani nabijebi prokurorebis damoukideblobis ganmtkitsebis, gavrtselebul dana­shaulta tsinaaghmdeg epektiani brdzolis, tana­ mshromelta kvalipikatsiis amaghlebis, sagamodziebo da saprokuroro sakmianobis khariskhis gaumjobesebis mimartulebit. uzrunvelqopil ikna shinagan sakmeta sami­ nistros depolitizatsia, romelits tsina kheli­ suplebis pirobebshi, adamianebis devnisa da dashinebis ert-ert mdzlavr iaraghad gamoiqeneboda. shinagan sakmeta saministroshi gankhortsielebuli repormis shedegad, represiaze orientirebuli politsiuri sistema gardaikmna preventsiaze orientirebul sistemad, romlis umtavres punktsiad danashaulis tavidan atsileba da mosakhleobistvis sachiro momsakhurebis mitsodeba ganisazghvra ganakhlda politsiis sakmianobis maregulirebeli sakanonmdeblo baza; gankhortsielda tsentraluri kriminaluri politsiis departamentis modernizatsia; mnishvnelovnad gapartovda saertashoriso sapolitsio tanamsh­romlobis masshtabebi organizebuli danashaulis tsinaaghmdeg brdzolis speroshi; daitsqo sasazghvro politsiis modernizatsiis, standartizatsiis da unipikatsiis masshtaburi programa; dainerga personalur monatsemta datsvis maghali standarti; gaaktiurda tanamshromloba evropoltan; gankhortsielda  -ze meti inprastrukturuli proekti da ganakhlda materialur-teknikuri baza; sheikmna migratsiis martvis samsakhuri da ashenda migrantta droebiti gantavsebis tanamedrove tsentri; gaumjobesda politsielta sotsialuri datsvis garantiebi. gatarebuli repormebis shedegad, politsiis momsakhurebis sandoobis komponentshi, msoplio ekonomikuri porumis  -  tslebis globaluri konkurentunarianobis indeksis mikhedvit, sakartvelos mdgomareoba  -  tslebis angarishtan shedarebit,   pozitsiit gaumjobesda da me-  adgilit ganisazghvra; organizebuli danashaulis komponentshi, amave indeksis mikhedvit, sakartvelos mdgomareoba  -  tslebis angarishtan shedarebit,   pozitsiit gaumjobesda da 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 prokuratura kvlavats ipunktsionirebs rogorts sazogadoebis interesebsa da sachiroebebze orientirebuli sistema, rats braldebulta da protsesis monatsile skhva mkhareta uplebebis maksimalur datsvas uzrunvelqops. danashaultan brdzolis speroshi shemushavdeba akhali midgomebi, daikhvetseba da evropul standartebtan kidev upro daakhlovdeba arsebuli sagamodziebo da saprokuroro praktika. gaizrdeba sazogadoebis chartuloba danashaulis preventsiis uzrunvelqopis protsesshi. rigiti prokuroris damoukideblobis uzrunvelqopis miznit, daikhvetseba prokurorta tanamdebobaze danishvnis, distsiplinuri pasukhis­ mgeblobis, gatavisuplebisa da tsakhalisebis (m.sh. datsinaurebis) sistema; shemushavdeba prokurorta sakmianobis gamchvirvale da miukerdzoebeli shepasebis kriteriumebi; gagrdzeldeba prokurorta gadamzadebisa da kvalipikatsiis amaghlebis programebi. shinagan sakmeta saministros sistemashi dana­ shaulis tsinaaghmdeg brdzolisa da sapolitsio sakmianobis maksimaluri epektianobistvis, dainergeba analizze dapudznebuli politsiis sistema, rats uzrunvelqops ghia da dakhuruli tsqaroebidan mighebuli inpormatsiis damushavebas, saprtkheebis identipitsirebas da matze droul reagirebas; politsiis sandoobisa da saimedoobis gazrdisatvis uzrunvelqopili ikneba sazogadoebis chartva usaprtkhoebasa da martltsesrigtan dakavshirebuli problemebis identipitsirebasa da gadatsqvetashi, agretve gadzlierdeba arasamtavrobo organizatsiebtan, sametsniero tsreebtan, mediastan da biznessektortan mudmivi komunikatsiis mekanizmebi; gagrdzeldeba kriminaluri politsiis modernizatsia kveqnis masshtabit, ris shedegadats mnishvnelovnad gaizrdeba gamodziebis khariskhi da shesadzleblobebi; gankhortsieldeba sagzao modzraobis usaprtkhoebis programa, romelits kveitta, mgzavrebis da mdzgholebis usaprtkhoebis amaghlebas moemsakhureba da gzebze sikvdilianobas sheamtsirebs; dagegmil vadebshi dasruldeba sazghvris martvis sistemis reporma, rats uzrunvelqops sasazghvro politsiis modernizatsias, standartizatsiasa da unipikatsias; dasruldeba sagangebo situatsiebis martvis ertiani sistemis chamoqalibeba, rats uzrunvelqops kmedit koordinatsias da stsrap reagirebas; gansakutrebuli quradgheba daetmoba aralegalur migratsias da mastan dakavshirebuli riskebis martvas, am kutkhit saministros shesadzleblobebis ganvitarebas da skhva utsqebebtan koordinatsiis amaghlebas; gaghrmavdeba tanamshromloba saertashoriso sapolitsio strukturebtan, gansakutrebit ki evropoltan; politsiis sistemis gamartuli punktsionirebis uzrunvelsaqopad, chamoqalibdeba adamianuri resursebis martvis kmediti sistema, rata karieruli tsinsvla daepudznos obiektur kriteriumebs, damsakhurebasa da kvalipikatsias; mnishvnelovani investitsia gankhortsieldeba shss akademiashi: dainergeba akhali programebi, ganakhldeba teknologiebi, akademiis bazaze sheikmneba politsiis saertashoriso sastsavlo tsentri; 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 demokratiuli ganvitareba politsiis sazogadoebastan daakhloebis kutkhit gagrdzeldeba politsiis repormireba imgvarad, rom sistema maksimalurad moemsakhuros sazogadoebastan tanamshromlobis mizans. uzrunvelqopili ikneba sakhelmtsipo usaprt­ samsakhuris damoukidebeli da kmediti sakmianoba da misi resursebis shemdgomi gadzliereba. khoebis 
 garantirebuli ikneba sakhalkho damtsvelis damou­kidebloba, misi aktiuri tanamshromloba sakartvelos parlamenttan da skhva sajaro struk­ turebtan.  . . mmartvelobis sistema, politikuri sistema da samokalako sazogadoeba   tslidan pundamenturi tsvlilebebi gankhortsielda khelisuplebis danatsilebis, teri­ toriuli martvisa da sajaro samsakhuris sistemebis gadzlierebis, agretve politikuri sistemisa da samokalako sektoris gajansaghebis tvalsazrisit. aghdga darghveuli balansi khelisuplebis sakanon­mdeblo, aghmasrulebel da sasamartlo shtoebs shoris da chamoqalibda khelisuplebis danatsilebis demokratiuli sistema. tvisebrivad gadzlierda sakartvelos parlamentis roli sakhelmtsipo mmartvelobis sistemashi - parlamentma realurad daitsqo konstitutsiit gatvalistsinebuli makontrolebeli punktsiis gankhortsieleba; uzrunvelqopil ikna sasamartlo sistemis damoukidebloba aghmasrulebeli khelisuplebisgan. khelisuplebis artserti shto ar sargeblobs sheuzghudavi da daubalansebeli dzalauplebit, rats uzrunvelqops sakhelmtsipos martvas demokratiuli standartebis shesabamisad. mnishvnelovani repormebi gatarda teritoriuli martvis sistemis gasaumjobeseblad. gadzlierda adgilobrivi tvitmmartvelobis sistema shemoghebul ikna gamgeblebisa da merebis pirdapiri archevis tsesi; munitsipalitetis sabiujeto shemosavlis damatebit tsqarod ganisazghvra metsarme pizikuri pirebis sashemosavlo gadasakhadi, ris shedegadats gaizarda munitsipalitetebis sakutari shemosulobebis khvedriti tsili mat saerto sabiujeto shemosulobebshi; transperis akhali sakhis - kapitaluri transperis shemoghebis sapudzvelze, munitsipalitetebs mietsat shesadzlebloba, sakhelmtsipo biujetidan konkurentul satsqisebze miighon damatebiti sakhsrebi sakutar uplebamosilebebshi shemavali kapitaluri proek­ tebis gansakhortsieleblad; daitsqo dagegmvis sashualovadiani da grdzelvadiani dokumentebis momzadeba da migheba; dasakhlebis saerto krebebisa da samokalako mrchevelta sabchoebis shemoghebit, gadaidga mnishvnelovani nabiji adgilobrivi tvitmmartvelobis gankhortsielebashi mokalaketa chartulobis gasaumjobeseblad. gadaidga 
 mnishvnelovani nabijebi sajaro sistemashi arsebuli naklovanebebis aghmosa­pkhvrelad. tvisebrivad amaghlda sajaro samsakhuris stabilurobisa da apolitikurobis khariskhi. pirvelad damoukideblobis aghdgenis samsakhuris 
 shemdeg, shemoghebulikna sajaro mokheleta konkursis gzit danishvnis savaldebulo tsesi.   tsels khelisuplebam miigho gadatsqvetileba sajaro samsakhurshi dzireuli repormebis gatarebis shesakheb. shedegad,   tsels sakartvelos parlamentma miigho „sajaro samsakhuris shesakheb“ akhali kanoni, romelits   tslidan amokmeddeba da shekmnis satanado samartlebriv sapudzvlebs sajaro samsakhuris repormis sisruleshi mosaqvanad da „kargi mmartvelobis“ printsipebis dasanergad. sakartvelo gadavida antikoruptsiuli politikis akhal etapze, aktiurad mushaobs koruptsiastan brdzolis preventsiuli mekanizmebi. utsqebatashorisi koordinatsiis gadzlierebis miznit, sheikmna antikoruptsiuli sabcho. pirvelad ikna shemoghebuli tanamdebobis piris konebrivi mdgomareobis deklaratsiis gadamotsmebis samartlebrivi charcho, romelits sajaro samsakhurshi koruptsiisa da interesta sheutavseblobis sakitkhebs mkatsrad gaakontrolebs da koruptsiastan brdzolis sistemur instituts shekmnis. koruptsiis tsinaaghmdeg brdzolis preventsiuli mekanizmis gasadzliereblad, shemushavda etikisa da ktsevis zogadi tsesebis ertiani dokumenti qvela sajaro datsesebulebisatvis, romelits   tslidan amokmeddeba. gatarebuli repormebis shedegad, msoplio martlmsajulebis proektis „kanonis uzenaesobis indeksis“   tslis monatsemebit, sakartvelo pirvel adgilzea koruptsiis dabali machveneblit aghmosavlet evropisa da tsentraluri aziis regionis   kveqanas shoris. gaumjobesda servisebis mitsodebis protsesi. progresulad vitardeba elektronuli momsakhureba. „iustitsiis sakhlis“ el-momsakhurebis gverdis meshveobit, shesadzlebeli gakhda  -mde momsakhurebis elektronulad migheba. elektronuli mtavrobis ganvitarebam kheli sheutsqo aseve gamchvirvale da ghia mmartvelobis gaumjobesebas. sakhelmtsipo datsesebulebebi sul upro aktiurad iqeneben elektronul veb-gverdebs sajaro inpormatsiis sazogadoebisatvis khelmisatsvdomobis uzrunvelsaqopad. gadaidga mnishvnelovani nabijebi politikuri stabilizatsiis mimartulebit. poli­ tikur spektrshi jer kidev maghalia polarizatsiisa da radikalizatsiis khariskhi, rasats politikuri partiebisa da mattan dakavshirebuli media­ sashualebebis ritorika da politikur diskusiebshi sidzulvilis enis partod gamoqeneba utsqobs khels. kanonmdebloba sheitsavs mtel rig kharvezebs, mat shoris normebs, romlebits piktiuri blokebis shekmnisa da privilegiebis skhvadaskhva archevnebtan dakavshirebis gzit, partiebs privilegiebis usamartlod mitvisebis shesadzleblobas adzlevs. qovelive es dabrkolebas ukmnis partiuli sistemis institutsionalizatsias. aghnishnuli problemebi aris im arademokratiuli politikuri garemos shedegi, romelits sakartveloshi   tslamde iqo chamoqalibebuli. politikuri sistemis saerto demokratizatsia, archevnebis demokratiuli printsipebis shesabamisad chatareba da politikuri partiebis maregulirebeli kanonmdeblobis dakhvetsa uzrunvelqops politikashi radikalizmis sistemis 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 demokratiuli ganvitareba shemtsirebas da daachkarebs partiuli sistemis institutsionalizatsiis protsess.  -  tslebshi, politikuri sistemis gasajansagheblad, daikhvetsa kanonmdebloba politikuri partiebis shesakheb - gaukmda represiuli normebi, romlebits   tslebshi opozitsiuri partiebis mkhardamcherebis shevitsroebis miznit gamoiqeneboda; iuridiul pirebs mienichat partiebis dapinansebis upleba; partiebis shemomtsirvelebisa da mati pinansebis shesakheb inpormatsiis gamotkhova shesadzlebeli gakhda mkholod sasamartlos meshveobit;  %-dan  %-mde shemtsirda partiis mier sakhelmtsipo biujetidan dapinansebis misaghebad dadgenili barieri.   tslis shemdeg sakartveloshi tvisebrivad sheitsvala saarchevno garemo. aghikveta archevnebis gaqalbebis praktika. saertashoriso tanamegobrobis saqoveltao shepasebit,   da   tslebis archevnebi demokratiuli printsipebis sruli datsvit chatarda. gadaisinja saarchevno olkebis sazghvrebi, ris sapudzvelzets pirvelad damoukideblobis aghdgenis shemdeg, saparlamento archevnebi sakartveloshi khmata tanastsorobis printsipis sruli datsvit chatardeba. mazhoritari deputatebis archevnebistvis datsesda  %-iani barieri, ritats amaghlda mati legitimatsiis khariskhi. archevnebis samartlianobis printsipis uzrunvelqopis miznit, gadaisinja „sakartvelos saarchevno kodeksis“ mteli rigi normebi - daikhvetsa kenchisqris dghis protsedurebi, kenchisqris shenobashi, otakhebsa da mimdebare teritoriaze tsesrigis datsvis normebi; sheizghuda spetsialuri ubnebis shekmna, kholo shss-s spetsialuri ubnebi mtlianad gaukmda; saarchevno siis dazustebisatvis autsilebeli printsipis − „erti adamiani − erti dokumenti“ uzrunvelsaqopad, ori tslis ganmavlobashi gaitsa milionze meti akhali piradobis motsmoba da a.sh. administratsiuli resursi, mat shoris dzalovani strukturebi, aghar gamoiqeneba amomrchevelze zetsolis sashualebad. adamianebs, mat shoris biznesmenebs, aghar akvt opozitsiuri partiebis mkhardacheris, agretve mat mplobelobashi arsebul mediasashualebebshi reklamis gantavsebis shishi. sagrdznoblad amaghlda sazogadoebis ndoba saarchevno administratsiis mimart. mnishvnelovnad amaghlda samokalako sektoris aktiurobis, agretve sajaro gadatsqvetilebata dagegmvisa da mighebis protsesshi misi chartulobis khariskhi. arasamtavrobo organizatsiebi akhortsieleben kmedit kontrols khelisuplebis sakmianobaze. khelisupleba ganakhortsielebs kmedit da samart­ lian politikas, rata uzrunvelqopili iqos mmartvelobis sistemis, politikuri sistemisa da samokalako sazogadoebis shemdgomi gadzliereba. politikuri partiebis, samokalako sektoris tsarmomadgenlebisa da ekspertebis satanado chartulobit, shemushavdeba konstitutsiuri kanonis proekti, romlis sapudzvelze sakartvelos konstitutsia srul shesabamisobashi ikneba moqvanili konstitutsionalizmis printsipebtan. konstitutsiis akhali redaktsia daepudzneba khelisuplebis 
 danatsilebis printsips da uzrunvelqops jerovani 
 balansis datsvas khelisuplebis sakanonmdeblo, aghmasrulebel da sasamartlo shtoebs shoris. daikhvetseba 
 mar­­tvis sistema: 
 administratsiul-teritoriuli 
 - sakonstitutsio repormis parglebshi, gadaisinjeba regionuli martvis sistema; - gadzlierdeba adgilobrivi tvitmmartveloba. subsidiarobis printsipis sapudzvelze gaizrdeba munitsipalitetebis uplebamosilebebi, romelta gankhortsieleba sotsialur– ekonomikuri ganvitarebis dagegmvis utsqvet da tanmimdevrul protsess daepudzneba. piskaluri detsentralizatsiis, agretve munitsipalitetebis uplebamosilebebsa da resursebs shoris shesabamisobis uzrunvelsaqopad, etapobrivad gaizrdeba adgilobrivi biujetebis shemosavlebis khvedriti tsili naerti biujetis shemosavlebshi; gadzlierdeba adgilobrivi tvitmmartvelobis gankhortsielebashi mokalaketa monatsileobis uzrunvelqopis mekanizmebi; sazogadoebrivi momsakhurebis khariskhis gaumjobesebisa da khelmisatsvdomobis uzrunvelsaqopad satanadod aghichurveba munitsipalitetebis teritoriuli organoebi; etapobrivad, mteli kveqnis mas­ shtabit gapartovdeba „sazogadoebrivi tsen­ trebis“ arsebuli praktika, romlis meshveobit gankhortsieldeba sakhelmtsipo da adgilobrivi sazogadoebrivi momsakhurebebis mitsodeba qovel dasakhlebashi, mmartvelobis organoebsa da mokalakeebs shoris pizikuri mandzilis miukhedavad. daikhvetseba sajaro samsakhuris sistema: - etapobrivad, chamoqalibdeba sajaro samsakhuris karieruli modeli, romelits uzrunvelqops mokheleta samsakhurshi aqvanas da karierul tsinsvlas obiekturi kriteriumebis shesabamisad; mkapiod motsesrigdeba mokheleebze premiebisa da danamatebis gatsemis, agretve mat mier sajaro resursit sargeblobis tsesi; - administratsiuli resursis shemtsirebis miznit, sajaro datsesebulebata mimdinare punktsiurinstitutsiuri analizis shedegebis ganzogadebis sapudzvelze, gankhortsieldeba charbi sajaro datsesebulebebis da datsesebulebebs shoris punktsiata gadaparvis identipitsireba; - uzrunvelqopili ikneba koruptsiis tsinaaghmdeg brdzolis kutkhit gadadgmuli nabijebis kmediti koo­rdinatsia, samokalako sazogadoebis char­ tu­lobis uzrunvelqopa, am mimartulebit ganatlebisa da sazogadoebis inpormirebulobis donis gazrda, antikoruptsiuli mekanizmebis danergva da gadzliereba. dainergeba konebrivi mdgomareobis deklaratsiebis monitoringis sis­ tema, rats khels sheutsqobs srulqopil monitorings, kerdzod deklaratsiebshi tsarmodgenili inpo­ rmatsiis sistsoris dadgenas; - daikhvetseba sajaro inpormatsiis khelmisatsvdomobis 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 demokratiuli ganvitareba maregulirebeli normebi da shemushavdeba kanoni inpormatsiis tavisuplebis shesakheb, rats uzrunvelqops inpormatsiis tavisuplebaze tsalkeul aktebshi gabneuli normebis konsolidirebas da sakanonmdeblo kharvezebis aghmopkhvras; kidev upro motsesrigdeba sajaro inpormatsiis gatsemis arsebuli praktika; - sheikmneba mtavrobis ertiani „pront (biznes) opisi“, sadats qvela sachiro sakhelmtsipo utsqeba kerdzo bizness erti panjris printsipit moemsakhureba; mokhdeba mtavrobis gadatsqvetilebebis mighebis drois reglamentireba. am miznit, mtavrobis administratsiashi sheikmneba strukturuli erteuli, romelits ganakhortsielebs mtavrobis tsevrta mier gadatsqvetilebis mighebis khangrdzlivobis, mushaobis protsesshi sazogadoebis chartulobisa da sakmianobis epektianobis monitorings utsqebebs shoris uketesi komunikatsiisa da epektiani mmartvelobis uzrunvelsaqopad. politikuri sistemis ganvitarebisa da partiuli sistemis institutsionalizatsiis khelshetsqobis miznit, 
 „kartuli otsneba“ uzrunvelqops politikuri partiebisa da archevnebis maregulirebeli kanonmdeblobis shemdgom dakhvetsas. sakonstitutsio repormis parglebshi, gadaisinjeba saarchevno sistema. politikur dzalebtan konsultatsiis sapudzvelze, daikhvetseba partiebis dapinansebisa da mati sakmianobis gamchvirvalobis uzrunvelqopis sakanonmdeblo mekanizmebi. „kartuli otsneba“ tavisi sakmianobit khels sheutsqobs sakartveloshi politikuri kulturis ganvitarebas da politikashi radikalizmis aghmopkhvras. „kartuli otsneba“ pasukhismgeblobas ighebs mom­ devno adgilobrivi, saprezidento da saparlamento archevnebis tavisupal, samartlian da mshvidobian garemoshi chatarebaze. „kartuli otsneba“ khels sheutsqobs sakartveloshi sektoris shemdgom ganvitarebas, samokalako kulturis amaghlebas da samokalako sazogadoebis tsarmomadgenlebis parto chartulobas sajaro gadatsqvetilebata mighebis protsesshi. samokalako 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 ekonomikuri ganvitareba  . ekonomikuri ganvitareba „kartul otsnebas“ akvs mkapio ekonomikuri khedva da konkretuli gegma, tu rogor unda ganvitardes sakartvelos ekonomika shemdgomi   tslis ganmavlobashi da rogor unda gamqardes grdzelvadiani mdgradi ganvitarebis sapudzveli. tsina khelisuplebebma ver uzrunvelqves kartuli ekonomikis pundamenturi gardakmna. kveqnis ekonomikuri ganvitarebis modeli ar itvalistsinebda grdzelvadiani ganvitarebis sapudzvlebis shekmnas. qovelive amas daemata tsina khelisuplebis dzaladobrivi metodebi da ekonomikis saqrdeni mtavari ghirebulebis - sakutrebis uplebis sruli ugulvebelqopa, ritats ekonomikam sabolood daitsqo chikhshi shesvla, sotsialuri garemo ki tslidan tslamde mdzimdeboda. „kartulma otsnebam“ shedzlo ekonomikis realuri gajansaghebis relsebze gadaqvana. sakhelisuplebo tsnekhis mokhsnit, sakutrebis uplebis ganukhreli datsvita da metsarmeobis khelshetsqobis mekanizmebis gamoqenebit, daitsqo stsrapi ekonomikuri ganvitarebis pundamentis mshenebloba. es protsesi sheuktsevadi gakhdeba, ristvisats „kartul otsnebas“ shemushavebuli akvs khedva da ganvitarebis gegma, romelits ekonomikuri ganvitarebis akhali etapis datsqebas guliskhmobs da romlis saboloo mizani mosakhleobis ketildgheobis donis amaghleba, sigharibis dadzleva da sakartvelos maghalshemosavliani kveqnebis rigshi chaqenebaa. „kartuli otsnebis“ ekonomikuri khedvit, kveqnis ekonomikuri ganvitareba unda epudznebodes tavisupali bazris printsipebs, romelits kerdzo sektoris gadzlierebis tsinapirobaa. chveni ekonomikuri politika, erti mkhriv, mimartuli ikneba kerdzo sektoris shemdgomi ganvitarebisken da kerdzo sektorshi arsebuli problemebis gadachrisken, rats khels sheutsqobs kveqanashi khelsaqreli da saimedo biznesgaremos chamoqalibebas, kholo, meore mkhriv, kveqnis ekonomikuri ganvitarebis sasurveli donis mightsevamde, uzrunvelqops mosakhleobis im penebis mkhardacheras, romlebits amas qvelaze metad sachiroeben. inkluziuri ekonomikuri zrda aris mtavrobis ekonomikuri politikis prioriteti. mdgradi ekonomikuri ganvitarebisatvis autsilebelia iseti modelis danergva, romlis pirobebshi, ekonomikuri zrdis paralelurad, mtsirdeba sigharibe da umushevroba mosakhleobashi. mtavrobis ekonomikuri politika, ekonomikur epekturobastan ertad, ikhelmdzghvanelebs sotsialuri usaprtkhoebis da samartlianobis printsipebit. dasakmebis shesadzleblobebis zrda, ganatlebis, jandatsvis da sotsialuri uzrunvelqopis sistemebis inkluziurobaze orientatsia am printsipebis ganmakhortsielebeli instrumentebia. grdzelvadiani ekonomikuri zrdis uzrunvelsaqopad, „kartuli otsnebis“ ekonomikuri politikis mizania ekonomikis paktorebis maksimaluri chartva kveqnis ganvitarebashi. am miznit shemushavebulia  -punktiani gegma, romelits mimartulia biznesis, rogorts ekonomikuri zrdis 
 mtavari mamodzraveblis ganvitarebaze, adamianuri resursebis potentsialis maksimalurad chartvaze kveqnis ganvitarebashi, inprastrukturis stsrap ganvitarebasa da ghia mmartvelobis printsipebis danergvaze.  . . makroekonomikuri stabiluroba chveni ekonomikuri politika epudzneba makro­ ekonomikuri stabilurobis, rogorts ekonomikuri ganvitarebis pundamentis, printsipebisadmi ert­ gulebas. piskaluri distsiplina, umushevrobis dabali done da pasebis stabiluroba, monetaruli politikis damoukidebloba, mimdinare angarishis depitsitis tandatanobiti shemtsireba da pinansuri sektoris stabilurobis shenarchuneba kveqnis grdzelvadiani ekonomikuri zrdis mnishvnelovani paktorebia. sakartvelo aris mtsire, ghia ekonomikis kveqana. shesabamisad, is ver ikneba izolirebuli regionsa da globalur ekonomikashi mimdinare movlenebisagan. tumtsa, stabiluri makroekonomikuri garemo mnish­ vnelovania negatiuri sagareo shokebis zemokmedebis sherbilebisatvis. bolo periodshi regionshi tsarmokmnilma shokebma da msoplioshi ekonomikuri zrdis tempebis shesustebam mnishvnelovani uarqopiti gavlena ikonia sakartvelos ekonomikaze. tumtsa, sakartvelom sheinarchuna regionshi gamorcheuli ekonomikuri zrdis machvenebeli. mnishvnelovania is garemoebats, rom sagareo shokebi ar gadaizarda inplatsiashi da pasebis stabiluroba shenarchunda. tsina khelisuplebisgan memkvidreobad mivighet dolarizatsiis maghali machvenebeli. gasul periodshi ganvitarebulma movlenebma tskhadqo, rom gatsemuli seskhebis dolarizatsiis maghali machvenebeli kveqnis ekonomikis mnishvnelovani problemaa, mosakhleobas mdzime tvirtad atsveba da imavdroulad, zghudavs ekonomikuri politikis instrumentebis epektianobas. „kartuli otsneba“ srulad atsnobierebs makro­ ekonomikuri stabilurobisa da sabiujeto protsesis epektianad tsarmartvis mnishvnelobas, ristvisats: - gagrdzeldeba kharjebis optimizatsiis utsqveti protsesi, rats mimartuli ikneba sakhsrebis gamotavisuplebaze da mat gadanatsilebaze prio­ ritetuli mimartulebebit. amastan, sheizghudeba administratsiuli kharjebis zrda; - sakhelmtsipo vali mtlian shida produkttan mimartebashi shenarchundeba im doneze, rome­ lits kveqnis stabilur sakredito reitings da dadebit sainvestitsio imijs uzrunvelqops; - ar gadzlierdeba sakhelmtsipos tsnekhi ekono­ mikaze; 
 - gaizrdeba biujetis gamchvirvaloba; - uzrunvelqopili ikneba programuli biujetis printsipebis srulqopa; 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 ekonomikuri ganvitareba - erovnuli bankis khelshe­ukhebeli; 
 damoukidebloba ikneba 
 - uzrunvelqopili ikneba piskaluri da moneta­ ruli politikis epektiani koordinatsia; - kheli sheetsqoba larshi dakreditebis zrdas.  . . dasakmeba „kartuli otsnebis“ ekonomikuri politikis erterti mtavari orientiri mosakhleobis dasakmebaa. arastsori politikis gamo, tsina khelisuplebam kveqana   atasi umushevrit chaibara da mmartveloba   atasi umushevrit daasrula, umushevrobis done ki  , %-dan  %-mde gaizarda. „kartuli otsnebis“ khelisuplebashi mosvlis shemdeg, aktsenti tsarmoebis ganvitarebaze gaketda. metsarmeobis khelshetsqobis programebis amokmedebit, gaikhsna da gapartovda asobit satsarmo, rats dasakmebis machvenebelze dadebitad aisakha.   tslis shemdeg, dasakmebulta raodenoba   atasit gaizarda, kholo umushevrobis done  %-dan  %mde shemtsirda. amastan, dasakmebis machvenebeli, dziritadad, kerdzo sektoris kharjze gaizarda. tu  -  tslebshi dasakmebulta saerto raodenobis  %-s sakhelmtsipo sektori sheadgenda,   tslidan es machvenebeli  %-mde shemtsirda. aghsanishnavia, rom gaizarda dakiravebit dasakmebulta raodenoba, kholo tvitdasakmebulebis shemtsirda - tvitdasakmebulebi dakiravebit dasakmebulta kategoriashi gadadian. msoplio ekonomikuri porumis  -  tslebis globaluri konkurentunarianobis angarishis mikhedvit, biznesis ketebis mkhriv, upirvelesi problema kvlav kvalipitsiuri samushao dzalis naklebobaa. amave dros, umushevroba rcheba mtsvave problemad. es situatsia natlad miutitebs shromis bazarze arsebul disbalansze. erti mkhriv, arsebobs motkhovna kerdzo sektoris mkhridan, tumtsa, es motkhovna ver kmaqopildeba im samushao dzalit, romelits shromis bazarzea tsarmodgenili. aghnishnuli disbalansis aghmosapkhvrelad da dasakmebis raodenobrivi da khariskhobrivi mach­ veneblis gasaumjobeseblad, „kartuli otsneba“ gegmavs shemdeg ghonisdziebebs: - gatardeba 
 ganatlebis reporma da pro­ pesiuli ganatlebis sistema ganvitardeba 
 dualuri (germanuli) modelis shesabamisad, romelits guliskhmobs damsakmeblis chartvas saganmanatleblo protsesshi. shedegad, gaizrdeba studentebis da momavali dasakmebulebis shromis bazrisatvis mzaobis khariskhi; - gankhortsieldeba shromis bazris motkhovnebis pundamenturi shestsavla da umaghlesi ganatleba daepudzneba ara asimetriul motkhovnas, rome­lits ramdenime dominirebuli propesiit shemoipargleba, aramed realur sachiroebebs, romlis tsinashets kveqana dgas. es ar sheekheba pundamentur da humanitarul metsnierebebs. shesabamisad, uzrunvelqopili ikneba shromis 
 bazarze arsebuli disbalansis aghmopkhvra; - „kartuli otsneba“ sheimushavebs kveqnis indus­ triuli ganvitarebis dokuments, romelits guliskhmobs ekonomikis zrdis mkhardamcheri akhali politikis shemushavebas. aghnishnuli dokumenti sapudzvlad daedeba ghonisdziebebs, romelits sakhelmtsipom unda gaataros kveqnis ekonomikuri zrdis dachkarebis da akhali samushao adgilebis shekmnis miznit; - „kartuli otsneba“ shemdgomi   tslis ganmavlobashi ganakhortsielebs dzireul repormebs, romlebits uzrunvelqops ekonomikis stsrap ganvitarebas da titoeuli ojakhis ketildgheobis amaghlebas   atasi akhali samushao adgilis shekmnit. es ikneba umushevrobis mkvetri shemtsirebisaken gadadgmuli mnishvnelovani nabiji: • mogebis gadasakhadis repormis shedegad, bizness gauchndeba meti shesadzlebloba, gaapartoos sakutari sakmianoba da damatebit shekmnas     samushao adgili; • biznesis mkhardamcheri sakhelmtsipo programebis gagrdzelebisa da akhali komponentebis damatebis shedegad, dasakmdeba     adamiani; • inprastrukturuli proektebis, avtobanis, shida saavtomobilo gzebis masshtaburi msheneblobis proektis gankhortsielebis shedegad, gachndeba damatebit     samushao adgili; • dagrovebiti sapensio sistemis amokmedebit shekmnili pinansuri resursis investitsiis shedegad sheikmneba damatebit     samushao adgili; • turizmis, turistuli momsakhurebis da turistuli inprastrukturis khelshemtsqobi ghonisdziebebis shedegad, am sektorshi damatebit sheikmneba     samushao adgili.  . . biznesgaremo   tslis shemdeg, sakartvelom ganitsada mnishvnelovani tsinsvla biznesgaremos gaumjo­ besebisa da tvalsazrisit. 
 metsarmeobis 
 khelshetsqobis 
 tsina khelisuplebis pirobebshi, chamoqalibda biznesze zetsolis totaluri praktika, gamartivebuli pormaluri administratsiuli protsedurebis mighma, ugulvebelqopili iqo biznesis ketebis qvela pundamenturi printsipi. sakutrebis uple­bis datsvis kutkhit, vitareba qoveltsliurad uaresdeboda da   tsels sakartvelo globaluri konkurentunarianobis reitingshi  -e adgils ikavebda. khelisuplebashi „kartuli otsnebis“ mosvlis shemdeg, damkvidrda sakutrebis uplebis ganukhreli datsvis printsipi. shedegad, kveqanam upretsedento tsinsvla ganitsada da reitingshi  -e adgilidan  -e adgilze gadainatsvla. aktiurad daitsqo metsarmeobis mkhardacheris miz­nobrivi programebis gankhortsieleba. sheikmna metsarmeobis ganvitarebis programa - „atsarmoe sakartveloshi“. programis parglebshi, bizness gauchnda realuri shesadzlebloba, isargeblos  - %- 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 ekonomikuri ganvitareba iani seskhit, rats upretsedento movlenaa kartul realobashi. mikro da mtsire biznesis khelshetsqobis miznit, programas daemata akhali komponenti  - -lariani grantebis programa, romlis parglebshi regionebshi pinansdeba biznesinitsiativebi. programis - „atsarmoe sakartveloshi“ parglebshi, sul dapinansda   akhali satsarmo, gaitsa   milion larze meti motsulobis sheghavatiani seskhi ekonomikis realur sektorshi, gankhortsielda   milionamde laris investitsia.   tslis shemdeg, mnishvnelovani tsinsvla dapiksirda inovatsiebisa da teknologiebis ganvitarebis mimartulebit, sadats   tslamde, globaluri konkurentunarianobis reitingis mikhedvit, mkvetri ukusvla aghinishneboda. sheikmna inovatsiebis da teknologiebis saagento, romelits monatsileobs kerdzo da sakhelmtsipo sektoris mier tsodnis, inovatsiebis da kvlevis shedegebis komertsializatsiasa da inovatsiuri metsarmeobis khelshetsqobashi. ashenda pirveli teknoparki sakartveloshi, romelits uzrunvelqops tsvdomas skhvadaskhva tipis maghalteknologiur danadgarebsa da servisebze. moetsqo dargobrivi samretsvelo inovatsiebis laboratoriebi - pablabebi. kveqanashi udides problemad iqo ktseuli venchoruli kapitalis ararseboba da startapebis dapinansebis mtsiri praktika. am mimartulebit, chvenma khelisuplebam gadadga upretsedento nabiji da daitsqo inovatsiuri biznesis khelshetsqobis programa ”startap sakartvelo”. proektis parglebshi, benepitsiarebs edzlevat sashualeba, biznesideis gansakhortsieleblad moipovon  -dan   laramde dapinanseba. maghalteknologiuri ideis avtorebs akvt unikaluri shesadzlebloba, mati ideebi ganikhilon da sheapason ashsh-dan, „silikonvelidan“ motsveulma maghalkvalipitsiurma spetsialistebma. „startap sakartvelos“ ukve akvs khelshesakhebi shedegebi. maghalteknologiuri ideebis konkursshi gaimarjva otsma benepitsiarma, romelta proektebs msoplios tsamqvanma ekspertebma dadebiti sheapaseba mistses. programis parglebshi, benepitsiarebs mietsat shansi, daipqron teknologiuri biznesis mtsvervalebi. maghalteknologiuri dargis startapebi moitsavs iset speroebs, rogoritsaa: aviakosmosuri tsarmoeba, avtomobilebi, khelovnuri intelekti, bioteknologiebi, bioinpormatika, kompiuteruli inzhineria, kompiuteruli metsniereba, inpormatsiuli teknologiebi, nanoteknologiebi, birtvuli pizika, elektromagnituri gamoskhiveba, robotika, nakhevargamtarebi da telekomunikatsia. „startap sakartvelo“ „kartuli otsnebis“ ert-erti umnishvnelovanesi mightsevaa. kveqanashi inovatsiuri da sitsotskhlisunariani biznesideebi dapinansebis gareshe aghar darcheba. khelisuplebam daitsqo tslebis ganmavlobashi bizne­ sistvis ert-ert umtavres problemad ktseuli sagadasakhado administrirebis reporma, rome­ lits tsina khelisuplebis mier biznesze zetsolis instrumentad gamoiqeneboda. samartliani sagada­ sakhado garemos shekmnis miznit, gankhortsielda 
 araerti sakanonmdeblo tsvlileba, mat shoris: sagadasakhado davalianebis idzulebiti gadakhdevineba daitsqeba mkholod sagadasakhado davis dasrulebis shemdeg; sagadasakhado shemotsmebis da gadasakhadis daritskhvis  -tsliani khandazmulobis vada shemtsirda   tslamde; sagadasakhado davis periodshi piris sabanko angarishze qadaghis dadeba mokhdeba mkholod sasamartlos tankhmobit; sagadasakhado shemotsmebas ganakhortsielebs mkholod sagadasakhado organo; gankhortsielda mogebis gadasakhadis reporma, rats   tslidan gaunatsilebel mogebaze gadasakhadis gaukmebas guliskhmobs; sakartveloshi tsarmoebuli soplis meurneobis produktsiis pirveladi mitsodeba gatavisuplda dghg-sgan, chatvlis uplebit; datsesda sagadasakhado sheghavatebi metsarmeebisatvis, romlebits sakmianoben maghalmtian regionshi; dabalshemosavliani pirebisatvis gapartovda sagadasakhado sheghavatebis areali da datsesda akhali sheghavatebi; mnishvnelovnad shemtsirda sagadasakhado jarimebis da sauravis odenobebi; gadamkhdelebs, romeltats bolo tslebshi aktivoba ar upiksirdebat, ukve chamoetserat   miliard larze metis odenobis sagadasakhado davalianeba. „kartuli otsneba“ biznesgaremos shemdgomi gaumjobesebisa da metsarmeobis khelshetsqobis miznit gaagrdzelebs aktiuri politikis gatarebas: - datsuli ikneba sakutrebis uplebis khelshe­ uvalobis printsipi - „kartuli otsneba“ rcheba aghnishnuli printsipis ertguli da aravis moutsevs sakutrebaze uaris tkma sakhelmtsipos mkhridan motquebis, idzulebis, mukaris, shantazhis tu dzalauplebis borotad gamoqenebis gamo; - uzrunvelqopili 
 ikneba sargebloba 
 sakutrebit 
 - amokmeddeba udzrav nivtze sakutrebis khelqopis an skhvagvari khelsheshlis aghkvetis administratsiuli (arasasamartlo) tsesi, rogorts sakutrebis uplebis datsvis epekturi sashualeba im shemtkhvevebistvis, rodesats sakheze ar ikneba saojakho, memkvidreobiti, samezoblo tu skhva sakhis dava. garda amisa, alternativis sakhit, sheikmneba am kategoriis davebze sasamartlo tsesit uplebis datsvis epektiani saprotseso mekanizmi da gamkatsrdeba kontroli sasamartlos gadatsqvetilebis aghsrulebis vadebze; sheuperkhebeli 
 - sheikmneba ertiani sivrtse, sadats qvela shesabamisi sakhelmtsipo utsqeba kerdzo bizness erti panjris printsipit moemsakhureba. shedegad, bizness sheumtsirdeba sakhelmtsiposgan shesabamisi momsakhurebis mighebistvis sachiro dro da resursebi; - kidev upro daikhvetseba da gaumjobesdeba arsebuli onlain servisebi, shesadzlebeli gakhdeba rogorts kompaniis onlain daregi­ strireba, aseve arsebul monatsemebshi tsvlilebebis onlain gankhortsieleba sajaro reestris erovnul saagentoshi misvlis gareshe; - gamotskhaddeba moratoriumi akhali litsenziebisa 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 ekonomikuri ganvitareba da nebartvebis shemoghebaze. aghnishnuli moratoriumi sheekheba nebismieri tipis sakmianobas, garda imisa, romelits imperatiulad motkhovnilia, rom iqos litsenzirebadi sakmianoba sakartvelos mier gapormebuli saertashoriso shetankhmebebit; - gamotskhaddeba moratoriumi akhali maregu­ lirebeli strukturebis shekmnaze, garda im shemtkhvevisa, tu es imperatiulad aris motkhovnili sakartvelos mier gapormebuli saertashoriso shetankhmebebit; - mokhdeba sametsarmeo sakmianobis gankhor­ tsie­lebastan dakavshirebuli ekonomikuri danashaulis dekriminalizatsia. gaukmdeba siskhlis samartlis pasukhismgebloba kmede­ bebistvis, romlebits tavisi shinaarsit sagadasakhado samartaldarghvevas tsarmoadgens, rogoritsaa sasakonlo zednadebis arasrulad an/da arastsorad shevseba (sakonlis raodenobis an/da pasis shemtsireba),   larze meti ghirebulebis sakonlis sasakonlo zednadebis gareshe transportireba, savaldebulo markirebas dakvemdebarebuli araaktsizuri sakonlis markirebis gareshe realizatsia, bughaltruli aghritskhvis tsesis darghveva; -   laramde gaizrdeba gadasakhadebisgan 
 tavis aridebisatvis siskhlis samartlis pasukhismgeblobis dakisrebis zghvari, rats 
   tslidan, khandazmulobis vadis   tslamde shemtsirebis ponze, mnishvnelovani epektis momtani ikneba biznesistvis; 
 - gamotskhaddeba siskhlis samartlis kodeksis  -e (qalbi sagadasakhado dokumentis damzadeba an gamoqeneba) da  -e (gada­ sakhadistvis tavis arideba) mukhlebit gatvalistsinebuli danashaulebis sruli amnistia. shesabamisad, siskhlissamartlebrivi 
 pasukhismgeblobisa da sasjelisagan gatavisu­ pldebian pirebi, romlebmats aghnishnuli danasha­ ulebi   tslis   ianvramde chaidines; 
 - shesadzlebeli gakhdeba daudzleveli dzalis, mat shoris stikiuri ubedurebis mokmedebis shede­ gad ganadgurebuli/dakarguli sasakonlomaterialuri paseulobebis chamotsera gamar­ tivebuli tsesit; - gankhortsieldeba 
 - shemushavdeba kontseptsia, romlis tanakhmad shesadz­ lebeli gakhdeba, sheikmnas spetsializebuli komertsiuli kolegiebi saerto sasamar­ tloebis sistemashi; - gamartivdeba biznesis durebi; 
 likvidatsiis protse­
