 sakmis 
 tsarmo­ 
 ebastan dakavshirebuli protsedurebis dasakhvetsad, gatardeba gadakhdisuunarobis sistemis reporma; 
 ekonomikis im dargebidan, romlebsats akvs damoukideblad punktsionirebisa da ganvitarebis potentsiali; 
 - uzrunvelqopili ikneba sagadasakhado stimu­ lebi biznesis ganvitarebistvis.   tslidan dzalashi sheva mogebis gadasakhadis akhali modeli, romlis mikhedvit satsarmos mier mighebuli mogeba daibegreba mkholod misi ganatsilebisas. shesabamisad, satsarmo mogebis gadasakhads gadaikhdis im shemtkhvevashi, tu mogebas gaanatsilebs dividendis sakhit mis partniorebze an araekonomikuri miznit gastsevs garkveul kharjebs. shedegad, bizness gauchndeba shesadzlebloba, damatebiti pinansuri sakhsrebi mimartos reinvestirebaze, kerdzod, akhali biznesis dasatsqebad, arsebuli tsarmoebis gadaiaraghebistvis an/da gapartoebistvis. es reporma ushualod mimartulia kveqanashi biznesis ganvitarebis, damatebiti samushao adgilebis shekmnis da ekonomikuri zrdis mkhardacherisken. biznessektorshi darcheba nakhevar miliardze meti lari, romlis reinvestireba gankhortsieldeba biznesis gapartoebis mimartulebit, rats aseve damatebiti shemosavlebis generirebas nishnavs. repormis shedegad, realuri mshp-is zrdis tempi   tsels dachkardeba  , , %-it. gamotavisuplebuli puladi sakhsrebis biznesis mier piksirebul aktivebshi investirebis shedegad, dasakmebasa da am machveneblis istoriuli damokidebulebis gatvalistsinebit,   atasi akhali samushao adgili mkholod am repormis parglebshi mkholod   tsels sheikmneba. jamshi,   tslis ganmavlobashi ki, gachndeba damatebit     samushao adgili. kveqnis mimdinare angarishis depitsiti, rats kveqnis ekonomikuri politikisatvis istoriulad ert-erti umtavresi gamotsvevaa, mkholod am repormis shedegad   tselitsadshi titkmis  %-it gaumjobesdeba, rats arsebuli prognozis mikhedvit, kveqnidan  -  mln ashsh dolarit naklebi valutis gadinebas nishnavs. 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 ekonomikuri ganvitareba  . . ekonomikuri repormebi sakartveloshi ekonomikuri zrdis stimuli­ rebistvis, zogadad biznesgaremos gaumjobesebis garda, “kartuli otsneba“ gegmavs masshtaburi repormebis gankhortsielebas.  . . . kapitalis bazris reporma kveqanashi ganvitarebuli kapitalis bazris arseboba guliskhmobs, sabanko dakreditebis paralelurad, kompaniebisatvis grdzelvadiani pinansuri resursebis mozidvis epektian shesadzleblobas. amit, kapitalis bazari kmnis konkurentul garemos ara mkholod dakreditebis, aramed danazogebis epektianad gadanatsilebis mimartulebit. metits, tu raime mizezit sabanko dakrediteba izghudeba, obligatsiebis bazari shesadzloa asrulebdes dambalanseblis rols. kapitalis bazris punktsia ara mkholod biznesisatvis pinansuri resursebis mitsodebaa, ganvitarebuli bazari kveqnis mosakhleobis danazogebis gantavsebis damatebiti instrumentitsaa. shedegad, ganvitarebuli da gamchvirvale kapitalis bazari khels utsqobs stabilur ekonomikur zrdas da mosakhleobis ketildgheobis amaghlebas. „kartuli otsnebis“ ert-erti dziritadi amotsana sakartvelos regionul pinansur tsentrad chamoqalibebaa. am miznis misaghtsevad, gankhortsieldeba shemdegi ghonisdziebebi: - kheli sheetsqoba konkurentuli garemos chamoqalibebas, rats gamoritskhavs bazris tsalkeuli segmentebis, instrumentebis an monatsileebis disk­riminatsias, upirates an monopoliur mdgomareobashi chaqenebas. sakhelmtsipo da kapi­ talis bazris regulatorebi uzrunvelqopen samartlianobis printsipebze dapudznebuli bazris monatsileta ghia da gamchvirvale sakmianobas; - daikhvetseba shesabamisi sagadasakhado dabegvris rezhimebi. aghnishnuli tsvlileba moiazrebs sagada­ sakhado sistemis upro metad ekonomikur zrdaze orientirebulobas, aseve skhvadaskhva pinansuri instrumentebis tanabar pirobebshi chaqenebas; - kheli sheetsqoba mosakhleobis pinansuri gana­ tlebis donis amaghlebas; - daikhvetseba momkhmarebelta da investorta up­ le­bebis datsvis garantiebi. maksimalurad datsuli ikneba tsvrili da gautvittsnobierebeli investorebis interesebi, rats kapitalis bazris skhvadaskhva segmentis ganvitarebis ert-erti umtavresi tsinapirobaa. aghnishnul protsesshi gansakutrebuli quradgheba daetmoba maregulireblis, saganmanatleblo, korpo­ratsiuli martvis da pinansuri aghritskhvianobis sakitkhebs. momdevno tslebshi, gankhortsielebuli repormis shedegad sakartveloshi chamoqalibebuli kapitalis bazari ikneba resursebis mozidvis maghalepektiani tsqaro. igi bazris qvela monatsiles mistsems sashualebas, miighos tanamedrove teknologiebze dapudznebuli sapinanso momsakhurebis sruli spektri. amastan, saertashoriso sauketeso praktikis 
 shesabamisi da mudmivad ganvitarebaze orientirebuli maregulirebeli garemo uzrunvelqops maghali donis sandoobasa da investorta datsulobas.  . . . sapensio reporma „kartuli otsneba“ gaatarebs sapensio repormas, romlis mizania kerdzo dagrovebit sapensio sistemaze gadasvla. aghnishnuli reporma kapitalis bazris shedarebit parto repormis shemadgeneli komponentia, vinaidan igi khels utsqobs grdzelvadiani pinansuri resursebis tsarmokmnas. sapensio repormis umtavresi amotsanaa mosakhleobis ketildgheobis amaghleba, agretve arsebuli sotsialuri sistemis piskaluri mdgradobis shenarchuneba. piskaluri stabilurobis gatvalistsinebit, kerdzo dagrovebiti pensia optimaluri modelia sapensio uzrunvelqopis adekvaturobis gaumjobesebis kutkhit. kerdzo sapensio sistema shesadzleblobas mistsems mokalakes, shekmnas danazogi, romelits tslebis ganmavlobashi dasakmebulis mier gamomushavebuli khelpasis pirdapirproportsiuli ikneba. garda amisa, kerdzo dagrovebit sapensio sistemas akvs ekonomikis mastimulirebeli epekti. kerdzo danazogebis zrda, rats nishnavs grdzelvadiani pinansuri resursis mobilizebas, mnishvnelovnad sheutsqobs khels adilobrivi kapitalis bazris ganvitarebas da sabolood, dadebitad aisakheba ekonomikur zrdaze. repormas ekneba shemdegi ekonomikuri epekti: - repormis gankhortsieleba realuri mshp-is zrdis machvenebels gazrdis damatebit  , - , %-it. damatebiti kapitalis gachena ekonomikashi khels sheutsqobs akhali samushao adgilebis shekmnas da   atasi akhali samushao adgilidan, romlis shekmnasats „kartuli otsneba“ gegmavs,  -  atasi adamiani mkholod am repormis shedegad sheikmneba; - repormis shedegad, kveqanashi larshi deno­ mini­rebul seskhebze grdzelvadiani sapro­tsento ganakvetebi daakhloebit  %-it shemtsirdeba. saba­ zro saprotsento ganakvetebis shemtsireba, erti mkhriv, stimuls mistsems metsarmeebs, ganakhortsielon damatebiti investitsiebi da gaapartovon saku­ tari biznesi, kholo, meore mkhriv, gaizrdeba erovnuli danazogebis grdzelvadiani machvenebeli kveqnis ekonomikashi, rats kveqnis mosakhleobis shemosavlebis zrdas sheutsqobs khels.  . . . mitsis reporma gankhortsieldeba sakhelmtsipo konebis inven­ tarizatsia, rats guliskhmobs mteli kveqnis masshtabit sakhelmtsipo konebis aghritskhvasa da ertian bazashi tavmoqras. aghnishnuli khels sheutsqobs sakhelmtsipo aktivebis martva-gankargvis protsess, gamouqenebeli aktivebis brunvashi chartvas, kveqanashi mitsis kadastris srulqopasa da inpormatsiaze khelmisatsvdomobis gazrdas. inventarizatsiis proekti dasruldeba   tslis bolos. 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 ekonomikuri ganvitareba dainergeba konebis gamartivebuli registratsia, rats pirvel rigshi gankhortsieldeba kerdzo mesakutreta interesebis gatvalistsinebit.   tslis   agvistodan amokmedda sajaro reestris shesakheb kanoni, romelits maksimalurad gaamartivebs da mokalakeebistvis khelmisatsvdoms gakhdis registratsiis protsess, tsaakhalisebs registratsias sasoplo sameurneo danishnulebis mitsis nakvetis registratsiisatvis momzadebuli sakadastro agegmviti/azomviti nakhazebis sapasuris anazghaurebis gzit. dgheisatvis, kveqanashi arsebuli mitsis nakvetebis  %-mdea registrirebuli. barierebis dadzleva gankhortsieldeba shemdegi gzebit: dainergeba saamzomvelo nakhazis ertiani standarti, proektshi chartuli amzomvelebi gaivlian sertipikatsias, sakhelmtsipo mokalakes daekhmareba sakutrebis damadasturebeli sabutebis modziebasa da davebis mogvarebashi. damtkitsebulia maghalmtian regionebshi pakto­ briv mplobelobashi arsebuli mitsis nakvetebis privatizebis khelshetsqobis programa da daitsqeba misi gankhortsieleba. programis mikhedvit, maghalmtian regionebshi mtskhovreb mokalakeebs, romlebsats sakartveloshi tslebis tsin chatarebuli mitsis repormis parglebshi ar miughiat sasoplosameurneo danishnulebis mitsis nakvetebi, magram sul mtsire   tslis ganmavlobashi paktobrivad ploben sasoplo-sameurneo danishnulebis mitsis nakvets, mplobelobashi simbolur pasad gadaetsemat arsebuli mitsis nakveti.  . . . sajaro-kerdzo partniorobis sistemis ganvitareba kveqnis ekonomikis ganvitarebisa da investitsiebis mozidvis ert-erti mnishvnelovani paktoria sajarokerdzo partnioroba. aghsanishnavia, rom ukanaskneli   tslis ganmavlobashi sakhelmtsiposa da bizness shoris tanamshromlobit araerti mnishvnelovani proekti gankhortsielda. sajaro-kerdzo partniorobis sistemis kidev upro gasadzliereblad, autsilebelia shesabamisi kanonmdeblobis dakhvetsa. im pirobebshi, rodesats masshtaburi inpra­ struk­turuli proektebi mnishvnelovan pinansur resursebs moitkhovs, gansakutrebit iset dargebshi, rogoritsaa energetika, transporti da skhv., tanamshromlobis aghnishnuli porma khels utsqobs proektis gankhortsielebastan dakavshirebuli riskebis gadanatsilebas sajaro da kerdzo sektorebs shoris da sakhelmtsiposa da biznesis mier resursebis mobilizebas, ritats upro realuri da martivi khdeba mnishvnelovani proektebis gankhortsieleba. amastan, sajaro-kerdzo partnioroba khels utsqobs sabiujeto danakharjebis shemtsirebas da shesadzleblobas adzlevs khelisuplebas, skhva speroebze mimartos sabiujeto sakhsrebi. garda amisa, inprastrukturuli proektebis gankhortsieleba pirdapir aisakheba ekono­ mikis zrdaze, damatebiti mushakhelis dasakmebasa da mosakhleobis ketildgheobaze. „kartuli 
 otsneba“ 
 ganavitarebs 
 shesabamis 
 kanon­mdeblobas da sistemas sajaro-kerdzo partniorobis gapartoebistvis. sistema khels sheutsqobs sakartveloshi investitsiebis shemodinebas da sakhelmtsiposa da biznesis mier mnishvnelovani inprastrukturuli proektebis upro stsrapad da epekturad gankhortsielebas.  . . . asotsirebis shetankhmebit gansazghvruli skhva ekonomikuri repormebi „kartulma otsnebam“ tsarmatebit daasrula molaparakebebi da kheli moatsera asotsirebis shetankhmebas evrokavshirtan. shetankhmebis gapormebis tsinapiroba iqo mteli rigi repormebis gankhortsieleba. asotsirebis shetankhmebis dghis tsesrigit uakhloes periodshi dagegmilia mnishvnelovani ekonomikuri repormebis gankhor­ tsieleba, romelits uzrunvelqops ekonomikis modernizatsias da sakartvelos bazris tavsebadobas evrokavshiris bazartan ertiani tamashis tsesebis damkvidrebis gzit.  . . sivrtsiti motsqoba sivrtsit-teritoriuli dagegmva aris kveqnis mdgradi ganvitarebis da tskhovrebis donis amaghlebis mnishvnelovani instrumenti. sivrtsit-teritoriuli dagegmva dakavshirebulia teritoriul–sivrtsiti aspektis sektoraluri politikis koordinatsiasa da integratsiastan. akedan gamomdinare, misi mtavari mizania sakmianobis metad ratsionaluri organizeba da ertmanetis sapirispiro politikuri amotsanebis shetankhmeba. teritoriul–sivrtsiti dagegmareba, rogorts tsesi, dakavshirebulia grdzelvadiani da sashualovadiani miznebis, teritoriuli strategiebisa da skhvadaskhva dargis politikis koordinatsiis gamovlenastan. teritoriul-sivrtsiti dagegmarebis sistema gvekhmareba ekonomikuri, sotsialuri da ekologiuri sargeblianobis uzrunvelqopashi. sakartvelos sivrtsit-teritoriuli dagegmvis amotsanebia: gaaumjobesos urtiertkavshiri kalaksa da sopels shoris; kheli sheutsqos maghalkhariskhiani mdgradi turizmis ganvitarebas, aseve evropisa da aziis damakavshirebel satransporto da lojistikur habad chamoqalibebas, shekmnas investirebistvis stimulebi da mimzidveli garemo, sheamtsiros garemoze mavne zemokmedeba. sivrtsit-teritoriuli dagegmvis parglebshi, ukve damushavebulia araerti dokumenti. sheikmna chokhatauris, batumis, ambrolauris, potis, rustavis, kaspis, zugdidis, chkhorotsqus, dushetis, urekishekvetilis mitsatsargeblobis gegmebi, khertvisivardzia-olodas kalakmsheneblobiti dokumentatsia. kveqnis sivrtsiti motsqobis mimartulebit, „kart­ uli otsneba“ gaatarebs aktiur politikas: - momzaddeba sakartvelos sivrtsiti motsqobis skema; - dasruldeba tbilisis generaluri gegma; 
 mitsatsargeblobis 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 ekonomikuri ganvitareba - momzaddeba akhmetis da mestiis munitsipalitetebis sivrtsiti motsqobis gegmebi, tushetis   da mulakhis temis   soplis ganashenianebis regulirebis gegmebi, mtskhetis, kobi-gudauris, bakuriani-didi mitarbis, bakhmaros, kobuletis, khelvachauris mitsatsargeblobis gegmebi; iqaltos khevis, shaoris, utseris ganashenianebis regulirebis gegmebi; - stsori dagegmarebit da gaazrebuli sivrtsiti motsqobit, sakartvelo gakhdeba otkhi sezonis turistuli kveqana, rats uzrunvelqops turizmidan akhali shemosavlebis mighebis da tslis ganmavlobashi mati stabiluri ganatsilebis sashualebas; - gagrdzeldeba tsqaltubos, samtskhe-javakhetis, qazbegi-gudauris, mtskheta-mtianetis, tushetis, rachis regionebshi turistuli inprastrukturis ganvitareba da tanamedrove, saertashoriso donis kurortebis shekmna; - kalakmsheneblobiti dokumentatsiis shesabamisad, mokhdeba gudauri-kobis, bakurianis, didvelis, kokhta-mitarbis, tetnuldi-hatsvalis, goderdzis samto-satkhilamuro kurortebis ganvitareba da arsebul kurortebze akhali mimartulebebis damateba. mat shoris gatvalistsinebuli ikneba kurortebis zapkhulis ganmavlobashi datvirtvis shesadzleblobebi.  . . tavisupali sagareo savachro urtiertobebi sakartvelo aris ghia kveqana. tavisupali savachro urtiertobebis damqareba danarchen msopliostan ekonomikuri politikis ert-erti dziritadi prioritetia. sakartvelo-evrokavshiris asotsirebis shetankhmebis, kerdzod, ghrma da qovlismomtsveli tavisupali vachrobis shetankhmebis gapormebit, kartul ekonomikashi sheikmna mnishvnelovani shesadzleblobebi eksportis zrdis, investitsiebis mozidvisa da kveqanashi produktiulobis zrdis kutkhit. mimdinareobs molaparakebebi chinetis sakhalkho respublikastan tavisupali vachrobis shesakheb, romelits uakhloes momavalshi unda dasruldes. shetankhmebis gapormeba dagegmilia   tsels. shedegad, gaizrdeba kartuli produktsiis saeksporto potentsiali da saeksporto bazrebis diversipitsirebuloba. „kartuli otsnebis“ mier gatarebuli ekonomikuri politikis ert-erti umtavresi mizania tavisupali vachrobis shetankhmebebit mighebuli shesadzleblobis epekturi da stsrapi gamoqeneba. „kartuli otsneba“ ghrma da qovlismomtsveli tavisupali vachrobis shetankhmebit tsarmokmnili shesadzleblobebis gamoqenebis miznit, gaagrdzelebs aktiuri politikis gankhortsielebas: - daekhmareba bizness akhal bazrebze shesvlashi. kerdzod, mokhdeba eksporttan dakavshirebuli kharjebis shemsubukeba, agretve eksporttan 
 asotsirebuli riskebis dazghveva; - ganvitardeba onlain platporma, romelits srul inpormatsias miatsvdis kartvel eksportiorebs mattvis saintereso bazrebze arsebuli mdgomareobis shesakheb, mat shoris, inpormatsias konkretul kveqanashi konkretul sasakonlo kodze mokmedi saimporto taripebis, datsesebuli motkhovnebis, agretve shesabamis kveqanashi konkretuli produktis tsarmoebisa da importis motsulobebis shesakheb; - kartuli produktsiis saeksporto gapartoebis khelshetsqobis miznit, komertsiuli atasheebis instituti; 
 bazrebis sheikmneba 
 - arsebuli tavisupali vachrobis shetankhmebebit gansazghvruli shesadzleblobebis maksimalurad asatviseblad da evrokavshiris motkhovnebtan shesabamisobashi mosaqvanad, gaizrdeba shesabamisi satsarmoebis sakhelmtsipo mkhardachera (rogorts pinansuri, ise teknikuri). es gansakutrebit sheekheba soplis meurneobis satsarmoebs; - amave dros, evrokavshirtan asotsirebis shetankhmebit gansazghvruli regulatsiebis gadmogheba gankhortsieldeba am shetankhmebit mkatsrad gansazghvrul vadebshi da sakartvelos ekonomikis taviseburebebis gatvalistsinebit. qoveli tslis dasatsqisshi mtavroba daamtkitsebs da gaasajaroebs misaghebi regulatsiebis nuskhas.  . . inprastrukturuli ganvitareba inprastrukturis gaumjobeseba sakartvelos regionebis ganvitarebis, saertashoriso satranzito proektebshi sakartvelos maksimaluri integrirebisa da ekonomikuri ganvitarebis stimulirebis umnishvnelovanesi tsinapirobaa.   tslis shemdeg, mnishvnelovnad gaizarda sagzao inprastrukturis ganvitarebis tempebi.  -  tslebshi avtobanze qoveltsliurad shendeboda sashualod   km, kholo  -  tslebshi -   km gza. mnishvnelovani pinansuri resursebi daikharja tsqalmomaragebis inprastrukturis msheneblobasa da ganakhlebaze.  -  tslebshi am mimartulebit gatseulma kharjebma nakhevar miliard lars gadaacharba. shedegad,    -ze met adamians sakartvelos regionebshi gauumjobesda sasmeli tsqlis mitsodebis grapiki da khariskhi. aktiurad grdzeldeba gazmomaragebis inprastrukturis msheneblobis protsesi. umnishvnelovanesi nabijebi gadaidgmeba internetizatsiis mimartulebit, ristvisats chvens gunds ukve gamotskhadebuli akvs interesta gamokhatva da shemdgomi   tslis ganmavlobashi „kartuli otsneba“ daasrulebs saqoveltao internetizatsiis proekts. „kartuli otsneba“ mkapio gegmit ganavitarebs kveqnis inprastrukturas: - sagzao inprastrukturis ganvitarebistvis „kartuli otsneba“ gegmavs revolutsiuri nabijebis gadadgmas. sakartvelos geograpiuli mdebareobis da satvirto gadazidvebis mzardi dinamikis gatvalistsinebit, gagrdzeldeba 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 ekonomikuri ganvitareba akhali magistraluri gzebis mshenebloba, arsebuli gzebis rekonstruktsia da sagzao inprastrukturis ganakhleba-modernizeba. kveqnis masshtabit ashendeba saertashoriso mnishvnelobis satranzito da regionebis damakavshirebeli shida saavtomobilo gzebi. es ikneba kveqnis kherkhemali, romelits qvela regions mchidrod daakavshirebs ertmanettan da dedakalaktan. geograpiuli mdebareoba aghar ikneba barieri biznesis tsarmoebisa da gadaadgilebistvis. es proekti gaadzlierebs sakartvelos mnishvnelobas regionshi da gazrdis misi, rogorts tranzituli habis datvirtvas.   tslamde daigeba   kmze meti sigrdzis,  ,  miliardi ashsh dolaris ghirebulebis sagzao inprastruktura, das­ ruldeba aghmosavlet-dasavletis avto­ banis mshenebloba. shedegad, sakartvelos 
 saavtomobilo gzebis kseli gakhdeba mimzidveli satranzito gadazidvebisatvis, khels sheutsqobs kveqanashi turizmis ganvitarebas, ganapira da maghalmtian regionebshi soplis meurneobis ganvitarebasa da regionebis dakavshirebas; - khariskhiani sasmeli tsqlis  -saatiani mitsodebis rezhimit mosakhleobis uzrunvelqopa „kartuli otsnebis“ ert-erti prioritetia. am miznis mightseva etapobrivad gankhortsieldeba momdevno ramdenime tslis ganmavlobashi.   
 tslistvis,  -saatiani tsqalmomaragebit uzrunvelqopili ikneba damatebit   atasi adamiani. aktiurad gagrdzeldeba 
 tsqalmomaragebis tsqalarinebisa da gamtsmendi nagebobebis mshenebloba-reabilitatsiis proek­ tebi mtel rig kalakebsa da soplebshi, mat shoris kutaisshi, zugdidshi, qvarelshi, khashurshi, potshi, urekshi, chiaturashi, gudaurshi, bakurianshi, bolnisshi, marneulshi, telavshi, tsqaltuboshi, kobuletshi, anakliashi, mestiashi, khonshi, vanshi, baghdadshi, onshi, abastumanshi, valeshi, tsagershi, norioshi, martqopshi, vaziansa da akhal samgorshi. gansakutrebuli quradgheba etmoba da uakhloes momavalshi dasruldeba tsqalmomaragebis sistemebis samsheneblo-samontazho samushaoebi panki­sis kheobis, kaspisa da karelis munitsi­ palitetebis sazghvrispira soplebshi, ris shedegadats   atasamde adamianisatvis mnishv­ nelovnad gaumjobesdeba sasmeli tsqlis mitsodebis khariskhi; - narchenebis martva evropuli standartebis shesabamisad gankhortsieldeba - kveqnis mtel teritoriaze amokmeddeba munitsipaluri nar­ chenebis shegrovebis servisebi, mokhdeba arsebuli nagavsaqrelebis shesabamisobashi moqvana standartebtan an dakhurva, agretve standartebis shesabamisad akhali regionuli nagavsaqrelebis motsqoba; etapobrivad dainergeba narchenebis separirebis da gadamushavebis sistemebi; - ashendeba  -kilometriani inprastruktura, ris shedegadats damatebit   atasi adamiani miighebs internets. shedegad, kveqnis mosakhleobis  %-ze mets ekneba internetze tsvdoma. 
  . . dargobrivi ekonomikuri politika sakartvelos ekonomikis dzireuli transpormatsiis globalur ghonisdziebebtan ertad, „kartuli otsnebis“ ekonomikuri politika mimartuli ikneba ekonomikuri zrdis mamodzravebeli dargebis gardakmna-ganvitarebaze.  . . . energetika „kartuli otsnebis“ energetikuli politikis umtavresi mimartulebaa kveqnis energetikuli usaprtkhoebisa da damoukideblobis khariskhis amaghleba, importirebul energoresursebze damo­ kidebulebis etapobrivi shemtsireba adgilobrivi energetikuli resursebis atvisebis, mitsodebis tsqaroebisa da marshrutebis diversipikatsiis gzit.   tslis shemdeg, mnishvnelovani nabijebi gadaidga kveqnashi generatsiis akhali obiektebis ganvitarebis mimartulebit, rats shesabamis tsiprebshi aisakha:  -  tslebshi shekmnili dadgmuli simdzlavris motsulobam   megavati, kholo  -  tslebshi -   megavati sheadgina.  -  tslebshi eksploatatsiashi shevida   hidroelektrosadguri, kholo   tslebshi -   elektrosadguri, mat shoris erti karis sadguri.  -  tslebshi potentsiur investorebtan gapormda   memorandumi, kholo  -  tslebshi es tsipri  -mde gaizarda.   tslebshi ashenda   kilometris maghali dzabvis elektrogadamtsemi khazebis inprastruktura.   tslebshi ashenda da eksploatatsiashi shevida   km, kholo  -  tslebshi -   km sigrdzis maghali tsnevis gazsadeni. elektroenergiis mzardi mokhmarebis ponze, maghal doneze narchundeba elektroenergiit tvituzrunvelqopis done. shah-denizis proektis me-  pazis parglebshi, sakartveloshi mimdinareobs samkhretkavkasiuri milsadenis gapartoebis samushaoebi - msheneblobis skhvadaskhva etapze dasakmdeba  -mde adamiani, gankhortsieldeba   mlrd ashsh dolaris investitsia. dasrulda da eksploatatsiashi shevida   mln evros ghirebulebis „shavi zghvis elektrogadamtsemi kselis“ proekti; sakartvelos energosistemas sheemata   hidroelektrosadguri, romelta sainvestitsio ghirebulebaa   mln. ashsh dolari. uakhloes momavalshi, eksploatatsiashi sheva kidev   hidroelektrosadguri, romelta sainvestitsio ghirebuleba   mlrd dolaramdea. eksploatatsiashi shevida gardabnis   mgvt simdzlavris maghalteknologiuri tboelektrosadguri; mimdi­ nareobs  -  mgvt simdzlavris adgilobriv kvanakhshirze momushave tboelektrosadguris proekti. mimdinareobs aghmosavlet-dasavletis magistraluri gazsadenis sruli reabilitatsia ( -  tsts.). dasrulda sakartveloshi pirveli mitsiskvesha gazsatsavis teknikur-ekonomikuri dasa­ buteba, romlis sapudzvelze unda gankhortsieldes  -  mln kuburi metris motsulobis gazsatsavis proekti. energetikuli politikis prioritetuli mimar­ tulebaa gazmomaragebisa da elekt­romomaragebis miznit inprastrukturuli proektebis gankhor­ 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 ekonomikuri ganvitareba tsieleba. tu  -  tslebshi gazmomaragebis kselshi mkholod   atasi abonenti chaerto,   tslebshi es machvenebeli   atass gastsda, anu   tselitsadshi gazis mitsodeba uzrunvelqopil ikna  %-it meti abonentistvis, vidre  -tslian ( ) periodshi.   tsels daitsqo da   tsels dasrulda okupirebuli teritoriebis gamqop khaztan mdebare   dasakhlebuli punktis gazipitsireba, ris shedegadats   ojakhs mietsa bunebrivi airis kselshi chartvis shesadzlebloba. aktiurad mimdinareobs elektripikatsiis protsesi. gansakutrebuli aktsenti ketdeba ushuko soplebze, ristvisats   tsels daitsqo proekti - „sinatle qvela sopels“, ris shedegadats dghemde elektroenergiis mitsodebis kselshi   ushuko sopeli chaerto. aktiurad grdzeldeba gamritskhvelianebis samushaoebi -   tslidan   atasamde abonenti individualurad gamritskhvelianda. „kartuli otsneba“ aktiurad gaagrdzelebs energetikis sektoris ganvitarebas da gadzlierebas: - khelisupleba

 otsnebam“ 
 khelisuplebashi 
 mosvli­ 
 stanave soplis meurneobis speroshi masshtaburi repormebi tsamoitsqo. shemushavda dargis ganvitarebis strategia ( - ), romelshits mkapiod aris gansazghvruli uakhloesi tslebis miznebi da amotsanebi: permerebis pinansuri mkhardachera, tsodnis amaghleba, akhali teknologiebis danergva, tsarmoebis tanamedrove standartebze gadasvla, adgilobrivi da saertashoriso bazrebis modzieba. mighebulia samokmedo gegma, sadats utsqebrivad aris gatserili qvela tipis aktivoba, teknikuri da pinansuri uzrunvelqopa, sistemuri reporma, ghrma da qovlismomtsveli tavisupali savachro sivrtsis shesakheb shetankhmebis valdebulebebi. pirvelad bolo   tslis ganmavlobashi, sheikmna dokumenti, romelmats unda uzrunvelqos dargis aktiuri, sheuktsevadi, dinamiuri da sistemuri ganvitareba. amastan, mimdinareobs mteli rigi institutsiuri repormebi, romlebits grdzelvadian perspektivashi, dadebit gavlenas moakhdens dargis mdgrad ganvitarebaze. mnishvnelovnad gaizarda soplis meurneobis sabiujeto dapinanseba, ris sapudzvelzets gankhortsielda araerti tsarmatebuli proekti: amokmedda mtsiremitsian permerta khelshetsqobis proekti, saidanats   atasamde glekhma   mln laris dakhmareba miigho, damushavda   atas hektarze meti mitsa; permerebs usasqidlod daurigdat   mln laramde ghirebulebis sasoplo-sameurneo inventari da mtsenareta movlis sashualebebi;   tslebshi dapinansda   akhali satsarmos shekmna, jamuri investitsiebis motsulobam sheadgina   milioni dolari; gapartovda da gadaiaraghda   satsarmo; sheghavatiani agrokreditis parglebshi gaitsa     seskhi (    seskhi       laris odenobit da     seskhi       ashsh dolaris odenobit); mevenakheebma kakhetsa da racha-lechkhumshi bolo sami tslis ganmavlobashi   milion laramde shemosavali miighes,   tsels kakhetisa da racha-lechkhumis mkhareebshi gadamushavda     tona qurdzeni, rats bolo   tslis rekorduli machvenebelia;  tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 ekonomikuri ganvitareba ghirebuleba -     lars, saidanats saagentos tanadapinanseba sheadgens     lars; damontazhda   erteuli setqvis satsinaaghmdego saraketo gamshvebi danadgari, ris shedegadats kakhetshi mosavali  %-it gaizarda; sareabilitatsio samushaoebi chautarda   km sairigatsio da   km sadrenazhe arkhs,   satave nagebobas,   satumb sadgurs da skhva hidroteknikur nagebobebs, teknikuri eksploatatsiis parglebshi gaitsminda da motsesrigda     km samelioratsio arkhi, garemontda an akhlit sheitsvala     erteuli skhvadaskhva hidroteknikuri nageboba; mravaltslovani kulturebis kvlevis mimartulebit aghdgenili da gashenebulia vazis endemuri   da introduktsirebuli   jishi. kmediti politikis shedegad, gachnda pozitiuri tendentsiebi tsarmoebis zrdis, saeksporto bazrebis gapartoebisa da soplis meurneobis sektorshi investitsiebis mozidvis tvalsazrisit. saministros dakvemdebarebashi sheikmna a(a)ip „proektebis martvis saagento“, romlis sakmianobis shedegad, mnishvnelovnad gaizarda soplis meurneobis dapinanseba sabanko sektoris mkhridan.   tsels gatsemuli seskhebis motsuloba soplis meurneobis sektorshi sheadgenda   mln lars, rats   tslis machvenebels khutjer aghemateba. „sasoplo-sameurneo kooperativis shesakheb’’ kanonis mighebis sapudzvelze sheikmna ssip sasoplosameurneo kooperativebis ganvitarebis saagento, romelits khels sheutsqobs kooperativebis sametsarmeo sakmianobis stimulirebas, mat mplobelobashi arsebuli mitsebis damushavebasa da ekonomikur brunvashi chartvas. chamoqalibda ssip „soplis meurneobis sametsnierotsentri“, romlis mizania soplis meurneobisa da sursatis tsarmoebis ganvitarebis, mtsenareta da tskhovelta agrobiomravalperovnebis shenarchunebis khelshetsqoba, mtsenareta jishebis gamotsdisa da saselektsio sadgurebis aghdgena, tskhovelta khelovnuri ganaqopierebisa da sanashene sakmianobis khelshetsqoba, teslisa da sargavi masalis standartebisa da sertipitsirebis sistemis shemushaveba, akhali teknologiebis gavrtseleba, kvleviti 
 sursatis uvneblobis, veterinariisa da mtsenareta datsvis speroshi riskebis shepasebis uzrunvelqopa, biometodebis shemushaveba da biomeurneobebis ganvitarebis khelshetsqoba, soplis meurneobashi dasakmebul pirta ekstentsia da skhv. „kartuli otsneba“ gaagrdzelebs aktiur agropo­ litikas, romlis mizani evrokavshiris stan­ dartebtan daakhloeba, maghali khariskhis agrosasursato produktsiis tsarmoeba da kveqnis importze damokidebulebis shemtsireba ikneba: - sasoplo-sameurneo dargshi kooperatsiis gan­ vitarebis mkhardachera ikneba „kartuli otsnebis“ agropolitikis strategiuli mimar­ tuleba. am mimartulebit, gankhortsieldeba sasoplo-sameurneo mitsis bazris reporma, 
 rats mimartuli ikneba sasoplo mitsebis pragmentatsiis aghmo­pkhvrisken, shemushavdeba partobebis konso­lidatsiis gegma; - sakhelmtsipo khels sheutsqobs mosavlis aghebis shemdgomi teknologiebis danergvas - shemna­ khveli, damkhariskhebeli, shemputavi, gada­ mmushavebeli da sadistributsio sektorebis ganvitarebas. amit uzrunvelqopili ikneba damatebuli ghirebulebis shemkmneli sruli tsiklis shemadgeneli komponentebis integratsia, rats aamaghlebs tsarmoebis konkurentunarianobas; - mtsiremitsiani permerebistvis amokmeddeba saqoveltao agrodazghvevis proekti, aghar darcheba dauzghveveli mosavali, rats mosakhleobas mnishvnelovan zarals aatsilebs; - gagrdzeldeba da kidev upro daikhvetseba agrodazghvevis proekti, rats khels sheutsqobs permerta interesebis datsvas da agrosektorshi meti pinansebis mozidvas; -   atas hektramde gaizrdeba meliorirebuli (tsqaluzrunvelqopili da drenirebuli) mitsebis partobebi. ganvitardeba da gaumjobesdeba sartsqavi (sairigatsio) da damshrobi (sad­ renazhe) sistemebi. dainergeba mortsqvis tana­ 
 medrove sistemebi. gankhortsieldeba epe­kturi proektebi tsqalshegrovebis speroshi. shemushavdeba epek­turi taripi da dainergeba permerta tsqaluzrunvelqopis martvis akhali sistema; - mnishvnelovani quradgheba daetmoba dargshi dasakmebulta tsodnis amaghlebas, rats khels sheutsqobs konkurentunarianobis zrdas; - gagrdzeldeba mushaoba permerebistvis pinan­ sebze khelmisatsvdomobis mimartulebit, ristvisats uzrunvelqopili ikneba pinansur institutebtan mchidro tanamshromloba da permerta shesabamisi tsodnisa da kvalipikatsiis amaghleba; - mnishvnelovani proektebi gankhortsieldeba saso­ plo-sameurneo teknikis khelmisa­tsvdomobis asamaghleblad; - kveqnis sasursato usaprtkhoebis uzrunvel­ 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 kartuli adgiltsarmoshobis, dasakhlebebisa da geograpiuli aghnishvnebis datsvis mimar­ 
 tulebit; 
 - klimatgonivruli soplis meurneobis prak­ tikis damkvidreba dargis ganvitarebis stra­ tegiis mnishvnelovani komponentia, ristvisats shemu­shavdeba shesabamisi saertoerovnuli da regi­ onuli programebi; - gaumjobesdeba monatsemta shegrovebis, gavr­ tselebis da gamoqenebis koordinirebuli statistikuri sistema. daikhvetseba soplis meurneobis produktsiis bazris sainpormatsio baza. permanentulad gagrdzeldeba saertashoriso bazris analizi. chatardeba sistemuri kvlevebi da momzaddeba shesabamisi rekomendatsiebi. sakhel­mtsipo marketinguli ghonisdziebebis dagegmvisa da gankhortsielebis protsesshi mudmivad itanamshromlebs kerdzo sektortan. 
 asamaghleblad, gagrdzeldeba saertashoriso satransporto sistemebshi integratsia da regionuli tanamshromlobis gaghrmaveba; - gankhortsieldeba satransporto sistemebis srulqopa saertashoriso standartebis shesa­bamisi satransporto inprastrukturis, multi­modaluri da intermodaluri gadazidvebisa da lojistikuri tsentrebis ganvitarebis khelshe­tsqobis gzit; - samokalako aviatsiis speroshi kheli sheetsqoba „ghia tsis“ politikis gatarebas; - mokhdeba „evrogaertianebasa da mis tsevr sakhelmtsipoebs da sakartvelos shoris ert­ iani sahaero sivrtsis shesakheb“ shetankhmebis implementatsia, rats uzrunvelqops sakartvelos samokalako aviatsiis speroshi prenis usap­ rtkhoebis, saaviatsio ushishroebis, garemos datsvis, momkhmarebelta uplebebis datsvisa da skhva mimartulebebis evropul doneze ganvitarebas da sakartvelos saaviatsio sivrtsis evropis ertian sahaero sivrtseshi integratsias; - kheli sheetsqoba mtsire aviatsiis da satransporto inprastrukturis ganvitarebas mtian regi­ onebshi, rats am regionebis ekonomikur tsinsvlas sheutsqobs khels; - gagrdzeldeba anakliis ghrmatsqlovani portis ganvitareba; - evrokavshirtan asotsirebis shetankhmebis shesaba­ misad, mokhdeba sakartvelos kanonmdeblobis daakhloeba transportis speroshi evroka­ vshiris direktivebsa da regulatsiebtan, rats khels sheutsqobs satransporto operatsiebis usap­ rtkhoebis zrdas. 
  . . . transporti 
  . . . turizmi 
 sakartvelos khelsaqreli geograpiuli mde­ ba­reobidan gamomdinare, mnishvnelovania erti­ ani satransporto sistemis chamoqalibeba da satranzito potentsialis maksimaluri gamoqeneba. am mimartulebit, „kartulma otsnebam“ ukve gadadga mnishvnelovani nabijebi. 
 turizmis ganvitareba „kartuli otsnebis“ erterti prioritetia. qoveltsliurad mzardia vizitorebis nakadi da turizmis sperodan mighebuli shemosavlebi. turizmi kveqnis ekonomikuri zrdis mnishvnelovani mamodzravebeli dzalaa. dargis ganvitarebis tvalsazrisit, sakartvelom didi progresi achvena. mnishvnelovnad gaizarda kveqanashi shemosuli saertashoriso mogzaurebis raodenoba da   tsels aghritskhuli  ,  milioni vizitoridan   tslistvis es machvenebeli  ,  milions gadatsda. arsebuli prognozit   tsels turizmidan mighebuli shemosavlebi  ,  mlrd ashsh dolars gadaacharbebs, kholo saertashoriso vizitebis raodenoba  ,  milions miaghtsevs. garda amisa, qoveltsliurad matulobs gantavsebis obiektebis ritskhvi rogorts saertashoriso klasis, ise sashualo klasis sastumroebshi. am mimartulebis khelshetsqobistvis, sakhelmtsipo programas - „atsarmoe sakartveloshi“ daemata sastumro biznesis ganvitarebis komponenti, romelits orientirebulia sakartvelos regionebshi sastumroebis msheneblobis tsakhalisebaze. 
 sapudzveli chaeqara saukunis proektis - anakliis sazghvao portis msheneblobas, romelits ara mkholod mnishvnelovan gavlenas moakhdens sakartvelos satranzito potentsialis amaghlebaze, aramed gazrdis sakartvelos rols regionshi da aktsevs mas lojistikur habad. dasrulda bako-tbilisi-qarsis rkinigzis proekti, romelits mnishvnelovnad amtsirebs aziasa da evropas shoris tvirtebis gadazidvistvis sachiro dros da chveni kveqnis gavlit damatebiti tvirtnakadebis mozidvis satsindaria. transportis speros shemdgomi ganvitarebisa da sakartvelos, rogorts regionuli habis, potentsialis srulad atvisebistvis, „kartuli otsneba“ gaatarebs aktiur politikas: - satranzito 
 derepnis 
 konkurentunarianobis 
 turizmis, rogorts prioritetuli dargis shemdgomi ganvitarebistvis, „kartuli otsneba“ ganakhortsielebs shemdeg ghonisdziebebs: 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 ekonomikuri ganvitareba - motsesrigdeba da ganvitardeba sagzao inpras­ truktura, ketilmoetsqoba kulturul dzeglebtan da skhva ghirsshesanishnaobebtan misasvleli gzebi, rats khels sheutsqobs turizmis stimulirebas; - gaaktiurdeba marketinguli aktivobebi miznobriv da potentsiur bazrebze, rats khels sheutsqobs meti utskhoeli turistis da shesabamisad, meti shemosavlis mozidvas kveqanashi; - mokhdeba datsuli teritoriebis gapartoeba da ekoturizmis khelshetsqoba, rats chveni kveqnis erterti mtavari simdidrea; - kheli sheetsqoba turizmis skhvadaskhva tipis ganvitarebas (mat shoris sameditsino, sportuli, ghvinis da a.sh.); - sakmiani turizmis ganvitarebis miznit, sakon­ ventsio biuros sashualebit mokhdeba meti maghalmkharjveliani turistis mozidva sakar­ tveloshi, aseve am mimartulebit investitsiebis tsakhaliseba da khelshetsqoba; - gansakutrebuli aktsenti gaketdeba momsakhurebis speroshi momushave personalis gadamzadebaze, momsakhurebis khariskhis saertashoriso standa­ rtebamde gazrdis miznit; - turizmis politikashi ert-erti strategiuli mimartuleba ikneba sakartvelos gadaktseva otkhi sezonis turistul kveqnad, rats uzrunvelqops turizmidan akhali shemosavlebis mighebis da tslis ganmavlobashi mati stabiluri ganatsilebis sashualebas; - zamtris kurortebis shemdgomi ganvitareba mokhdeba gaazrebuli ganvitarebis da ganashe­ nianebis gegmebis mikhedvit, mat shoris gatvalistsinebuli ikneba kurortebis zapkhulis ganmavlobashi datvirtvis shesadzleblobebi; - kheli sheetsqoba sakhelmtsipo da kerdzo sektorebs shoris tanamshromlobis gaghrmavebas turistuli produktis shekmnisa da marketingis kutkhit; -  %-it gaizrdeba da   tslistvis   milions gadaacharbebs saertashoriso mogzaurebis rao­ denoba; - titkmis gaormagdeba saertashoriso turizmidan mighebuli shemosavlebi da „kartuli otsnebis“ mmartvelobis shemdgomi  -tsliani tsiklis bolos  ,  mlrd dolars miaghtsevs; - turizmtan asotsirebul industriebshi samushao adgilebis sashualo tsliuri raodenoba gaizrdeba aranakleb   atasit.  . . regionuli ekonomikuri politika „kartuli otsnebis“ ekonomikuri politikis erterti prioriteti regionebis ganvitareba da mat shoris utanastsorobis aghmopkhvraa. tslebis ganmavlobashi arastsorad tsarmartulma da spontanur gadatsqvetilebebze dapudznebulma politikam ekonomikis asimetriuli ganvitareba gamoitsvia. regionebshi shemtsirda ekonomikuri aktivoba, 
 gaizarda utanabroba dedakalaksa da regionebs shoris. biznesis mtlian brunvashi tbilisis tsili   tsels arsebuli  %-dan   tslistvis  %mde gaizarda. ugulvebelqopil ikna tsalkeuli regionebis mravalmkhrivi ekonomikuri ganvitarebis potentsiali, ramats mdzime kvali datova regionul ekonomikaze. „kartul otsnebas“ akvs regionuli ganvitarebis strategiuli khedva, romelits epudzneba evrokavshiris regionebis ekonomikuri da sotsialuri ganvitarebis gatanabrebis politikis midgomebs, guliskhmobs integrirebul, dargtashoris da teritoriaze morgebul ganvitarebis dagegmvas da shesabamisi regionuli politikis gankhortsielebas.   tslis shemdeg shemushavda da damtkitsda titoeuli regionis ganvitarebis strategia da samokmedo gegma.   tsels damtkitsda „ -  tslebis sakartvelos regionuli ganvitarebis programa“, romelits gansazghvravs sakartvelos regionuli politikis dziritad miznebsa da amotsanebs, prioritetebsa da ghonisdziebebs, mati dapinansebis konkretul tsqaroebs. programis saerto biujeti daakhl.   miliardi laria. rogorts aghnishnuli programis, ise tskhrave regionis ganvitarebis strategiis gansakhortsieleblad, shemushavebuli da amokmedebulia shesabamisi samokmedo gegmebi da monitoringis instrumentebi, romlebits saertashorisod aprobirebuli sauketeso analo­ gebis mikhedvit momzadda. „kartuli otsneba“ gansakutrebul quradghebas utmobs maghalmtiani regionebis ganvitarebas. shemushavda da amokmedda „maghalmtiani regionebis ganvitarebis shesakheb“ kanoni, romlis mizani maghalmtiani regionebis sotsialur-ekonomikuri progresis mastimulirebeli sheghavatebis gansazghvra da maghalmtian regionebshi mtskhovreb pirta ketildgheobis donis amaghlebaa. am miznis misaghtsevad maghalmtian dasakhlebebshi mtskhovreb pirtatvis kanoni itvalistsinebs mtel rig sotsialur sheghavatebs: kanonis amokmedebis shemdeg dabadebul pirvel da meore bavshvze   tslis ganmavlobashi qoveltviurad gaitsema dakhmareba   laris, mesame da shemdeg bavshvze   tslis ganmavlobashi -   laris odenobit; sakhelmtsipo pensiisa da sotsialuri paketis mimgheb pirebs dautsesdat  %-iani danamati; mastsavleblebs dautsesdat sakhelpaso danamati, sabazo tanamdebobrivi sargos aranakleb  %-is odenobit; maghalmtian dasakhlebashi mudmivad mtskhovrebi pirebi, romelta shemosavali ar aghemateba     lars, sashemosavlo gadasakhadisgan tavisupldebian; sajaro skolebsa da propesiul saganmanatleblo datsesebulebebs, romlebits mdebareobs maghalmtian regionshi, gaezardat vaucheruli dapinanseba; spetsialuri programebis monatsile mastsavleblebs dautsesdat damatebiti anazghaureba khelpasis aranakleb  %is odenobit;   tslis   ianvridan anazghaurdeba elektroenergiis kharjebis  % (araumetes   kvt. saatisa tveshi); datsesda qoveltviuri danamati ekimebistvis, pensiis ormagi odenobit, kholo ektnebistvis - pensiis odenobit; mosakhleoba zamtris periodshi uzrunvelqopili ikneba 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 ekonomikuri ganvitareba gatbobit. garda sotsialuri sheghavatebisa, kanoni itvalistsinebs metsarmeebisatvis spetsialuri sagadasakhado sheghavatebis shemoghebasats: metsarme pizikuri pirebi da satsarmoebi tavisupldebian sashemosavlo, konebisa da mogebis gadasakhadebisgan   tslis vadit; sakutrebashi arsebuli mitsis nakveti tavisupldeba konebis gadasakhadisgan. amzhamad, mimdinareobs mushaoba mtis ganvitarebis strategiis da sakhelmtsipo programis shemushavebistvis, romlis sapudzvelzets ganisazghvreba sashualovadian periodshi damatebit gansakhortsielebeli autsilebeli ghonisdziebebi, strategiuli miznebi da amotsanebi. maghalmtian regionebshi sheghavatebis shemoghebis mizania maghalmtian regionebshi adgilobrivi tsarmoebis ganvitareba, investitsiebis tsakhaliseba da samushao adgilebis shekmna, rata uzrunvelqopil iknes maghalmtian dasakhlebebshi mtskhovrebi adamianebis ketildgheobis donis amaghleba, adgilobrivi mosakhleobis dasakmebis khelshetsqobit demograpiuli vitarebis gaumjobeseba da kveqnis mteli teritoriis tanabari sotsialur-ekonomikuri ganvitareba. „kartuli otsneba“ ganakhortsielebs kmedit poli­tikas regionebis stsrapi da tanabari ganvi­ tarebistvis: - uzrunvelqopili ikneba regionebis dabalan­

 sotsialuri ganvitareba  . sotsialuri ganvitareba  . . janmrtelobis datsva da sotsialuri uzrunvelqopa „kartulma otsnebam“ khelisupleba mdzime sotsia­ luri problemebis, sigharibisa da umushevrobis dzalze maghali machveneblis, sakhelmtsipos kmediti sotsialuri politikis ararsebobis ponze chaibara. mosakhleobis umravlesoba, mat shoris sashualo pena, jandatsvis servisebis khelmisatsvdomobis problemis gamo, janmrtelobis da sitsotskhlis dakargvis an ukiduresi gagharibebis saprtkhis tsinashe idga.   tslis archevnebis shemdeg, chvenma khelisuplebam sapudzveli chauqara sakhelmtsipos sotsialuri pasukhismgeblobis printsipze dapudznebul janmrte­ lobisa da sotsialuri datsvis politikas, romlis shemdgomi srulqopa sakartveloshi titoeuli adamianis ghirseul tskhovrebas da ketildgheobas uzrunvelqops.  . . . janmrtelobis datsva jandatsvis biujeti   tslis shemdeg upretse­ dentod, titkmis  , -jer gaizarda. 
 kmaqopilia hospitalur doneze mighebuli gadaudebeli sameditsino momsakhurebit. qovelives shedegad, mkvetrad gaizarda rogorts pirveladi jandatsvis ( %-it), ise statsionaruli momsakhurebis ( -jer) mokhmareba, rats, rogorts amas saertashoriso gamotsdileba achvenebs, zrdis sakartvelos mokalakeebis sitsotskhlis khariskhs - janmrteli da unarshezghudulobisagan tavisupali sitsotskhlis sashualo khangrdzlivobas. aghnishnulis dasturia ukve mightseuli shedegebi bavshvta sikvdilianobis shemtsirebis sakhit, rashits mnishvnelovani roli janmrtelobistvis gazrdilma sakhelmtsipo dapinansebam da sameditsino momsakhurebaze gaiolebulma tsvdomam sheasrula. janmrtelobis msoplio organizatsiis ekspertta shepasebit, sakartvelom jandatsvis sektorshi gata­ rebuli repormebit achvena, rom drois dzalze mtsire monakvetshi shesadzlebelia umnishvnelovanesi tsvlilebebis gankhortsieleba. saqoveltao jandatsvis programis garda, khortsieldeba jandatsvis spetsializebuli mima­ rtulebebis programebi, romelta umetesobis dapinanseba,   tseltan shedarebit, gaormagda, kholo ramdenime mnishvnelovani programa   tslis shemdeg dainerga: - msoplio masshtabit, sakartvelo gakhda pirveli kveqana, sadats khortsieldeba upretsedento 
 - reperaluri momsakhurebis sakhelmtsipo programis parglebshi, damatebit, gansa­ 
 kutrebuli sameditsino sachiroebebis shemtkhvevashi, rogorts sakartveloshi, ise sazghvargaret, dapinansda   atasze meti shemtkhveva. amastan, pirvelad   tslidan dainerga reperaluri programis dapinansebis samartliani kriteriumebi, rats patsientebs adzlevs tanabar shesadzleblobas, sakhelmtsiposgan miighon sasitsotskhlod autsilebeli dakhmareba;

 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sotsialuri ganvitareba ertiani platporma da gaerostan aktiuri tanamshromlobit, „inovatsiuri dapinansebis“ globaluri dialogis mnishvnelovani monatsile. solidarobis pondis dapudznebis shemdeg, sakartveloshi, usakhsrobis gamo, registrirebuli shemtkhvevebidan, simsivnit daavadebuli artserti bavshvi da akhalgazrda ar daghupula; - dedata da bavshvta janmrtelobistvis gazrdilma sakhelmtsipo dapinansebam da maghali khariskhis sameditsino momsakhurebaze gaiolebulma tsvdomam mnishvnelovani roli sheasrula dedata da bavshvta sikvdilianobis shemtsirebashi. mnishvnelovnad gaizarda jandatsvis geograpiuli adgilobriv doneze gansazghvruli prioritetebis sapudzvelze, sakartvelos titoeul munitsipalitetshi ashenda da aghichurva sul mtsire erti ambulatoria. sul ashenda da aghichurva   ambulatoria, mat shoris - gamqopi khazis mimdebare   sopelshi. qvela raionshi punktsionirebs pirveladi jandatsvis tsentrebi. tanamedrove standartebis shesabamisad aris reabilitirebuli sakartvelos statsionaruli pondis  %-ze meti. maghalmtiani regionebis mosakhleobisatvis jandatsvis servisebis motsulobis da geograpiuli khelmisatsvdomobis uzrunvelsaqopad, sakhelmtsipom   saavadmqopo gamoisqida operatori kompaniebisgan da uzrunvelqo mati sruli simdzlavrit operireba. khelmisatsvdomoba.

 punktsionirebisatvis. dgheisatvis, statsionaruli datsesebulebebis  %-ze meti kerdzo mplobelobashia da titkmis qvela matgani monatsileobs sakhelmtsipo programebis gankhortsielebashi. kerdzo hospitalebs shekmnili akvt khelsaqreli garemo punktsionirebisatvis. jandatsvis sektoris dapinansebis mnishvnelovanma zrdam da saqoveltao jandatsvis programis amokmedebam kheli sheutsqo saavadmqopoebshi reinvestirebis shesadzleblobebs - inprastrukturisa da aparaturis ganakhlebas, rats dzalze mnishvnelovania patsientebistvis sameditsino momsakhurebis khariskhis gaumjobesebis tvalsazrisit. am politikis shedegad, mkholod  -  tslebshi kveqanashi   akhali kerdzo klinika gaikhsna, rats stsori jandatsviti strategiis kidev erti dadasturebaa. sakhelmtsipo khels utsqobs parmatsevtul sek­ torshi da kerdzo sadazghvevo bazarze jansaghi konkurentsiis ganvitarebas. gansakutrebuli quradgheba etmoba sameditsino 
 momsakhurebis khariskhisa da normebis shesrulebis sakitkhebs.

 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sotsialuri ganvitareba gaumjobesda devnilta uplebebis datsva. gaukmda   tslamde arsebuli sakhelisuplebo praktika, romelits martlzomier mplobelobashi arsebuli satskhovrebeli partebidan devnilta idzulebit gamosakhlebas da tbilisshi devnilta gansakhlebis akrdzalvas itvalistsinebda. gaormagda devnilta shemtseoba. aktiurad mimdinareobs devnilta satskhovrebeli partebit uzrunvelqopis protsesi. prioritetebis mikhedvit kanonmdeblobit gansazghvrulia obiekturi kriteriumebi, romelta sapudzvelze devnils an devnil ojakhs enicheba upiratesoba satskhovrebeli sakhlis mighebisas. daikhura   ngrevis saprtkhis matarebeli obiekti da am obiektebshi mtskhovrebma  -ma devnilma ojakhma satskhovrebeli bina reabilitirebul an akhalashenebul korpusebshi miigho. soplad sakhlis proektis parglebshi, saministrom   devnil ojakhs, kholo ipotekuri seskhit sakhlis shedzenis proektis parglebshi -   devnil ojakhs sheudzina sakhli, reabilitirebul da akhalashenebul korpusebshi satskhovrebeli parti ki    -ze metma devnilma ojakhma miigho. satskhovrebeli shenobebis reabilitatsiis programis parglebshi, saministrom munitsipalitetebis tanadapinansebit reabilitatsia chautara   obiekts.    -ze met devnil ojakhs daukanonda satskhovrebeli partebi da es protsesi grdzeldeba. sakhelmtsipom devnili ojakhebistvis sotsialuri paketebis gankhortsielebashi (kira, ertjeradi puladi dakhmareba da skhv.)   milion larze meti dakharja. devniltatvis srulad daipara martlzomier mplobelobashi gadatsemul satskhovrebel partebshi arsebuli elektroenergiisa da bunebrivi airis davalianeba.

 shetsqvita 
 ekomigrantebis usaprtkho adgilebshi gansakhlebis 
 programa.   tslidan, „kartulma otsnebam“ daitsqo ekomigrantebis gansakhleba akhali kriteriumebit. am khnis ganmavlobashi, saministrom  -ze meti sakhli sheidzina ekomigranti ojakhebistvis da daitsqo satskhovrebeli sakhlebis dakanonebis protsesi mattvis, visats sakhlebi sakhelmtsipom   tslamde sheudzina. am programis parglebshi,   ekomigranti ojakhi ukve gakhda satskhovrebeli sakhlis mesakutre. sakhlebisa da mitsis nakvetebis dakanonebis protsesi grdzeldeba da tslis bolomde satskhovrebeli partis mesakutre  -mde ekomigranti ojakhi gakhdeba. „kartuli otsneba“ akhortsielebda tanmimdevrul politikas demograpiuli mdgomareobis gasaumjobeseblad. shemushavda demograpiuli usaprtkhoebis kontseptsia da gatarda konkretuli ghonisdziebebi demograpiis gasaumjobeseblad. sakhelmtsipo gansakutrebul quradghebas utmobs mtashi arsebul demograpiul problemebs. shemushavda akhali sakhelmtsipo politika khandazmulebistvis. shedegad, kveqanam miigho pozitiuri demograpiuli tsvlilebebi: gaumjobesda bunebrivi matebis machvenebeli, iklo bavshvta sikvdilianobam, shemtsirda abortebis raodenoba, gaizarda kortsinebata ritskhvi. gansakutrebit gazrdilia mesame da shemdegi akhalshobilebis raodenoba im regionebshi, sadats khortsieldeba mattvis pinansuri dakhmareba. 
 sheikmna kanonmdebloba, romlis mizania titoeuli dasakmebulistvis shromis ghirseuli pirobebis uzrunvelqopa. represiuli narkopolitika chanatsvlda sakhel­mtsipos dabalansebuli narkopolitikit. mnishvnelovnad gaizarda jandatsvis servisebze khelmisatsvdomoba damokidebuli pirebisatvis. gaukmda zedozirebis shemtkhvevebis sameditsino personalis mier politsiisatvis tsnobebis praktika. sakhelmtsipos mier mighebuli zomebis shedegad, kveqanashi  %-it shemtsirda kustaruli narkotikebis, kholo  %-ze metit - e.ts. „bionarkotikis“ mokhmareba. narkotikuli danashaulisa da narkotranzitis tsinaaghmdeg brdzolam upretsedento masshtabebs miaghtsia. ganisazghvra parmatsevtis pasukhismgebloba psikotropuli medikamentebis uretseptod gatsemaze. daitsqo politikis shemushaveba azartul tamashebze arasrultslovanta khelmisatsvdomobis shemtsirebis miznit. „kartuli otsnebis“ sotsialuri datsvis politikis dziritadi printsipebia: sighatakis dadzleva da sigharibis shemtsireba, sotsialuri dakhmarebis sistemis epektianoba, samartlianoba da gamchvirvaloba, dasakmebis motivatsiis gazrda da khelshetsqoba. mosakhleobis sotsialuri mdgomareobis shemdgomi gaumjobesebis miznit: - daikhvetseba sotsialuri datsvis sistema; uzrunvelqopili ikneba sistemis punktsionireba obiektur kriteriumebze daqrdnobit imgvarad, rom gamoiritskhos subiekturi paktorebi; gamkatsrdeba monitoringis sistema; - dainergeba dagrovebiti sapensio sistemis akhali modeli, romelits gakhdeba sapensio asakshi ghirseuli arsebobis garantia. dagrovebiti sistema guliskhmobs tanadapinansebas dasakmebulis, damsakmeblisa da sakhelmtsipo biujetis mkhridan; - dainergeba sakhelmtsipo programa - „tskhovreba grdzeldeba“, romlis parglebshi kerdzo kompaniebi tsakhalisdebian sapensio asakis kvalipitsiuri pirebis dasakmebisatvis; - khelisupleba gaagrdzelebs devnilta satskho­ vrebeli partebit uzrunvelqopis epektian politikas. ukve mimdinareobs da uakhloes momavalshi dasruldeba iseti msheneblobebi, rogoritsaa zugdidshi   tormetsartuliani korpusi   ojakhistvis, kutaisshi   tekvsmetsartuliani korpusi   ojakhistvis, gorshi   atsartuliani korpusi   ojakhistvis, tsqaltuboshi   atsartuliani korpusi   ojakhistvis da mtskhetashi   korpusi   devnili ojakhistvis. damatebit,   tsels gorshi damtavrdeba  -biniani akhladashenebuli korpusis remonti, borjomshi ki  - biniani korpusis reabilitatsia. mokhdeba  -mde binis shesqidva menasheneebisgan tbilissa da skhva did kalakebshi. soplad sakhlis proektis parglebshi mokhdeba sul mtsire   devnili ojakhistvis 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sotsialuri ganvitareba satskhovrebeli sakhlis shedzena.    -ze met devnil ojakhs, romelsats sakutrebashi akvs gadatsemuli satskhovrebeli parti, agretve mat mier shekmnil binatmesakutreta amkhanagobebs sakutrebashi gadaetsemat saerto sargeblobis partebits (skhvenebi, sardapebi da skhv.). gagrdzeldeba kerdzo mesakutreebisgan im satskhovrebeli partebis gamosqidva, romlebits devnilebs akvt dakavebuli. am proektis parglebshi, sul mtsire   devnili ojakhi binit dakmaqopildeba. paralelurad, mimdinareobs mushaoba, erti mkhriv, donorebtan, kholo, meore mkhriv, investorebtan, rata kerdzo da sajaro partniorobis parglebshi ashendes akhali satskhovreblebi devnilebistvis rogorts kalakebshi, ise soplad. mnishvnelovnad gadzlierdeba mtsire sametsarmeo sakmianobisa da devnilta kooperatsiis khelshetsqoba sakhelmtsipos mkhridan. gagrdzeldeba ekomigranti ojakhebistvis satskhovrebeli sakhlebisa da mitsis nakvetebis dakanonebis protsesi. dagegmilia kveqnis masshtabit  -mde ekomigranti ojakhistvis sakhlebis shedzena; - demograpiuli mdgomareobis gaumjobesebis miznit, gadzlierdeba shesabamisi sakhelmtsipo institutebis roli; sakhelmtsipo tsaakhalisebs mravalshvilianobas; momzaddeba sotsialuri paketi mravalshviliani mshoblistvis; gadzlierdeba saqoveltao jandatsvisa da skhvadaskhva sotsialuri programebi demograpiuli mdgomareobis optimizatsiis tvalsazrisit. gadzlierdeba khandazmulta politikis skhvadaskhva mimartulebebi, gadzlierdeba shin movlis programebi. problemebis mkone ojakhebtan mimartebashi gaizrdeba sotsialuri mushakis roli; - mokhdeba sasjelis liberalizatsia msubuki narkotikebis mokhmarebastan mimartebit. sakhelmtsipo gaaumjobesebs narkodamokidebuli pirebisatvis jandatsvis servisebis khelmisatsvdomobasa da khariskhs. preventsiuli programebit, sakhelmtsipo uzrunvelqops narkotikebis ukanono mokhmarebashi adamianebis, gansakutrebit - akhalgazrdebis chabmis tavidan aridebas; - sakhelmtsipo, evrokavshiris tsevri sakhelmtsipoebis sauketeso praktikis gatvalistsinebit, shei­ mushavebs regulatsiebs azartuli tamashebis khelmisatsvdomobis shezghudvis kutkhit, gansa­ kutrebit arasrultslovnebtan da damokidebul pirebtan mimartebashi. gamkatsrdeba sakhelmtsipo kontroli regulatsiebis shesrulebaze. gadzli­ erdeba preventsiuli saganmanatleblo komponenti, rata tavidan avitsilot mosakhleobis parto penebis, gansakutrebit akhalgazrdebis, azartul tamashebshi chabma; - khelisupleba ganakhortsielebs kmedit dasa­ kmebis politikas. saamisod gadzlierdeba inst­ itutsiuri mekanizmi da uzrunvelqopili ikneba mchidro koordinatsia samushaos madziebelta da damsakmebelta shoris. sakhelmtsipo permanentulad 
 ganakhortsielebs shromis bazris detalur kvlevas da inpormatsiul dakhmarebas gautsevs samushaos madzieblebs propesiis archevis, momzadebisa da gadamzadebis kutkhit. sakhelmtsipo aktiurad sheutsqobs khels potentsiuri damsakmeblebis chartulobas propesiuli gadamzadebis protsesshi.  . . ganatleba ganatlebis sistemis ganvitareba „kartuli otsnebis“ ert-erti umnishvnelovanesi prioritetia. chveni mizania imgvari sistemis chamoqalibeba, romelits bavshvebis, akhalgazrdebisa da zrdasrulebis satanado teoriuli tsodnit aghchurvisa da praktikuli unarebis gamomushavebastan ertad, uzrunvelqops erovnuli da zogadsakatsobrio ghirebulebebis sighrmiseulad gaazrebas, mati samokalako tsnobierebis amaghlebas.   tslis shemdeg, ganatlebis speroshi gankho­ rtsielda umnishvnelovanesi tsvlilebebi. mtavrobam ganatleba prioritetad gamoatskhada.   tslis ganmavlobashi, ganatlebis dapinanseba   mln larit gaizarda. ganatlebis sistemis martvis avtoritaruli praktika chaanatsvla martvis demokratiulma praktikam.   tslidan, daitsqo ganatlebis sistemis martvis depolitizatsia. dghes saganma­ natleblo datsesebulebebs rogorts kanon­mdeb­ lobit, ise paktobrivad, garantirebuli akvt akademiuri, administratsiuli da pinansuri avtonomia; gankhortsielda mandaturis samsakhuris dzireuli reporma, ris shedegadats moikhsna politikuri tsnekhi da mandaturis mtavari punktsia bavshvis usaprtkhoebaze zrunva gakhda. sagrdznoblad gaizarda saministros mushaobis gamchvirvalobis khariskhi; mnishvnelovnad daikhvetsa ganatlebis sistemis martvisa da dapinansebis mekanizmebi; gaizarda ganatlebis khelmisatsvdomoba; kmediti nabijebi gadaidga ganatlebis khariskhis gaumjobesebis mimartulebit. sistemuri tsvlilebebi gankhortsielda adreuli da skolamdeli ganatlebis sistemashi. sakhelmtsipo 
 srulad apinansebs adreul da skolamdel ganatlebas sajaro datsesebulebebshi, ris shedegadats kveqnis masshtabit  %-it gaizarda aghsazrdelebis ritskhvi. pirvelad sheikmna kanoni „skolamdeli aghzrdisa da ganatlebis shesakheb“ da ganisazghvra sakartveloshi adreuli da skolamdeli aghzrdisa da ganatlebis saqoveltao khelmisatsvdomobis, ganvitarebisa da standartebis uzrunvelqopis samartlebrivi sapudzvlebi. kanonis shesabamisad, skolamdel datsesebulebebshi ganatleba da aghzrda gakhdeba ertiani protsesi. gaeros printsipebis shesabamisad, bavshvis sauketeso interesebis gatvalistsinebit, gansazghvrulia ganatlebis, usaprtkhoebis, kvebis, higienis, inprastrukturisa da materialur-teknikuri bazis maghali standartebi, romelits savaldebuloa qvela sajaro tu kerdzo skolamdeli datsesebulebistvis. mnishvnelovani repormebi gatarda zogadi ganatlebis speroshi.   tseltan shedarebit,

 sotsialuri ganvitareba momdevno   tslis ganmavlobashi, gankhortsieldeba sistemuri tsvlilebebi, rata ganatlebisa da metsnierebis sistema gakhdes chveni kveqnis demokratiuli, ekonomikuri da sotsialuri ganvitarebis mqari sapudzveli. uzrunvelqopili ikneba utsqveti ganatleba. ganatlebis sistema ikneba khariskhze, khelmisatsvdomobasa da inkluziaze orientirebuli. kmediti nabijebi gadaidgmeba imisatvis, rom sakartvelos ganatlebis sistemam regionshi lideris pozitsiebi daikavos da regionul saganmanatleblo tsentrad gadaiktses. adreuli da skolamdeli ganatleba 
 - saqoveltao khelmisatsvdomobis gazrdis miznit, sajaro datsesebulebebshi adreuli da skolamdeli ganatleba darcheba upaso; - adreuli da skolamdeli ganatlebis tanabari maghali khariskhis uzrunvelsaqopad, qvela sajaro da kerdzo adreul da skolamdel datsesebulebashi   tslidan amokmeddeba ertiani khariskhis standartebi, sakhelmtsipo saganmanatleblo standartebi, inprastrukturisa da materialurteknikuri bazis maghali standartebi, kvebisa da higienis ertiani standarti. uzrunvelqopili ikneba usaprtkhoeba da aradzaladobriv garemo; - amokmeddeba aghmzrdelebisa da aghmzrdelpedagogebis akhali propesiuli standarti. daitsqeba aghmzrdelisa da aghmzrdel-pedagogis propesiebis popularizatsia, kvalipitsiuri kadrebis momzadeba da propesiashi akhalgazrda kadrebis mozidva, agretve skolamdel ganatlebashi dasakmebulta motivatsiis amaghleba sotsialuri garantiebis gaumjobesebit; - gadzlierdeba

- tavisupali gakvetilebi, romelits mostsa­ vleebis interesebze ikneba morgebuli, gakhdeba saskolo tskhovrebis ganuqopeli natsili. sakhelmtsipo khels sheutsqobs mostsavleta mrava­ lperovan aktivobebs da proektebs, romlebits mat daekhmareba analitikuri, kreatiuli, shemokmedebiti da inovatsiuri azrovnebis, gunduri mushaobisa da liderobisa da sametsarmeo unarebis, aseve samokalako da sotsialuri kompetentsiebis ganvitarebashi, tsaakhalisebs jansaghi tskhovrebis tsessa da sportul aktivobebs;  propesiuli ganatleba - propesiuli ganatlebis sistemashi dainergeba 
 dualuri stsavlebis midgoma sajaro-kerdzo partniorobis gzit, sadats kvalipitsiuri 
 kadrebis mosamzadeblad sakhelmtsipo da satsarmo gainatsileben kompetentsiebs, propesiuli ganat­­lebis teoriuli da satsarmoo praktikis komponentebis mimartulebit; - shromis bazris kvlevis sapudzvelze, sakhelmtsipo gansazghvravs propesiuli ganatlebis tsal­ keul prioritetul mimartulebebs da uzrunvelqops damsakmeblebis srulpasovan chartvas propesiuli programebis shemushavebis, gankhortsielebisa da studentta shepasebis pro­ tsesebshi; - propesiuli ganatleba pokusirebuli ikneba, rogorts mozardebisa da akhalgazrdebis, ise zrdasrulebis saganmanatleblo sachiroebebze. sheikmneba zrdasrulta ganatlebis sistema. kerdzo sektortan tanamshromlobit amokmeddeba propesiuli momzadeba-gadamzadebis mraval­ perovani programebi. paralelurad, sheikmneba propesiuli ganatlebidan umaghles ganatlebashi gadasvlis moknili mekanizmebi, sistema gakhdeba upro ghia da inkluziuri; - dasakmebisatvis sachiro unarebis ganvitarebis paralelurad, samushao adgilebis shekmnis stimulirebisa da kerdzo sektoris gadzlierebis miznit, aseve prioriteti ikneba sametsarmeo ganatleba. propesiis dauplebastan ertad, studentebi istsavlian metsarmeobas. amgvarad, momzaddeba mtsodne kadri, romelits dasakmebis garda, sakhelmtsipos tu sabanko sektoris mier gatarebul sametsarmeo sakmianobis mkhardamcher ghonisdziebebshi (konkursebi, dapinansebebi, startapebis tsakhaliseba) monatsileobas da biznesis datsqebas sakutari propesiis shesabamisad shedzlebs; - amokmeddeba evropuli midgomebis shesabamisad momzadebuli khariskhis uzrunvelqopis modeli da erovnuli kvalipikatsiis charcho, rats khels sheutsqobs studentta da dasakmebulta mobilobas da utsqveti ganatlebis sistemis chamoqalibebas; propesiul saganmanatleblo datsesebulebebs kheli sheetsqobat ganakhortsielon ertoblivi programebi evropul da skhva tsarmatebul sastsavleblebtan ertad, moamzadon kadrebi saertashoriso standartebis shesabamisad; - propesiuli ganatlebis mastsavleblebisatvis 
 amokmeddeba propesiuli ganvitarebis mtsqobri sistema, tsakhalisebuli ikneba mati sastsavlo vizitebi sazghvargaret. sakhelpaso politika daepudzneba tsodnis, gamotsdilebisa da mightseuli shedegebis analizs; - ashsh-isa da sakartvelos mtavrobebs shoris khelmotserili atastsleulis gamotsvevis kompa­ ktit,   mln ashsh dolari gamoiqopa  -  tslebshi, shromis bazris motkhovnebis shesabamisi saertashoriso standartis propesiuli ganat­ lebis akhali programebis danergvis mkhardacheris miznit; - ganvitardeba propesiuli saganmanatleblo datsesebulebebis inprastruktura da sajarokerdzo partniorobis pormatshi gapartovdeba arsebuli geograpiuli kseli. umaghlesi ganatleba - umaghlesi ganatlebis dapinanseba orien­ tirebuli ikneba kveqnis ganvitarebis sachiro­ ebebze, sazogadoebrivi tskhovrebis prio­rite­ tebsa da ekonomikis gadzlierebaze. shromis bazris analizis sapudzvelze ganisazghvreba da dapinansdeba umaghlesi ganatlebis priori­ tetuli mimartulebebi; - dainergeba saertashoriso standartebis shesaba­ misi umaghlesi ganatlebis khariskhis martvisa da dapinansebis akhali, epekturi modelebi; avtorizatsiisa da akreditatsiis akhali, shedegebsa da ganvitarebaze orientirebuli standartebi da protsedurebi orientirebuli ikneba khariskhis maghali standartis uzrun­velqopaze. gankhortsieldeba metsnieruli kvlevis integratsia stsavlebis protsesshi; - dainergeba 
 akhali, integrirebuli saba­ kalavro–samagistro stsavlebis modeli 
 mastsavleblis momzadebis sistemis gaumjobesebis miznit. umaghlesi ganatlebis mkone pirta­ tvis sakhelmtsipo da kerdzo umaghles saganma­ natleblo datsesebulebebshi amokmeddeba mas­tsa­ vleblis momzadebis akreditebuli ertts­liani saganmanatleblo programebi, sadats sakhel­ mtsipos mier qoveltsliurad dapinansdeba  -mde piri da kheli sheetsqoba skolebshi mat dasakmebas; - mkhardacherili ikneba spetsialuri programebi sakartveloshi da sazghvargaret sametsniero tsentrebsa da universitetebshi moghvatse tsamqvani kartveli metsnierebis umaghlesi ganatlebis sistemashi reintegratsiis miznit; - khelisupleba gansakutrebulad sheutsqobs khels umaghlesi ganatlebis protsesshi tanamedrove teknologiebis rolisa da mnishvnelobis zrdas, mat shoris, distantsiuri stsavlebis ganvitarebas; - khelisupleba khels sheutsqobs umaghlesi ganat­ lebis internatsionalizatsias da sauketeso saertashoriso gamotsdilebis gaziarebas; 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sotsialuri ganvitareba - sakartvelos regionul saganmanatleblo tsentrad pozitsionirebis miznit, gankhortsieldeba utskhoeli studentebis sakartvelos umaghles sastsavleblebshi mozidvis masshtaburi proekti „istsavle sakartveloshi“. 
 - kutaisshi ashendeba teknologiuri universiteti, romelits tsamqvani regionuli tsentri gakhdeba zusti, sabunebismetqvelo, matematikuri da sainzhinro mimartulebit. metsniereba - gankhortsieldeba mkhardamcheri ghonisdziebebi sakartvelos dzlier, regionul sametsniero tsentrad gadaktsevistvis; - kveqnis ekonomikis, strategiuli ganvitarebis motkhovnebisa da sazogadoebis sachiroebebis gatvalistsinebit mokhdeba prioritetuli sametsniero dargebis identipikatsia da mati gadzlierebis mkhardachera; - kheli 
 sheetsqoba sazghvargaret sametsniero tsentrebsa da universitetebtan sametsniero tanamshromlobas da ertoblivi proektebis gankhortsielebas, utskhoeli metsnierebis sametsniero kvlevebs sakartveloshi da kartveli metsnierebisas - msoplio mnishvnelobis sametsniero tsentrebshi, agretve kartveli metsnierebis mier utskhoel mkvlevarebtan ertoblivi kvleviti programebis gankhortsielebas. uzrunvelqopili ikneba akhalgazrdebis chartulobis khelshetsqoba metsnierebashi miznobrivi programebis danergvit;

 tanamedrove sametsniero- 
  . . kultura, sporti, akhalgazrdobis politika „kartuli otsnebis“ mmartvelobis pirobebshi mokhda kulturis, akhalgazrdobis politikisa da sportis speroebis sruli depolitizatsia.   
 tslis shemdeg, qoveltsliurad izrdeba ganvitarebistvis sakhelmtsipos mier gamoqopili dapinanseba. evropastan asotsirebis shetankhmebis tanakhmad, sakartvelos kulturisa da dzeglta datsvis saministrom sheimushava da mtavrobam daamtkitsa „kulturis strategia  “, romelits gansazghvravs sakhelmtsipos khedvas, miznebs da amotsanebs kulturis sektorshi. sakartvelo evrokavshiris aghmosavlet partniorobis kveqnebs shoris pirvelia, romelits evrokavshiris programis - „shemokmedebiti evropis“ tsevri gakhda. gaizarda sakhelovnebo umaghles sastsavleblebshi propesor-mastsavleblebis anazghaureba, mimdinareobs propesiuli programebis dapinanseba, uzrunvelqopilia sastsavleblebis studentebis utskhoetshi gagzavna.   tslidan, sarestavratsio, sakonservatsio da sareabilitatsio samushaoebi chautarda  kulturuli memkvidreobis dzegls, ristvisats daikharja   mln larze meti. kulturis 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sotsialuri ganvitareba da akhalgazrdobis sakmeta saministros mier dapudznda erovnuli sportuli pederatsiebis aghiarebis da dapinansebis sabcho, sportis speros gamchirvale punktsionirebisa da stabiluri sakhelmtsipo mkhardacheris uzrunvelqopis miznit. sakhelmtsipos mier sportis speroshi bolo   tslis mandzilze gamoiqo upretsedentod didi tankha,   milion larze meti odenobit. es tankha mokhmarda skhvadaskhva sportuli sakheobis ganvitarebas, sportuli inprastrukturis msheneblobareabilitatsias, saertashoriso sportuli ghonisdziebebis chatarebas, miznobrivi programebis gankhortsielebas, tsarmatebuli mokmedi tu veterani sportsmenebis sotsialur mkhardacheras. sakartvelom umaspindzla araert mnishvnelovan saertashoriso sportul ghonisdziebas da iktsa regionul sportul tsentrad, rats sportuli turizmis ganvitarebis ert-erti autsilebeli tsinapirobaa.   tslis shemdeg, titkmis gaormagda propesiul sportshi chabmul pirta raodenoba. ganvitarda sportuli inprastruktura. sheikmna sportuli inprastrukturis ganvitarebisatvis sakhelmtsiposa da kerdzo sektoris tanamshromlobis pretsedenti, rats khels sheutsqobs kerdzo investitsiebis mozidvas sportis speroshi da sportuli obiektebis martvis tsakhalisebas. dasrulda otsamde sruliad akhali, saertashoriso standartebis shesabamisi sportuli obiektis mshenebloba, mat shoris amierkavkasiashi pirveli sportuli kompleksi tbilisshi, romelits srulad aris adaptirebuli shshm pirtatvis. sakartvelos   munitsipalitetshi damontazhda  -mde gare savarjisho motsqobiloba. sakartvelos mtavrobam daamtkitsa „sakartveloshi sportuli inprastrukturis ganvitarebis sakhelmtsipo miznobrivi programa“. aseve shemushavda da mtavrobis mier damtkitsda „sakartveloshi pekhburtis ganvitarebis ( -  tsts.) sakhelmtsipo programa“. mnishvnelovani tsinsvla aghinishneba saertashoriso asparezze kartveli sportsmenebis tsarmatebebis kutkhit: kartvelma sportsmenebma moipoves     medali:   - okro,   - vertskhli,   - brinjao. kartveli olimpielebi rios   tslis olimpiur tamashebze tsardgnen   sportsmenit sportis   sakheobashi (orive rekorduli machvenebelia) da moipoves   okros,   vertskhlis da   brinjaos medali. aghsanishnavia, rom kartveli paraolimpielebi rios   tslis paraolimpiur tamashebze tsardgebian akamde qvelaze didi -   sportsmenis shemadgenlobit.   tslis msoplio chempionatze sakartvelos moragbeta nakrebi msoplios   sauketeso gunds shoris mokhvda da pirvelad avtomaturad moipova momdevno msoplio tasis sagzuri. amastan, sakartvelos moragbeta nakrebi istoriashi pirvelad avida msoplio reitingis me-  sapekhurze. shemushavda akhalgazrdobis politikis ganvi­ tarebis programa. sakartvelos mtavrobam daamtkitsa „sakartvelos sakhelmtsipo akhalgazrduli politikis dokumenti“ da „sakhelmtsipo akhalgazrduli politikis ganvitarebis samokmedo gegma (  –   tsts.)“. saministros da misi sakveutsqebo organizatsiebis mier ukve gankhortsielda 
  -mde proekti, romelta ushualo monatsile an benepitsiari iqo    -ze meti akhalgazrda. aktiurad mushaobs saministros bavshvta da akhalgazrdobis ganvitarebis pondi. pondis erterti umtavresi misiaa bavshvta da akhalgazrduli organizatsiebis inovatsiuri proektebis mkhardachera, romelta shoris akhalgazrdebis dasakmebis khelshetsqoba sotsialuri metsarmeobis proektebis dapinansebis gzit (gansakutrebit regionebshi) pondis umnishvnelovanes prioritetad iktsa. bolo   tslis mandzilze, pondis mier dapinansda   sotsialuri metsarmeobis proekti. saerto jamshi,   tslis mandzilze, pondma daapinansa  -ze meti proekti, romelta jamurma ghirebulebam daakhloebit  ,  mln lari sheadgina. aghsanishnavia, rom dapinansebuli proektebis  %-ze meti regionebshi gankhortsielda. punktsionirebs bavshvta da akhalgazrdobis erovnuli tsentri, romlis misiaa gansakutrebuli sachiroebebis mkone jgupebze zrunvis khelshetsqoba, bavshvebis da akhalgazrdobis intelektualuri, pirovnuli, propesiuli da pizikuri potentsialis gamovlenis da ganvitarebisatvis shesabamisi pirobebis shekmna, bavshvta da akhalgazrduli turizmis ganvitarebis khelshetsqoba da skhv. tsentris proektebs shoris, aghsanishnavia anakliisa da shaoris momavlis banakebi. aghsanishnavia saministros da misi sakveutsqebo organizatsiebis tanamshromloba arasamtavrobo sektortan, aseve arasamtavrobo sektoris monatsileoba akhalgazrduli politikis shemushavebis protsesshi, risi dasturitsaa ertoblivad shemushavebuli akhalgazrduli sakmianobis ganvitarebis strategia. momdevno   tslis ganmavlobashi, kulturis, sportisa da akhalgazrduli politikis speroshi gatardeba shemdegi ghonisdziebebi: kultura • gaizrdeba kulturisa da dzeglta datsvis speros dapinanseba; • daikhvetseba kulturasa da dzeglta datsvastan dakavshirebuli kanonmdebloba. shemushavdeba kulturuli memkvidreobis kodeksi, romelits shekmnis kulturuli memkvidreobis datsvis satanado sakanonmdeblo sapudzvlebs. shemu­ shavdeba kvelmokmedebis shesakheb kanoni, romelits uzrunvelqops kulturis speros dapinansebis alternatiuli gzebis modziebas da dapinansebis diversipikatsias; • kulturis martva upro ghia, gamchvirvale da inkluziuri gakhdeba. gaizrdeba ekspertta da propesionalta chartuloba gadatsqvetilebis mighebis, dargobrivi strategiebis shemushavebis protsesshi; • gaizrdeba kulturis khelmisatsvdomoba parto sazogadoebisatvis, gansakutrebit regionebis mosakhleobistvis, etnikuri umtsiresobebisa da shshm pirebisatvis. gankhortsieldeba inpras­ trukturuli proektebi kulturis da dzeglta datsvis memkvidreobis shesanarchuneblad. mokhdeba kulturis popularizatsia mosakhleobis 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sotsialuri ganvitareba parto penebisatvis, kheli sheetsqoba mediisa da mautsqeblis potentsialis gamoqenebas kulturisa da shemokmedebiti sektoris popularizatsiisa da ganvitarebisatvis; • mokhdeba 
 kulturis integrireba skhva dargebis, gansakutrebit ekonomikur politikashi. gadzlierdeba komunikatsia kulturis 
 speros mushakebsa da biznesstrukturebs shoris, partnioroba sakhelmtsipo da kerdzo sektorebs shoris. kheli sheetsqoba kulturis speros potentsialis sametsarmeo mimartulebit atvisebas, mat shoris retsvis traditsiuli erovnuli mimartulebit. programa „shemokmedebiti sakartvelos“ parglebshi, sakhelmtsipo khels sheutsqobs shemokmedebiti industriebis ganvitarebistvis sachiro sivrtseebsa da datsesebulebebs: laboratoriebs, inkubatorebs. shemushavdeba shemokmedebiti industriebis tsakhalisebis mekanizmebi. gaumjobesdeba kulturis saeksporto potentsialis atviseba, aseve kartuli kulturis internatsionalizatsia da misi globalur kontekstshi tsarmochena; • gankhortsieldeba proektebi digitizatsiis khelshesatsqobad;

 akhalgazrdobis politika - gadzlierdeba 
 akhalgazrduli sakmianobis mkhardachera sakhelmtsipos mkhridan, mat shoris 
 arapormaluri saganmanatleblo programebis, hobi-ganatlebisa da rekreatsiuli proektebis dapinansebis kutkhit; 
 - gaizrdeba adgilobrivi tvitmmartvelobebis ro­li akhalgazrduli politikis mimartulebit; - gaizrdeba sotsialuri satsarmoebis dapinanseba, gansakutrebit - regionebshi; - ashendeba   akhali akhalgazrduli banaki; - akhalgazrduli turizmis khelshetsqobis miznit gaormagdeba kempingtsentrebis da turistuli bilikebis raodenoba; gaormagdeba sotsialuri tu akhalgazrduli kapeebis raodenoba; - gaghrmavdeba evrokavshirtan tanamshromloba akhalgazrdobis mobilobis, mokhaliseobis khelshetsqobis da arasamtavrobo organizatsiebis ganvitarebis miznit; - gaumjobesdeba 
 arasamtavrobo sektortan tanamshromloba akhalgazrduli proektebis 
 khelshetsqobisa da ganvitarebistvis; 
 - gaizrdeba shshm pirebis inkluziaze orientirebuli arapormaluri ganatlebis programebis mkhar­ dachera, mat shoris mat dasakmebaze orientirebuli proektebis raodenoba. 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva  . sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva kveqnis grdzelvadiani, mshvidobiani da mdg­ radi ganvitarebis sapudzveli usaprtkhoebis, stabilurobisa da ketildgheobis uzrunvelqopaa. chveni mizania tanamedrove, stabiluri, ganvi­ tarebuli demokratiis evropuli sakhelmtsipos aghmsheneblobis protsesis gagrdzeleba da misi khariskhobrivad upro maghal doneze aqvana. am miznis mightsevis sauketeso gza kveqnis evropuli integratsiaa. sakartvelo rtul da tsvalebad geopolitikur garemoshi imqopeba. arsebuli globaluri da regionuli gamotsvevebis gatvalistsinebit, kveqnis suverenitetisa da usaprtkhoebis ganmtkitsebisatvis sakartvelos nato-shi integratsias da ashsh-tan, rogorts mtavar strategiul partniortan, tanamshromlobis shemdgom gaghrmavebas alternativa ara akvs. aghnishnuli mimartulebebit saertashoriso tanamshromlobis gaghrmaveba kveqnis grdzelvadiani ekonomikuri ganvitarebis autsilebeli komponentis - stabiluri da prognozirebadi politikurekonomikuri garemos pormirebis shesadzleblobas idzleva. kveqanashi stabiluri da prognozirebadi garemos pormirebis obiekturi sachiroeba aseve ualternativos khdis rusetidan momavali saprtkheebis minimizatsiisa da ratsionaluri politikis autsileblobas, kveqnis deokupatsiis, teritoriuli mtlianobisa da strategiuli interesebis datmobis gareshe. kveqnis evropuli da evroatlantikuri integratsiis gagrdzelebisa da rusettan ratsionaluri politikis tsarmartvis sapudzvelze usaprtkho da stabiluri garemos chamoqalibeba, kveqnis sainvestitsio mimzidvelobis zrdisa da evrokavshirtan ghrma da qovlismomtsveli tavisupali vachrobit ganpirobebuli sargeblis maksimalurad epektianad gamoqenebis satsindars tsarmoadgens. qovelive es sakartvelos mosakhleobis ketildgheobis amaghlebisa da zogadad, kveqnis grdzelvadiani ganvitarebis autsilebeli tsinapirobaa. zemoaghnishnuli miznis misaghtsevad, chveni sagareo politikis prioritetebia: - usaprtkhoebisa da suverenitetis ganmtkitseba, deokupatsia da teritoriuli mtlianobis aghdgena; - evropuli da evroatlantikuri integratsia; - kveqnis tavdatsvisunarianobis gadzliereba; - amerikis sheertebul shtatebtan tanamshromlobis gaghrmaveba; 
 strategiuli 
 - rusetis pederatsiastan konpliktis mshvidobiani daregulireba; - mezobel da urtiertobebis 
 regionis ganmtkitseba 
 sakhelmtsipoebtan da strategiuli 
 proektebis ganvitareba; - sakartvelos ekonomikuri mimzidvelobisa da kulturis popularizatsia msoplio masshtabit; - sazghvargaret mqopi sakartvelos mokalakeebis uplebebis datsva da diasporastan mchidro kavshirebis ganmtkitseba.  . . usaprtkhoebisa da suverenitetis ganmtkitseba, deokupatsia da teritoriuli mtlianobis aghdgena kveqnis usaprtkhoebisa da suverenitetis ganmtkitseba, deokupatsia da teritoriuli mtlianobis aghdgena mkholod mshvidobiani gzit aris shesadzlebeli. am mimartulebit gasuli otkhi tslis ganmavlobashi aktiuri mushaoba mimdinareobda. sakartvelos
