 gatarda 
 sakartvelos 
 okupirebuli teritoriebis shemdgomi aghiare­ bis riskebis minimumamde shesamtsireblad. 
 kerdzod, gagrdzelda diplomatiuri urtiertobebis damqarebis protsesi shoreuli regionebis kveqnebtan, ganeitralda rusetis intensiuri dzaliskhmeva saertashoriso asparezze okupirebuli regionebis „damoukideblobis“ aghiarebis mimartulebit. mnishvnelovani dzaliskhmevis shedegad, mokherkhda   tsels vanuatus, kholo   tsels tuvalus mier sakartelos okupirebuli regionebis 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva damoukideblobis aghiarebis ukan gatsveva da orive kveqnis mier sakartvelostan diplomatiuri urtiertobebis damqareba. shedegad, khutidan samamde shemtsirda im sakhelmtsipota raodenoba, romlebmats, rusetis kvaldakval, sakartvelos okupirebuli regionebis damoukidebloba aghiares. sakartvelos aktiuri diplomatiuri nabijebis shedegad, mightseul ikna upretsedento shedegebi qvela shesabamisi saertashoriso organizatsiis parglebshi sakartvelos teritoriuli mtlianobis, suverenitetis, okupirebul teritoriebze matskhovrebelta da idzulebit gadaadgilebul pirta dabrunebis uplebebtan dakavshirebit 
 saertashoriso sazogadoebis mtkitse pozitsiis konsolidatsiis kutkhit: 
 -   tsels pirvelad da mas shemdeg qoveltsliurad evropis sabchos ministrta komiteti ganikhilavs da ighebs gadatsqvetilebebs sakitkhze: „evropis sabcho da konplikti sakartveloshi“, romelshits khazgasmitaa aghnishnuli, rom sakartvelos regionebis - apkhazeti da tskhinvalis regioni/ samkhret oseti - mimart rusetis pederatsiis mier gankhortsielebuli nabijebi, gansakutrebit aliansisa da strategiuli partniorobis/ integratsiis shesakheb e.ts. khelshekrulebebis dadeba dzirs utkhris regionshi usaprtkhoebisa da stabilurobis gamqarebisken mimartul dzaliskhmevas, ashkarad arghvevs sakartvelos suverenitetsa da teritoriul mtlianobas. shesabamisad, ministrta moadgileebis komiteti moutsodebs rusetis pederatsias, sheacheros da gaaukmos es protsesi da daemorchilos saertashoriso samartlis valdebulebebs, mat shoris   tslis   agvistos tsetskhlis shetsqvetis shesakheb shetankhmebas da mis   tslis   sektembris saimplementatsio ghonisdziebebs.   tslis gadatsqvetilebashi khazgasmulia, rom rusetis pederatsia aris am teritoriebze paktobrivi kontrolis ganmakhortsielebeli sakhelmtsipo; -   tslis   ivliss, tbilisshi mimdinare eutos saparlamento asambleis  -e sesiis parglebshi mighebul ikna kartuli mkharis mier initsirebuli rezolutsia sakheltsodebit „konplikti sakartveloshi“; -   tslis   ivniss, gaero-s adamianis uplebata sabchos  -e sesiis parglebshi, pirvelad gaketda gantskhadeba sakartvelos apkhazetisa da tskhinvalis regionebshi adamianis uplebebisa da humanitaruli mdgomareobis shesakheb, romelsats   sakhelmtsipo sheuertda; - evrokavshirtan mchidro tanamshromlobit, grdzeldeba evrokavshiris sadamkvirveblo misia sakartveloshi, romelits am etapze tsarmoadgens ertadert saertashoriso mekanizms konpliktis monitoringis kutkhit sakartvelos teritoriaze. ert-erti 
 umnishvnelovanesi 
 prioritetia 
 idzu­lebit gadaadgilebul pirta menturi uplebis datsva da mati 
 punda­ 
 sakutar 
 sakhlebshi nebaqoplobit, usaprtkhod da ghirseulad dabrunebis uzrunvelqopa, rats kvlav ugulvebelqopilia saokupatsio rezhimis mkhridan. kartuli mkharis dzaliskhmevit, aghnishnuli sakitkhi dgas da shenarchundeba saertashoriso diskusiebis dghis tsesrigshi da saertashoriso tanamegobrobis quradghebis tsentrshi, vidre ar ikneba mightseuli am pundamenturi uplebis realizeba. bolo tslebshi, gaizarda gaeros generalur asambleaze „apkhazetidan, sakartvelo da tskhinvalis regionidan/samkhret oseti, sakartvelo idzulebit gadaadgilebul pirta da ltolvilta statusis shesakheb” (shesastsorebelia) rezolutsiis mkhardamcherta raodenoba.   tsels rezolutsias mkhari  -ma,   tsels -  -m,   tsels -  -ma, kholo   tsels -  -ma sakhelmtsipom dauchira.   tsels mkhardamcherta raodenobam pirvelad gadaacharba im kveqnebis ritskhvs, romeltats tavi sheikaves, rats tskhadqops, rom sakartvelos aktiuri diplomatiis shedegad, saertashoriso tanamegobroba sul upro natlad atsnobierebs sakartvelos okupirebuli regionebidan idzulebit gadaadgilebul pirta mudmiv satskhovrebel adgilas dabrunebis pundamenturi uplebis datsvis (aghdgenis) mnishvnelobas.   tslis oktombershi sakartvelos mtavrobis dadgenilebit shekmnili sakhelmtsipo komisiis parglebshi mavtulkhlartebis da skhva bari­ 
 kadebis siakhloves mtskhovrebi mosakhleobis sachiroebebze reagireba sakhelmtsipom ert-ert 
 prioritetad daisakha, iseti rtuli gamotsvevebis ponze, rogoritsaa ukanono dakavebebi, gadaadgilebis tavisuplebis da sameurneo mitsebze tsvdomis shezghudva da a.sh. mati mdgomareobis gasaumjobeseblad da tslebis ganmavlobashi dagrovili problemebis gadasachrelad, mnishvnelovani nabijebi gadaidga. 
 mimdinareobda mushaoba adamianis uplebebis saertashoriso mekanizmis amokmedebisatvis okupirebul teritoriebze, risi sachiroebats gansakutrebit kritikulia akhalgoris da galis raionis mosakhleobisatvis, romlis uplebebi ukheshad irghveva da izghudeba, mat shoris galshi mshobliur, kartul enaze ganatlebis mighebis sheudzleblobis sakhit, rats gansakutrebit mtkivneulia mosakhleobisatvis.   tslidan daitsqo kvartaluri angarishebis momzadeba sakartvelos okupirebul teritoriebze adamianis uplebata mdgomareobis shesakheb, rats miznad isakhavs saertashoriso tanamegobrobis inpormirebas sakartvelos okupirebul teritoriebze am mimartulebit arsebuli mdgomareobis shesakheb. sakartvelos khelisupleba epekturad akhortsielebda “okupirebuli teritoriebis 
 mimart” sakartvelos sakhelmtsipo strategias, 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva nabijebi skhvadaskhva servisis khelmisatsvdomobis gazrdiskenats. magalitad, zugdidis raionis sopel rukhshi moetsqo mskhvili savachro kompleksi da   tslistvis dasruldeba mshenebloba mravalpropiliani sameditsino klinikisa, romelits mteli regionistvis, mat shoris okupirebuli teritoriebis matskhovreblebisatvis, saintereso da mimzidvel obiektad iktseva. gaaktiurda kontaktebi, gansakutrebit samo­ kalako sazogadoebisa da sakhalkho diplomtiis khazit. 
 gadaidga mnishvnelovani humanitaruli khasiatis nabijebi, rogoritsaa tsiteli jvris shuamavlobit konpliktis shedegad ugzo-ukvlod dakargulta samarkhebis modziebis, neshtebis identipitsirebisa da gadasvenebis protsesis tsarmartva, patimrobashi mqopi pirebis gatsvla, garemos datsvisken, kerdzod, kolkhuri bzis gadarchenisken mimartuli aktivobebis gankhortsieleba, saarkivo masalebis mitsodeba da a.sh. mchidro tanamshromloba samshvidobo protsesis mimart mkhardacheris mobilizebis miznit, rogorts ormkhriv, ise saertashoriso pormatebshi. mnishvnelovania iseti aktorebis epekturi chartuloba, rogorebits arian: evrokavshiri, gaero, euto, ashsh, evrosabcho da skhva partniorebi, romelta midgoma kveqnis suverenitetis da teritoriuli mtlianobis, saertashoriso samartlis printsipebis da adamianis uplebebis pativistsemas epudzneba. 
 dapirispirebebis dadzlevis, ndobis aghdgenisa da sherigebis amotsanebis misaghtsevad, 
 sadats aseve mnishvnelovania sakhalkho diplomatiis da samokalako sazogadoebis, sazogadoebrivi moghvatseebis, shereuli ojakhebis, kalebis, akhalgazrdebis roli; - tsaakhalisebs konpliktit dashorishorebul khalkhtashoris kontaktebs, saerto interesebze dapudznebul tanamshromlobas, rats khelovnuri gamqopi khazebis orive mkhares mtskhovrebi mosakhleobis humanitarul da pragmatul sachiroebebs, propesiuli jgupebis tu skhvadaskhva dargis ekspertebis (ekologebis, kulturis moghvatseebis, zhurnalistebis, meditsinis mushakebis da a.sh.) tanamshromlobis interesebs ukavshirdeba; - gaagrdzelebs 
 konpliktit dazaralebul adamianebze, mat shoris devnilebze zrunvas, 
 okupirebul teritoriebsa da saokupatsio khazis siakhloves mtskhovrebi mosakhleobis uplebebisa da usaprtkhoebis datsvas da mati mdgomareobis gaumjobesebas da am amotsanis shesasruleblad: 
 tsarimarteboda 
 partniorebtan 
 gaagrdzelebs da gaaaktiurebs qvela shesabamisi pormatis da instrumentis gamoqenebas devnilta dabrunebis ganu­ qopeli uplebis datsvisa da am uplebis realizebistvis; 
 gaaaktiurebs mushaobas okupirebul teri­ toriebze adamianis uplebata moni­ 
 toringisa da datsvis saertashoriso mekanizmebis amokmedebisatvis, aseve 
 chven gavagrdzelebt saertashoriso tanamegobrobis dzaliskhmevis shemdgom konsolidatsias da tanmimdevruli, mshvidobiani da pragmatuli politikis gatarebas usaprtkhoebisa da suverenitetis ganmtkitsebis, deokupatsiisa da teritoriuli mtlianobis aghdgenis miznit. kerdzod, sakartvelos khelisupleba: - mimartavs 
 dzaliskhmevas mshvidobis uzrunve­ lqopis, usaprtkhoebis riskebisa da shesadzlo

 diplomatiur dzaliskhmevas okupirebuli regionebis araghiarebis politikis gatarebistvis; 
 - mimartavs aktiur dzaliskhmevas deokupatsiis amotsanisken, rusetis mkhridan tsetskhlis shetsqvetis shetankhmebis shesrulebis uzrunvelqopis, okupirebul teritoriebze saertashiriso usap­rtkhoebis mekanizmebis amokmedebis, ro­ gorts rusettan saertashoriso pormatshi molaparakebebis, ise saertashoriso mkhardacherisa da zetsolis mobilizebis gzit; - khels sheutsqobs pirdapir dialogs kar­ tvelebsa da apkhazebs, kartvelebsa da osebs shoris, mimartavs dinamiur dzaliskhmevas 
 okupirebul teritoriaze mtskhovrebi mosakhleobis, mat shoris, gansakutrebit, motsqvladi galis da akhalgoris raionebis matskhovrebelta usaprtkhoebis, uplebrivi da humanitaruli mdgomareobis gaumjobesebisatvis;

 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva evrokavshirtan da skhva partniorebtan tanamshromlobis pormatebidan; 
 maksimalurad gamoiqenebs qvela rele­ vantur saertashoriso platpormas sakartvelos samshvidobo politikis miznebis gankhortsielebis, kveqnis usaprtokhebis ganmtkitsebis da humanitaruli gamotsvevebis mogvarebis khelshetsqobisatvis;

 gaaaktiurebs 
 tanamshromlobas partni­ orebtan, megobar sakhelmtsipoebtan, saer­tashoriso organizatsiebtan, arasa­ mtavrobo sektortan, donor orga­ nizatsiebtan samshvidobo amotsanebis mkhardasacherad, mat shoris, omit dashorishorebul sazogadoebebs shoris pirdapiri dialogis da sherigebis protsesis tsakhalisebis, ndobis aghdgenisken mimartuli konkretuli proektebis, konpliktit dazaralebuli mosakhleobis humanitarul sachiroebebze reagirebis, sakhalkho diplomatiis da saerto interesebze dapudznebuli tanamshromlobis khelshetsqobis gzit;

 rezhi­mis 
 evrokavshirtan savizo liberalizatsiis samokmedo gegmis 
 evrokavshirs gansakutrebuli roli enicheba sakartvelos usaprtkhoebisa da teritoriuli mtlianobis mkhardacheris sakmeshi. kerdzod, evrokavshiri, gaerostan da eutostan ertad, zhenevis saertashoriso diskusiebis tanatavmjdomarea, mkhars uchers araghiarebis 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva asambleashi, „aghmosavlet partniorobis“ samo­ kalako sazogadoebis porumsa da „aghmosavlet partniorobis“ adgilobrivi da regionuli mmartvelobebis konperentsiashi. 
 amotsana da sakartvelos usaprtkhoebis ganmtkitsebisa da stabiluri ganvitarebis tsinapiroba. sakartvelo mizanmimartulad ganagrdzobs svlas nato-s tsevrobisaken. 
 sakartvelos mtavrobam, asotsirebul kveqnebs shoris ert-ertma pirvelma, uzrunvelqo evroka­ 
 bolo otkhi tslis ganmavlobashi, nato-sakar­ tvelos urtiertobebi gansakutrebulad aktiuri da shinaarsobrivad datvirtuli iqo.   tsels 
 vshirtan integratsiis protsesshi samoka­lako sazogadoebis chartuloba, rogorts asotsirebis 
 shetankhmebis gankhortsielebis dagegmvis, ise shesru­ lebis monitoringis tvalsazrisit. 
 sakartvelos tsinsvla evrointegratsiis mimartulebit dadebitad shepasda  -  
 tslebshi gamartul asotsirebis sabchos skhdomebze. sakartvelo tsarmochinda, rogorts „aghmosavlet partniorobis“ lideri kveqana asotsirebis shetankhmebis shesrulebis tvalsazrisit. chveni amotsanaa srulad da epektianad iknas gamoqenebuli kveqnis evrointegratsiit ganpiro­ bebuli shesadzleblobebi. evrointegratsiis protsesit gatvalistsinebuli repormebi mnishvnelovania maghali standartebis damkvidrebis da tsarmatebuli transpormatsiis misaghtsevad. am miznit: - gagrdzeldeba asotsirebis shetankhmebis, rome­­ lits moitsavs ghrma da qovlismomtsveli tavi­ supali vachrobis sivrtsis komponents, epektiani gankhortsieleba; - gagrdzeldeba tanamshromloba migratsiis saki­ tkhebze da uvizo mimosvlis amokmedebis sapudz­ velze, sheikmneba meti shesadzleblobebi chveni mokalakeebistvis; - gagrdzeldeba institutsiuri da sektoraluri in­ teg­ratsia evrokavshirtan; 
 da 
 usaprtkhoebis 
 politikis 
 umnishvnelovanesi 
 shedga chrdiloatlantikuri sabchos mesame, kholo   tsels - natos samkhedro komitetis pirveli viziti sakartveloshi.   tslis 
 ivlisshi gamartul nato-s varshavis samitze mighebuli gadatsqvetilebit,   tsels sakartveloshi chrdiloatlantikuri sabchos meotkhe viziti gaima­ rteba. sakartvelostvis, rogorts aspiranti kveqnistvis, mnishvnelovani iqo   tslis natos uelsis samiti, romelzets aliansma miigho gadatsqvetileba sakartvelostvis “arsebit ghonisdziebata paketis“ shemushavebisa da urtiertobis tvisebrivad akhal doneze gadasvlis shesakheb. aghnishnul gadatsqvetilebata sapudzvelze,   tslis agvistos bolos, aliansis generaluri mdivnis, iens stoltenbergis vizitisas, nato- 
 sakartvelos ertoblivi tsvrtnisa da shepasebis tsentri dapudznda.   tslis ivnisshi, tavdatsvis institutsiuri aghmsheneblobis skola gaikhsna. nato-sakartvelos „arsebiti 
 paketit“ gansazghvruli valdebulebebis drouli da khariskhiani shesrulebit, kartuli mkhare khels utsqobs kveqnis tavdatsvisunarianobis ganmtkitsebasa da natoshi gatsevrianebistvis momzadebas. uelsis samitze sakartvelo aseve miitsvies “partniorobis tavsebadobis initsiativasa” da “gadzlierebuli shesadzleblobebis jgupshi” (shvedettan, pinettan, avstraliasa da iordaniastan ertad). amastan, kartuli kvedanaqopi   tslidan sheuertda natos stsrapi reagirebis dzalebs, rats kidev upro daaakhloebs sakartvelos alianstan. 
 nato-sakartvelos „arsebit pakettan“ ertad, sakartvelos natoshi integratsiis dziritadi instrumentebia tsliuri erovnuli programa da nato-sakartvelos komisia. aghnishnuli instrumentebis epektiani gamoqenebit, sakartvelo tsarmatebit akhortsielebs demokratiuli ganvi­ tarebisa da tavdatsvisunarianobis gadzlie­rebisken mimartul repormebs. sakartvelom mnishvnelovani politikuri da praktikuli mkhardachera miigho natos varshavis samitze, rats aliansshi integratsiis gzaze mightseuli progresis aghiarebis shedegia. samitma daadastura   tslis nato-s sagareo ministerialis gantskhadeba, rom sakartvelos ukve akvs qvela praktikuli instrumenti, rata moemzados aliansis tsevrobistvis. amave dros, sakartvelosatvis gatsevrianebis samokmedo gegmis minicheba rcheba politikuri protsesis natsilad. varshavis samitze tsalsakhad khazi gaesva, rom sakartvelos akvs qvelaze ghrma da qovlismomtsveli urtiertobebi alianstan da aliansis ghia karis politika dzalashia. 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva varshavis samitze mighebul ikna umnishvnelovanesi gadatsqvetilebebi sakartvelostvis tavdatsvis speroshi natos damatebiti dakhmarebis gatsevis shesakheb. 
 gadzlierda „arsebiti paketi“ da mighebul ikna akhali initsiativebi, mat shoris iseti mnishvnelovani 
 mimartulebebit, rogoritsaa: sahaero tavdatsvis shesadzleblobebis ganvitareba, ertoblivi tsvrtnebi da stsavlebebi, shavi zghvis usaprtkhoebis sakitkhebze tanamshromloba, strategiuli komunikatsia. 
 sakartvelom daamtkitsa, rom akvs politikuri neba da shestsevs unari, mnishvnelovani tsvlili sheitanos saerto evroatlantikuri usaprtkhoebis uzrunvelsaqopad, rats chveni kveqnis samkhedro mosamsakhureebis avghanetshi mimdinare mtkitse mkhardacheris misiashi monatsileobit dasturdeba. amastan, saertashoriso operatsiebshi sakar­ tvelos monatsileoba khels utsqobs sakartvelos sheiaraghebuli dzalebis propesi­onalizmis gazrdas, natostan tavsebadobis donis amaghlebas, tavdatsvis speroshi mnishvnelovani repormebis gatarebasa da sakartvelos saertashoriso imijis, rogorts aliansis sando da kmeditunariani partnioris, gamqarebas. sakartvelos natoshi gatsevrianebis amotsanebs, aseve kveqnis teritoriul mtlianobasa da suverenitets aktiurad uchers mkhars natos saparlamento asamblea, romlis skhdoma   tsels sakartveloshi gaimarteba. aliansshi integratsiis dachkarebis miznit: - arsebuli praktikuli instrumentebis gamoqenebit movemzadebit natos tsevrobistvis; - gagrdzeldeba nato-sakartvelos „arsebiti paketis“ epektiani gankhortsieleba, rats uzrunvelqops kveqnis tavdatsvisunarianobis ganmtkitsebasa da natostan tavsebadobis zrdas; - gagrdzeldeba nato-sakartvelos komisiis pormatshi alianstan aktiuri tanamshromloba; - tsarmatebit gagrdzeldeba tsliuri programebis gankhortsieleba; 
 erovnuli 
 - sakartvelo kvlav ikneba aliansis mnishvnelovani partniori saertashoriso usaprtkhoebis ganmtkitsebis sakmeshi; -   tsels sakartveloshi gaimarteba natos saparlamento asambleis skhdoma. kveqnis evropuli da evroatlantikuri integ­ ratsiis shesakheb strategiuli komunikatsiis mizani sazogadoebashi kveqnis evroatlantikuri kursis maghali mkhardacheris shenarchunebaa. ukanaskneli tslebis ganmavlobashi, antidasavluri propaganda gadzlierda da gamotsvevad iktsa ara mkholod sakartveloshi, aramed - mtel evropashi da mis mighmats. gadzlierebuli antidasavluri propagandis miukhedavad, epekturi strategiuli komunikatsiisa da sazogadoebis inpormirebis protsesis koordinirebit, chven shevdzelit demokratiuli 
 mmartvelobis pirobebshi sakartvelos evropuli da evroatlantikuri integratsiis maghali mkhardacheris shenarchuneba. 
 chveni mizania sakartveloshi arsebuli tradi­ tsiulad emotsiuri mkhardacheris gamqareba gatsnobierebuli archevanit. dghes sazogadoeba metad inpormirebulia, tu ratom aris sasargeblo da mimzidveli sakartvelos evropuli gza. qovelive es gaamqara chvenma khelshesakhebma shedegebmats - asotsirebis shetankhmebis gapormebam, tavisupali vachrobis shesadzleblobebma da pozitiurma daskvnam uvizo mimosvlaze.  -  tslebshi, komunikatsiisa da inpo­ rmatsiis shesakheb strategiis parglebshi, mtavrobam 
 ganakhortsiela  -ze meti aktivoba: shekhvedrebi, treningebi da seminarebi, mat shoris sainpormatsio ghonisdziebis/kampaniis pormatshi. gankhortsielda araerti satelevizio proekti da kampania uvizo mimosvlasa tu asotsirebis shetankhmebis sargebelze. mtavroba tanamshromlobs arasamtavrobo organizatsiebtan da  -ze meti aseti proektis 
 mkhardacherit, kveqanashi strategiuli komunikatsiis koordinirebit, vaghtsevt shesabamis shedegs. sakartvelo iqo ert-erti pirveli, romelmats skhvadaskhva saministroebshi shekmna strategiuli komunikatsiis departamenti da samagalitoa chveni tanamshromloba natosa da strategiuli komunikatsiebis danaqopebtan. 
 evrokavshiris akhladshekmnil 
 epektiani strategiuli komunikatsiis gankhortsi­ elebis miznit: - gagrdzeldeba 
 antidasavluri propagandis tsinaaghmdeg kmediti ghonisdziebebis gankhor­ 
 tsieleba inpormatsiis, strategiuli komu­ nikatsiis da ara kontrpropagandis an skhva arademokratiuli sashualebebis gamoqenebit; - gagrdzeldeba aktiuri sainpormatsio kampa­ nia, romlis mizania sakartvelos mosakh­ leobistvis zusti, amomtsuravi da obiekturi inpormatsiis mitsodeba evrokavshirisa da natos, evroatlantikuri integratsiis protsestan dakavshirebuli gamotsvevebisa da shesadzleblobebis, aseve kveqnis mier gansakhortsielebeli repormebis taobaze; - gagrdzeldeba 
 tanamshromloba

 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva operatsiebshi monatsileobistvis, uzrunvelqops samokalako khelisuplebis mkhardacheras stikiuri da teknogenuri ubedurebis dros, adekvaturad pasukhobs rogorts sazghvrebidan momdinare tavdaskhmis saprtkheebs, ise pirdapir samkhedro agresias. arsebuli usaprtkhoebis gamotsvevebis shesamtsireblad mnishvnelovania tavdatsvis sistemis sruli transpormatsia da iseti tavdatsviti shesadzleblobebis shekmna, romelits ekonomikuri da diplomatiuri shekavebis paktorebtan tanapard samkhedro shesadzleblobebs ganavitarebs da amgvarad, sakmarisi shekavebis paktoris shekmnit, sakartvelos sasitsotskhlo interesebis datsvas shedzlebs. chveni kveqnis natoshi gatsevrianebisken ganukhreli stsrapva stsored am miznis tanazomieria. kveqnis mshvidobiani ganvitarebis uzrunvelsaqopad, suverenitetisa da damoukideblobis dasatsavad, sakartvelos samkhedro dzalebi unda iqos mdzlavri shemakavebeli paktori agresoristvis, agretve mnishvnelovani argumenti omis preventsiisatvis. dzlieri da epektiani tavdatsvis sistemis chamosaqalibeblad, „kartuli otsneba“ daamtkitsebs da ganakhortsielebs  -tslian programas, romelits gakhdeba kveqnis tavdatsvis akhleburi khedvis tskhovrebashi gatarebis strategiuli gegma da sapudzvlad daedeba samkhedro dzalebis transpormatsiisa da modernizatsiis protsess. aghnishnuli programis gankhortsieleba daepudzneba samkhedro speroshi dghemde arsebul mightsevebs, sheiaraghebul dzalebshi mimdinare tsarmatebul programebs, nato-sakartvelos ertobliv proektebs, agretve samkhedro dzalebis repormirebis printsipulad akhal khedvebs, romlebits ganvitardeba shemdegi   mimartulebit: - strategia da martva - tavdatsvis dagegmvisa da martvis sistemebis integrirebis khariskhis gazrda resursebis prioritetuli mimartulebebit epektianad mimartvis da gadanatsilebis miznit; - dzalebis optimizatsia - samkhedro shesadz­ leblobebis dabalansebuli ertianobis shekmna, rats ganapirobebs kveqnis usaprtkhoebis amotsanebis shesrulebas; - dzalebis mzadqopna - kritikul paktorebze pokusireba sistemuri ganvitarebis mimar­ tulebit: personali, aghchurviloba, ganat­lebatsvrtnebi da mdgradoba; - institutsiuri repormebi - tavdatsvis samini­ stros martvis mekanizmebis tanmimdevruli dakhvetsa sheiaraghebuli dzalebis operatiuli motkhovnebis kmediti mkhardacheris uzrun­ velsaqopad; - saertashoriso chartuloba - samkhedro shesadz­ leblobebis, agretve nato-s da partniori kveqnebis dzalebtan tavsebadobis gazrdis miznit, saertashoriso programebsa da aktivobebshi monatsileoba. khedvis tsarmatebit realizatsiisatvis: - sabolood gaimijneba kompetentsiebi gene­

 ristvisats uzrunvelqopili ikneba kveqnis saerto erovnuli resursebisa da shesadzleblobebis stsori ganatsileba; blobebi, 
 - sheiaraghebul dzalebshi ganvitardeba spetsialuri danishnulebis dzalebis shesadzleblobebi; 
 - gagrdzeldeba samkhedro politsiis repormireba.  . . amerikis sheertebul shtatebtan strategiuli tanamshromlobis gaghrmaveba bolo otkhi tslis ganmavlobashi, ghrmavdeboda strategiuli tanamshromloba amerikis sheertebul shtatebtan, rogorts sakartvelos mtavar mokav­ shirestan. strategiuli partniorobis kartiis komisiis 
 pormatshi, regularulad imarteboda qoveltsliuri plenaruli skhdomebi da samushao jgupebis shekhvedrebi otkhive tematuri mimartulebit: usaprtkhoeba 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva da tavdatsva; ekonomika, vachroba da energetika; demokratiuli mmartveloba da samokalako sazogadoeba; khalkhtashorisi urtiertobebi da kulturuli gatsvlebi.   tsels, sakartveloshi ashsh-s sakhelmtsipo mdivnis vizitis parglebshi, kheli moetsera sakartvelosa da ashsh-s shoris tavdatsvisa da usaprtkhoebis speroshi partniorobis gaghrmavebis memorandums, romelits guliskhmobs 
 upretsedento tanamshromlobas or kveqanas shoris am mimartulebit da mimartulia sakartvelos tavdatsvisa da usaprtkhoebis uzrunvelqopisken.   tsels pirvelad chatarda maghali donis savachro da sainvestitsio dialogi amerikis 
 savachro tsarmomadgenelisa da sakartvelos vitse-premieris shekhvedris parglebshi, romlis drosats aseve shetankhmda ertoblivi sainvestitsio da inpo-komunikatsiebis da inovatsiebis speros printsipebi. gagrdzelda ekspertuli gankhilvebi savachro sakitkhebtan dakavshirebit, mat shoris ashshstan tavisupali vachrobis shesakheb shetankhmebis gapormebis shesadzleblobis gankhilvis kutkhit. aseve, gankhilul ikna sakartvelos tanamshromlobis shesadzebloba ashsh-s monatsileobit shekmnil regionul savachro platpormebshi. mtavrobebis khelshetsqobit da monatsileobit gankhortsielda savachro da sainvestitsio misiebi rogorts ashsh-shi, aseve sakartveloshi. mnishvnelovania or kveqanas shoris arsebuli vachrobisa da investitsiebis maghali donis dialogis pormatis parglebshi gamartuli shekhvedrebi. ganmtkitsda 
 da 
 gaghrmavda 
 tanamshromloba ganatlebis, jandatsvis, tavdatsvis, usapr­ tkhoebis, demokratiuli institutebis ganvitarebisa da gadzlierebis kutkhit. 
 ashsh-s kongresshi sheikmna sakartvelos megobarta jgupi, romlis mierats initsirebul ikna sakartvelos teritoriuli mtlianobis mkhardamcheri rezolutsia. 
 aghsanishnavia ashsh-is mier sakartvelostvis gamoqopili dakhmarebis zrda skhvadaskhva mnishvnelovani mimartulebit, mat shoris   tslis piskaluri biujetis proektis parglebshi. tsarimarteboda 
 aktiuri 
 tanamshromloba amerikis arasamtavrobo sektortan da kvle­ vit tsentrebtan. 
 partniorobis shesakheb urtiertgagebis memorandumi gapormda. ashsh-is administratsiis maghali donis tsarmo­ madgenlebisa da ashsh-is kongresis mkhridan saka­ rtvelos mkhardamcheri gantskhadebebi tskhadqops ashsh-is mtkitse mkhardacheras sakartvelos erovnuli interesebis mimart. sakartvelo gaagrdzelebs ashsh-tan, rogorts sakar­tvelos mtavar strategiul partniortan, urtiertobebis shemdegom gaghrmavebas. kerdzod: - gaghrmavdeba strategiuli tanamshromlobis pormatit gansazghvruli mushaoba; - gaghrmavdeba ashsh-tan partnioroba 
 sakart­ velos tavdatsviti shesadzleblobebisa da sheiaraghebuli dzalebis institutsiuri ganvi­ tarebisatvis; 
 - gaghrmavdeba ashsh-tan sametsniero da ganatlebis speroshi tanamshromloba; 
 - gaghrmavdeba savachro da sainvestitsio urti­ ertobebi. 
  . . rusetis pederatsiastan konpliktis mshvidobiani daregulireba   tslis saparlamento archevnebis shemdeg, sakartvelos khelisuplebas umdzimesi memkvidreoba ergo rusettan urtiertobis tvalsazrisit.   tslis agvistos omis humanitarul da materialur zarals daemata rusetis mier apkhazetisa da tskhinvalis aghiareba da 
 regionis 
 damoukideblobis 
 sakartvelos mtlianobis paktobrivi khelqopa. 
 teritoriuli 
 sakartvelostan mimartebit ruseti agrdzelebs saertashoriso samartlis dziritadi printsipebisa da   tslis   agvistos tsetskhlis shetsqvetis shetankhmebit aghebuli valdebulebebis ugulvebelqopas, mizanmimartulad akhortsielebs ukanono kmedebas sakartvelos okupirebul regionebshi, rats guliskhmobs sokhumsa da tskhinvaltan integratsiis shesakheb e.ts. khelshekrulebebis gapormebas, okupirebuli teritoriebis shemdgom militarizatsias, saokupatsio khazis gastsvriv mavtulkhlartebis, khelovnuri barierebis da e.ts. sazghvris aghmnishvneli banerebis instalatsias. masshtaburi khasiati akvs adgilobrivi kartuli mosakhleobis uplebebis ukhesh khelqopas. bolo otkhi tslis ganmavlobashi sakartvelo-rusetis urtiertobata qvelaze rtuli sakitkhebi regularulad ganikhileboda zhenevis saertashoriso konsultatsiebis pormatshi. intsidentebis preventsiisa da matze 
 reagirebis mekanizmebis amokmedebam sashualeba mogvtsa shegvemtsirebina, tsina tslebtan shedarebit, tragikuli shemtkhvevebi saokupatsio khazis mimdebare regionebshi. rusetis mimart pragmatulma politikam, ormkhrivi dialogis datsqebam da tsarmoebam, 
 chven dasavlel partniorebtan aktiurma tanamshromlobam mnishvnelovnad sheamtsira sheiaraghebuli konpliktis ganakhlebis albatoba, 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva rats kveqnis, aseve shidapolitikuri, regionuli usaprtkhoebisa da stabilurobis ganmtkitsebis erterti umnishvnelovanesi paktoria. moskovtan ormkhrivi dialogis shedegad, gadaidga mnishvnelovani nabijebi savachro-ekonomikur, satransporto 
 da 
 humanitarul 
 speroebshi. 
  -  tslebshi, sakartvelos eksportma rusetshi asobit milioni dolari sheadgina. mnishvnelovani mogeba nakhes kartulma satransporto kompaniebma. ormkhrivi dialogis pormatshi, shevdzelit chveni mokalakeebis gatavisupleba, romlebits rusetshi ikhdidnen mravaltslian sasjels jashushobis braldebit.   tsels, rusetis pederatsiis mkhridan sagrdznoblad gamartivda savizo motkhovnebi sakartvelos mokalakeebisatvis. gaizarda sakartveloshi rusetidan turistta raodenoba   tseli am tvalsazrisit rekorduli ikneba.   tslis ivlisshi, sakartvelos sasargeblod mighebul ikna strasburgis adamianis uplebata evropuli 
 sasamartlos 
 gadatsqvetileba 
 sakmeze - „sakartvelo rusetis tsinaaghmdeg“, romelits ekheba  -  tslebshi rusetis pederatsiis mier sakartvelos mokalaketa etnikuri nishnit deportatsias. 
 dialogi rusettan da pragmatuli urtiertoba ama tu im speroshi ar guliskhmobs raime kompromiss kveqnis sasitsotskhlo interesebis kharjze. pirikit, am politikis mtavari mizania sakartvelos deokupatsia da gamtlianeba, misi mdgradi ganvitarebisatvis shesabamisi sagareo pirobebis shekma. chveni khelisupleba kvlav gaagrdzelebs rusettan mimartebashi pragmatul politikas, romelsats tsalsakhad mkhars ucheren chveni dasavleli partniorebi.  . . mezobel da regionis sakhelmtsipoebtan urtiertobebis ganmtkitseba da strategiuli proektebis ganvitareba sakartvelos sagareo politikis ert-erti prioritetia mezobel sakhelmtsipoebtan, shavi da kaspiis zghvis regionis, aseve evropisa da aziis kveqnebtan mchidro politikuri da ekonomikuri urtiertobebis chamoqalibeba da mati shemdgomi ganvitareba. gasuli otkhi tslis ganmavlobashi tsarmatebit mimdinareobda urtiertkhelsaqreli tana­ mshromlobis ganmtkitseba mezobel sakhelmtsipoebtan - azerbaijantan, turkettan da somkhettan. chamoqalibda tanamshromlobis akhali pormatebi. sheikmna turkettan maghali donis strategiuli tanamshromlobis sabcho premier-ministrebis doneze. gapartovda urtiertkmedeba sakartveloazerbaijani-turketis sammkhriv pormatshi da is regionuli strategiuli tanamshromlobis tsarmatebul mekanizmad iktsa. khortsieldeba tanmimdevruli, urtiertobata shemdgom ganvitarebaze orientirebuli tanam­ shromloba traditsiul partniorebtan - ukrainasa da moldovastan. am kveqnebtan ormkhrivma tanam­shromlobam damatebiti mnishvneloba 
 sheidzina samive kveqnis evrokavshirtan asotsirebis shetankhmebis khelmotseris gatvalistsinebit. ukrainasa da moldovastan sapudzveli chaeqara tsarmatebul sammkhriv tanamshromlobas, romelits evrointegratsiis speroshi urtiertkmedebasa da gamotsdilebis urtiertgaziarebas guliskhmobs. grdzeldeba ormkhrivi tanamshromloba evropis ormkhrivi urtiertobebis dghis tsesrigshi gansakutrebuli aktsentebi ketdeboda savachro-ekonomikur speroshi arsebuli potentsialis maksimalurad gamoqenebaze, satranzito-satra­ nsporto derepnebis ganvitarebaze, energou­ saprtkhoebis uzrunvelqopis sakitkhebsa da kulturul-saganmanatleblo proektebis gankhor­ tsielebaze. kveqnebtan. 
 gaghrmavda tanamshromloba akhlo aghmosavletisa aziis kveqnebtan. upretsedentod gaizarda am regionis kveqnebis ekonomikuri interesi sakartvelosadmi, gaghrmavda sainvestitsio, savachro, satranzito da turistuli kavshirebi iaponiastan, chinettan, indoettan, samkhret koreastan, israeltan, irantan da arabul kveqnebtan. sakartvelo aktiurad mushaobs aziis pinansur institutebtan. da 
   tslis   marts pekinshi sakartvelom da chinetma gaapormes memorandumi „abreshumis gzis ekonomikuri sartqelis ganvitarebistvis tanamshromlobis shesakheb“, romelits or kveqanas shoris attsleulebis ganmavlobashi arsebuli megobruli urtiertobebis kidev upro gaghrmavebasa da regionuli proektebis ganvitarebas guliskhmobs. amastan, sakartvelo gakhda pirveli kveqana regionshi, romelmats daitsqo molaparakebebi chinettan tavisupali savachro rezhimis shetankhmebastan dakavshirebit. gamotsvevad rcheba saertashoriso terorisa da agresiisagan momdinare saprtkheebi. am mkhriv, mnishvnelovania antiteroristuli koalitsiis parglebshi chven partnior kveqnebtan koordinirebuli da epekturi tanamshromloba. aktualuri rcheba chvens ushualo samezobloshi, samkhret kavkasiashi, aseve ukrainasa da akhlo aghmosavletshi, regionis skhva tsertilebshi mimdinare konpliktebisa tu usaprtkhoebis skhva umnishvnelovanesi sakitkhebi. regionis da skhva partnior kveqnebtan mimartebashi sagareo politikis prioritetebia arsebuli ormkhrivi politikuri, savachro-ekonomikuri da khalkhtashorisi kavshirebis gaghrmaveba da sakartvelos ekonomikuri da kulturuli potentsialis popu­larizatsia. gansakutrebuli quradgheba daetmoba akhali abreshumis gzis parglebshi inkluziuri, konkurentuli da epektiani regionuli proektebis gankhortsielebas transportis, energetikis, aseve khalkhtashorisi kontaktebis gaghrmavebis mimar­tulebit. mezobel sakhelmtsipoebtan, shavi da kaspiis zghvis regionis, aseve evropisa da aziis kveqnebtan mchidro politikuri da ekonomikuri urtiertobebis chamoqalibebisa da mati shemdgomi ganvitarebis miznit: 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva - gaghrmavdeba tanamshromloba mezobel, regi­ 
 porumi gaimarteba regularulad. 
 - gaghrmavdeba tanamshromloba ukrainastan da moldovastan evrointegratsiis sakitkhebze; 
   tsels sakartvelo gakhda aziis inpras­ trukturis sainvestitsio bankis ert-erti dampudznebeli kveqana, rats udaod sheutsqobs khels 
 onis da skhva partnior kveqnebtan; 
 - gaghrmavdeba ormkhrivi tanamshromloba evropis kveqnebtan prioritetuli mimartulebebit; - gagrdzeldeba epektiani tanamshromloba usa­ prt­khoebis sakitkhebze partnior kveqnebtan; - gapormdeba tavisupali vachrobis shesakheb shetankhmeba chinettan; 
 - gaaktiurdeba dzaliskhmeva sazghvargaretis kve­ qnebtan ormkhriv doneze politikuri, 
 ekonomikuri, kulturuli da skhva sektoruli sakhelshekrulebo-samartlebrivi urtie­ rto­bebis dasamqareblad. 
  . . msoplios masshtabit sakartvelos ekonomikuri mimzidvelobisa da kulturis popularizatsia sakartvelos ert-erti umtavresi prioritetia aktiuri ekonomikuri diplomatiis tsarmoeba, rats guliskhmobs sakartveloshi gatarebuli repormebisa da mightsevebis sazghvargaret aktiur tsarmochenas, utskhouri investitsiebis mozidvis, teknologiebisa da inovatsiebis shemotanis, eksportis zrdisa da saertashoriso ekonomikur protsesebshi kveqnis srulpasovani monatsileobis khelshetsqobas. dzaliskhmeva mimartulia kveqnis satransporto– satranzito potentsialis srulqopilad atvisebisa da erovnuli tsarmoebis ganvitarebisken. mimdinareobs 
 aktiuri 
 mushaoba 
 sazghvargaret 
 sakartvelos diplomatiuri misiebis ekono­ mikuri mimartulebis gasadzliereblad. 
 movakhdinet ekonomikur mimartulebaze pasukhismgebeli diplomatebis identipitsireba, mimdinareobs mati treningebi da kvalipikatsiis amaghleba, shesabamisi instruktsiebit da masalebit saelchoebis uzrunvelqopa. aseve, datsqebulia mushaoba komertsiuli tsarmomadgenlebis sistemis shekmnaze. grdzeldeba 
 mushaoba 
 sakartvelos gavlit energoderepnebis ganvitarebis mimartulebit 
 mskhvili erovnuli da regionuli inprastrukturuli proektebis gankhortsielebas. grdzeldeba mushaoba msoplios liberalur bazrebtan integratsiis mimartulebit. dasrulda 
 bernshi kheli moetsera tavisupali vachrobis shesakheb shetankhmebas. 
 sakartvelos diplomatiuri misiebis meshveobit mimdinareobs aktiuri mushaoba sakartvelos

 kheli moetsera   okms, kholo   kveqanastan mimdinareobs molaparakebebi. ekonomikuri diplomatiis parglebshi, urad mimdinareobs sakartvelos da

 sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva - kheli sheetsqoba sakartveloshi akhali tekno­ logiebisa da inovatsiebis shemotanas; 
 - kheli sheetsqoba sakartvelos mtsire da sashualo biznesis internatsionalizatsias;

 sakartvelos ekspor­tio­ rebisa da biznesinteresebis utskhour bazrebze lobireba; 
 - kheli sheetsqoba kartvel da utskhoel bizne­ 
 smenebsa da biznesgaertianebebs shoris pir­dapiri kavshirebis damqarebas da tanam­ 
 shromlobis ganvitarebas, gagrdzeldeba utskhoetshi kartuli biznesis interesebis datsva.  . . sazghvargaret mqopi sakartvelos mokalakeebis uplebebis datsva da diasporastan mchidro kavshirebis ganvitareba 
 sakartvelos sagareo politikis ert-erti mtavari prioritetia sazghvargaret mqopi sakartvelos mokalakeebis uplebebis datsva, matshi kartuli enisa da tvitmqopadobis shenarchuneba da sazghvargaret mtskhovreb tanamemamuleebtan kontaktebis ganmtkitseba. kartuli diaspora umnishvnelovanes rols asrulebs chveni kveqnis ekonomikur da sotsialur ganvitarebashi. gasuli   tslis ganmavlobashi, diasporebtan urtiertobebis gaumjobesebis da kveqnis ganvitarebis protsesshi aktiurad chartvis miznit, mnishvnelovani ghonisdziebebi gankhortsielda, romelta shoris aghsanishnavia: - sakonsulo aghritskhvaze dadgomis shemtkhvevashi adgilsamqopel kveqanashi satskhovreblis shesakheb tsnobis tsardgenis autsileblobaze sagareo sakmeta ministris brdzanebis gaukmeba; - utskhoetshi gardatsvlili sakartvelos mokalakis samshobloshi gadmosvenebis protsedurebisa da gadmosvenebastan dakavshirebuli kharjebis sakhelmtsipos mier daparvis tsesis gansazghvra; - sazghvargaret mokmedi   sakvirao skolis,   polkloruli ansamblis,   sportuli gundis da   skhva diasporuli organizatsiis mkhardachera saskolo, sastsavlo, sportuli da satsekvao pormebis da instrumentebis mitsodeba; - diasporuli akhalgazrduli programis („diasporuli stazhireba“, „iqavi sheni kveqnis akhalgazrda elchi“) datsqeba; - „diasporuli veb-portalisa“ da „diasporis elektronuli bibliotekis“ shekmna; - distantsiuri stsavlebisa da „onlain skolis“ gakvetilebis gadatsemis uzrunvelqopis miznit opitsialuri veb-gverdis shekmna da kartuli enis, sakartvelos istoriisa da geograpiis modulebis mkharetmtsodneobis elementebita da shesabamisi simulatsiebit momzadeba, satesto gakvetilebis chatsera; - turketis respublikis sajaro skolebshi kartuli enis stsavlebis uplebis mopoveba da kartuli enis stsavlebis sruli programuli natsilis momzadeba; 
 - saberdznetis respublikis sajaro skolebshi kartuli enis stsavlebis sapilote programis datsqeba; - utskhoetshi mtskhovrebi sakartvelos mokala­ keebisatvis sameditsino programebis gankhortsieleba da mkhardachera; - dabrunebuli emigrantebisatvis sareintegratsio samtavrobo programis datsqeba; - levilis shatos da mamulis sakartvelosatvis gadmotsemis tsinastsar ganzrakhulobata dokumentis khelmotsera. bolo tslebshi, araerti diasporuli investitsia ganakhortsielda soplis meurneobis, turizmis, meditsinisa da skhva speroebshi. bolo   tslis ganmavlobashi, mimdinareobda aktiuri mushaoba sakartvelodan sazghvargaret sakartvelos mokalakeebis legaluri gadaadgilebis protse­ durebis gamartivebis miznit. gapormda uvizo mimosvlis shesakheb khelshekrulebebi, rogorts diplomatiuri da samsakhurebrivi pasportebis, ise ordinaluri pasportebis mplobeltatvis. am ukanaskneltatvis vizis mighebis valdebulebisagan gatavisuplebis taobaze shetankhmebebi khelmotseril ikna da dzalashia: israeltan, braziliastan, argentinastan, chilesa da urugvaistan. garda amisa, vizebis gatsemis protseduris gamartivebis shesakheb shetankhmebebi khelmotseril ikna shveitsariasa da norvegiastan. mnishvnelovania shemdgomi nabijebis gadadgma sakhelmtsiposa da diasporas shoris urtiertobis intensipikatsiis, sistematizatsiisa da arsebuli problemebis ertiani dzaliskhmevit mogvarebis miznit. diasporastan urtiertobashi chveni umtavresi amotsanaa sazghvargaret sakartvelos popularizatsia da diasporashi arsebuli sainvestitsio da intelektualuri resursis kveqnis ganvitarebis protsesshi chartva, diasporeli investorebis meshveobit damatebiti samushao adgilebis shekmna da inovatsiebis stimulireba. kerdzod: - gaizrdeba utskhoetshi mtskhovrebi sakartvelos mokalakeebisa da sakartveloshi mati ojakhis tsevrebis chartuloba sametsarmeo da inovatsiebis khelshemtsqob samtavrobo („atsarmoe sakartveloshi“, „danerge momavali“, „iapi krediti“), tanainvestirebis („damtsqebi biznesis (startapis) khelshetsqoba“, „mikro da mtsire biznesis khelshetsqoba“) da sagranto („reintegratsiis khelshetsqoba“, „dasakmebis khelshetsqoba“) prog­ ramebshi; - kheli sheetsqoba utskhoetshi mtskhovrebi sakartvelos mokalakeebis samshobloshi ghirseul dabrunebas da uzrunvelqopili ikneba „erti panjris“ printsipze dapudznebuli sainpormatsio-sakonsu­ ltatsio servisi; - gadzlierdeba samshobloshi dabrunebuli sakar­ tvelos mokalakeebisatvis sareintegratsio samtavrobo programa; 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 sagareo urtiertobebi, usaprtkhoeba da tavdatsva - gadaikhedeba utskhoetshi mtskhovrebi tanamemamulis samartlebrivi statusis da motsmobis gatsemis tsesi, misi sakartvelos migratsiis strategiastan, savizo da sainvestitsio politikastan tavsebadobis uzrunvelqopis miznit; - kheli sheetsqoba sazghvargaret sakvirao skolebs, gadamzaddebian pedagogebi da shemushavdeba ertiani sastsavlo programa; - ganakhldeba da ganvitardeba akhalgazrduli proektebi da sazapkhulo banakebi; - kheli sheetsqoba utskhoetshi kartuli enisa da literaturis popularizatsias da kartuli enis shemstsavleli kursebis kselis ganvitarebas; 
 - shemushavdeba da gankhortsieldeba levilis mamulis, rogorts kulturul-istoriuli tsentris, ganvi­tarebis samokmedo gegma; - ganisazghvreba „diasporul organizatsiad“ aghia­ rebis kriteriumebi, kheli sheetsqoba diasporuli organizatsiebis strukturul gadzlierebas; - sakartvelodan sazghvargaret sakartvelos mokalakeebis legaluri gadaadgilebis pro­ tsedurebis gamartivebis miznit, gagrdzeldeba mushaoba partnior kveqnebtan khelsaqreli saimigratsio rezhimebis misaghtsevad. 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 mtavrobis   punktiani gegma 
 „kartuli otsnebis“ mmartvelobis ganvlil   tselitsadshi kveqnis ganvitarebistvis mnishvnelovani sapudzveli sheikmna. ekonomika da biznesi gatavisuplda sakhelmtsipo tsnekhisgan, sakutrebis uplebis ganukhreli datsvit da kerdzo sektorze orientirebuli gadatsqvetilebebit sheikmna stabiluri da usaprtkho biznes garemo, mokhda pundamenturi tsinsvla demokratiuli ganvitarebis qvela mimartulebit, sapudzveli chaeqara sakhelmtsipos sotsialuri pasukhismgeblobis printsipze dapudznebul janmrtelobisa da sotsialuri datsvis politikas, romelmats uamravi adamianis sitsotskhlis gadarchena da ojakhebis gagharibebis tavidan atsileba uzrunvelqo. qvela pundamenturi mimartulebit sakartvelos pozitsiebi gaumjobesda msoplioshi gavleniani da avtoritetuli organizatsiebis reitingebshi. „kartulma otsnebam“ shekmna tanamedrove, dasav­ luri tipis ekonomikis msheneblobis tsinapiroba da pundamenti. aseve, chven davamtkitset, rom sotsialuri politika umnishvnelovanesia chvens prioritetebshi da kvlavats gavagrdzelebt sotsialur solidarobas manam, sanam chvens kveqanashi iknebian adamianebi, romlebits amas sachiroeben. dghes, ukve droa, rom gankhortsieldes mnishvne­ lovani tvisobrivi tsvlileba kveqnis ekonomikashi, mokhdes seriozuli garghveva da daitsqos ekonomikis stsrapi ganvitarebis etapi. stsored am miznit, „kartul otsnebas“ gaachnia ekonomikuri zrdis dachkarebis   punktiani gegma, romelits srulad pasukhobs tanamedrove sakhelmtsipos msheneblobis mtavar gamotsvevebs. aghnishnuli gegmit, chveni gundi pokusirebas moakhdens zustad im mimartulebebze, romlebits moitans tvisobriv tsvlilebebs kveqnis ganvitarebashi, uzrunvelqops ekonomikis stsrap zrdas da mosakhleobis ketildgheobis amaghlebas. kveqnis stsrapi ganvitarebistvis,   punktiani gegmit „kartuli otsneba“ ganakhortsielebs: ekonomikur repormas; ganatlebis repormas; kveqnis ganvitarebas motsqobit; 
 optimaluri 
 sivrtsiti 
 mmartvelobis repormas. ekonomikuri reporma orientirebuli ikneba kerdzo sektoris maksimalur tsakhalisebaze da 
 mis gadzlierebaze. am mimartulebit gagvachnia gadatsqvetilebebis mteli paketi, romelits chvens kveqanashi biznesis ketebas upro mimzidvels da momgebians gakhdis. sheikmneba mnishvnelovani sagadasakhado stimulebi, biznesi aghar daibegreba mogebis gadasakhadit mogebis reinvestirebis shemtkhvevashi. aghnishnuli repormit, biznesektorshi darcheba aseulobit milioni lari, rats tsaakhalisebs investitsiebs, daachkarebs ekonomikur zrdas da shekmnis atiatasobit samushao adgils. chvenma gundma ganakhortsiela mnishvnelovani tsvlilebebi sagadasakhado kanonmdeblobashi, romelits tsina khelisuplebis represiuli mankanis mnishvnelovani shemadgeneli natsili iqo. sagadasakhado garemo biznesis mimart ikneba kidev upro megobruli da maksimalurad tsaakhalisebs investitsiebs. sasamartlos gadatsqvetilebis gareshe veghar mokhdeba biznesis angarishebis daqadagheba; kompaniebis sagadasakhado shemotsmebis vada ikneba reglamentirebuli da gaukmdeba ekonomikuri danashaulistvis tsinastsari patimrobis gamoqeneba gansakutrebuli shemtkhvevebis garda. aghnishnuli nabijebi bizness mistsems met tavisuplebas da gaachens ganvitarebis damatebit potentsials ekonomikashi. „kartuli otsnebis“ mnishvnelovani monapovaria biznesis datsqebis khelshetsqoba. kartul sinamdvileshi mokhda upretsedento pakti, rodesats kveqanashi gachnda „startapebis“ dapinansebis instrumenti. artserti biznes-idea, romelsats gaachnia ganvitarebis potentsiali ar rcheba dapinansebis gareshe. „startapebis“ dapinanseba ikneba stsrapi ganvitarebis   punktiani gegmis ert-erti mtavari mimartuleba. gankhortsieldeba ganatlebis reporma. dai­nergeba germanuli dualuri ganatlebis sistema, sadats kerdzo sektortan ertad mokhdeba kadrebis gadamzadeba da kvalipitsiuri kadrebis mosamzadeblad sakhelmtsipo da satsarmoebi gainatsileben kompetentsiebs, propesiuli ganatlebis teoriuli da satsarmoo praktikis komponentebis mimartulebit. shromis bazris kvlevis sapudzvelze, sakhelmtsipo gansazghvravs propesiuli ganatlebis tsalkeul prioritetul mimartulebebs da uzrunvelqops damsakmeblebis srulpasovan chartvas propesiuli programebis shemushavebis, gankhortsielebisa da studentta shepasebis protsesebshi. sheikmneba zrdasrulta ganatlebis sistema. utsqveti ganatlebis printsipebis danergva propesiul ganatlebas 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 mtavrobis   punktiani gegma khelmisatsvdoms gakhdis ara mkholod saskolo asakis akhalgazrdebistvis, aramed, asakis sheuzghudavad, qvela im piristvis, visats akhali propesiis daupleba surs. sistema gakhdeba upro ghia da inkluziuri. amaghldeba pedagogebis kvalipikatsia, ris shedegadats gaizrdeba sashualo ganatlebis khariskhi. umaghlesi ganatleba daepudzneba ekonomikis sachiroebebs da motkhovnilebebs. shromis bazris analizis sapudzvelze, ganisazghvreba da dapinansdeba umaghlesi ganatlebis prioritetuli mimartulebebi. kveqnis ekonomikis, strategiuli ganvitarebis motkhovnebisa da sazogadoebis sachiroebebis gatvalistsinebit, mokhdeba prioritetuli sametsniero dargebis identipikatsia da mati gadzlierebis mkhardachera. ganatlebis reporma uzrunvelqops adamianuri kapitalis ganvitarebas da mis maksimalur, epektian chartvas kveqnis ganvitarebashi. sivrtsiti motsqobis skema ikneba kveqnis ganvitarebis mtavari charcho. sivrtsit-teritoriuli dagegmva aris kveqnis mdgradi ganvitarebis da tskhovrebis khariskhis amaghlebis mnishvnelovani instrumenti. kveqnis ganvitarebis potentsialis optimalur atvisebas gadamtsqveti mnishvneloba akvs tanamedrove sakhelmtsipos msheneblobashi. stsored amitom, sivrtsiti motsqoba aris stsrapi ekonomikuri zrdis   punktiani gegmis natsili. 
 stsori sivrtsiti-teritoriuli dagegmvit gavaumjobesebt urtiertkavshirs kalaksa da sopels shoris, khels shevutsqobt turizmis ganvitarebas, gavadzlierebt evropis da aziis damakavshirebeli satransporto derepnis da lojistikur punktsias. sivrtsiti motsqobis repormis parglebshi momzaddeba kalakebis da soplebis ganashenianebis regulirebis gegmebi, tsertili daesmeba kaotur ganashenianebas. stsori sivrtsiti motsqobit sakartvelo gakhdeba otkhi sezonis turistuli kveqana, rats uzrunvelqops turizmidan akhali shemosavlebis mighebis da tslis ganmavlobashi mati stabiluri ganatsilebis sashualebas. mteli sakartvelos masshtabit daproektdeba da daigeba regionebis damakavshirebeli satransporto kseli, romelits qvela regions mchidrod daakavshirebs ertmanettan. geograpiuli mdebareoba aghar ikneba barieri biznesis tsarmoebistvis da gadaadgilebistvis. sakartvelos saavtomobilo gzebis kseli gakhdeba mimzidveli satranzito gadazidvebisatvis, khels sheutsqobs kveqanashi turizmis ganvitarebas, ganapira da maghalmtian regionebshi soplis meurneobis ganvitarebasa da regionebis dakavshirebas. stsori dagegmarebit da gaazrebuli sivrtsiti motsqobit sakartvelo epektianad aitvisebs kveqnis ganvitarebis potentsials da msoplio rukaze gadzlierdeba sakartvelos, rogorts tranzituli habis mnishvneloba. 
 mmartvelobis reporma uzrunvelqops sakhel­ mtsipo servisebis dakhvetsas da utsqebebis mushaobis epektianobis amaghlebas. upro stsrapi ekonomikuri zrdistvis chven gvchirdeba mmartvelobis epektianobis gazrda. repormis parglebshi, sheikmneba ertiani „pront opisi“, sadats qvela shesabamisi sakhelmtsipo utsqeba bizness erti panjris printsipit moemsakhureba. es ikneba mnishvnelovani nabiji biznesistvis sakmianobis gamartivebis mimartulebit. biznesi dazogavs dros da resurss. mtavrobis gadatsqvetilebebis mighebis dro ikneba reglamentirebuli, mtavrobis administratsiashi sheikmneba strukturuli erteuli, romelits mtavrobis tsevrta mier gadatsqvetilebis mighebis khangrdzlivobis monitorings ganakhortsielebs. gadzlierdeba sazogadoebis chartuloba mmartvelobis protsesshi da uzrunvelqopili ikneba protsesebis epektiani monitoringis sashualeba. 
 mokhdeba onlain momsakhurebebis dakhvetsa da gaumjobeseba, akhali distantsiuri servisebis damateba da sakhelmtsipo servisebis sapasuris optimizatsia. aghnishnuli repormebi uzrunvelqops ekonomikis upro stsrap zrdas da tvisobriv gardakmnas kveqnis ganvitarebashi. mmartvelobis reporma uzrunvelqops stsrapi ganvitarebis miznis misaghtsevad sachiro gadatsqvetilebebis stsrap da epektian aghsrulebas.   punktiani gegmis gankhortsielebit chven mivighebt tanamedrove, ganvitarebuli da saertashoriso standartis inprastrukturis mkone kveqanas, shromis bazris sachiroebebis shesabamisi adamianuri resursit, usaprtkho da stabiluri biznes garemoti da epektiani sakhelmtsipo mmartvelobit. stsored es komponentebi ganapirobebs upro stsrap ganvitarebas da ketildgheobis zrdas. es aris gza, romelits tvisobriv gardatekhas sheitans kveqnis ekonomikashi da mas stsrapi ganvitarebis relsebze gadaiqvans. sakartvelo „kartuli otsnebis“ mmartvelobis periodshi damoukideblobis aghdgenis shemdeg pirvelad mokhvda sashualoze maghalshemosavlian kveqnebshi. magram, amistvis kveqanas   tseli daschirda. am tempebit ganvitareba khilul momavalshi kveqanas ver miiqvans ketildgheobis maghal donemde. sachiroa tvisobrivad akhali midgoma, romelits uzrunvelqops ganvitarebis sheuktsevad protsess. sachiroa aktsentebis gadatana grdzelvadian ganvitarebaze, natsvlad populisturi ideebisa, romelits mimartulia amomrchevlis gulis mogebaze da ara kveqnis tsinsvlaze. chven, stsored chveni   punktiani gegmit movakhdent tvisobriv gardatekhas kveqnis ekonomikashi da davitsqebt ganvitarebis akhal, stsrap etaps. mmartvelobis gasuli   tslis ganmavlobashi chven shevkmenit sapudzveli imistvis, rom titoeulma ojakhma igrdznos ketildgheoba, mmartvelobis shemdgom   tselitsadshi, konkretuli gegmit, chven mivaghtsevt am mizans. 
 tavisupleba, stsrapi ganvitareba, ketildgheoba! 
 shinagan sakmeta saministrom tbilisshi momkhdar sazarel mkvlelobastan dakavshirebit pirveli komentari gaaketa. rogorts utsqebashi gamartul sagangebo bripingze aghinishna,   tslis kalis mkvlelobis braldebit dakavebulia   piri. dakavebultagan erti -   tslis gogona moklulis shvilia, meore gogonas sheqvarebuli, danareni   piri ki mati megobari.

 biznesisa da ekonomikis tsentris aprikel liderta programa 
  -  agvistos, biznesisa da ekonomikis tsentrma aprikel politikur liderta delegatsias umaspindzla , romelits gatarebuli repormebisa da demokratizatsiis gamotsdilebis gatsnobis miznit etsvia sakartvelos, saertashoriso asotsiatsiis - ‘’biznesisa da parlamentis saertashoriso dialogi’’ - rekomendatsiit da mkhardacherit. 
  -katsiani delegatsia sakartvelos aprikel liderta programis parglebshi estumra, kongos demokratiuli respublikis prezidentobis kandidatis da ertian kongoelta partis dampudzneblis kristian malangas khelmdzghvanelobit. 
 programis parglebshi shedga shekhvedrebi sakartvelos khelisuplebisa da arasamtavrobo organizatsiebis tsarmomadgenlebtan, sakhalkho damtsveltan, politikur partiebtan, biznes-asotsiatsiebtan, metsarmeebtan; spetsialuri turebi moetsqo: iustitsiis sakhlshi, sakartvelos agrarul universitetshi, erovnul bankshi, penitentsialuri sistemis da sakartvelos shinagan sakmeta saministros sakveutsqebo datsesebulebebshi, mat shoris: politsiis akademia, sagangebo situatsiebis martvis saagento, momsakhurebis saagento da gadaudebeli dakhmarebis operatiuli martvis tsentri „ “. 
 aprikelma stumrebma moinakhules aseve samebis sakatedro tadzari, gaetsnen dzveli tbilisis kulturul ghirsshesanishnaobebs, kartuli ghvinis istorias da daagemovnes rogorts evropuli, aseve traditsiuli teknologiit damzadebuli skhvadaskhva sakheobis kartuli ghvino. 
 programis dasasruls,   agvistos, sakartvelos parlamentis erovnuli bibliotekis sagamopeno darbazshi, pondi kristalis mkhardacherit, gaimarta saertashoriso konperentsia “sakartvelos repormebi - magaliti aprikisatvis?” sadats, samive sektoris tvalsachino tsarmomadgenlebma delegatsiis tsevrebs gauziares sakartvelos gamotsdileba sami dziritadi mimartulebit: demokratia, kargi mmartveloba da adamianis uplebebi; ekonomika da biznesgaremo; ganatlebis reporma: risi shetavazeba sheudzlia sakartvelos? 
 evraziis pondis proekti “ekonomika da zhurnalistika” itvalistsinebda ekonomikis sakitkhebze momushave akhalgazrda kartveli, azerbaijaneli da somekhi zhurnalistebis gadamzadebas, matipropesiuli donis amaghlebas. 
 proekti gankhortsielda: damoukidebel zhurnalistta saertashoriso aliansis – damoukidebel zhurnalistta kavshiris (sakartvelo. 
 azerbaijanis kal-zhurnalistta asotsiatsiis (azerbaijani) 
 lektsiebis garda, ekonomikis sakitkhebze momushave akhalgazrda zhurnalistebs, vtavazobt ekonomikasa da zhurnalistikashi qvelaze khshirad khmarebuli terminebis ganmartebas da inglisur akronimebsa da abreviaturas. krebulis am natsilis datserisas, saredaktsio kolegiam gamoiqena shemdegi literatura: 
 k.r.makkoneli, s.l.briu- ekonomiksi 
 shenishvna: 
  . lektsiebi ibechdeba shemoklebit. 
  .imis gamo, rom lektsiebi ikitkheboda   tslis sektembridan, zogiertma movlenam, mkitkhvelis mier krebulis tsakitkhvis dghistvis, dakarga aktualoba, sheidzina skhva mnishvneloba, tumtsa ar daukargavs mimzidveloba ekonomikis sakitkhebze momushave zhurnalistebistvis.

 damoukidebel zhurnalistta saertashoriso aliansis 
 gamgeobis tavmjdomare 
 kartuli zhurnalistika dghes 
 dametankhmebit, albat, adamiani tavisuplad– tavis uplad aris shobili. samtsukharod, kartuli sazogadoebistvis ase nanatri tavisupleba mdzime jvari aghmochnda, anarkiad ikna aghkmuli da shedegmats ar daaqovna– bolo  -  tselia sakartveloshi ganukitkhaoba da kaosi supevs. 
 rats sheekheba zhurnalistebs, gamonakliss arts isini tsarmoadgenen, zhurnalistebits amave sazogadoebis tsevrebi arian da analogiuri ghirebulebebit khelmdzghvaneloben. 
 gasuli saukunis  -iani tslebidan kartuli zhurnalistikistvis daitsqo akhali era, era sitqvis tavisuplebisa. sheidzleba mavani shegvekamatos, rom“mochvenebitia qvelaperi, arts sakartveloa taviuspali da arts misi mediao” da cheshmaritebis martsvali, albat, amashits aris, magram absoluturad tavisupali, rogorts amboben, mkholod gizhia. tavisupleba, rogorts adrets aghvnishnet, ar nishnavs qvelapris uplebas. rodesats sazogadoebis mavani tsevri tavisuplebebs itsavs, mas unda akhsovdes, rom sakutari uplebebis datsva ar nishnavs skhvisi uplebebis shelakhvas. 
 samtsukharod, es martivi cheshmariteba qvelas avitsqdeba, mat shoris chvens kolegebsats. albat, unda gvtsodnoda, rom   tsliani“damokidebuli” qopa,   tslis ganmavlobashi chamoqalibebuli mentaliteti,   tselitsadshi ver sheitsvleboda. tskhadia, unda tsinastsarve gangvesazghvra, magram. . . 
 mshoblis sikharuls sazghvari ara akvs, rodesats tvalqurs adevnebs, tu rogor tamashobs misi pirmsho satamashoebit, magram ubedurebaa, rodesats igive satamashoebit zrdasruli admiani ertoba. droa, chvents, zhurnalistebits davvazhkatsdet da sabavshvo askidan gamovidet. 
 erti pormatsiidan meoreshi gadasvla rtuli da mtkivneuli protsesia. sakartvelo, romelits peodalizmidan, sheidzleba itkvas, ise gadavida sotsializmshi(skhva sakitkhia, iqo tu ara is, rats chven gaviaret, sotsializmi, misi klasikuri gagebit), rom kapitalizmis pirobebshi praktikulad ar gvitskhovria. mit umetes gasagebia,tu ratom ver gaitavisa chveni kveqnis mosakhleobis absoluturma umravlesobam sabazro ekonomikis printsipebi, ratom mokhda aseti ghrma diperentsiatsia sazogadoebashi, ratom aghmochnda mosakhleobis daakhloebit   protsentis khelshi mteli simdidre d aratom tskhovrobs danarcheni sighatakis zghvarze (zogi zemot, zogits kvemot). 
 ai, stsored ak iqo sachiro masmediis tanadgoma, sabazro ekonomikis protsesis ganmarteba, misi garduvalobis, autsileblobis propaganda, mosakhleobis eiporiidan gamoqvana. samtsukharod, es ar mokhda. ar mokhda imitom, rom tavad zhurnalistta korpusi, masobrivi inpormatsiis sashualebebi ar aghmochndnen amistvis mzad. verts aghmochndebodnen. zhurnalistebis dzveli taoba tavad ver erkveoda da verts epueboda sabazro ekonomikas. akhalgazrdebs ki tsodnats aklda da gamotsdilebats (gamonaklisze ar vlaparakob). 
 gakhsovt, albat,  ra periodi iqo– gautavebeli kinklaoba kartvelebs shoris, romelits siskhliani gadatrialebita da samokalako omit dasrulda. tumtsa ra dasrulda, akhlats khom samokalako omshi vart chaplulni, magram amjerad “tsiv omshi”.  jgupebd, klanebad, regionebad daqopili sakartvelos mosakhleoba, sinamdvileshi shors aris realobis aghkmisagan, mas, iseve, rogorts saertod adamians, “siskhli stsquria”. gaikhsenet, msoplios mraval kveqanashi, mat shoris ganvitarebulsa da demokratulshits ki, rogori aghtatsebit umzeren kharis tsamebas koridaze, adamianebis dasiskhlianebul sakheebs tsesebis gareshe brdzolis dros da a.sh. 
 makhsovs, rogori siamovnebit vuqurebdit  -iani tslebis pirvel nakhavarshi sakartvelos parlamentis skhdomebs. ara, is ki ar gvaghelvebda tu ra kanonebs ighebda parlamenti, ra momavals gvimzadebdnen, ra kveqanas vashenebdit, aramed is, tu vin vis sheuratskhqopda, sheaskhamda tsqals, sheaginebda, gaartqamda. stsored aman ganapiroba is, rom gadashli gazets,  chartav televizors tu radios da. . . ighvreba boghma, balghami. rats upro metia siskhli da sibindzure, meti mkitkhveli, maqurebeli da msmeneli hqavs sainpormatsio organos. samtsukharod, imis natsvlad, rom masmedias mosakhleobis inpormirebulobis, ganatlebis, intelektis, sulierebis, zneobis donis amaghlebaze ezruna, tavad davida “qviteli presis” doneze, momkhmareblis qvelaze mdabali motkhovnilebebis dakmaqopilebaze gaaketa orientatsia (ikneb arts aris gasakviri, sabazro ekonomika khom motkhovna-motsodebazea agebuli). 
 martali gitkhrat, medikosebis mshurs, erti mshvenieri printsipi akvt - “tu ar shegidzlia daekhmaro, nu avneb” (martalia mravalma medikosma daivitsqa es printsipi, magram davitsqeba ar arsebobas khom ar nishnavs). 
 chvents am printsips avighebt sapudzvlad. zhurnalistebi, romlebits treningebs gadian evraziis pondis proektis (“ekonomika da zhurnalistika”) parglebshi moismenen chveni kveqnisa da utskhoeli speitsialistebis lektsiebs, gaetsnobian samkhret kavkasiis kveqnebis masmediis mushaobas, praktikas gaivlian masobrivi inpormatsiis sashualebebshi, moamzadeben internet-biuletens “samkhret kavkasiis kveqnebis ekonomika”, monatsileobas miigheben internet-konperentsiebshi, chamoqalibdebian propesionalebad, romlebits ekonomikuri sakitkhebis gashukebisas isaubreben ekonomikur problemebze, mati gadachris gzebze da ara imaze, tu erti partiis tsarmomadgenlebma rogor stsemes motsinaaghmdege partiis tsarmomadgeneli, romelighats ekonomikuri kanonis gankhilvisas. 
 tskhadia, tsema-tqepasats akvs tavis adgili zhurnalistikashi, magram ekonomikuri problemebis gankhilvisas igi tsentralur temad ar unda tsarmovachinot. 
 chveni survilia, zhurnalistebi, romlebits monatsileoben evraziis pondis proektshi - “ekonomika da zhurnalistika”, iqvnen obiekturni, miukerdzoebelni, erkveodnen sakitkhebshi, romlebzets tseren, itsavdnen zhurnalituri etikis normebs, emsakhurebodnen kveqnis ekonomikuri dzlierebis, misi mosakhleobis ketildgheobis donis amaghlebas. 
 bodishs gikhdit, martiv cheshmaritebebze rom gesaubrebit, magram: 
 nu shegeshindebat avtoritetebis, gaakritiket nebismieri– tu migachniat, rom kritikas imsakhurebs, magram nu sheuratskhqopt, tsils nu dastsamebt respondents. 
 sakamato sakitkhis gankhilvisas nu ahqvebit emotsiebs, “ketilismsurvelta” rchevebs, nu moektsevit ert-erti mkharis gavlenis kvesh - mousminet qvelas, autsileblad orive dapirispirebul mkhares, kholo daskvna gamoitanet piradad, mkholod kanonze daqrdnobit. 
 iqavit pasukhismgebeli qovel tkvens sitqvaze, qovel daskvnaze. 
 ebrdzolet uzustobas. tkveni nebismieri masala unda pasukhobdes mkitkhvelta kitkhvebs da ar tovebdes “tetr lakebs”. 
 tu respondenttan saubrisas rame ver gaiget, nu dauknevt “chkvianuri gamometqvelebit” tavs tankhmobis nishnad, ikve gaarkviet, rats tkventvis gaugebari iqo. nu shegeshindebat imisa, rom dagtsineben gautvittsnobiereblobis gamo. gatsilebit uaresia, rodesats shegatqoben, rom “uazrod” akanturebt tavs. tu avadmqopuri tavmoqvareoba gatsukhebt, gakhsovdet, rom kveqnad ar arsebobs adamiani, romelits zedmitsevnit erkveodes absoluturad qvela sakitkhshi. bodishs gikhdit aseti sastiki gamotkmebis gamo, magram minda gavamakhvilo tkveni quradgheba im shetsdomebze, romlebits stsored akhalbeda zhurnalistebs mosdit. 
 gakhsovdet, zhurnalisti ar emsakhureba pirovnebas – raoden maghali tanamdebobats ar unda ekavos mas. banalurad zhghers, magram tkven kveqnisa da khalkhis msakhuri brdzandebit. etsadet gaaertianet eri, nu daupirispirebt khalkhs ertmanets. ebrdzolet tezisis – “gatishe da ibatone” qovel gamovlinebas. 
 aseti shegonebebi usasrulod sheidzleba isminot, magram mkholod tkven individualur tvisebebze, sulier samqaroze, intelektze, nichze,  ojakhisshvilobazea damokidebuli, tu ras miighebt da ras uarqopt, ra gzas airchevt. 
 vinaidan umaghlesi ganatleba natsils mighebuli gakvt, natsili ki jer kidev stsavlis protsesshia, chavtvalot, rom garkveuli sapudzveli gagachniat. ekvstviani spetsialuri kursi ekonomikasa da zhurnalistikashi kidev upro gaadzlierebs tkveni ganatlebis sapudzvlebs, mitumetes, rom lektorebad cheshmaritad umaghlesi donis kartveli da utskhoeli spetsialistebi gveqoleba. miukhedavad amisa, dghes maints minda gagatsnot msoplio zhurnalistur praktikashi aprobirebuli erti martivi metodi imisa, tu rogor unda datserot inpormatsia. es dzalze martivia. ai, is ekvsi kitkhva, razets unda gastset pasukhi, gasagebi da saintereso rom iqot mkitkhvelistvis: 
 ra?      - ra mokhda? 
 vin?     - vis gamo mokhda es? vin gaaketa es? misi asaki, skesi, shesakhedaoba, tanamdebobada, saertod qvelaperi, 
 rasats kavshiri akvs momkhdartan 
 sad?      - sad mokhda es? 
 rodis?   - shemtkhvevis dro da tarighi 
 rogor?  - rogor mokhda es? mietsit ganmarteba momkhdars 
 ratom?   -  ratom mokhda es? 
 tu imdens shesdzlebt, rom tavidan aitsilebt abstraktul msjelobas da gamoiqenebt konkretul detalebs, mashin konkurentunarian zhurnalistad chamoqalibdebit. 
 ai, khom khedavt, ra martivia iqo zhurnalisti?! 
 shenishvna – danarcheni lektsiebis nebismier enaze targamani shegidzliat dagvikvetot. 
 qvela khalkhi imsakhurebs im khelisuplebas, romelits hqavs! kidev ertkhel sazogadoebrivi ganatlebebisa da samokalako sazogadoebis arsebobis autsileblo... 
 aris khelovnebis nimushebi, romlebits msoplio sagandzurs miekutvneba. aris pilmebi, romlebsats kinematograpiis shedevrebad aghiareben. msopliosi namdvilad... 
 ( . .   "redaktoris sveti")   „dadis da sitsrues avrtselebs!?“ brdzana premierma ivanishvilma prezident saakashvilz... 
  . .    .qopili khelisuplebis ltolvilebisadmi damokidebuleba araadamianuri iqo. zrunva chven tanamemamuleebze, romlebits sakutar kveqanash... 
  . .   sakartvelom, iseve rogorts postsotsialisturi, postsabchota  sivrtsis mravalma kveqanam, gasuli saukunis  - –iani tsle... 
 barbi da misi sauketeso megobrebi - tereza da rene, mondomebuli tanmovarjisheebisgan gadaiktsevian saidumlo agentebad. am tavgadasavalshi, gogoebi ertmanettan kargad atavseben parkurs da tanvarjishs… 
 rodesats nanos babua moulodnelad avad gakhda, ushishari shvilishvili da misi sauketeso megobari lili gamoiqeneben mankanas, romelits ekhmareba mat zomis shemtsirebashi da tsavlen sarisko mogzaurobashi babuis gadasarchenad… 
   tslis sektemberi. prangul mtis patara sopelshi qvela aghsanishnavs omis damtavrebas. sebastiani gaizarda - is ukve   tslisaa. beltan ertad isini moutmenlad elian anjelinas dabrunebas. tumtsa, mogvianebit gairkveva, rom gogona moqva aviakatastropashi alpebis mighma tqis shuagulshi. mtelma sopelma imedi dakarga, garda sebastianis babua tsezaris, romelits itsnobs piers - katss, romelsats sheudzlia daekhmaros anjelinas povnashi 
 sabedistsero shemtkhvevitobit ashsh–is prezidentis dzaghli tedi ert–erti mogzaurobis dros daikarga. dzaghls poulobs patara, chveulebrivi bichuna sakhelad deni. aravin ujerebs mas, rom tedi prezidentis dzaghlia. deni gadatsqvitavs gaiktses bavshvta sakhlidan, rom daubrunos tedi patrons… 
 mamiko charli khintoni da pil reisoni sakutar tavze igheben bavshvta sazapkhulo banakis khelmdzghvanelobas. ara akvt aranairi tsarmodgena rogor itskhovron ughran tqeshi, dapakhpakhebuli da nakhevrad dangreuli shenobebis remontze da mousvenar bavshvebtan urtiertobaze. charli da pili maleve kargaven situatsiaze kontrols. rom qvelaperi sabolood ar mospon da ar dakargon samushao, charli dasakhmareblad idzakhebs tavis mamas polkovnik baka khintons, romeltanats didi khania kavshiri gatsqvetili akvs. da akhla man unda daamqaros banakshi tsesrigi, sheinakhos kolektivi da astsavlos bavshvebs gamdzleoba da shemtsqnarebloba… 
 lemurebi aghmochndnen kundzulze milionobit tslis tsin da tandatan ganitsades evolutsia asobit skhvadaskhva sakheobebit. dghes, es unikalur tskhovelebi gadashenebis saprtkhis kvesh arian… 
 es aris ikingis da misi drakoni ukbilos tavgadasavlebis gagrdzeleba cherchetis kundzulze, drakonebis mtsvrtnelebis jguptan ertad, romeltagan titoeuls ukve hqavs sakutari drakoni. seriali itsqeba srulmetrazhiani pilmi “rogor movarjulot drakoni” movlenebis shemdeg, sadats ikingi mimemgzavreba mis ertgul drakon ukbilostan da skhva bavshvebtan ertad skhva adgilebshi, sadats isini aghmoachenen sruliad akhal drakonebs, ipovian akhal tavgadasavalebs da sheebrdzolebian akhal borotmokmedebs. 
 moukherkhebeli uolesi da misi ertguli dzaghli gromiti nadiroben utsnur tskhovelze, romelmats mati stapilos da kartopilis mosavali gaanadgura bostneulis konkursis tsin… 
 patara bichi sakhelad maksi dasajes da tavis sadzinebelshi chaketes. is ebrdzvis motsqenilobas, itsqebs otsnebas da tsotakhanshi mikhvdeba, rom otakhi romelshits is chaketes gakra da otakhis natsvlad aghmochndeba patara navshi, romelits utsnob sanapiros miuakhlovdeba. kveqana sadats bichi aghmochnda, mtavari gmiri tsarmoadges qvelaze sazarel tskhovels, da am tskhovelebs maksi erti gamokhedvit atvinierebs. sazareli tskhovelebi gadatsqveten am utsnauri arsebis meped aghiarebas. ertkhelats bichunas moenatreba sakhli, sadats is namdvilad uqvart…. 
 sashualo skolis ori sruliad ganskhvavebuli mostsavle, gadatsqvitavs parulad tsavides musikalur mosmenaze, rats mtel mat tskhovrebas da skolasats tavdaqira aqenebs… 
 akhali sagadasakhado kodeksis tanakhmad, gadamkhdelebis uplebebs ori akhali instituti daitsavs: pinansta ministris tavmjdomareobit sheikmneba khuti tsevrisgan shemdgari auditorta sabcho. premier-ministrma prezentatsiisas aghnishna, rom tuki dajarimeba daemukreba kompanias, romelits manamde sagadasakhado gadatsdomebis gareshe sakmianobda, sagadasakhados moutsevs am sabchosgan moipovos kompaniis dajarimebis upleba. sagadasakhado kodeksis samushao versiashi  -e mukhli ambobs, rom tu sagadasakhado shemotsmebis shedegebze gadatsqvetilebis migheba aqalibebs arsebulisagan ganskhvavebul dabegvris an sanktsiis gamoqenebis printsips, sagadasakhado organos upleba akvs, mimartos auditorta sabchos, romelits tavis mkhriv, uplebamosilia mimartvidan araugvianes   dghisa miighos gadatsqvetileba aghnishnuli printsipis/metodis gamoqenebis an argamoqenebis shesakheb. auditorta sabchos gadatsqvetilebis shesruleba savaldebuloa sagadasakhado organosatvis. am mukhltan dakavshirebit ramdenime problema arsebobs. pirveli - tu sagadasakhado organo ar ikneba valdebuli, mimartos auditorta sabchos da, meore mkhriv, tu tviton auditorta sabcho ar ikneba valdebuli, rom miighos gadatsqvetileba, mashin sruliad gaugebaria, saertod ratom unda arsebobdes es damatebiti rgoli. meore - ukve arsebobs davebis sabcho, romelits ighebs sagadasakhado davastan dakavshirebul gadatsqvetilebebs. mesame - amave kodeksis  -e mukhli aregulirebs stsored imas, rasats emsakhureba auditorta sabcho - aqalibebs administrirebis ertian praktikas. kerdzod, im shemtkhvevashi tu davebis sabchos gadatsqvetileba dabegvris an sanktsiis datsesebis ganskhvavebul printsips an metods nergavs, an tu igi mnishvnelovania ertiani praktikis chamoqalibebisatvis, gadatsqvetilebis mighebidan   tvis vadashi sakartvelos pinansta ministri gamostsems sajaro gadatsqvetilebas. amdenad, sajaro gadatsqvetileba ukve asrulebs im sakmes, rats auditorta sabchos evaleba. meore akhali institutia sagadasakhado ombudsmeni, romelits zedamkhedvelobas gautsevs sakartvelos teritoriaze gadasakhadis gadamkhdelta uplebebisa da kanonieri interesebis datsvas, gamoavlens mati darghvevis paktebs da khels sheutsqobs darghveuli uplebebis aghdgenas. „gvinda bizness sagadasakhado tskhovreba gavumartivot”, - ganatskhada premier-ministrma. ert-erti mtavari problema, romelits metsarmeebs gansakutrebit atsukhebt, aris mati satsarmoebis dalukva sagadasakhado shemotsmebebis dros; kompaniebi mnishvnelovnad zaraldebian, damtsqebi biznesistvis ki, khangrdzlivi shemotsmebis pirobebshi, sheidzleba gakotrebis saprtkhets gachndes. akhali sagadasakhado kodeksis  -e mukhlis me-  punkti mkholod zogadad ambobs, rom sagadasakhado kontrolis protsedurebma, gonivrul parglebshi, ar unda daarghvios piris sakmianobis chveuli ritmi da ar unda gaacheros misi sakmianoba. akhal kodeksshi isev ar aris gatserili, ra shemtkhvevashi da ra vadit sheidzleba satsarmos dalukva misi shemotsmebis miznit. amdenad, sagadasakhado sistemis mimart sandoobis amaghleba da biznesistvis sagadasakhado tskhovrebis gamartiveba didtsilad ikneba damokidebuli imaze, tu sabolood ra pormit damtkitsdeba kodeksi. 
 am sakitkhtan dakavshirebit, “humaniti jorjiasa” da “sapartnioro pondis” ertoblivi preskonperentsia sastumro “redisonshi shedga”, romelsats parmatsevtuli kompaniebis khelmdzghvanelebits estsrebodnen. 
 rogorts “sapartnioro pondis” aghmasrulebelma direktorma, davit saganelidzem ganatskhada, khelmisatsvdomi preparatebis realizatsiis proekti sakartvelos mtavrobis gadatsqvetilebis sapudzvelze “humaniti jorjiasa” da “sapartnioro pondis” mier ertoblivad khortsieldeba. 
 “preparatebis importi shemdgom etapze preparatebis adgilobrivi tsarmoebit chanatsvldeba. aghnishnul proektshi “sapartnioro pondis” chartvis mizania adgilobrivi parmatsevtuli satsarmos amokmedebamde uzrunvelqopili iqos sakartvelos bazarze khariskhiani medikamentebis mitsodeba sul mtsire   %-it dabali pasebit, rats mnishvnelovanad sheamtsirebs saqoveltao jandatsvis programit gatvalistsinebul medikamentebis kharjebsats. aghnishnuli miznit “sapartnioro pondma” mtavrobis tankhmobit “humaniti jorjias” miznobrivi seskhi gamouqo. aseve, stsored mtavrobis gadatsqvetilebit shedis karkhnis msheneblobis kapitalshi sapartnioro pondi. 
 khelisuplebis mizani mightseulia, sameditsino preparatebi iapdeba. es iqo tsinasaarchevno dapirebats. rats sheekheba “humaniti jorjias” mier shemotanili medikamentebis khariskhs, jandatsvis saministro akontrolebs da sakartvelos saaptiako dakhlebze sertipikatisa da shesabamisi dokumentatsiis gareshe verts erti medikamenti ver mokhvdeba. me vamaqob, rom “humaniti jorjia” aleksandre mashkevichis sakhels ukavshirdeba. is gakhlavt msoplioshi tsnobili biznesmeni, romelits sakartvelos parmatsevtuli bazrit dainteresda da mskhvili investitsiis gankhortsielebasats gegmvas, radgan miachnia, rom chvens kveqanashi aris datsuli biznesi, mimzidveli sagadasakho rezhimi da sainvestitsio pirobebi”, – ganatskhada saganelidzem. 
 “humaniti jorjias” investitsiebi gatvlilia grdzelvadian periodze da mati mizania konkurentuli garemos khelshetsqoba, khariskhian sameditsino momsakhurebaze khelmisatsvdomobis gazrda da medikamentebze pasebis shemtsireba. 
 “humaniti jorjia”, es aris dinamiurad ganvitarebadi kompania, romelits ambitsiuri gegmebit shemodis sakartvelos parmatsevtul bazarze da surs damkvidrdes parmatsevtul biznesshi, rogorts khelmisatsvdomi, usaprtkho da khariskhiani preparatebis mimtsodebeli kompania”, – natkvamia “sapartnioro pondis” inpormatsiashi.

 nato-m ruset-sakartvelos   tslis agvistos omis me-  tslistavtan dakavshirebit dokumenturi pilmi moamzada. “sakartvelos gadautsqveteli konplikti”, - ase etsodeba pilms, romelshits motkhrobilia im devnilta istoriebi, romlebsats sheiaraghebuli konpliktis gamo, sakutari sakhlebis datoveba moutsiat.
